Chapter 1630: Birth of a Saint

Li Fan not only had no intention of scolding him but even looked excited.

"Traversing the Mountains and Seas, I finally found someone who shares my ideals today!"

Saying this, Li Fan casually unleashed a flame.

The raging fire instantly ignited the remnants of the possibility.

Ho Gan Immortal, who was originally hostile, was stunned.

"If I wish to overturn the Mountains and Seas, fellow Daoist, would you join me?"

Li Fan asked with extreme sincerity.

The last remnants of possibility were completely burned away in the True Spirit's fire.

The waves of Dao Annihilation surged towards them.

Above Li Fan's head, a solitary sail was suspended, resisting the Devouring of Dao Annihilation.

As for Ho Gan Immortal's situation, it was quite strange.

It was as if an invisible vortex existed around him, and the Dao Annihilation that flowed and eroded, after a period of circulation, was actually directed towards other areas of the Mountains and Seas.

Naturally, innocent possibilities suffered as a result, but Ho Gan Immortal, who had already left the state of Dao Comprehension, no longer felt any guilt in his heart.

In the turbulent Dao Annihilation, Li Fan and Ho Gan Immortal faced each other.

"Overturn the Mountains and Seas?" Ho Gan Immortal carefully savored these four words.

"The great tide of Dao Annihilation surges mightily. Follow it and prosper, defy it and perish! The Shore and the Saint Dynasty are but like striking a stone with an egg. Hopeless struggle only brings ridicule!"

"Why not follow the general trend, destroy the Mountains and Seas, and return to the Divine Stars. When order is rebuilt in the future, perhaps you and I can be canonized for our merits!"

"Fellow Daoist, what do you think?" Li Fan said with extreme fervor.

The Mountains and Seas seemed to fall into deathly silence.

Only the surging waves of Dao Annihilation silently devoured the innocent and unsuspecting possibilities.

"What kind of trash..."

Silently gazing at Li Fan, Ho Gan Immortal actually uttered such an evaluation after a while.

"Die!"

As if too lazy to waste words with Li Fan, Ho Gan Immortal reached out towards Li Fan from afar and grabbed.

Not only were the surrounding Dao Annihilation and Li Fan's unleashed True Spirit Fire affected, forming shackles like a vortex of confinement, but Li Fan's heart also immediately flashed with his past actions.

Destroying the Profound Yellow Realm, destroying the Utmost Dark Star Sea, destroying the high walls, destroying the Northern Star Sea, destroying the Primordial, igniting the Mountains and Seas...

The scale of the calamities created gradually expanded.

The number of beings who died in the calamities also increased exponentially.

What was originally just a string of numbers now transformed into specific faces, roaring in anger within Li Fan's heart.

As if vengeful spirits were coming to claim their lives!

Facing these countless vengeful spirits he had caused the deaths of, if Li Fan harbored the slightest guilt, he would have been affected, his mind shaken, or even lost control, and finally swallowed by these evolved vengeful spirits.

But...

Li Fan watched these suddenly appearing countless vengeful spirits with extreme indifference from beginning to end. His heart was completely motionless.

He even had a hint of doubt in his eyes.

As if these deceased vengeful spirits had nothing to do with him!

If Ho Gan Immortal's "What does it have to do with me?" was a fierce conflict between his remaining conscience and his self, then Li Fan's "What does it have to do with me?" was a simple, emotionless rhetorical question.

Ho Gan Immortal still had remnants of conscience.

Then Li Fan was...

Facing Li Fan, who was even more like "Ho Gan Immortal" than himself, Ho Gan Immortal inexplicably felt a sense of fear and instinctively wanted to escape.

However, before him, strands of True Spirit Fire suddenly erupted, blocking his path.

"Where are you going, fellow Daoist? Could it be that you believe the Mountains and Seas can still be saved?" Li Fan questioned sternly.

His previous actions were precisely for this sentence.

His voice was like thunder, striking Ho Gan Immortal's heart. Ho Gan Immortal's body trembled violently.

"Can the Mountains and Seas be saved?"

Li Fan pressed relentlessly, continuing to question.

The True Spirit Fire and the waves of Dao Annihilation complemented each other.

As water drowned and fire burned, a terrifying wave of annihilation spread through the Mountains and Seas. Even though, at first, it only affected a negligible amount of possibility.

But with Li Fan's insistent questioning, this terrifying catastrophe spread at an unimaginable speed.

Watching as it became unstoppable!

Trapped between the True Spirit Fire and the Dao Annihilation, having tried several times to escape but finding no way out, and seeing the spreading catastrophe covering the land, the increasingly pressured Ho Gan Immortal finally couldn't hold on any longer.

He roared in a choked voice, "Of course the Mountains and Seas can be saved! The one who can save the Mountains and Seas is only me, the Virtuous Immortal!"

Finally, Li Fan had forced out the deepest thought in his heart.

Li Fan, however, relentlessly continued to question, "Virtuous Immortal? Who exactly are you?"

"Do you have Dao? Do you have Virtue?"

Ho Gan Immortal refused to answer, staring at the Mountains and Seas gradually being engulfed by water and fire, his heart growing increasingly anxious.

He rushed left and right, trying to break through Li Fan's blockade.

However, his strength was already inferior to Li Fan's. The True Spirit Fire and the waves of Dao Annihilation were powers that could even devour the Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan was not confronting him head-on, but merely using the power of burning mountains and annihilating seas to surround him.

Ho Gan Immortal, with all his might, was for a time helpless, like a trapped beast in a cage, letting out sounds of pain.

"Do you have Dao? Do you have Virtue?"

Li Fan's questioning never stopped.

Each sound was like a sharp sword, piercing into Ho Gan Immortal's heart.

Ho Gan Immortal's eyes turned red, and even blood tears flowed out: "I saved the Mountains and Seas, how can I be without Virtue? I saved the Mountains and Seas, how can I be without Dao?"

The first "I saved the Mountains and Seas" was a thought, an idea.

The latter "I saved the Mountains and Seas" was concrete action and measures.

Hearing Ho Gan Immortal finally roar out this sentence, Li Fan nodded with satisfaction.

Then, his eyes revealed a cold glint, and with a wave of his hand, the True Spirit Fire burned even more vigorously.

More possibilities were affected by the flames, which surged towards the sky, completely obscuring Ho Gan Immortal's vision.

He could no longer see the Mountains and Seas, only endless flames.

From Ho Gan Immortal's perspective, it was equivalent to Li Fan burning the Mountains and Seas before his eyes.

Not only that, Li Fan then sternly questioned, "The Mountains and Seas were burned to ashes before your eyes. Did you save the Mountains and Seas?"

"How can you have Dao?"

With a final blow, Ho Gan Immortal was struck by lightning, his body stiffening andmotionless.

"Do I have Dao? Do I have Dao? Do I have Dao..."

He kept muttering to himself.

Finally, the firelight flickering in his pupils gave him the answer.

"The Mountains and Seas are burned to ashes, I have no Dao."

"I have Virtue, but no Dao."

"I have Virtue, but no Dao..."

The moment he said this, Ho Gan Immortal's body instantly became translucent.

And behind Li Fan, another figure quietly appeared.

However, Li Fan seemed to have expected his appearance!

"Because he is devoid of virtue, he lost his face."

"Your lack of virtue is not due to being affected by Ho Gan Immortal. It is because you are truly devoid of virtue!"

"Ho Gan Immortal appears to be without virtue, but in reality, he has virtue. Because all sins are committed for the sake of saving the Mountains and Seas. If the Mountains and Seas are saved, all sins will be erased."

"Virtuous Immortal, Virtuous Immortal. Ho Gan Immortal is Virtue, and you are..."

"Dao!"

With rhythmic claps, it came from the figure behind Li Fan.

It was the Faceless Immortal!

"A brilliant deduction!"

"I didn't expect you to be able to see our true nature. I thought I could use your strength to temporarily hinder his progress, but I never imagined you would do better than I expected."

"You were even able to directly categorize him."

"Truly amazing!"

The Faceless Immortal licked his lips with enjoyment as he looked at the incorporeal Ho Gan Immortal.

Ho Gan Immortal, who was not the slightest bit resistant, was absorbed into the Faceless Immortal's body.

After a moment of stillness, the aura emanating from the Faceless Immortal swelled exponentially!

As if a mortal ascended to immortality in one day!

The Faceless Immortal, who was originally extremely weak and only at the True Immortal level, now seemed to have not only inherited Ho Gan Immortal's realm and strength but also achieved some kind of qualitative transformation in his cultivation.

From the realm of Transcension, he took a step towards the path of becoming a Saint!

With the two united, the figure of Ho Gan Immortal, or rather, the [Virtuous Immortal], became more solidified.

His voice also changed. At first, it was a superposition of two voices, and then it gradually merged completely, no longer distinguishing between them.

"It has been 100,000 years in the Immortal Realm, and today I am finally complete."

"Thank you, fellow Daoist, for your help!"

The Virtuous Immortal, having completed his path to enlightenment, actually bowed to Li Fan!

"However, there is one point where you are mistaken."

"I am not Dao, and he is not Virtue."

"Dao and Virtue separated, yet Dao and Virtue are not separated."

"He is also like this."

The Virtuous Immortal's originally ethereal face slowly grew features.

He looked at Li Fan and smiled, saying: "Before we were finally [qualified], I was Dao, and he was Virtue. He was Virtue, and I was Dao."

"It's just that we chose different paths of evolution."

"I abandoned Virtue, he stuck to Virtue."

"However, my chosen Dao did not bring me the power I expected."

"And the Virtue he upheld, of saving the Mountains and Seas, and acting unscrupulously, has allowed his strength to advance by leaps and bounds."

"Originally, I was at a disadvantage and was about to fail in this race."

"Unexpectedly, unexpectedly..."

The Virtuous Immortal said with great emotion.

"Virtuous Immortal, Virtuous Immortal. Dao gives birth to Virtue, and Virtue transforms into Dao. Dao and Virtue cannot be separated!"

"This is the foundation of our existence. Even if we evolve in different directions, this point has not disappeared. If one completely loses Dao, or completely loses Virtue..."

"The basis of its existence will disappear. The consequence..."

The Virtuous Immortal's smile instantly vanished: "Is to return to one's original self."

Facing the seemingly unexpected situation, Li Fan was not alarmed.

Instead, he looked at the newly enlightened Virtuous Immortal with great interest: "So, now, do you have more Dao or more Virtue? Did you achieve enlightenment through Virtue, or through Dao?"

The Virtuous Immortal shook his head: "Whether it is Dao or Virtue is not important. What is important is who can truly reach the end."

"The victor is the Saint."

A vast aura surged from the Virtuous Immortal's body.

Like a surging wind, it instantly repelled the raging True Spirit Fire and the waves of Dao Annihilation.

Even while conversing, the Virtuous Immortal's aura had been continuously expanding.

Now, as if breaking through some kind of shackle, the intensity of his aura's expansion increased hundreds of times over.

The flames and Dao Annihilation that could devour the Mountains and Seas were suppressed by this aura of becoming a Saint.

A world-shattering radiance surged from a corner of the possibility, shooting up into the sky.

It shook the Mountains and Seas!

"Although you helped me achieve enlightenment. However..."

The [Virtue], who had just attained Sainthood, looked at Li Fan, but a strange expression suddenly appeared in his eyes.

Without any warning, his left palm pressed down like the sky collapsing.

Without even finishing a sentence, he offered Li Fan no time to react!

At the same time, it seemed as if sensing the birth of a new Saint, the Shore, the Saint Dynasty, and other areas of the Mountains and Seas,

Simultaneously cast their attention.

[Virtue] completely ignored them, his target solely being Li Fan.

"So..."

"You Saints are really annoying."

A hazy water curtain-like mist enveloped Li Fan.

As if in a state between reality and illusion, the palm of Virtue that descended from the sky passed through Li Fan's body as if it were empty space.

It was unable to cause any harm!

Virtue seemed to have anticipated this, his eyes showing a hint of surprise as he stared at the mist on Li Fan's body.

He opened his mouth, as if about to say something.

But in the end, he did not speak.

Instead, he began to chant solemnly.

Bound by Virtue's palm, Li Fan's vision of the Mountains and Seas disappeared.

It was just like Ho Gan Immortal's situation before, trapped between the True Spirit Fire and the Dao Annihilation.

What a cycle!

In Li Fan's eyes, the world became chaotic.

Black and white energies surged from all directions.

They formed a vortex around Li Fan, rotating slowly.

As the vortex spun, the water curtain mist rippled layer by layer!

"Is this... the power of a Saint?"

"It's nothing special!"

Li Fan smiled with difficulty.

Under the cover of the mist-like water curtain, his body even became nine-tenths transparent.

Bai Shuyue had reincarnated nearly thirty times, and Li Fan had not idled away his time.

With each True Reversion, his understanding of the transformation of true and false deepened.

"What is true becomes false, and what is false becomes true..."

Li Fan had already achieved a minor success in his understanding of these seven characters.

Coupled with the accumulation of these twenty-eight lifetimes, he had reached the threshold for qualitative breakthrough.

This layer of water curtain mist outside his body was precisely the defense he had woven with the transformation of true and false.

Covered by the mist-like water curtain, he was in a state of true and false, virtual and real.

Even a Saint could not harm him in the slightest!

Originally, Li Fan had not deduced this divine ability to such an extent, and the water curtain mist could only last for three breaths.

But after witnessing [Virtue] become a Saint with his own eyes, Li Fan's mind was filled with inspiration, like countless fireworks igniting, bursting forth intensely.

Especially the scene where Ho Gan Immortal and the Faceless Immortal were both in an uncertain state between Dao and Virtue, which gave Li Fan inspiration.

True and False, Dao and Virtue.

In the hidden heavens and earth, there were some similarities.

Li Fan gained insights through analogy, and suddenly understood, thus managing to weave this water curtain mist outer layer.

And it was precisely because of this divine ability that Li Fan could remain calm even after witnessing the birth of a Saint and not immediately perform True Reversion.

Li Fan, in front of the illusions of the Nine Saints, had no power to resist.

Having personally experienced the magnificent power of the Saints on the Shore, Li Fan was certain that this [Virtue], who had just attained Sainthood, seemed to be somewhat weaker than those true Saints.

But he was indeed of the same caliber.

If not for the protection of the power of true and false, Li Fan's transcendent strength would have been like an ant before him!

With no room for resistance.

But now...

Even though activating the power of true and false came at a great cost.

His own existence was gradually disappearing as a result.

But after all, he had truly resisted [Virtue]'s suppression!

Even before the water curtain mist protecting him completely dissipated, Li Fan's situation, although seemingly precarious.

In reality, he was as stable as Mount Tai!

From the depths of the Mountains and Seas, rays of light seemed to be approaching.

Their aura did not seem to be weaker than the [Virtue] who had just attained Sainthood.

The protective mist of true and false on his body was also about to be completely consumed.

"True Reversion!"

Li Fan looked up at [Virtue] outside the giant black and white vortex and silently uttered.

Chapter 1631: Secretly Peeping at the Dao of Virtue

A hazy mist emanated from Li Fan, spreading outwards, instantly covering mountains and seas!

The black and white energies intertwined, forming a giant vortex around [Virtue], attempting to reveal its form within the mist.

But ultimately, it was to no avail.

The mist grew denser.

Eventually, it engulfed everything around Li Fan, including the various streams of light observed at the last moment.

The water curtain mist, layer by layer, concealed everything. The world plunged into darkness.

One year anchored!

Successfully True Reverted, Li Fan, having escaped the suppression of [Virtue], remained motionless for a long time.

He chose to retain his aunt's memories from the previous simulation.

"The spring water, imbued with the life force of the entire Mountain and Sea Realm, continuously flowed, indeed capable of resurrecting my aunt, who had only recently passed away with her body intact."

"But it was a slow process, requiring at least a hundred years. In the previous life, only fifty years had passed, and my aunt's consciousness had not yet fully awakened..."

After carefully reviewing his aunt's memories to ensure there were no flaws, Li Fan then chose to pass them on to her.

With True Reversion in hand, everything was under control.

In this 'Cultivating Saints' plan, Li Fan held absolute initiative.

The possibility of Bai Shuyue discovering the truth behind the scenes was virtually zero.

At least, not before she became a Saint.

...

Bai Shuyue felt as though she had a very long dream.

In the dream, she had barely escaped from the Faceless Immortal and was heading towards the star sea outside the high wall when she encountered an unknown starry hand.

To avoid the fate of being imprisoned, she resolutely chose to commit suicide.

"Oh, right. It wasn't a dream."

"It was my experience from the previous life," Bai Shuyue rubbed her temples, which ached faintly.

"I don't know if it's my imagination, but I feel like this revival took longer than previous ones."

"Could it be..."

Bai Shuyue's brows suddenly furrowed, and her heart trembled.

"My number of rebirths is not actually infinite, is it?"

"This is certainly not good news for me..." Bai Shuyue became somewhat worried.

Although Bai Shuyue was not a pessimistic person.

But infinite rebirths versus limited rebirths were entirely different matters.

"I wonder what my rebirths are related to. Does each rebirth consume something unknown? Will the number of times increase as my strength grows?"

Bai Shuyue's thoughts ran wild, unable to be controlled.

Setting aside the speculation, the revived Bai Shuyue had already secretly made up her mind. She would no longer listen to the Boundless Wall's instigation to seek cultivation grounds outside the Profound Yellow Realm. Instead, she would diligently cultivate within the Profound Yellow Realm. Judging from her previous life's experience, the outside world was a hundred times more perilous than the Profound Yellow Realm!

Meanwhile, Li Fan, while playing the role of his aunt's good nephew, was also recalling his experiences from the final moments of his previous life.

He had long harbored suspicions about the true moral identity of the Faceless Immortal and Ho Gan Immortal, which was why he didn't hesitate to use the True Spirit Burning technique to force out Ho Gan Immortal's true identity.

However, Li Fan had originally intended to witness Ho Gan Immortal and the Faceless Immortal's frustration after their identities were exposed, but he never expected that...

The Faceless Immortal and Ho Gan Immortal would merge and achieve Sainthood!

Since when did becoming a Saint become so simple?

Although Li Fan did not yet understand how they achieved Sainthood, the concept of being 'the only one in all realms, equal to all mountains and seas' should be the minimum requirement for a Saint.

"When Dao and Virtue merge, one can achieve Sainthood."

"Does this mean that the Faceless Immortal and Ho Gan Immortal, after splitting from Dao and Virtue, were originally unique existences in all realms?"

After some contemplation, Li Fan gained some insight.

"Indeed. If it were the original [True Immortal of Dao and Virtue], perhaps other possibilities within the mountains and seas would have had his counterparts. However, the Faceless Immortal and Ho Gan Immortal were beings that did not exist in the mountains and seas. They were products hatched by the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue using a secret art called [Dao and Virtue Split]. From the moment of their birth, they were unique to the mountains and seas."

"The unification of multiple selves, which others strive for with great effort, was achieved so easily by this True Immortal of Dao and Virtue with just a single technique..."

"However, the ability to split a unique entity of the mountains and seas, this [Dao and Virtue Split] technique itself is extraordinary."

Having quickly resolved the first doubt, Li Fan was still baffled by the second question.

How did Ho Gan Immortal and the Faceless Immortal achieve the same status as the mountains and seas?

After much thought, Li Fan could not find a logical explanation.

He could only speculate that it might be related to the peculiar state they were in.

"Dao and Virtue, seemingly separated yet intrinsically linked, should have been intertwined, making them difficult to distinguish."

"But I forcefully defined their attributes, causing Dao and Virtue to completely split."

"It is like the collapse and transformation of the Great Dao. In that instant, perhaps an enormous amount of energy was released. Much like the chain reaction I knew before my transmigration..." Li Fan fell into wild imagination.

After all, even with the current Li Fan, he could only imagine the answers.

The principles of achieving Sainthood were, in themselves, one of the greatest secrets of the mountains and seas. If Li Fan could unravel the secret of Sainthood merely by observing and simple contemplation, then the number of Saints in the entire mountains and seas would not be so scarce.

"To find the answer, I must start by investigating the Faceless Immortal and the Ho Gan Immortal."

"Although the Faceless Immortal is weak, he has always hidden himself well. It is difficult to even find his whereabouts, let alone capture him alive."

"As for Ho Gan Immortal… I already know that he appears in that possibility at fixed intervals. Perhaps I can set up an ambush in advance."

"Of course, all of this depends on the reset of the mountains and seas after True Reversion is activated."

"The True Immortal of Dao and Virtue, who achieved Sainthood, has been reduced to his original form!"

In fact, Li Fan was not too worried about this.

If [Dao and Virtue] still existed, with the might of a Saint, the vast mountains and seas would undoubtedly allow Him to pinpoint Li Fan immediately.

But now, so much time had passed since Li Fan's True Reversion, yet the mountains and seas remained tranquil.

This was enough to prove that there was no Saint named [Dao and Virtue] in the mountains and seas at this stage!

"The authority of True Reversion surpasses that of the mountains and seas."

"Or perhaps..."

"True Reversion does not reset the mountains and seas. Instead..."

Recalling his own discovery about intuition, Li Fan's heart stirred with a new conjecture.

But like the secret of achieving Sainthood through Dao and Virtue, it was merely an imagined theory without any supporting evidence.

Li Fan could only suppress it in his heart for now.

Having undergone nearly thirty cycles of reincarnation, Li Fan's understanding of the transformation between true and false had reached a new level.

The water curtain mist could withstand the suppression of [Virtue], who had just achieved Sainthood.

Confronting a Saint with transcendence.

This was indeed an astonishing feat in the mountains and seas. However, Li Fan did not feel overconfident.

"The remnants left in the Shore, although mere illusory projections of Saints, the combined might of the Nine Saints is far greater than the [Virtue] I witnessed. My ability to resist [Virtue] does not guarantee my survival against the illusory projections of the Nine Saints. Therefore, the 'Cultivating Saints' plan must continue."

"However... investigating the secret of the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue's path to Sainthood can be carried out simultaneously."

Li Fan left a trace of his illusory projection in the original Profound Yellow Realm and then leaped forward, heading towards the possibility where he witnessed the achievement of Sainthood by Dao and Virtue in his previous life.

"Ho Gan Immortal and the Faceless Immortal should not be underestimated. Preparations must be made in advance!"

Compared to the scenes of destruction Li Fan had witnessed before, the current possibility was still full of life.

The most significant difference from the original possibility was the absence of Duke Shou Qiu.

The Immortal Realm was mostly destroyed by the initial wave of Dao Annihilation.

But precisely because of this, this Immortal Realm was not directly annihilated. Instead, it survived as scattered islands amidst the Dao Annihilation tide!

In his previous encounters with the Dao Annihilation, Li Fan had already understood that the Dao Annihilation seemed to possess its own unique consciousness.

The stronger the resistance, the more intense its assault. However, if there was almost no room for resistance before the Dao Annihilation, the Dao Annihilation would remain relatively calm for a considerable period.

It would slowly erode until the remaining areas were completely consumed.

The numerous lower realm star seas remaining in the original possibility were in such a situation.

And in this possibility, the same situation applied to the Immortal Realm.

The Immortal Realm was divided into tens of thousands of scattered islands by the Dao Annihilation, with no Three Saints, no Immortal Emperors, and severed communication.

Even nameless True Immortals were rare, let alone transcendent beings.

"A possibility like this has almost no value to Ho Gan Immortal."

"Why did he come here to comprehend the Dao?"

Ho Gan Immortal's method of comprehending the Dao had been clearly explained by the Faceless Immortal. It involved using the calamities he created himself to exhaust the remaining conscience within his body.

This ensured that the fundamental 'Virtue' within him would not be affected by his actions.

"Ho Gan Immortal's place of comprehending the Dao must have been carefully selected."

"If I'm not mistaken, here, for Ho Gan Immortal, or rather, the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue, there is something extremely important, either a person or an event."

"However, the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue is not a native of this possibility."

The scattered Immortal Sea was not large, especially for a transcendent being like Li Fan.

Since no clues could be found for the time being, a thorough investigation was necessary.

Besides, there was still ample time to prepare before Ho Gan Immortal's arrival.

It took Li Fan a full five years to finally discover something potentially related to the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue on an Immortal Island in the Immortal Realm.

"These eyebrows and eyes bear a striking resemblance to the [Virtue] after achieving Sainthood."

"Could it be that this is the descendant of the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue in this possibility?"

Li Fan looked at a female True Immortal within the territory, a rare sight without immortal servants, and pondered.

If, under the rule of Wu Wei in the past, immortal servants were not regulated, then in this place, under the will of the island's owner, the beings who were originally immortal servants were able to shed their 'servant' status.

Although not True Immortals, they enjoyed everything that a True Immortal did.

They could even connect to the Infinite Sea and the Divine Mountains above!

However, none of them had achieved immortality through their own efforts. They all relied on the benevolence of that female True Immortal.

In the complete Immortal Realm, the Immortal Emperors and the Immortal Court controlled the access permissions for ordinary True Immortals to enter the Infinite Sea.

But in this fragmented Immortal Island possibility, this female True Immortal held the authority of the former Immortal Emperors.

And she bestowed it unconditionally upon all her subjects.

Everything could become immortal!

These beings were also extremely respectful towards her, but not in the way of servants towards a master.

Rather, it was a pure respect born from the grace they had received.

The female True Immortal, a suspected descendant of Virtue, was also extremely satisfied with the attitude of the island's inhabitants. They mingled harmoniously, creating a peaceful idyll.

"Ho Gan Immortal inherited the name of Virtue."

"But it's just a child's game," Li Fan sneered disdainfully.

His merciless gaze locked onto all the True Immortals on the island.

Instantly, it was as if ten thousand miles of ice had frozen over.

The inhabitants of the island, including the female True Immortal, were all frozen in place.

From her mind, Li Fan confirmed her identity.

Although not a descendant of the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue, she had an intricate connection with him.

In this possibility, when the world-ending Dao Annihilation descended, the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue had attempted to follow the example of the original Duke Shou Qiu and reverse the tide, saving lives from the catastrophe.

However, unfortunately, the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue's strength was simply not enough to contend with Dao Annihilation of such magnitude.

He tragically died in the Dao Annihilation.

But the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue did not die in vain. He did manage to save quite a few lives.

The female True Immortal on the island was one of them.

Although a long time had passed since that catastrophe, and most of the beings in the scattered Immortal Sea had forgotten the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue,

She had not.

She had even taken it upon herself to become the new True Immortal of Virtue and deliberately altered her appearance to resemble her benefactor.

She acted with [Virtue]!

Saving, educating!

"However, this is confined to this possibility. It even has something to do with Ho Gan Immortal's comprehension of the Dao..."

At that moment, it was difficult to fathom the cultivation method of [Virtue].

Li Fan decided not to alert them and to observe secretly from hiding.

He withdrew his gaze, and the frozen True Immortals on the island returned to normal.

They had no inkling of Li Fan's arrival.

Life and activities continued as before.

Li Fan remained hidden, quietly setting up, patiently waiting.

Until...

Rolling black mist descended from the sky without warning.

It swept across the entire world.

This black mist did not possess any substantial lethality. Even if living beings came into direct contact with it, they would not suffer any harm.

However...

Their actions and thoughts would change because of it.

Without any warning, they would wield their knives against those around them, and even betray their benefactors, turning against them and attacking them.

"Great kindness is great enmity, losing virtue leads to the proliferation of Dao..."

Naturally, there were no karmic retributions in this possibility. After committing acts of betrayal, not only did these people not suffer any retribution,

Instead, they became stronger, as if they had absorbed immortal elixirs, their strength rapidly increasing.

Those who lost virtue became even more formidable.

Endless slaughter ensued, spreading throughout the entire possibility.

And Ho Gan Immortal hid above the scattered Immortal Sea, at the very core of the flowing black Dao mist.

Li Fan could sense that Ho Gan Immortal's attention was largely focused on the female True Immortal.

Even though the island had descended into moral chaos, she still did not give up trying to save everyone.

But with insufficient ability, all efforts were in vain.

Ho Gan Immortal, however, had no intention of letting her go.

Nor did he directly harm her.

Instead, he manipulated the black Dao mist, transforming the once utopian island into a terrifying purgatory.

The female True Immortal could not perceive the existence of the black mist raging in the world.

In her eyes, the people she had always gotten along with so harmoniously had, for some unknown reason, turned against each other.

It was as if they had become enemies who would fight to the death.

And she, the island master, had become the target of everyone's attack.

Even though she still tried to embody Virtue, she would ultimately not stand by and let herself be killed by these people.

Thus, she fought back.

Her strength far surpassed that of the other True Immortals on the island.

In the ensuing melee, it was inevitable that some blows would be too heavy.

And with every drop of blood that stained her hands, her face, which had imitated the appearance of the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue, would fade a little.

Slowly shedding the Virtue face, she reverted to her original appearance.

"Can the word 'Virtue' be borne by you?"

Ho Gan Immortal's voice was filled with a sense of loneliness, and the black mist, like smoke, raged outwards.

Chapter 1632: Wonderful Theory Becomes Sage Reason

As if hearing Ho Gan Immortal's soft sigh, the female True Immortal, who had reverted to her original appearance, looked bewildered.

Looking around, she tried to find the figure of her "savior."

However, the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue eventually did not appear.

Just as it happened once, it happened again. After becoming accustomed to killing, without any burden on her heart, it had almost become instinct. In this Immortal Island Star Sea, the female True Immortal was practically invincible. In the past, all other beings survived the Dao Annihilation tribulation because of her protection.

But now, their savior had turned into a killing machine, mowing down their lives emotionlessly.

And under the influence of the mysterious black mist, these ants still rushed towards the island master, unafraid of death.

In the beginning, a flicker of unwillingness would occasionally flash across the female True Immortal's face, but as the slaughter continued, her expression slowly became calm.

She even began to feel impatient.

And the murmuring words of the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue echoed in time.

"A pretended 'Virtue', formed by emotions and conscience, might last for a while. But ultimately, it cannot be maintained forever."

"When swords are at your throat and you are in a desperate situation, can you still talk of Virtue?"

"When misunderstood and opposed by the world, can you still talk of Virtue?"

"When the path ahead is dark and there is no hope, can you..."

"Still talk of Virtue?"

"Only those who can still act virtuously are the true [Virtue]."

"Clearly, you are not." Ho Gan Immortal's voice was tinged with loneliness and mockery.

As if her true nature, hidden beneath the mask, had been exposed, the female True Immortal became enraged, her expression gradually turning ferocious. Her immortal power surged, like thousands of sharp blades cutting through the air, intending to destroy everything she saw.

However, how could a mere True Immortal surviving in an isolated possibility contend with Ho Gan Immortal, who had reached the Transcendent realm?

The shadowy black Dao mist remained unmoved.

But after repeated slaughter, the raging black mist, from its initial diffused state, slowly condensed.

It transformed into thick, colossal pillars, spanning the Star Sea.

Li Fan looked down from above and saw clearly.

These black heavenly pillars were inscribed with the words [Dao] and [Virtue]!

The female True Immortal seemed to be trapped in the very center of the [Virtue] cage. No matter how hard she struggled, even if she bruised herself, she could not break free.

"Those who seek [Virtue] will ultimately be bound by Virtue and then suffer backlash."

As if to confirm Ho Gan Immortal's words, the female True Immortal's body seemed to be corroded by the black mist, slowly turning pitch black.

She struggled, trying to escape the carbonized state.

But every attempt at self-rescue only pushed her faster towards complete annihilation.

Before long, the female True Immortal had completely become a part of the black Dao mist, merging into the towering heavenly pillars of Virtue.

And with her demise, there were no more living beings left on this Immortal Island possibility.

Silence filled the heavens and the earth.

Only Ho Gan Immortal's concluding words echoed: "Only by integrating Virtue into instinct. Not by pursuing Virtue, but by becoming Virtue!"

Absorbing the life force of all beings on this Immortal Island, the heavenly pillars of Virtue, under Ho Gan Immortal's faint voice, expanded once more.

They even spanned the entirety of the Dao Annihilation Sea, which had divided the tens of thousands of Immortal Islands, instantly enveloping the entire possibility.

Under the shackles of Virtue, billions of living beings ushered in the apocalypse.

"You all died by killing each other."

"Your demise has nothing to do with me."

"Nothing to do with me?"

If the first phrase still held a trace of hesitation, the second "nothing to do with me" was already filled with absolute certainty.

Ho Gan Immortal's eyes held a faint glint of tears, but his face was already cold.

Ho Gan Immortal silently observed the beings of this possibility.

And Li Fan, hidden in the shadows, quietly watched Ho Gan Immortal.

"Ho Gan Immortal never kills directly."

"Instead, he uses True Immortal Seal Scripts, black Dao mist, or other methods to indirectly commit murder."

"Although there is no direct karma, there is indirect karma. This action is not Ho Gan Immortal deceiving himself and others. It is..."

Li Fan observed Ho Gan Immortal's extremely subtle expressions and fluctuations in his aura, and his insight deepened: "Burning away the remaining conscience, what's left in terms of action and thought are all instincts, all 'Virtue'. This is Ho Gan Immortal's cultivation method."

"However, during the process of burning away his conscience, his mind is also severely impacted. By indirectly committing murder, he can form a psychological comfort barrier, acting as a buffer."

"From the current situation, Ho Gan Immortal has very little remaining conscience. With a few more such instances, he might achieve the perfect state of his own Virtue cycle. By splitting himself, and then gathering the true intent of Virtue, he can achieve the status of a Saint."

Watching the Immortal Island possibility gradually lose its vitality under the suppression of the heavenly pillars of Virtue, Li Fan's thoughts paused slightly.

"If it were just ordinary acts of burning away conscience, it shouldn't have helped Ho Gan Immortal so much."

"Otherwise, with the boundless mountains and seas, he could have become a Saint by simply slaughtering randomly."

In his sea of consciousness, Li Fan savored the scene of Ho Gan Immortal refining this world with the black Dao mist dozens of times.

He watched every scene carefully.

"In the original possibility, this female island master must have had an extraordinary relationship with Ho Gan Immortal. In other words, her position in Ho Gan Immortal's heart was extremely important. Just like my aunt to me."

"The more it is so, the greater the impact of her slaughter. The effect of burning away conscience would also be better."

Combining his own experiences, Li Fan had some conjecture about why this possibility was so important to Ho Gan Immortal.

Whether it was the female island master, or Ho Gan Immortal, or even Li Fan himself, or any living being in the mountains and seas.

When they gradually become accustomed to killing, they become indifferent to it.

But if they are indifferent, how can they burn away their remaining conscience?

"As conscience is gradually lost, the threshold will become higher and higher. Ordinary world-ending methods will no longer shake Ho Gan Immortal's heart in the slightest. Only by personally burying someone they deeply care about, like fire adding oil to the flames, can they break through the final barrier."

"With Ho Gan Immortal's talent, he must have foreseen this scenario when Dao and Virtue split. Thus, he specifically saved these important moments for the end."

"Brilliant!"

The True Immortal of Virtue was indeed a peerless genius of the mountains and seas.

What happened in the previous life had already proven the correctness of his path. With perfect Virtue, he would achieve Sainthood.

He was ruthless to others and to himself.

His inner conscience was gradually devoured. It was imaginable how much torment Ho Gan Immortal's heart had endured in this process.

But once a decision was made, he would follow it unswervingly. No matter who or what, nothing could stop him.

"This is only the path Ho Gan Immortal has taken."

"What about the other half of the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue, the Faceless Immortal?"

"Perhaps his path to achieving Sainthood is not much weaker than Ho Gan Immortal's."

Li Fan pondered silently, waiting for Ho Gan Immortal to finish this period of cultivation.

After the Immortal Island possibility was completely destroyed, Ho Gan Immortal, with a faint smile, swallowed the vast heavenly pillars of Virtue into his belly.

Then, with a slight smile, he was about to leave.

Li Fan finally spoke: "Fellow Daoist, please stay!"

Ho Gan Immortal looked warily at the suddenly appearing Li Fan.

His ability to remain hidden and evade his senses was enough to indicate this person's strength.

And in Ho Gan Immortal's perception, there seemed to be no such powerful being in the mountains and seas.

Therefore, he became even more wary.

However, he would not be frightened by Li Fan like this. Ho Gan Immortal looked coldly at Li Fan, waiting for him to speak further.
