"I see you are also cultivating [Virtue]?"

As soon as these words were spoken, Ho Gan Immortal, who had been able to maintain his composure, could not help but raise his eyebrows.

"Also?" He carefully observed Li Fan, and after a long examination, he could not detect any trace of 'Virtue' in his 'Dao'.

However, it was understandable. Ho Gan Immortal was not far from achieving perfect Sainthood. If there were anyone else cultivating the same Dao in the mountains and seas, he would surely have sensed it.

And this person who appeared so suddenly was clearly not among them.

"Do you think I'm blind!" Ho Gan Immortal's voice gradually turned cold.

It seemed that if they disagreed, he would attack.

However, Li Fan seemed completely unfazed by the other party's malice, and he retorted with a smile: "Could it be that you think I am talking nonsense?"

"Fine, observe this."

Li Fan pointed afar towards the mountains and seas, towards another possibility not far from the Immortal Island Star Sea.

"The Dao Annihilation tribulation suffered by that world is slightly less severe than the Immortal Island. The billions of living beings within are full of life, far surpassing this place."

With a flick of his finger, a spark of flame suddenly appeared in the possibility Li Fan pointed to.

In just a moment, it turned into a raging inferno.

It engulfed the Immortal Realm and the lower realm star seas.

This was not a grand spectacle for Ho Gan Immortal. He showed no fluctuation in his expression.

But what surprised him was that the person who appeared inexplicably before him was also indifferent.

Ho Gan Immortal sized up Li Fan again. He could sense that Li Fan was not a person with an evil heart or a loss of reason. Yet, he could destroy a possibility so lightly.

Moreover, when the flames began to spread beyond the possibility, gradually affecting a larger area of the mountains and seas, he showed no panic at all.

"Do you see me and call me [Virtue]?" Li Fan asked with a smile.

"Without Dao, without Virtue, without emotions, without righteousness," Ho Gan Immortal answered with only eight words.

Although he did not know the reason why Li Fan could remain so indifferent, based on his confidence in his own cultivated Dao, Ho Gan Immortal gave such an answer.

Li Fan sighed, "Fellow Daoist, you misunderstand me deeply! Actually, I am here to help you."

"Oh?"

"I have come specifically to help Fellow Daoist achieve Sainthood and reach the Saintly rank of the mountains and seas!" Li Fan said with utmost seriousness.

Ho Gan Immortal, who had been able to remain calm until then, could no longer hold back and let out a cold laugh.

"All nonsense, not a single true word. Your strength is not weak, and it's impossible for you to be aimlessly passing time with me? Could it be that you are delaying for time?"

"Are you his helper?" Ho Gan Immortal's expression changed as if he had thought of something.

"Fellow Daoist, you worry too much. I merely encountered Fellow Daoist by chance. Seeing your flow of Virtue completing its cycle, and seemingly only one step away from the final Saintly rank, I was overcome with interest and could not help but reveal myself."

"If my guess is correct, the 'he' you mentioned is the other half of [Dao and Virtue Split]. Is that correct?"

The moment the words [Dao and Virtue Split] were spoken, Ho Gan Immortal's expression completely changed.

He stared intently at Li Fan, and thousands of streams of black mist swirled around him like a whirlwind.

The black mist, which could drive all living beings in an entire possibility into madness and mutual slaughter, had no effect on Li Fan.

He continued to speak calmly: "Although you appear to be a Virtuous Immortal without virtue, you are actually cultivating Virtue. As for the other you, he is truly without Virtue, actually cultivating Dao..."

Li Fan slowly recounted what he had deduced from his experiences in the previous life.

Ho Gan Immortal became increasingly astonished and unsettled. This was arguably his greatest secret.

It could be said that in the entire mountains and seas, besides themselves, no one else should have known all of this.

How could this person before him know all of this?

"Could it be?" Ho Gan Immortal's heart suddenly stirred.

Because his own Dao path deviated from conventional worldly understanding, after transcending, Ho Gan Immortal did not go to the so-called Shore, nor the Saint Dynasty, nor any other place.

He merely cultivated in seclusion.

But he had heard of the Shore Saints and Emperor Tai Wei.

It was said that in the eyes of Saints, only the survival of the mountains and seas as a whole mattered. The lives within the mountains and seas, and even ordinary possibilities, were not of great importance to them.

Only Saints truly possessed the qualifications and power to save the mountains and seas.

Therefore, they occasionally helped and enlightened those in the mountains and seas who could achieve Sainthood.

Could it be that this person was a reincarnation of a Saint?

If not, how could he have spoken his secret so accurately? And he even arrogantly claimed to help him achieve Sainthood?

The more Ho Gan Immortal thought about it, the more likely it seemed.

His tone also became more respectful: "May I ask, Fellow Daoist, where lies the opportunity for Sainthood?"

"Achieving Sainthood lies not with you, nor with me, but with him!" Li Fan's hand pointed towards a location in the mountains and seas.

Although not explicitly stated, Ho Gan Immortal understood Li Fan's meaning.

"Dao and Virtue split, yet Dao and Virtue are not separated."

"This peculiar characteristic is the fundamental basis for your independent existence. If either party loses this characteristic..." Li Fan smiled meaningfully.

"It will become the foundation for the other to achieve Sainthood!"

Ho Gan Immortal naturally knew that Li Fan's words were correct.

But Dao and Virtue were interdependent. Even with the secret art of Dao and Virtue splitting, it was difficult to completely sever the two.

How could one easily make the other 'lose its characteristic'?

"The key lies in..."

"Virtue loses Dao, Dao leaves Virtue." Ho Gan Immortal was still contemplating, but Li Fan had already revealed the truth in a single sentence.

"Your pursuit is to save the world. If you witness the mountains and seas being destroyed and are powerless to do anything, you will have lost [Dao]."

"As for his pursuit, it is to achieve the Dao. If he witnesses the destruction of the mountains and seas and remains indifferent, then he has lost [Virtue]."

Li Fan's words struck Ho Gan Immortal like lightning, leaving him trembling.

Chapter 1633: Eternal Silence Spiritual Sludge Accumulates

"Loss of Dao! Loss of Virtue!"

In Ho Gan Immortal's mind, scenes of the true spirit fire burning through and the mountains and seas being annihilated flashed before his eyes.

If he were to witness such a scene and be powerless to intervene, he would be deemed as having 'lost Dao'.

And the other him, who remained indifferent from beginning to end, would be deemed as having 'lost Virtue'.

Dao and Virtue completely separated, and the cycle no longer turning. It was likely that their very existence would be unsustainable!

"With a single sentence, it revealed the method for killing the [True Immortal of Dao and Virtue]. This person..."

"Even if he is not a Saint, he is not far from it!"

Ho Gan Immortal almost broke out in a cold sweat. He now believed Li Fan's words to be fifty to sixty percent true.

Perhaps this person had truly come to help him on his path to Sainthood.

At the very least, he was an ally, not an enemy!

After all, based on the knowledge and strength Li Fan had displayed so far, it was entirely possible that he could help the other True Immortal of Dao and Virtue to destroy him!

Ho Gan Immortal's demeanor became increasingly respectful: "Fellow Daoist, what is the certainty of success?"

"Calculating with intention against the unsuspecting... ten out of ten."

"However, the one who unties the bell must be the one who tied it. The path to Sainthood still requires your own personal effort."

"I can only offer reasonable suggestions," Li Fan said, his demeanor calm and collected, noticing Ho Gan Immortal's shift in attitude.

Ho Gan Immortal quickly nodded: "This is only natural!"

"The other me, although weak in strength, is extremely vigilant and hides himself well. More importantly, he seems to have the help of an expert. I have tried to probe him several times in the past, but each time I was inexplicably blocked."

"Moreover, the scene of forcing him into a corner is likely to be fatal to me as well. How can I eliminate him while ensuring my own safety?" Ho Gan Immortal continued to seek advice.

"This is simple. Burning the mountains and seas is not truly burning them. It is merely a pretense."

"You know this, but he does not. This is the crucial difference."

"Deceiving him with falsehood, and making falsehood become truth..."

For some reason, as Li Fan spoke, he suddenly paused, deep in thought.

Ho Gan Immortal became somewhat hesitant: "Fellow Daoist, is there something wrong?"

"It's nothing. Just... suddenly thought of something else." After a moment of silence, Li Fan regained his senses, and a handful of flames suddenly appeared in his palm.

"What do you think of this fire?"

Ho Gan Immortal recognized this flame as the terrifying power that had casually annihilated an entire possibility.

Even observing it from afar, Ho Gan Immortal felt an uncontrollable sense of dread.

He had no doubt that this was a destructive force comparable to the Dao Annihilation tribulation.

But after observing it for a long time, Ho Gan Immortal could not determine its origin.

He could only awkwardly praise: "Fellow Daoist's divine abilities are truly profound."

Li Fan did not mind and outlined his plan to Ho Gan Immortal: "With this flame, coupled with provoking the Dao Annihilation tribulation, I can create a sealed arena for you and him."

"To make the deception as realistic as possible, I will burn a large area of mountains and seas. Therefore, within the arena, you will see countless mountains and seas, and possibilities, being annihilated in the fusion of fire and water."

"What you need to do is confront him and seize the opportunity to prove his [Lack of Virtue]."

Ho Gan Immortal gazed at Li Fan's palm, where the flames flickered, seemingly truly seeing endless mountains and seas being engulfed in fire.

He couldn't help but shudder.

"Such a grand scale, will there be no problem?" he asked somewhat uncertainly.

Li Fan chuckled: "No problem, no problem! Although the mountains and seas are vast, they are not the end result. As long as we can create a new Saint, everything else is negotiable."

Such unwavering confidence and nonchalance reassured Ho Gan Immortal.

Previously, in order to eliminate the remaining conscience within him, he had also committed various world-ending acts, but they were all limited to specific possibilities.

Compared to Li Fan's act of burning vast swathes of mountains and seas, his actions were mere trifles.

And such magnanimity and unbridled demeanor further convinced Ho Gan Immortal of Li Fan's 'Saintly' identity.

"Note that to achieve the effect of deception, you must not only deceive him but also deceive yourself. While my display of power is close to reality, if you, who are truly within it, remain indifferent, it will be an obvious flaw and will not achieve the desired effect," Li Fan said slowly, looking at Ho Gan Immortal.

"Deceive myself?" Ho Gan Immortal frowned slightly.

"Think carefully and prepare yourself. I can see that you still have some hesitation. When the time is right, I will come to find you again."

"Fellow Daoist, wait..."

Before Ho Gan Immortal could finish speaking, Li Fan's figure had already disappeared.

Hidden within the mountains and seas, his whereabouts were unknown.

Only the flames in his palm remained, continuing to burn.

Ho Gan Immortal stood in place for a long time, and finally, slowly approached the raging flames.

A scorching heat emanated, as if the very foundation of his existence was being ignited by the flames.

The black Dao mist formed a whirlwind, enveloping the flames, attempting to extinguish them.

However, the flames remained unmoving in the wind.

Instead, the black Dao mist was continuously consumed, quickly becoming extremely thin.

"The true horror of this fire lies in..."

"It seems capable of consuming my true spirit?"

Ho Gan Immortal was suddenly startled, as if scalded, and quickly retreated, distancing himself from the true spirit fire.

His eyes revealed extreme caution.

"Using the true spirit as fuel, killing eight hundred enemies while losing eight hundred oneself, is undoubtedly a forbidden art."

"Why does that person use it so effortlessly?"

Even if Ho Gan Immortal racked his brain, he could not figure it out.

He could only conclude that Li Fan's true spirit was extremely profound and inexhaustible, making him indifferent to such consumption.

"Only Saints in the mountains and seas can achieve such effortless execution."

Ho Gan Immortal thought to himself. If it were just one clue pointing to Li Fan's Sainthood, Ho Gan Immortal might still have some doubts.

But now, every anomaly displayed by Li Fan pointed to the same answer.

So Ho Gan Immortal had no choice but to believe.

"I have heard that Saints of the Shore can traverse the Eternal Void."

"That is a place where the concept of [existence] itself ceases to be, the remnants after an entire segment of mountains and seas have been devoured by Dao Annihilation."

"Utter emptiness."

"But if one can traverse and return, they can filter and bring back..."

"True spirit."

"It is like sediment formed after the destruction of the mountains and seas, a stagnant marsh. Traversing through it, one would be stained by the mud."

"Perhaps this is why he can use the true spirit flames so recklessly."

Ho Gan Immortal naturally coveted such a divine ability.

But alas, although the divine ability was good, it could only be observed and not used.

Otherwise, even with his genius, after using it once or twice, he would become just like everyone else.

Chapter 1634: Spiritual Rules

"The unification of multiple selves in other possibilities can also increase one's own true spirit. However, the true spirit foundations of selves in different circumstances are not the same. Furthermore, during the process of multiple self unification, one cannot completely absorb the true spirit of other selves."

"The amount absorbed varies from person to person. The higher the conversion efficiency, the greater the potential for Sainthood."

"When all of one's selves in the remaining possibilities of the entire mountains and seas have been absorbed, yet the opportunity for Sainthood is still not glimpsed..."

"Then the hope is slim."

"Unless there is the Tai Wei Sacred Medicine, or the accumulated true spirit brought back by Saints from the Eternal Void, or other sacred artifacts to assist..."

After a period of contemplation, Ho Gan Immortal finally returned to Li Fan's proposed 'arena' plan.

"Deceive him, and deceive myself."

"He and I are one, and we have mutual senses. The closer we are, the more accurate the sense. How can this be achieved?"

"Unless we make the deception a reality. But in doing so, I myself will fall into danger."

Ho Gan Immortal's expression fluctuated between delight and dismay.

If Li Fan were someone he knew and trusted, he might have seriously considered it. But this person's origins were mysterious, and his motives unclear.

The risk was too great!

If it were any ordinary matter, the always cautious Ho Gan Immortal would not even consider it. But this was about achieving Sainthood!

"A Saint! The pinnacle of the mountains and seas. The ultimate expert who can transcend this section of the mountains and seas."

"Why did I choose the Dao of Virtue in the first place, wasn't it for the goal of becoming a Saint..."

Therefore, even though he knew the road ahead was fraught with peril, and it was highly likely to be a trap.

Ho Gan Immortal had never given up the thought of trying.

"As he said, I am indeed not ready." After standing for a long time, filled with hesitation, Ho Gan Immortal sighed deeply.

In fact, it was not only Ho Gan Immortal who was not fully prepared.

Even Li Fan himself was not fully prepared.

He had witnessed the might of the True Immortal of Virtue after achieving Sainthood.

Even a Saint who had just attained that status was not something that could be schemed against by a transcendent being. In the face of absolute power disparity, any conspiracy or trickery was useless!

Li Fan would not be so overconfident as to attempt the act of an ant trying to swallow an elephant.

"The best outcome would be to refine both Ho Gan Immortal and the Faceless Immortal simultaneously, using their combined Virtue and Dao to achieve my great endeavor."

"However, the probability of this is very low."

"The True Immortal of Dao and Virtue was originally one entity. After splitting, if either side fails, the other side will absorb it much faster than an outsider like me."

"So, it is highly likely that one party will win in the arena and then achieve Sainthood."

Li Fan had already prepared himself mentally for this.

After all, his initial goal was to understand the secret of achieving Sainthood through the merging of Dao and Virtue, and he had gained some insight.

If Virtue could achieve Sainthood in this way, perhaps other Great Daos in the mountains and seas could also do so.

"Besides repeatedly observing the process of the True Immortal of Dao and Virtue achieving Sainthood, perhaps I can also rely on him to explain it himself."

"Ho Gan Immortal is a virtuous person. My helping him achieve Sainthood is like a second life. After becoming a Saint, the secret of Virtue will no longer be needed. It would not be difficult for him to tell me."

"The prerequisite is that he must not see [True Reversion] within me."

A wisp of blood flowed from Li Fan's body, converging into a humanoid shape in the void before him.

Although it was only formed from blood, the moment it took shape, it seemed to be imbued with sentience, first bowing to Li Fan.

Then it curiously looked around.

Li Fan used his finger as a brush, constantly writing on the blood figure.

Body, limbs, facial features.

He carved them out one by one.

"From today onwards, you are Li Fan."

"When true becomes false..."

"False also becomes true!"

As the final stroke of the 'dotting the eyes' was completed, Li Fan's true form exhaled a breath of silvery-white mist towards the blood figure.

As if flesh and blood were merging, after the mist was completely absorbed.

The Li Fan that appeared before him was another him!

Identical in appearance and soul to Li Fan.

Even Bai Shuyue, if she were present, would probably not be able to distinguish which one was her beloved nephew.

This was not a simple clone, but a creation imbued with the transformation of true and false, capable of deceiving even the keenest observer!

It was like a new extension of his own body.

But True Reversion was divided.

In his past reincarnations, Li Fan had created numerous clones.

Saint Emperor Li Ping, Li Buren, etc.

But this one before him was undoubtedly his masterpiece.

Li Fan carefully examined it and shook his head slightly with a hint of regret.

"It's still a bit short of the theoretical optimal state."

"It's the allocation of spirituality!"

"If I could retain the memories of True Reversion, and actively transfer a portion of my infinite spirituality to this clone, I might be able to achieve true self-replication and creation."

Li Fan felt no aversion or fear towards creating another self.

Because of his characteristic of infinite spirituality.

It was destined to be unique and unrepeatable.

Other clones, no matter how true, could not possess this unique characteristic that spanned the entire mountains and seas.

"Spirituality, potential, or perhaps, true spirit."

"I am still unclear what it truly is."

"However, as I observe the continuous transformations of my aunt through rebirth, I have already vaguely glimpsed its traces."

"The transformation of true and false in True Reversion, I can learn and imitate."

"This method of splitting spirituality, perhaps it is not impossible to learn!"

Li Fan was creating and refining another self, intending to deceive Ho Gan Immortal in the future.

Meanwhile, he turned his attention to his aunt in the Profound Yellow Realm.

Although he had firmly decided not to blindly follow the Boundless Wall's advice anymore.

Bai Shuyue still sought out the wondrous artifact from the Saint Monarch's Palace as soon as she was reborn.

After some interaction, the two gradually returned to their optimal state of companionship.

Surprisingly, although they had not gone through life-and-death crises together in this life, the Boundless Wall's trust in Bai Shuyue remained undiminished.

Perhaps it was due to the Boundless Wall's unique intuition.

After Bai Shuyue diligently cultivated within the Boundless Wall for a hundred years.

The Boundless Wall began to grow impatient, just like in the previous life.

"Too slow, too slow! When will you transcend? It'll take ages at this rate! Why not..."

Bai Shuyue completely ignored the Boundless Wall's suggestion.

"Hey, why don't you trust me!" The Boundless Wall became anxious when it saw Bai Shuyue's indifference.

Bai Shuyue retorted: "Weren't you a guard at the Saint Monarch's gate? Why do you lack such patience? It's only been a hundred years."

The Boundless Wall huffed and puffed, saying: "It is precisely because I have endured such hardships in the past that I don't want to wait idly like this anymore."

"However, I understand your fear of the outside world. If you really don't want to leave the Profound Yellow Realm..."

After some thought, the Boundless Wall had an idea.

"I can faintly sense the aura of my colleagues from the Taiyi Palace here."

"Perhaps their divine power can be borrowed!"

Chapter 1635: Meditating and Calculating the Boundless

"I once mentioned to you that in the past Dao Palace, the 'Young Master,' the meditation cushion, the green lamp, and the whisk were the four most miraculous items."

"I sense the aura of my colleagues here, and it is precisely that 'Young Master'!"

Bai Shuyue's trust in the Boundless Wall had dropped to an extreme low, and she was somewhat skeptical: "Even if he is indeed that 'Young Master' from the Taiyi Palace back then, do you even have any interaction with him? Borrow his divine power... can it really be done just by saying so?"

The Boundless Wall coughed lightly, its large single eye rolling around: "If we were to approach him directly, it would naturally not work. Of course, there must be methods."

"The 'Young Master' has a similar personality to the Saint Monarch, learning much of his temper but not his abilities. He always shouts about how 'Taiyi came before the Immortals, and Wuji came even before Taiyi.' In reality..."

The Boundless Wall spoke with a hint of sarcasm: "Everyone respects him, but it's all because of the Saint Monarch's reputation. If he weren't the Saint Monarch's disciple, even with his myriad special qualities, he would have been captured and refined into a magical treasure long ago. Yet he prides himself on it, oblivious."

Bai Shuyue was somewhat puzzled: "But if this 'Wuji' dares to make such a bold claim, he must have some special abilities, right? He's at least a 'Young Master' disciple of the Immortal Realm, while you're just a tile from the Dao Palace. Do you dare to scheme against him?"

Challenged by Bai Shuyue, the Boundless Wall became indignant: "What do you know? I've disliked him for a long time. It's just that out of respect for the Saint Monarch's might, I never dared to act, only pondering it in my heart."

"Now that the Saint Monarch is gone..."

The Boundless Wall said proudly: "By planning with intent while he acts without, how can it be difficult to deal with a mere 'Wuji'? It's a piece of cake."

Bai Shuyue nodded: "Alright, then I will wait here and listen for your good news of success. You may go!"

The Boundless Wall's expression immediately stiffened. It pressed its large, exposed head close to Bai Shuyue, grinning sheepishly: "Although I have a clever plan, I cannot do it alone. I need a helper."

"Don't rush to refuse, listen to me slowly."

The holographic projection of the single eye shattered, reverting to its original form. A faint green light emanated from the Boundless Wall, revealing a scene of primordial chaos.

"Speaking of which, the 'Young Master' does have grounds for his arrogance. Do you know what [Wuji] is?"

"Born at the beginning, existing before the Dao. The first of all things, noble beyond measure. All the Great Daos in the world we inhabit must yield to him when they see him. It can be said that the 'Young Master' doesn't need to make a move; simply standing there makes him almost invincible."

As the explanation unfolded word by word, the proud and solitary figure of the Grand Heavenly Master also appeared in the shifting image of the Boundless Wall. When Wuji appeared, it was as if the chaotic heavens and earth parted. His 'nobility' was evident.

"Then you still want to plot against him? Isn't that seeking your own death?" Bai Shuyue frowned, staring at Wuji's figure.

"Hehe, continue listening. While this is his greatest strength, it is also the root of his weakness. The 'Young Master' is indeed noble in the Great Daos of our world. But for the Great Daos of other worlds..."

"Have you ever heard the phrase, '[I am a barbarian]'?" the Boundless Wall chuckled.

Although Bai Shuyue did not understand the specific meaning of this phrase, she was not foolish. After a moment of thought, she understood.

"You mean, the 'nobility' of Wuji does not apply to the Great Daos of other worlds?"

"Precisely!"

The Boundless Wall responded excitedly.

The scene reflected in the image suddenly showed a thick stone pillar, which swung down decisively towards the proud and solitary Wuji.

Wuji cried out in pain, his face showing fear, instinctively reaching out to block. But how could he block it?

He took the hit squarely, and his figure instantly shattered.

"There are treasures from other worlds inside your belly?" Bai Shuyue finally realized.

"Hmph, hmph, hmph." The Boundless Wall snorted proudly.

Then, it lowered its voice: "The Taiyi Sacred Palace was built by the Saint Monarch himself. Most of the materials were sourced locally by the Saint Monarch. However, some of the pillars, the main supports, came from elsewhere!"

"When I first arrived, I didn't know their origin."

"But these pillars have been difficult for me to digest over the years. So, I can only guess their origin."

The Boundless Wall said, slowly spitting out a golden, brilliant jade pillar.

It was only a broken section, thirty-three feet long, with no beginning or end.

The surface of the jade pillar originally seemed to be engraved with patterns, but after years of digestion by the Boundless Wall, they had become blurry and indistinct. However, the sacred aura of the jade pillar remained undiminished.

"This pillar is one of the main supports of the [Taiyi Hall] deep within the Sacred Palace. Although it was originally an inanimate object, it absorbed the Saint Monarch's aura day after day, and it has cultivated a trace of spirituality."

"Try telling it to be small!"

Bai Shuyue followed its instructions, and indeed, the jade pillar moved according to her will, instantly transforming into a wieldable jade staff. Although she knew nothing of staff techniques, she could vaguely sense that by simply wielding the jade pillar itself, it possessed incredible destructive power.

The Profound Yellow Realm's Dao Integration was lethal on contact.

However, Wuji was a disciple of the Saint Monarch of the Immortal Realm. Asking Bai Shuyue, who was merely at the mortal realm, to ambush him...

Even with the aid of an exotic item, the possibility of success was minuscule.

"That's why we need to cooperate!"

Seeing that Bai Shuyue still hesitated, the Boundless Wall continued to persuade her relentlessly: "I will use the pretext of visiting an old acquaintance to go and visit him. At that time, I will deliberately say something that will shock his mind. While he is stunned, you will leap out from within me and strike him with all your might."

"You must know that the 'Young Master' relies on his innate characteristics and looks down on all other beings from the bottom of his heart. He would never imagine that I would dare to suddenly attack him. Furthermore, apart from the Dao of Wuji, his other divine abilities are mediocre. Practice hard, and as long as you get close, even if he reacts, he will be no match for you."

The Boundless Wall made continuous assurances.

Then, the Boundless Wall expounded at length on the advantages of Wuji.

"If you can refine the Dao of Wuji, the predicament of this realm can be resolved instantly."

"You can choose a suitable area to cultivate, and no longer need to research this 'new method'..."

Bai Shuyue was, after all, soft-hearted.

Unable to resist the Boundless Wall's persuasion for many days, she finally agreed.

"This is the [Heaven-Overturning Staff Technique]. I have forgotten where I learned it. But rest assured, it is definitely an extremely powerful divine ability. Combined with the jade pillar I gave you, it can indeed possess the power to overturn the heavens and earth!"

"Of course, the most important thing is the first strike. It must be fast, accurate, and ruthless..."

This staff technique was clearly not an ordinary divine ability.

It seemed to contain the profound principles of controlling the Dao within it. Even with Bai Shuyue's comprehension and the Boundless Wall's assistance, it took her a full three years to achieve minor success.

"Oh, and to prevent you from being overwhelmed by the 'Young Master's' aura, it's best to put on some protective gear." Before departing, the Boundless Wall examined Bai Shuyue again, pondering.

With that, it spat out a conical hat and a straw cloak from within itself, asking Bai Shuyue to put them on.

These two items looked somewhat tattered and exuded an unpleasant odor. However, the Boundless Wall, which had produced them, appeared extremely pained.

It was far more cautious than when it had given her the jade pillar.

"You must return these two items to me after the job is done," it muttered.

Bai Shuyue chuckled and nodded in agreement.

After putting on the conical hat and straw cloak, she immediately felt a great difference in her surroundings.

Because in her past reincarnations, Bai Shuyue had experienced various bizarre and unusual ways of dying, including being immobilized by golden needles and then dismembered.

Therefore, Bai Shuyue, living in the Profound Yellow Realm, was actually extremely uneasy.

Even though she knew she had the ability to be reborn again and again.

But this time, after awakening, it seemed to have taken a longer time. The various uncertainties further intensified her anxiety.

But now...

Hidden beneath the conical hat and straw cloak, all these anxieties within her heart had vanished!

She inexplicably felt a surge of extreme confidence.

Even if storms raged and floods swept the world outside,

As long as she wore this attire, the tempests outside would not be able to harm her!

"This..."

"This is not your illusion!" As if sensing Bai Shuyue's inner thoughts, the Boundless Wall continued.

"This conical hat and straw cloak were habitually worn by a frequent visitor to the Taiyi Sacred Palace in the past. This person enjoyed observing the spectacle of Dao Annihilation devouring mountains and seas. He often wore a conical hat and a straw cloak, personally going to the edge of the Dao Annihilation tide to observe the scenes of mountains and seas being destroyed..."

With just a few brief sentences, Bai Shuyue was terrified.

"Although these two items are somewhat worn from his long use, they still retain a trace of [Eternity]'s residual aura. Resisting the 'Young Master's' aura is not a problem!" the Boundless Wall said confidently.

"Eternity... Could it be the name of the other Saint Monarch?"

"Not at all, not at all." The Boundless Wall quickly shook its head. "In the vast Immortal Realm, from ancient times to the present, there have only been three Saints. However, [Eternity] might be only half a step away from achieving Sainthood, interacting with the Saint Monarchs as equals."

"When the Taiyi Saint Monarch was around, he often visited. I even received his guidance..."

The Boundless Wall seemed lost in memory, falling into an uncharacteristic moment of silence.

After a long while, it regained its senses and continued: "These two treasures, because they were often worn by Eternity, have also been infused with some of the Great Dao of Eternity. When you wear them, the immense sense of security you feel comes from this!"

"These are truly my most treasured possessions..."

Bai Shuyue narrowed her eyes, recalling the myriad treasures emitted by the Boundless Wall when facing the Faceless Immortal in her previous life, whether these two items were among them.

However, she was too busy escaping for her life at the time to notice such details.

She could only assume that the Boundless Wall was not lying.

After getting fully dressed, holding the jade staff, Bai Shuyue calmly centered herself and slowly practiced the Heaven-Overturning Staff Technique once more.

With her state at its peak and everything prepared,

The Boundless Wall swallowed her into its belly.

Then, it transformed into a streak of light and quietly flew towards the Dao Origin State of the Profound Yellow Realm.

"Hmm? Why aren't you nervous anymore, now that the moment has come?"

Sensing Bai Shuyue's emotional state within its belly, the Boundless Wall asked strangely.

Bai Shuyue smiled and did not answer.

"Even if it fails, it's just another go."

Before long, they had reached the Dao Origin State.

As the Boundless Wall slowly approached, a simple Dao Palace, originally hidden and invisible in the sky, inexplicably revealed itself.

"Heh, he's quite competent. He really thinks he's a Saint!" the Boundless Wall muttered inwardly.

It emitted a stream of blue light towards the heavens.

"Before the Saint Monarch's gate, I seek an audience with the 'Young Master'!"

The Heavenly Gate, which had remained motionless for millennia, awakened from its slumber upon sensing the aura emitted by the Boundless Wall.

The gates of the Dao Palace suddenly opened.

The Boundless Wall, familiar with the layout of the Heavenly Gate, skillfully navigated its way to the deepest part, where the Grand Heavenly Master, Wuji, resided.

Pushing open the door, what greeted the Boundless Wall's eyes were two figures, one large and one small. The smaller one was naturally the Grand Heavenly Master.

And the one sitting before the Grand Heavenly Master was...

"My goodness, Saint Monarch!"

Even though his figure was extremely blurry, the Boundless Wall, as a loyal guard dog, recognized him at a glance.

Its mind went blank, and it immediately slumped down.

Bai Shuyue, hidden within the Boundless Wall, who had no concrete understanding of the Saint Monarch and was therefore not as terrified as the Boundless Wall, found the latter's pathetic display amusing and mentally criticized it.

But she dared not make a sound, for fear of being detected.

She could only try her best to conceal herself, silently waiting for the opportune moment to strike.

"Rise, my master has long since departed. This is merely an illusory projection left behind."

The Grand Heavenly Master looked at the trembling Boundless Wall below and chuckled, slowly speaking.

"An illusory projection?"

A thousand thoughts flashed through its mind. The Boundless Wall, which had already prepared to have its spiritual intelligence stripped away and be turned back into a gate-guarding tile, was stunned upon hearing the Grand Heavenly Master's words. Instantly, it felt relieved.

"So it was just a false alarm!"

At that moment, a surge of anger rose within it: "How dare you, Wuji, use the Saint Monarch's image to trick me and make me look like a fool!"

It cursed the Grand Heavenly Master thousands of times in its mind, but outwardly, the Boundless Wall remained respectful.

"You have made the 'Young Master' witness your incompetence!" The Boundless Wall said.

This address of 'Young Master' greatly pleased the Grand Heavenly Master.

It was as if he were reliving the days when all the Immortal Emperors respectfully bowed to him during the Saint Monarch's reign.

"The destruction of the Immortal Realm was a long time ago."

"After so much time has passed, it is unexpected that we would meet again in the lower realm..." The Grand Heavenly Master sighed wistfully.

"All thanks to the benevolence and protection of the 'Great Master' and the 'Young Master'!" the Boundless Wall said shamelessly.

The Grand Heavenly Master seemed somewhat curious: "The Dao Annihilation descended abruptly, and I escaped in a rather sorry state. How were you able to escape unscathed and survive to this day?"

The Boundless Wall replied obsequiously: "Having cultivated under the Saint Monarch's tutelage for so many years, I have at least managed to preserve my life. However, I was also heavily injured, and it has taken me all these years to recover."

"And now, after regaining consciousness, I sensed the aura of the 'Young Master' nearby. So, I rushed to pay my respects."

The Boundless Wall's words were plausible, and the Grand Heavenly Master nodded slightly, asking no further questions.

In reality, the reason he awoke from his seclusion and opened the door today was entirely because the Boundless Wall was indeed an item from the Taiyi Sacred Palace in the past.

As for the Boundless Wall itself...

He truly did not care about it.

Chapter 1636: Each Has Their Own Fortune

"Time flows, and the world changes. I never expected that after so many years, amidst the vast Taiyi Palace, it would be the two of us meeting again today."

The Grand Celestial Master squinted at the Boundless Wall, observing it for a moment, and nodded slightly, "It seems you are doing quite well."

The Boundless Wall chuckled, "All thanks to the blessings of the Young Master and the Master. Otherwise, how could I have achieved this today? But it's still far inferior to you, Young Master. This Dao Palace is quite magnificent, quite like the old days!"

"It's just a minor effort, for the sake of remembering times past." Tian Du The Grand Celestial Master, also known as [Wuji], had always enjoyed flattery when he was in the Immortal Realm.

Despite experiencing everything, this trait had not changed.

Especially since the other party was an old acquaintance from the Taiyi Palace, it made the Grand Celestial Master feel a long-lost joy.

He had initially intended to send him away after the brief meeting and continue his cultivation and comprehension.

But now, he felt no need to rush.

The Boundless Wall, with all its cunning, managed to coax the Grand Celestial Master into becoming increasingly arrogant.

Finally, the Boundless Wall's single eye rolled around, looking towards the illusory projection of Taiyi.

"Young Master, why is this illusory projection of the Master so realistic? The first moment I saw it, my whole body felt weak from fright."

The Grand Celestial Master chuckled, "Although Master has ascended, he still left behind an illusory projection to solidify the heavens that were about to collapse. Although it is merely an illusion, it still possesses some of Master's divine might. Although you have made some progress over the years, to distinguish them at a glance..."

"That would still be wishful thinking."

The Boundless Wall was enraged by the Grand Celestial Master's words but still maintained a respectful demeanor, continuing to listen.

"When Master was around, he was the Great Dao of [Taiyi] in this world. Now that Master is gone, only this illusory projection remains, yet it is still enough to represent [Taiyi]."

"However, the Immortal Realm is destroyed, and the Great Dao is incomplete, so the Dao of Taiyi has also undergone corresponding changes..."

"This [Taiyi] now is not the [Taiyi] of the past."

The Grand Celestial Master's words were somewhat convoluted.

But the Boundless Wall and Bai Shuyue, inside the Boundless Wall, could all understand.

The Boundless Wall stared intently at the illusory projection of Taiyi, an irrepressible greed rising in its heart.

But the might of the Saint Monarch, like an instinct, pressed down on its heart, making the Boundless Wall hesitate to act.

"With the great majesty of the Master, since this illusory projection remains, he should be able to contact him through it," the Boundless Wall tentatively said with envy.

The Grand Celestial Master snorted, "What you said does have some truth to it. However, it is based on the premise that Master wishes to 'perceive.' "

"Precisely because Master's true strength is too great, even if he left ordinarily, only leaving behind an illusory projection of himself, he can still perceive everything around him through this projection. This is contrary to his original intentions."

"So he used the method of [Immortal Ascension], truly severing the existence he left in this world, completely severing the connection. In essence, it is no different from falling."

"This illusory projection is merely the [Taiyi] of this world, not Master himself. If you truly wish to contact Master, you are more likely to succeed by reciting Master's name a thousand times in your heart every day than by relying on this projection."

The Boundless Wall was instantly relieved, "Then I am at ease."

"Hmm?"

The Boundless Wall's reaction was somewhat unexpected to the Grand Celestial Master. As he was momentarily stunned, he saw a figure leap out of thin air.

Holding a white staff, hidden within a straw cloak and conical hat, it swung down towards him, striking his head!

"You seek death!"

The Grand Celestial Master was enraged and laughed.

He could not believe that a mere tile from Taiyi Palace in the past dared to attack him.

"Could it be that I misjudged? Is it not the main body, or has it been taken over by someone else?"

The first thought that flashed through the Grand Celestial Master's mind was such an idea.

Although full of shock, the Grand Celestial Master's actions did not stop.

"Since you have seen Wuji, why do you not dissipate!"

As the pride of [Wuji], even though he had glimpsed Bai Shuyue's movements moments before, he still did not dodge or retreat.

He said lightly.

But in the next instant, he realized something was wrong.

That staff seemed familiar, and it was unaffected by the Great Dao of Wuji.

And that conical hat and straw cloak...

Having comprehended the Great Dao of Taiyi for many years, the Grand Celestial Master had evolved countless forms of the Great Dao within his own heart. His memories of the past had become somewhat blurred.

But the simultaneous appearance of the jade pillar, conical hat, and straw cloak awakened the depths of his past.

"These are all relics from Taiyi Palace?"

The Grand Celestial Master, both shocked and enraged, lost his composure and retreated.

However, the person holding the staff pursued him like a shadow, getting closer and closer.

The staff carried immense power, approaching him.

"Insolent!"

Seeing that he could no longer retreat and was forced to unleash his ferocity, the Grand Celestial Master pointed a finger at the person in the straw cloak. Instantly, hundreds of thousands of different figures, like a rain of swords, shot out.

Each figure could find a prototype among the beings of Yuandao State.

They were all tools the Grand Celestial Master used to comprehend the Great Dao of Taiyi, and now, transformed into divine abilities, they possessed the power to destroy the heavens and annihilate the earth.

Like a torrential downpour, they bombarded Bai Shuyue.

If not for her eternal straw cloak providing protection, she would have turned to dust in an instant.

Although obstructed, the momentum of the Heaven-Overturning Staff Technique did not diminish.

While wielding the staff, Bai Shuyue also noticed the countless figures blooming outside, like fireworks.

"It seems that each image corresponds to a Great Dao?"

"Taiyi, born innately, derives the Dao of myriad things..."

The comprehension accumulated over nearly thirty reincarnations was truly terrifying, allowing Bai Shuyue to gain insights even while fighting.

Originally, these Daoist shadows were obstacles, but as Bai Shuyue comprehended and adapted, she gradually found herself at ease!

In the eyes of the Grand Celestial Master, this scene was extremely horrifying.

The person holding the staff seemed to understand all the Great Daos in the world, just like himself.

His killing moves seemed useless against her.

He could only watch helplessly as the Heaven-Overturning Staff descended towards his head.

In a daze, the Grand Celestial Master recalled the events of the past.

A True Immortal, not yet named, had found his way to the front of Taiyi Palace through unknown means. Although blocked by restrictions, he refused to leave, insisting on meeting the Saint Monarch.

However, Taiyi Saint Monarch no longer concerned himself with the affairs of the Immortal Realm.

The Grand Celestial Master stepped forward, intending to send him away.

"Immortal Elder, please be merciful and just inform him. Let me see the Saint Monarch."

The person still refused to leave, even pulling out a jade slip, attempting to bribe the Grand Celestial Master: "This is a staff technique I happened to comprehend, possessing the power to overturn the heavens and earth. Immortal Elder, if you review it, you will surely gain some insight..."

With the Grand Celestial Master's discerning eye, how could he value the insights of a True Immortal who had not yet attained an unnamed status?

This person's attempt to curry favor failed and instead angered the Grand Celestial Master.

He swatted the jade slip to the ground and forcibly expelled the True Immortal.

"This staff technique, it seems to be the one recorded in that jade slip?"

"Why did that person insist on seeing Master back then?"

Before his consciousness plunged into darkness, these thoughts flashed through the Grand Celestial Master's mind.

...

*Clang!*

Like the sound of metal striking metal, continuous and unending, it echoed through the nine heavens.

Bai Shuyue, holding the jade staff, struck the Grand Celestial Master directly on the forehead.

Although the Grand Celestial Master was knocked unconscious, the jade pillar also suffered from the phản lực, and countless cracks instantly appeared on its surface.

"Quickly, quickly, before he wakes up, control him!"

The Boundless Wall was extremely excited, revealing its true form and emitting a myriad of divine lights.

Some of them transformed into ropes, binding the unconscious Grand Celestial Master.

While others seemed to be directly discarded in the corner, as if only to make space for suppressing the Grand Celestial Master.

A huge crack appeared in the center of the Boundless Wall, like a gaping maw.

Countless ropes attached to the Grand Celestial Master, slowly pulling him into it.

"This Wuji is not dead yet?" Bai Shuyue mumbled.

"Although he is a bit foolish, he is still the Great Dao of Wuji! How could he be killed by a single staff strike? It's just that his consciousness has been temporarily shaken, and he has lost consciousness."

"Hurry and help me drag him into my belly and refine him slowly!"

"Hahaha, I never thought this brat would suffer such a fate today!"

The Boundless Wall cheered jubilantly, and Bai Shuyue quickly helped.

Although the Grand Celestial Master was merely a child, dragging him felt like moving a mountain.

After much effort, they finally managed to move him into the Boundless Wall.

The Boundless Wall released boundless light.

The halo distorted and struggled, as if the Grand Celestial Master had already woken up and was about to break free.

Bai Shuyue watched anxiously from the side.

Fortunately, it seemed that after consuming so much over the years, the Boundless Wall’s appetite had grown.

Finally, the Grand Celestial Master’s struggles became fainter and fainter, eventually returning to calm.

"Is it alright now?"

"Temporarily. It will take a long time to truly digest him, and your help will be needed." Perhaps because it had eaten too much, the Boundless Wall's thoughts were affected, responding very slowly and sometimes incoherently.

However, Bai Shuyue, who had developed great默契 with the Boundless Wall, could still barely understand its meaning.

"Let's go quickly and find a safe place."

The Boundless Wall could no longer move and urged Bai Shuyue to carry it away.

Bai Shuyue pointed at the illusory projection of Taiyi, who had witnessed the entire capture of the Grand Celestial Master but remained indifferent, and hesitated, "This... what about it?"

"I feel that the value of this illusory projection might even surpass that of Wuji."

"Your intuition is indeed correct. However, we should not covet the illusory projection of the Saint Monarch."

The Boundless Wall, usually greedy, said such words, which surprised Bai Shuyue.

But since the Boundless Wall had said so, Bai Shuyue harbored no further greed.

She quickly fled.

The Tian Du of Yuandao State returned to its previous state of deathly silence.

Only the illusory projection of Taiyi sat silently, standing tall.

After an unknown amount of time passed, a figure arrived outside Tian Du.

Its state and appearance were somewhat strange, without a physical form, covered in a layer of pale blue halo.

Like a feather, it slowly floated into Tian Du.

Without any obstruction, following the memories of its past life, it went straight to the illusory projection of Taiyi.

The sound of praising the Dao, which had disappeared with the absence of the Grand Celestial Master, once again resounded.

The blue feather, bathed in the sound of Taiyi praising the Dao, actually revealed a faint golden light!

...

Regarding the events in Taiyi Palace, the Boundless Wall and Bai Shuyue were naturally unaware.

At this moment, they were still on the run. The Boundless Wall was explaining to Bai Shuyue the reason why it abandoned the illusory projection of Taiyi.

"Firstly, what Wuji said may not be true. He said it was purely an illusory projection?"

"What if the Master can perceive everything that happens around him through the illusory projection? Although I do not think highly of Wuji, in the eyes of the Master, his status might indeed be more important. If I dare to act against him, and he discovers it, I fear I will be punished." the Boundless Wall muttered.

"Secondly... too much of a good thing spoils it. Wuji's Great Dao alone is enough for us to digest for a while. With the illusory projection of Taiyi as well, it would only distract us."

Bai Shuyue eyed the Boundless Wall suspiciously, "Are you by any chance possessed by Wuji? These words do not sound like something you would say. Too much of a good thing spoils it?"

"Hmph. Do not think that I hid so many treasures before just because I wanted to devour them all. Of course, that is partly the reason. But the most important thing is to keep them in reserve. Perhaps they can save my life at a critical moment."

"If I can find better ones, I will replace them. If not, it is not impossible to devour them slowly."

The Boundless Wall shook its head and its beard.

Recalling the methods the Boundless Wall used to save her from the faceless figure in her previous life, Bai Shuyue nodded slightly.

"You are about to digest and refine Wuji, and you are still afraid of the Saint Monarch's punishment? Perhaps you can hide for a while, but you will have to face him eventually, right?" Bai Shuyue asked again.

"Who said I am going to truly devour Wuji?"

"I do not want to become the new Wuji. The fundamental purpose is not to help you break through your cultivation bottleneck?" the Boundless Wall retorted reproachfully.

Bai Shuyue was stunned.

"It is only to temporarily confine him within my belly for a period of time and borrow his strength. When you transcend, I will release him. And with his temperament, he will certainly not speak of being captured by us..." the Boundless Wall said smugly.

"Try to hold me tightly."

The Boundless Wall suddenly said to Bai Shuyue.

Bai Shuyue reached out and gently stroked the Boundless Wall, whose color had become somewhat strange.

A sense of chaotic emptiness arose in her heart.

"No wonder he was so arrogant... Is this [Wuji]?"

It was not a matter of whose Dao was strong or weak, but rather a suppression of seniority, like an elder looking at a junior.

Holding the Boundless Wall infused with Wuji, Bai Shuyue scanned the Xuanhuang world.

She felt that all the constraints in the world, the crisscrossing net of the Great Dao of Heaven and Earth,

Were no longer as indestructible as before.

It was as if with a mere extension of her hand, she could tear them all apart!

"Perhaps we don't need to find another safe place to cultivate."

"We can disregard all the rules within the Xuanhuang Realm itself," Bai Shuyue suddenly spoke.

"This is the miraculous use of Wuji! How about it, am I not right! This is only the initial stage. Later, when Wuji compromises further, we can borrow even more strength."

"So, stop researching this 'new method'. Just cultivate diligently and break through as soon as possible."

Hearing this, Bai Shuyue showed a rare hint of hesitation.

Chapter 1637: The Path of Immortal Execution Ascends

Despite experiencing so much, Bai Shuyue had not forgotten her dear nephew.

The reason she had the idea of creating a new method earlier was partly for Li Fan's cultivation.

Moreover, Bai Shuyue vaguely had a premonition that the potential and prospects of the new method would surpass ordinary cultivation methods.

"The Boundless Wall's perspective is limited to this lifetime."

"And my ambition is for dozens, even hundreds of lifetimes to come! I cannot scheme against Wuji before each reincarnation. Not only is it troublesome, but there is also the possibility of failure, wasting a reincarnation opportunity."

"The new method..."

"Cannot be abandoned!"

"However, this does not conflict with my temporary cultivation of the old method to quickly improve my realm. With higher strength, my perspective will naturally change, and deducing the new method will be more efficient."

In an instant, various thoughts flashed through Bai Shuyue's mind, and she nodded to the Boundless Wall, saying, "Don't worry, I have my own considerations."

Putting aside the deduction of the new method for now, Bai Shuyue, relying on the power of Wuji, disregarded the paradoxical rules of the Heaven-Bestowing Celestial Venerables within the Xuanhuang Realm and focused on cultivation.

As for resources, with the Boundless Wall's sponsorship, there was no need to worry.

The terrifying spirituality accumulated over thirty reincarnations was now revealed.

After more than ten days of seclusion, Bai Shuyue felt an invisible barrier blocking her path.

Ahead...

There was no longer a way forward.

"According to ancient immortal cultivation texts, I have now reached the end of the mortal realm, the pinnacle of Dao integration."

"If seeking immortality is hopeless, one can only seek the method of eternal life. Either by borrowing the power of the rules of heaven and earth, or by relying on treasures that extend life."

"A realm that countless cultivators throughout history have dreamed of, I have reached in ten days."

"Cultivation... is unexpectedly easy."

Bai Shuyue looked up at the sky and let out a long sigh.

Honestly, even she herself had not expected her cultivation speed to be so terrifying.

So much so that after emerging from seclusion, she was momentarily unable to react.

Let alone the Boundless Wall.

The Boundless Wall, which had been constantly urging her to cultivate quickly, fell into an unusual silence after witnessing Bai Shuyue's cultivation speed without any restrictions.

It even seemed somewhat frightened, quietly distancing itself, no longer as close as before. Bai Shuyue found it amusing: "You went to great lengths to make me cultivate, and now that I've truly worked hard, you're acting like this."

"What is the reason?"

The Boundless Wall mumbled, "I just suddenly thought of something frightening."

"Frightened?"

"Perhaps, in other worlds, you are an incredibly important figure, but in this world, you are suppressed by the special environment of the Xuanhuang Realm, and thus have always remained a mortal. If you meet your other selves from other worlds after transcending..."

"Wouldn't that be like a lamb falling into a tiger's den?"

The more the Boundless Wall thought about it, the more it felt it made sense, its expression becoming increasingly gloomy, like an eggplant left out in the frost, sighing.

"How could it be like a lamb falling into a tiger's den?" Bai Shuyue suddenly became curious.

At this moment, she did not yet understand the truth of the Mountains and Seas, the parallel existence of countless possibilities, let alone the cultivation method of transcended beings unifying themselves.

The Boundless Wall briefly explained, and then Bai Shuyue's expression became solemn.

"In that case, even after transcending, it might not necessarily be safer? Instead, it might become more dangerous due to exposure?"

"Under normal circumstances, those who reach the realm of transcendence have no need to worry about these things. After all, even if there are infinite possibilities in the Mountains and Seas, it is extremely rare for multiple selves to achieve transcendence. But with your monstrous talent, it's hard to say." The Boundless Wall sighed.

Having high cultivation talent was indeed a good thing, but if it was too high, it was not necessarily a good thing.

This was something the Boundless Wall had not considered before.

However, as someone who knew herself, Bai Shuyue was well aware of the source of her heaven-defying talent.

"Other selves in other worlds, if they don't have the ability to reincarnate continuously, would certainly not be like me." Bai Shuyue understood in her heart and felt slightly relieved.

Even though she knew the truth, she could not explain it to the Boundless Wall and simply maintained an awkward silence.

In the midst of the silence, Bai Shuyue couldn't help but let her thoughts wander again, becoming curious about the truth behind her continuous reincarnation.

"If I keep reincarnating, what about the other me in other worlds?"

"What kind of power is controlling all of this?"

When she was still a mortal, Bai Shuyue did not feel much fear towards her ability to reincarnate continuously, considering it merely a lucky gift.

But now, as she was just one step away from becoming an immortal, she saw everything more clearly because of it.

This was a divine power that even True Immortals could not reach or imagine!

The more she thought about it, the more she felt her own insignificance and powerlessness before it.

The Boundless Wall and Bai Shuyue both fell into a long silence, but their fears were not the same.

After a long while, it was finally the Boundless Wall that broke the silence.

"Damn it, I still believe my intuition. This should not be a misfortune, but a great blessing!" he gritted his teeth and said.

Bai Shuyue snapped back to reality, shaking her head with a sneer, "Let's take it one step at a time. I was originally just a mere mortal, and now I have lived so many more lifetimes. Even if I die abruptly, it will have been worth it. Why think about so many things for no reason?"

After this interlude, the two officially discussed the method of ascending to immortality.

"Immortals, unlike mortals, possess the power of [Mountains and Seas]."

"The mountains above impart the high status of immortals; the infinite sea provides endless sources..."

Like any other being hearing the truth of Mountains and Seas for the first time, Bai Shuyue's mind was deeply shaken. The power of immortals far exceeded their imagination.

"No wonder the difference between immortals and mortals is like a chasm," Bai Shuyue marveled internally.

The Boundless Wall continued, "Your current realm is sufficient. If the Immortal Court were still in existence, and I could secretly obtain an Imperial Decree from the Immortal Emperor, I could make you an immortal on the spot. However..."

"The Immortal Realm is destroyed, and even with the supplies in my belly, they are probably useless now."

Bai Shuyue was somewhat puzzled, "How much have you swallowed into your belly?"

The Boundless Wall rolled its large eye, "What do you know? Having provisions in my belly gives me peace of mind. If it weren't for my foresight in hoarding so many supplies in the past, how could I have survived the great tribulation of the Immortal Realm's destruction?"

"Perhaps it's precisely because I've eaten too much that my current strength is not as good as before." Bai Shuyue scoffed.

"There is some truth to that. However..." The Boundless Wall's large eye rolled, speaking with some self-satisfaction, "The strength I pursue is actually quite different from you cultivators."

Having been together for so many lifetimes, this was the first time Bai Shuyue had heard the Boundless Wall say such a thing. After thinking about it, her eyes revealed disbelief, "Could it be that your ultimate pursuit is still..."

"That's right! My wish is to become the foremost pillar of talent in the Mountains and Seas!" the Boundless Wall declared solemnly.

After some teasing, the previous oppressive atmosphere completely dissipated.

To perform the act of slaying immortals with the body of a mortal should have been a fantastical tale.

But with the Great Dao of Wuji in hand, it was not impossible.

Chapter 1638: The Empty and Profound Is But a Plaything

"Possessing a sharp weapon, the urge to kill arises."

Feeling the aura of Wuji surrounding her, Bai Shuyue's heart suddenly surged with heroic spirit.

True Immortals, Nameless True Immortals, so what?

With the body of a mortal, it is not impossible to slay them!

Bai Shuyue's first thought was of the Star Sea Origin True Intent outside the Xuanhuang Realm.

"Although you have the ambition to slay immortals, you must proceed step by step!"

However, with her current strength, even without using Wuji or the power of True Immortal Seal Scripts, Ou Shangtian would not be her match. Choosing him as a target would be pure bullying.

Fortunately, the Boundless Wall quickly resolved Bai Shuyue's concerns: "Even if immortal artifacts transform into mortals, they cannot completely shed their past immortal identities. As long as we are near them, I can generally sense them. Leave the matter of finding opponents to me!"

Having gradually become accustomed to the Boundless Wall's various magical abilities, Bai Shuyue nodded in agreement.

One person and one tile began to search the vast Xuanhuang Realm.

The first suitable opponent they found was named Kong You.

It was said that she was a renowned beauty in the Myriad Immortal Alliance. Even Bai Shuyue, upon seeing her for the first time, could not help but sigh, wondering how such a captivating creature could exist in the world.

"Inside this young lady's body is a piece of the Taiyin Jade Pendant, originating from the Immortal Realm. It was originally a body of extreme Yin and extreme softness, a rare cultivation prodigy in the world. However, someone implanted half a piece of incomplete Taiyang璞玉 into her."

"Naturally! Someone is deliberately tormenting her! When Yin and Yang are imbalanced, she is consumed by lust. She must have a male companion who holds the other half of the Taiyang璞玉 to help her resolve it. Even if the other party is a mortal with no strength to even tie a chicken, she can only accept whatever is offered, or even actively seek intimacy."

The Boundless Wall examined Kong You, seeing through her secrets completely, "And, in this process, she cannot enjoy any of the benefits brought by the harmony of Yin and Yang. All of it goes to the other half. Tsk tsk tsk, the people of the Xuanhuang Realm play so well..."

"Enough!" The Boundless Wall was interrupted by Bai Shuyue's cold voice when it was halfway through speaking.

Although Bai Shuyue had lived alone for more than ten years and had long forgotten about romantic love, she was, after all, a woman and understood the torment such methods would bring to a woman.

"Kong You has reached the Dao Integration realm, yet she is still treated as a plaything. I imagine the person behind this must be one of those Law-Imparting Elders from the Myriad Immortal Alliance. While the two were communicating telepathically, Kong You, who had been inexplicably blocked, had already made her move.

Renowned among the cultivators of the Myriad Immortal Alliance, Kong You did not rely solely on her beauty. Her own strength was also not to be underestimated.

With the accompanying Taiyin power, combined with the Dao Integration soul, [Youse], she wove thousands of obscure threads, harming and trapping enemies invisibly.

Taiyin is endless and inexhaustible. Even in a frontal attrition, few in the same realm could match her.

But...

She could not withstand a single strike from Bai Shuyue.

This was the first time Bai Shuyue had actively attempted to manipulate the power of the Great Dao of Wuji to fight an enemy.

As if her abilities were suddenly stripped away, the power of Taiyin suddenly abandoned her, and the thousands of threads woven by Kong You slowly dispersed in the air.

Her hidden figure was also stunned and exposed.

Bai Shuyue struck her directly on the forehead.

A moment later, feeling Bai Shuyue's cold gaze, the Boundless Wall quickly changed its tune, "To toy with people's hearts like this is truly deserving of death!"

Despite being indignant, Bai Shuyue did not lose her composure. After having the Boundless Wall investigate again and confirm Kong You's words were true, Bai Shuyue finally made up her mind.

"The next person to test our skills will be the one behind this."

"Can you help me find out who it is?"

Sensing Bai Shuyue's unprecedented rage, the Boundless Wall dared not refuse in the slightest.

After helping Kong You retrieve the half piece of Yang Jade from her body, it swallowed it whole.

After a while, it spat out a complete piece and handed it to Kong You.

"Little lady, reabsorb this Jade. With your cultivation level, you will achieve a perfect balance of Yin and Yang within a few years. From then on, you will no longer be controlled by others!" The Boundless Wall coughed lightly and said in a slow voice.

Kong You seemed to not dare to believe it. Tremblingly, she took the Yang Jade, feeling the familiar yet strange complete aura. Even after enduring countless hardships, she had never shed a tear, but now, she cried.

Solemnly putting away the Yang Jade, she kowtowed to thank the two for their life-saving grace.

"Hmm, it feels good to be a good person occasionally. Although I lost some of the supplies in my belly." The Boundless Wall shook its head and beard.

As if it had touched some spiritual intuition, she vaguely felt as if she were about to touch upon a truth.

Unfortunately, the feeling flashed by and disappeared before she could grasp it.

The Boundless Wall's next words pulled her back to reality, "With the method of Yin-Yang Jade restraint broken, and the carefully crafted toy damaged, the person behind it will surely be furious and come looking for us. We just need to wait patiently here."

As Bai Shuyue had predicted, the hidden figure behind this unexpectedly did not come looking for Kong You for a long time, unlike someone whose beloved toy had been broken and who would be furious.

Being attacked by an outsider in his own world.

Chapter 1639: The Mountains and Seas Do Not Spare Immortals

Hearing that there were many other toys like herself, the Law-Imparter Feng, had died, Kong You's face showed an extremely complex expression.

"Oh, I remember him, it's him!"

Even the secrets of Immortal Emperors and Saint Monarchs were not beyond his knowledge. At first, the Immortals thought his words were exaggerated, but after the Hundred Knowledge Immortal wrote a secret record of the Immortal Emperors, the entire Immortal Realm believed him!"

Once released, it caused the Immortal Emperors to fly into a rage and order the Hundred Knowledge Immortal to be captured."

"This action by the Hundred Knowledge Immortal even angered a hidden Emperor who had been in seclusion for many years. He personally took action and forcibly erased the Immortal Emperor's Secret Record, which had already spread among the Immortals, from everyone's memories..."

"What happened afterward?" Bai Shuyue asked.

"What else could happen? His extremely arrogant behavior even angered the Saint Monarch. Naturally, he was captured and suppressed. After this, people finally understood the reason why the Hundred Knowledge Immortal was called [Hundred Knowledge]."

"It wasn't because of the Great Dao he cultivated, but because he forged an immortal artifact called [As If Intent]!"

"Living beings are cautious and guarded towards others. But towards themselves, they have no such defenses. It was precisely by using this principle that the Hundred Knowledge Immortal spent the first half of his life gathering countless treasures, finally forging such a heaven-defying immortal artifact, [As If Intent]!"

"We beings, traversing the Great Dao, are like shadows of the Great Dao. But As If Intent could do, [to make shadow imitate shadow]. To become the shadow of the Dao's shadow! Upon seeing it, one would instinctively feel a sense of closeness, even mistaking it for themselves... It was extremely bizarre, even Immortal Emperors couldn't escape it. The shadow of As If Intent covered almost the entire Immortal Realm, seeing through everyone's hearts. Such malicious behavior was universally condemned, resulting in no one willing to speak on his behalf after he was suppressed. After many years, his deeds have almost completely disappeared from people's minds."

"If I weren't so knowledgeable, I would have almost forgotten this past event."

The Boundless Wall slowly narrated a past event.

However, Bai Shuyue listened with a frown.

"Are you sure you haven't misremembered?"

"Misremember? How is that possible? Don't question my memory!" The Boundless Wall finally called itself "this great master" again, showing great indignation at Bai Shuyue's doubt.

"But I always feel that there are many inconsistencies in the story you told, and even some parts are contradictory..." Bai Shuyue murmured.

"Illusion, it's definitely your illusion!?" the Boundless Wall swore confidently.

Bai Shuyue, however, firmly believed in her judgment: "The shadow of the Dao's shadow, everything is like me. This ability is indeed unbelievable, but what does it have to do with the name [As If Intent]? You said you angered the Saint Monarch, and although I haven't seen the Saint Monarch's true face, I know he possesses supreme divine abilities and cultivation. Even the destruction of multiple possibilities might not be taken seriously by the Saint Monarch. Why would such a trivial matter as leaking secrets infuriate the Saint Monarch? And..."

"Be careful, be careful." After Bai Shuyue's reminder, the Boundless Wall also slowly realized the inaccuracies in its memory. But it quickly realized something and hurriedly stopped Bai Shuyue from continuing.

"I understand now, this Hundred Knowledge Immortal, is [Vast Seas Unforgiven]!"

"Vast Seas Unforgiven?"

"A person so wicked that even after the Dao Annihilation crisis ends and the Mountains and Seas are rebuilt, they will not be forgiven! It is said that they will be eternally suppressed in the depths of the Shore, never to be free for generations..." the Boundless Wall whispered.

"Good heavens, how did a shard of an immortal artifact made by such a villain fall into the Xuanhuang Realm? This is not good. Let me think, why did I escape to the Xuanhuang Realm back then? Was it truly a coincidence?" The Boundless Wall muttered to itself with some fear.

Bai Shuyue, however, was still contemplating, unable to connect [As If Intent] with the grave crime of Vast Seas Unforgiven.

Meanwhile, Law-Imparter Jiang, who had been observing the shifting expressions and constant glances cast upon him by the two, felt an inexplicable sense of unease.

He said sternly, "Seniors, please rest assured. I already know the details of this matter. Feng indeed deserved to die, and even failed in his duty as a Law-Imparter. The Myriad Immortal Alliance will not pursue this matter. Instead, we should thank the seniors for helping the Myriad Immortal Alliance eliminate a corrupt element!"

"Seniors, you were right earlier. I have indeed been too lenient with other Law-Imparters. Perhaps I should truly reorganize things..."

After saying this, Law-Imparter Jiang prepared to hastily take his leave.

"Wait!" the Boundless Wall called out to him.

"Let me take a good look first!"

Law-Imparter Jiang did not know what the Boundless Wall wanted to look at so intently.

But it was likely related to his innate special ability.

Although he instinctively wanted to refuse, a streak of green light enveloped him.

His heart startled, and he tried to resist with magic, but it was like sinking into mud; he could not exert any of his strength.

He could only let the other party gaze upon him.

Law-Imparter Jiang secretly lamented, but there was nothing he could do. He could only try his best to activate his "Everything is like me" characteristic to its extreme, in order to protect himself.

"What are you looking for?" Bai Shuyue asked the Boundless Wall, which was acting so mysteriously.

"I'm looking to see if I can find the memories of his arrival in the Xuanhuang Realm from this fellow." The Boundless Wall's green light continued to swirl.

Its tone had also become unprecedentedly serious.

"I always thought that the Young Master and I coming to the Xuanhuang Realm at the same time was a coincidence. But recently, while searching the vast Xuanhuang Realm with you, I have discovered traces of so many incredible powers..."

"And this is just the tip of the iceberg! It's truly unimaginable what else this small Xuanhuang Realm hides. That's why I was afraid and had to confirm it again."

The green light flickered, displaying the entire life of Law-Imparter Jiang.

From the thousands of years he presided over the Myriad Immortal Alliance, to when he was a mere mortal disciple of a Law-Imparter, and even to his ignorant childhood. Although not every detail was revealed, most of his past was exposed to Bai Shuyue and the Boundless Wall.

Although Law-Imparter Jiang could not move, his face turned extremely red with shame and indignation.

However, the instigator, the Boundless Wall, was completely uninterested in these facts.

The green light continued to shine, attempting to probe even further back into the past.

The time spent on this investigation was longer than all the previous ones combined.

The Boundless Wall seemed to become "thinner" due to the immense consumption.

Finally, a change occurred.

The tide of Dao Annihilation swallowed Mountains and Seas; the Immortal Realm shattered, immortals died like ants.

Terrible scenes unfolded, as if the Boundless Wall was transported back to the time of the great tribulation.

The Boundless Wall's body trembled uncontrollably with fear.

The Immortal Realm was shattered, but a fragment of light broke free from its prison.

Like a meteor, it streaked across the disintegrating Immortal Realm, doing its best to avoid the constantly approaching tide of Dao Annihilation.

After constant traversal, it finally escaped the Immortal Realm and arrived in the lower star seas.

However, as if sensing something or being attracted by something.

While fleeing through the lower star seas, it suddenly changed direction.

Towards the direction of Xuanhuang!

During this period, as if to evade pursuit, the flowing light itself underwent changes.

Until it finally merged into the tiny Xuanhuang Realm.

...

*Buzz!* With a humming sound, the green light exploded.

A nearly invisible crack appeared on the Boundless Wall, and the Boundless Wall emerged from the reconnaissance.

Law-Imparter Jiang, now free, fled in a panic.

Bai Shuyue was about to pursue him, but was stopped by the Boundless Wall's frantic voice.

"Don't go after him, run quickly!"

"Run? Run from what?" Bai Shuyue was slightly stunned.

"Disaster has struck. My probing of the past scenes of the Immortal Realm's destruction has attracted the attention of Dao Annihilation! The tide of world destruction is coming!"

As if confirming the Boundless Wall's words, at this moment, the Xuanhuang Realm, the Utmost Dark Star Sea, and even the entire Primordial Possibility,

All fell into a brief silence.

A moment later, like a vast tidal roar, a deafening roar faintly came from beyond the heavens.

As if dark clouds were pressing down, the sky turned eerily black.

And all living beings felt a sense of impending doom in their hearts.

"This feeling, this feeling..."

"Run quickly!" the Boundless Wall screamed.

But it was already too late.

For some unknown reason, the Dao Annihilation triggered by the Boundless Wall's probe into Law-Imparter Jiang's past memories was unprecedentedly powerful.

It even surpassed that caused by Li Fan.

Even the illusory projection left by Shou Qiu could not withstand it.

And it arrived so quickly.

The high walls shattered, the Primordial collapsed.

Including Bai Shuyue and the Boundless Wall, the living beings of the Primordial Possibility were instantly swallowed.

Only Li Fan's figure managed to escape in time.

Chapter 1640: Shan Hai Immortal Outer Heaven

"Vast Seas Unforgiven Immortal? What the heck is that..."

This Dao Annihilation came so abruptly that even Li Fan, who had been watching from the sidelines, barely had time to react and nearly perished in the Dao Annihilation.

However, having experienced great storms, Li Fan quickly calmed down after his narrow escape.

"I didn't expect the Law-Imparter Jiang's [Everything is like me] ability to have such an origin."

With Li Fan's experience, he could tell at a glance that the Hundred Knowledge Immortal and the immortal artifact [As If Intent] were definitely not as simple as the Boundless Wall initially described.

"Angering the Saint Monarch, Vast Seas Unforgiven. Could it be that this Hundred Knowledge Immortal is one of the two beings suppressed in the Eternal Heavenly Steps of the Shore?"

"And this strange reaction from the Dao Annihilation tide..."

In his past numerous close encounters with Dao Annihilation, Li Fan had already confirmed that Dao Annihilation possessed some kind of consciousness. Or rather, if Dao Annihilation were regarded as an army marching forth, then there was a supreme commander orchestrating the Dao Annihilation's attack.
