The army advanced, infiltrating everywhere; encircling and slowly eroding; encountering fierce resistance, it would dispatch more troops to crush the enemy completely...

But this time, upon sensing something related to the Hundred Knowledge Immortal, Dao Annihilation's reaction was different from usual.

"It's as if a scout discovered the trace of the target enemy, and instantly summoned the main force, pointing straight towards it!"

Li Fan felt a sudden shock in his heart.

"The essence of Dao Annihilation is the merging of Mountains and Seas. It is the return of the power of [Stars], transcending the Mountains and Seas. Merely a fragment of an immortal artifact forged by it could cause such a commotion in Dao Annihilation."

"In a sense, could this Hundred Knowledge Immortal, or rather, [As If Intent], be worthy of the attention of [Stars]?"

Instinctively, Li Fan felt a sense of curiosity.

"Perhaps I can glean more from Law-Imparter Jiang's memories, but there is no longer an opportunity in this lifetime."

"Let's wait for the contest of virtue and reason."

Li Fan glanced towards the area beyond the Mountains and Seas.

Instead of seeking refuge in other possibilities, he simply unfurled a lone sail of Mountains and Seas and drifted on the tide of Dao Annihilation.

Feeling the surging undercurrents of Dao Annihilation, Li Fan had a realization: "Even though the Primordial was destroyed, they have not given up their search. This means that in the eyes of Dao Annihilation, the annihilation tide of this magnitude could not possibly kill the Hundred Knowledge Immortal. If he disappeared, it must be because he had once again escaped and hidden."

"To evoke such emotional turmoil among the Saints of the Shore, he is truly extraordinary!"

Li Fan recalled his encounters with the Saints in his simulations. They always appeared calm and confident. Even when observing Huizhen and his own infinite spirituality, it was the same.

It was hard to imagine what the Hundred Knowledge Immortal had done to warrant the Saints personally intervening to suppress him.

"The source of Law-Imparter Jiang's power, that fragment that escaped during the destruction of the Immortal Realm, is perhaps only one of the remaining traces of the Hundred Knowledge Immortal on the Shore."

"Even so, Dao Annihilation attaches such importance to it."

From all this, it could be inferred that the Hundred Knowledge Immortal, or [As If Intent], might play a crucial role in this great battle between Dao Annihilation and the Mountains and Seas.

Not to mention deciding the outcome, but at the very least, it could significantly alter the current stalemate.

"In that case, this Hundred Knowledge Immortal is also unique to the Primordial."

"What's going on? Is this possibility I'm in becoming too outrageous?"

"Not only Shou Qiu, a Saint, but also such a character?"

"Plus Jing Fen, Dao De, King Xuanyuan and his wife..."

"Not to mention me, and Huizhen."

"They said a single possibility has an upper limit on potential. So why..."

Li Fan frowned deeply.

"Perhaps, I picked the right name for the Primordial back then by accident?"

But observing the facts, it was contrary to this.

The Primordial Immortal Realm had long been destroyed. The remaining parts had been destroyed countless times.

There was nothing special about it.

"Where exactly did things go wrong?" Li Fan keenly sensed the deep contradiction.

Everything seemed so strange and disharmonious.

"Theoretically, in times of prosperity, talent emerges. If the foundation of a single possibility is sufficient to produce so many powerhouses of the Mountains and Seas, then that possibility cannot be too weak. But now..."

Li Fan drifted with the current, floating on the Dao Annihilation, hidden within the Mountains and Seas, contemplating this issue.

Within the Mountains and Seas, time does not pass.

After an unknown period, after witnessing the scenes of other nearby possibilities where the Immortal Realm was still prosperous, Li Fan was enlightened. A thought flashed through his mind.

"I always thought the Primordial Immortal Realm had been destroyed long ago. But..."

"What if, I say, what if Emperor Tian Luo's plan had succeeded?"

Emperor Tian Luo's method of saving the world was to promote the Immortal Realm to a higher level. Transcending the Mountains and Seas would naturally allow them to escape Dao Annihilation. Although it sounded like fantasy, the original plan was unknown.

The fact that he had many supporters at the time suggested that the plan had some feasibility.

Even if the probability was extremely small, it was not entirely impossible for it to succeed.

If Emperor Tian Luo had truly achieved transcendence with the Primordial Immortal Realm at that time...

Then the anomalies of the Primordial would seem reasonable.

After transcending, the foundation of the entire possibility would undergo a qualitative change, benefiting countless beings in the Primordial. Even the "residue" shed during the transcendence process would have an impact. Mediocre talents would become geniuses, and geniuses would become peerless geniuses.

Surpassing the ordinary, standing out from the crowd. Those who originally had an upper limit of only Nameless True Immortal could now aspire to the realm of transcendence.

"Perhaps, this is the only way to explain why the small Primordial produced so many transcendent beings."

"And..."

"I should have realized long ago that the Mountains and Seas are boundless, with infinite possibilities, and that [Huizhen]'s choice of [Primordial] might not have been a coincidence."

"What is special is not only the Xuanhuang Realm, but also the [Primordial]."

"It is precisely by inheriting the resources of the Primordial that the small Xuanhuang Realm appears to be so full of hidden dragons and crouching tigers."

Thinking of this, as if clearing away the fog, Li Fan felt that everything suddenly became smooth.

Although all of this was his "guess" so far.

But Li Fan's intuition, like a guiding light, told him at the moment he "guessed" it, that this might be the truth.

"It's truly incredible."

Faced with this outcome, Li Fan himself fell silent for a long time.

Precisely because it was too bizarre, even though there were already various signs before, Li Fan had not thought in this direction.

Nor did he dare to think so.

However, by chance in this lifetime, upon learning of the existence of the [Hundred Knowledge Immortal], Li Fan suddenly broke through his previous limitations.

But greater questions followed.

"Who exactly is Emperor Tian Luo?"

"Where did the Primordial Immortal Realm go after successfully transcending?"

Chapter 1641: The End of the World Saint

Perhaps only a Saint Sovereign could know the answer to this question.

With Li Fan's current strength and realm, overthinking was futile.

Concealing himself within the Dao Annihilation, observing everything around him, Li Fan let out a long sigh until this disturbance completely subsided: "The Mountains and Seas are boundless. Beyond the Mountains and Seas, are there still Mountains and Seas?"

"What indeed are Stars and Creator Gods?"

At this moment, Li Fan stood outside the ruins of the Primordial, as if he had returned to the wreckage of Xuanjing City, gazing upon the grand scenery of the cultivation world for the first time with mortal eyes.

"That moment, just like this moment."

"Only now, I am no longer the simple Grand Tutor Li of the past!"

"Even if my body is like an ant, I possess the power to overturn the heavens and earth."

This was the absolute confidence Li Fan had gained through countless cycles of reincarnation, after understanding True Reversion, understanding his own infinite spirituality, and understanding intuition.

"The path ahead is distant and vague, but I will surely walk it to its end."

"Neither Dao nor Saint Venerable can stop me in the slightest."

"Let's give it a try!"

There was no grand declaration, nor any fiery passion.

Li Fan simply uttered these words faintly in his heart.

Only the remaining Mountains and Seas served as witness.

...

In order to probe the secret of achieving Sainthood through Dao and Virtue, Li Fan spent the next period selecting a remote region of possibility clusters, far from the Shore and outside the influence of the Taiwei Sacred Dynasty.

He then scattered his True Spirit Seeds everywhere.

"Such a vast expanse of Mountains and Seas, burning up in an instant. If one were trapped within without knowledge, it would be truly difficult to distinguish truth from falsehood, and one would only feel that the end of the Mountains and Seas had truly arrived." Li Fan narrowed his eyes, mentally simulating the scenario and nodding with satisfaction.

"I just don't know how Ho Gan Immortal is preparing."

Although they did not have a pre-arranged method of contact between them, Li Fan had deliberately left a trace of his aura before departing.

If Ho Gan Immortal had made up his mind, he would surely contact him following that trace.

"Let's wait a bit longer."

"If he hesitates for too long..."

"Perhaps I can find the Faceless Immortal again."

In Li Fan's hand, the stone statue of the Faceless Immortal from the Xuanhuang Realm was enveloped by flowing silver light.

Although the Dao Annihilation tide of the Primordial had arrived suddenly, the Immortal of Dao and Virtue would not perish so easily.

The lingering traces of immortal power within the Faceless Immortal statue were proof of this.

"When the Primordial collapsed, and I escaped, I seemed to see two or three other figures. However, amidst the Dao Annihilation tide, escaping was paramount, and I did not see them clearly."

"And there probably wasn't the Faceless Immortal among them. This brat..."

"Truly cautious!"

Ho Gan Immortal did not make Li Fan wait too long.

One day, while Li Fan was still drifting within the Mountains and Seas, his heart suddenly stirred.

He then transmitted his current location.

After waiting for a moment on the spot, a wisp of black and white energy traversed the Dao Annihilation and descended before him.

Compared to the last time he saw him, Ho Gan Immortal's own flow of Virtue had progressed further.

He was not far from Li Fan's previous state as a Saint of Virtue!

"It seems you have made up your mind and resolved the remaining conscience within your heart beforehand. Decisive!" Li Fan observed and praised slowly.

"It's either success or death." Ho Gan Immortal cupped his hands, his expressionless.

"Before the grand plan begins, I still have a question in my heart. Can Fellow Daoist enlighten me?"

"Speak freely." Li Fan smiled.

"Fellow Daoist, are you a Saint?" Ho Gan Immortal stared intently at Li Fan, his gaze burning.

It was as if he wanted to engrave Li Fan's every subtle expression into his memory.

"Saint?" Li Fan chuckled disdainfully and spoke frankly: "Fellow Daoist, you are thinking too much."

"If I were a Saint, I'm afraid that the [Virtue] of the Mountains and Seas would not be left for the two of you to attain!"

Li Fan's words did not seem like a lie. Upon receiving the answer, Ho Gan Immortal let out a long sigh.

But then, his brows furrowed, and a greater doubt surged in his heart.

"I know your doubts. Why do I understand you two so well? And why do I possess this divine ability to burn the Mountains and Seas?"

"I cannot reveal the specific details. However..."

"There are mountains beyond mountains, and seas beyond seas. Whatever happens in the world is not surprising," Li Fan said calmly.

These words had a greater impact on Ho Gan Immortal's heart than the revelation that Li Fan might be a Saint of the Mountains and Seas.

"Mountains beyond mountains? What does that mean?"

"Could it be that this person comes from another Mountain and Sea?"

His heart trembling violently, Ho Gan Immortal's mind flashed with the ancient legend in an instant.

The reason why Saints were willing to go one after another, traversing the Eternal Void, to the previous segment of Mountains and Seas, and jointly undertake the mission of saving the Mountains and Seas with countless cultivators from different time periods.

It was originally because someone had come from the end of the Mountains and Seas, defying the current and crossing over.

It ignited hope.

If not for this initial spark, the beings of the Mountains and Seas might still be fighting amongst themselves, without a unified goal.

"Perhaps this person comes from a different time of the Mountains and Seas?"

"Having crossed the Eternal Void several times, this could explain why his True Spirit is almost inexhaustible."

"Moreover, meeting for the first time, he directly claims to help me achieve Sainthood..."

In Ho Gan Immortal's mind, countless thoughts flashed by.

All the previous doubts seemed to have a perfect explanation.

"Although only the Saint realm allows one to traverse the Eternal Void. But as he said, the Mountains and Seas are boundless. No matter what happens, it is not surprising. Perhaps he was severely injured during the crossing and fell from his realm."

"Or perhaps, what he said was that he is not a Saint from our spacetime Mountains and Seas."

"Regardless, the most crucial thing is..."

"Since this person is not a Saint, then I don't need to worry so much!"

His gaze finally became resolute, and Ho Gan Immortal cupped his hands again: "I have learned."

"Fellow Daoist, when will your plan be executed?"

"I am ready to confront the other party head-on." His tone was calm and fearless.

"So be it!"

"There's no time like the present!"

Li Fan said, tossing the stone statue of the Faceless Immortal from the Xuanhuang Realm over.

"With this object, can you track his whereabouts?"

A flicker of surprise flashed in Ho Gan Immortal's eyes: "Given his cautious nature, he actually left such a flaw."

The black and white energies of Dao and Virtue enveloped the stone statue of the Faceless Immortal.

Slowly, a face grew on the originally ethereal face of the statue.

It resembled Ho Gan Immortal somewhat, but was not entirely the same.

Instead, it was more similar to the Saint Sovereign of Virtue that Li Fan had seen in his previous life.

"He is me, and I am him. Although Dao and Virtue have split..."

"But with this medium, it is not difficult to connect with him."

"Hmph, refusing to speak? In that case..."

The black and white energies grew more concentrated.

Weaving into a mist.

Under the dense fog, the stone statue seemed to come alive.

It actually slowly turned its head and looked towards a certain direction in the Mountains and Seas.

Suddenly...

"How is this possible? He's already dead?"

Accompanying Ho Gan Immortal's incredulous cry, as if seeing something forbidden, the stone statue's head was also broken off simultaneously.

It fell to the ground!

Chapter 1642: The Instigator of the Same Origin

One stone stirred a thousand ripples!

The Annihilation of the Dao seemed to sense something, and the tide gradually rose.

Li Fan felt something was amiss, his spirit instantly tensed, fully prepared to enact his True Reversion.

Fortunately, this unknown, bizarre power only severed the stone statue's head. It did not take any further action.

Ho Gan Immortal, while startled, touched his own neck.

At the moment the stone statue's head fell, he felt as if he too had suffered an attack.

Ho Gan Immortal's flow of Virtue was in near perfection. He considered himself only one step away from the realm of a Saint.

Yet, when facing that strange power just now, he felt as if he had no power to resist!

How was this possible?

Could it truly be the work of a Saint?

"Can you grasp its origin?" Li Fan asked with a solemn expression.

Ho Gan Immortal gazed into the mountains and seas for a long time before shaking his head and replying, "It came erratically and mysteriously... difficult."

"Besides, even if I could sense it, I wouldn't dare to delve deeper."

"My other self, though weaker in strength, still possesses the true intent of Virtue. His power transcends, it would be extremely difficult to kill him."

Ho Gan Immortal's words were clearly implied.

However, Li Fan held a different opinion.

Even a being like the Hundred Knowledge Immortal, who allegedly threatened the safety of the entire segment of mountains and seas, was not killed by the various Saints, but merely suppressed in the eternal heavenly steps.

The Faceless Immortal, though lacking virtue, had not committed any morally bankrupt acts to date.

The Saints had no reason to intervene.

"Then, besides them, who else in the mountains and seas possesses such strength?"

Both men fell into an eerie silence.

The sudden demise of the Faceless Immortal had completely shattered their plan.

Ho Gan Immortal's path to Sainthood was temporarily dashed, and Li Fan's intention to glimpse the true meaning of Virtue also fell through.

Faced with this unexpected turn of events, Li Fan, while inwardly shocked, also felt a surge of inexplicable anger.

"In my previous life, the Faceless Immortal lived quite well. This time, however, he died mysteriously. Is it related to the destruction of the Primordial or the Hundred Knowledge Immortal?"

"I can clearly still feel the remnants of his immortal power on the Faceless Immortal statue..."

Li Fan couldn't help but look at Ho Gan Immortal with suspicion.

As if sensing Li Fan's question, Ho Gan Immortal could only explain with helplessness: "The flow of Virtue is ceaseless; this is our divine ability to avoid calamity. Wherever we leave our traces, there will be residual traces of Virtue. It can be seen as a special clone we leave behind. If the main body unfortunately perishes, as long as there are still residual traces of Virtue in the mountains and seas, we can be reborn from the destruction."

"It should have been like this," Ho Gan Immortal said heavily, his expression extremely grim.

"Now, he is truly dead."

Ho Gan Immortal pointed to the beheaded stone statue: "Although there are still traces of Virtue flowing on it, it has lost its 'main backbone' that should have existed. Even if the Virtue can revive on its own in the future, he will not return."

"This is true death."

Li Fan vaguely heard a hint of shared sorrow and undeniable fear in Ho Gan Immortal's words.

After all, he and the Faceless Immortal were two sides of the same coin, separated from Virtue.

If that unknown, bizarre entity could kill the Faceless Immortal, it could also kill Ho Gan Immortal!

"Not only did it kill the main body, but it also erased it as an individual from the mountains and seas."

"All the preparations made in the past became irrelevant the moment he disappeared."

"This is a true method of annihilation!"

While the method was terrifying, what made Li Fan more uneasy was its sudden appearance without warning and its ethereal, untraceable nature.

Li Fan had traveled nearly a tenth of the mountains and seas. Coupled with the vast influence of the Saint Dynasty that spanned the mountains and seas, there were few unknown realms left for Li Fan.

He had thought so himself.

The sudden appearance of this bizarre force that killed the Faceless Immortal was a great shock.

It was like every time he thought he had fully explored the secrets of the Xuanhuang Realm, the Xuanhuang Realm would always give him another surprise.

More importantly...

This force seemed to be very close to him!

If the mountains and seas were seen as a gradually familiar pond, then now, a terrifying monster lurking in the depths of the water was ready to devour anyone.

How could this not make Li Fan feel shocked and angry?

The shock and anger were not due to the opponent's power, but the unknown.

The Saints of the Shore and Emperor Tai Wei were indeed powerful, but Li Fan could avoid them if he couldn't provoke them.

What he feared was this kind of entity, powerful enough to threaten Li Fan, yet always lurking in the shadows.

If he were unlucky, perhaps one day, while Li Fan was roaming the mountains and seas, he might stumble right into it.

Unable to suppress the unease in his heart, Li Fan made a decision: he would take advantage of the lingering clues from the Faceless Immortal's death to probe for more information about the perpetrator.

Not necessarily to fully ascertain the perpetrator's identity, but at the very least, to ascertain the general region they occupied in the mountains and seas. Before he had sufficient strength to avoid danger, he would try his best to steer clear of them.

With this thought, Li Fan looked at Ho Gan Immortal again and sneered, "You're scared?"

"The opportunity to become a Saint is right before your eyes, yet it was cut short by a single blow. As the saying goes, obstructing someone's path is like killing their parents."

"You two are one, two sides of Virtue. His death is like your own demise."

"The person who killed your entire family is right in front of you, and you choose to flee?"

"Do you not even have the courage to investigate?" Li Fan stared intently at Ho Gan Immortal.

Ho Gan Immortal fell into silence again, appearing quite hesitant.

"If that's the case, then forget I said anything. I didn't expect the legendary True Immortal of Virtue to be so timid," Li Fan tutted and shook his head.

"You don't need to provoke me. Rather, I'm somewhat curious why you are so concerned about this murderer?" Ho Gan Immortal countered.

"Firstly, it's because I'm upset about losing the opportunity to witness the birth of a Saint. Secondly..."

Li Fan's gaze was distant: "I suspect this murderer is someone I have been tracking."

This statement once again stirred the waves within Ho Gan Immortal's heart: "Are you so sure you can help me become a Saint?"

"If Virtue were complete, then it would be almost certain. But now... perhaps we have to wait for many years, for Virtue to flow and a new non-virtue to arise. I hope that by then, this segment of mountains and seas will still exist, and you will still be alive," Li Fan said with an enigmatic smile.

Having said that, his figure began to fade, about to depart.

"Wait!" At the last moment, Ho Gan Immortal suddenly called out.

"Let's try it for now. I hope that when the time is right again in the future, you can help me again!"

After all, the temptation of becoming a Saint was too great. Even if it was just a vague promise with no foundation, Ho Gan Immortal was unwilling to give it up just like that.

"Easily said! Rest assured, if there's an opportunity, I will definitely help you become a Saint!" Li Fan said proudly.

After reaching an agreement, Ho Gan Immortal looked at the severed head of the Faceless Immortal statue ahead and took a deep breath.

Then, he reached out and grabbed his own head, muttering in a low voice.

He actually tore his own head from his body.

"Please reside, precious one," Ho Gan Immortal's head, held in his own hands, glared with wide eyes, murmuring in a low voice.

Ho Gan Immortal's body, however, moved rather stiffly, step by step towards the Faceless Immortal statue.

Finally, holding his head with both hands with extreme solemnity, he placed it on the statue's glowing neck.

The stone body of the Faceless Immortal, Ho Gan Immortal's head.

The two, originally one, underwent extremely miraculous changes upon their combination.

It was as if the Faceless Immortal, who had been completely dead, was now resurrected!

As if experiencing everything the Faceless Immortal had gone through in his life, a trace of fear gradually appeared on Ho Gan Immortal's face.

His limbs flailed uncontrollably, as if instinctively trying to escape.

But whether in reality or in his memory, he could not escape.

Fear finally turned into despair.

"My life is forfeit!"

With a mournful cry, Ho Gan Immortal's head shot up into the sky, detaching from the statue.

The same scene replayed, but this time, a large amount of blood gushed out from the stone statue's body!

Only a moment later, the flying head regained clarity in its eyes.

While searching for his own body, it cried out: "Quick, run!"

Li Fan's reaction was even faster.

When he sensed the bizarre force striking again, severing Ho Gan Immortal's head, and even tending to spread to the surroundings. Li Fan had already ignited the True Spirit Fire seeds he had pre-buried in various possibilities.

Instantly, fierce flames raged, burning mountains and boiling seas!

Forming a terrifying wall of light and heat, it blocked the probing tentacles of power from the depths of the mountains and seas.

What was originally intended to trap the True Immortal of Virtue had now become a lifeline for saving them both.

And it was precisely because of this method that even though they were in extreme danger, Li Fan did not enact True Reversion.

The True Spirit Fire incinerated the possibilities, shattering them. With the loss of support, the tide of Dao Annihilation was immediately drawn in.

The surging water and fire swallowed the mountains and seas.

In an instant, it was like the end of the world!

At this moment, Ho Gan Immortal, who had found his separated body and reattached his head, regained his normal state and stared at the scene before him, stunned.

He never imagined that Li Fan would be so reckless!

Burning the vast mountains and seas as he pleased!

"What are you still愣住 for? The fire is raging, if you don't run now, when will you?"

Li Fan shouted lowly, pulling Ho Gan Immortal back to reality.

At that moment, without any hesitation, he instinctively followed Li Fan into the flames.

After all, the great fire was ignited with Li Fan's spiritual essence as fuel. With Li Fan leading the way, Ho Gan Immortal was not scorched by the True Spirit flames. He only managed to evade the successive waves of the Dao Annihilation tide.

Speeding out of the water and fire blockade, far from numerous possibilities, as the flames gradually receded, the sense of impending crisis in their hearts slowly dissipated. Only then did the two of them slow down.

Ho Gan Immortal looked back at the already burnt-out ruins of the mountains and seas, swallowed by the Dao Annihilation, still feeling the shock.

After a long while, he cupped his hands towards Li Fan and sighed with admiration: "If not for your decisive action, Fellow Daoist, igniting the mountains and seas, we truly would have been doomed this time."

Li Fan's expression turned solemn: "Do not slander me. When did I ever set fire to the mountains and seas in such a shocking and heinous manner? It was clearly the work of the villain who sought to kill us!"

Ho Gan Immortal was stunned by this remark.

Then he let out a wry laugh.

"Did you gain anything from suffering such a great tribulation?" Li Fan asked.

Ho Gan Immortal nodded, then shook his head.

"I used the method of unified Virtue to see a scene from my other self's life. But it was only for the last short period."

"And the assailant never truly revealed their form from beginning to end. Therefore..."

"Their true identity remains unknown."

"But I remembered the place of their demise and their aura. If we meet again, I will be alerted in advance."

This result was within Li Fan's expectations: "Can you point the direction?"

Ho Gan Immortal marked a location in the mountains and seas.

"It should be around here."

"Hmm?"

Li Fan stared at the fleeting phantom of mountains and seas before him and felt a sense of familiarity.

"This place is..."

Ho Gan Immortal also noticed Li Fan's strangeness and quickly asked, "Could it be that Fellow Daoist knows this place?"

Li Fan remained silent for a long time before slowly uttering a few words.

"Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation, Realm of Birth and Destruction!"

"Realm of Birth and Destruction?" Ho Gan Immortal repeated in a low voice. With his knowledge, he had never heard of such an existence within the mountains and seas.

He couldn't help but believe Li Fan's earlier statement that the murderer might be someone he had been tracking for a long time.

In fact, even after a hundred cycles of reincarnation, Li Fan had only heard of the Realm of Birth and Destruction once.

It came from the memory of the Taiyi Sacred Scripture, stolen from the Primordial Realm!

A long time ago, when that dark figure named "Zhu Kong," who stole thirty True Immortal Runes from the Taiyi Sacred Scripture, was being pursued by the Dao Comprehension Immortal, he was from the Realm of Birth and Destruction.

Besides Zhu Kong, there were four others. Together, they resisted the attack of the Dao Comprehension Immortal.

The Dao Comprehension Immortal called them the "Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation."

In order to retrieve the stolen thirty True Immortal Runes, the Dao Comprehension Immortal pursued Zhu Kong but never returned.

The danger of the Realm of Birth and Destruction was evident.

Relying on the faint connection with the stolen True Immortal Runes from the Taiyi Sacred Scripture, Li Fan knew the general location of the Realm of Birth and Destruction.

Therefore, in his subsequent travels through the mountains and seas, he deliberately avoided it.

Now it seemed he had indeed evaded a calamity.

"After so many years, have these so-called Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation become this powerful?"

"That sense of crisis I felt just now..."

"Even if they are not Saints, they are not far from it."

"Of course, it is also possible that it is due to the combined efforts of the Five Sovereigns."

"I wonder how the Faceless Immortal managed to provoke such a formidable foe?" Li Fan's mind raced with countless thoughts.

At the same time, he felt relieved.

The mountains and seas were still the same mountains and seas he knew. There was no suddenly appearing, fatal enemy.

It was just that the target he needed to be wary of had increased exponentially.

"Next, Fellow Daoist, what are your intentions?"

After experiencing such a major upheaval, and still holding onto Li Fan's promise of helping him become a Saint, Ho Gan Immortal looked at the contemplative Li Fan and asked.

Li Fan glanced at Ho Gan Immortal and said gravely, "I intend to go to the Realm of Birth and Destruction to investigate."

"Are you willing to accompany me?"

Chapter 1643: The Calamity of the Five Saints Reversing the Spirit

"Fellow Daoist, is what you say true?" Ho Gan Immortal froze, his expression showing clear hesitation.

"Heh, of course..."

"Not true," Li Fan's tone suddenly shifted.

"Although I have pursued them for a long time, their strength has undergone a qualitative change compared to before. Now, it seems, the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation working together possess power close to that of a Saint, which I cannot currently match. We need to plan carefully..."

Li Fan's honest words surprised Ho Gan Immortal.

"Do you know what kind of beings these Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation are?" Li Fan asked.

Ho Gan Immortal shook his head.

"They are entirely different from the Saints of the Shore or the Saint Emperor Tai Wei. Their goal is not to save the Mountains and Seas, but like great daos that steal from a nation, they forcibly take rare items from various possibilities to fill themselves, aiming to create possibilities that rival the Mountains and Seas, or even transcend them and face Dao Annihilation," Li Fan gazed into the depths of the Mountains and Seas, his voice melancholic, as if he had personally visited the Realm of Birth and Destruction.

"How can this be allowed? If they steal a part, won't the Mountains and Seas lose a part of their foundation, and our chances of resisting Dao Annihilation decrease?" Ho Gan Immortal, being a cultivator of Virtue, was enraged upon hearing this.

"Furthermore, this action is almost equivalent to remaking the Mountains and Seas. Is it that easy? Not to mention that the five of them combined barely possess Saintly cultivation. Even if five true Saints worked together, they might not be able to achieve it. Otherwise, why would the Saints of the Shore endure hardships to traverse the Eternal Void?"

"Originally, I thought so too. I believed the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation were merely engaging in meaningless actions, a death throe. But now..."

Li Fan suddenly thought of Emperor Tian Luo's successful plan to lead the Primordial Immortal Realm to transcendence, and the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation personally visiting the Primordial Realm to steal True Immortal Seal Scripts from the Supreme Dao Scripture.

Judging by the expression of the Dao Comprehension Immortal at that time, the thirty stolen True Immortal Seal Scripts were certainly not simple.

"If my guess is correct, and the Primordial Immortal Realm truly transcended the Mountains and Seas, then it might not be impossible for the Realm of Birth and Destruction to repeat this story."

As this thought flashed through his mind, Li Fan continued, "Their strength has grown beyond my expectations. The Realm of Birth and Destruction is likely the same. This shows how much of the Mountains and Seas' foundation they have secretly stolen."

"Perhaps they are still lacking now. But if they continue like this..."

In Ho Gan Immortal's mind, an image appeared of a group of shadowy figures, silently roaming various parts of the Mountains and Seas, stealing resources.

An uncontrollable anger rose in his heart. If it weren't for the fact that he was truly no match for the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation, he would have almost dragged Li Fan to investigate the Realm of Birth and Destruction himself.

Seeing Ho Gan Immortal's subtle shift in expression, Li Fan nodded inwardly, gaining a deeper understanding of his temperament. Smiling, he said, "Although the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation are audacious, we have no need to worry excessively. After all, the Mountains and Seas are not ours alone, but the collective undertaking of all Immortals, Saints, and Saint Emperors."

"The Saints and Saint Emperors are fighting beyond the Eternal Void, in even more ancient timelines. How could they allow such parasites to exist in their rear?"

Ho Gan Immortal pondered, "Fellow Daoist, you mean..."

"We merely need to spread the news of the Realm of Birth and Destruction and then watch from the sidelines. Although the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation are strong, how can they be stronger than the foundation of the Shore?"

Ho Gan Immortal felt somewhat awkward, "Due to the unique nature of my cultivation path, I have always been wary of the Shore and have never gone there. I only vaguely know the names of the Saints of the Shore."

"It's alright, I have my methods. Just watch, Fellow Daoist."

As he spoke, a figure appeared before Li Fan, exactly identical to his true form. Except for its distorted face, making its specific appearance unclear, its aura was indistinguishable from Li Fan's.

But in Ho Gan Immortal's eyes, it seemed like another independent entity.

"This avatar technique of Fellow Daoist..." The more he observed and pondered, the more shocked Ho Gan Immortal became. This clone he created was almost identical to the 'other self' generated through his method of separating Dao and Virtue. However, his was solely reliant on the special nature of the Great Dao of Virtue, and even after separation, Dao and Virtue still had intertwined connections. For example, just now, he could use the same method to sense the memories of his other self before its demise.

And Ho Gan Immortal could sense that the clone created by Li Fan's divine ability of avatar cultivation... seemed to be a completely independent individual.

Almost instantly, Ho Gan Immortal understood what Li Fan was about to do. Just as he thought, the newly created Li Fan received his mission, and intense flames erupted around his body. After a moment of brewing, he transformed into a streak of light and vanished into the Mountains and Seas.

The True Spirit Great Fire, which had not yet subsided, was reignited. This time, the new Li Fan was even more unbridled, rapidly traversing through the Dao Annihilation and igniting every possibility it passed.

"Fellow Daoist, you this..." Ho Gan Immortal's eyelids twitched as he watched.

Li Fan merely smiled and waved his hand. If the previous True Spirit Great Fire that isolated the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation was limited to a corner of the Mountains and Seas, then the disaster Li Fan was now creating had the potential to spread across a vast area. Even if left to burn, the early demise of this segment of Mountains and Seas was not impossible.

Knowing that the Shore would inevitably respond, Li Fan calculated the time and decisively dispelled a wisp of his divine consciousness left on the avatar. This divine consciousness was not for communicating with the avatar, but as a catalyst for using the True Spirit Annihilation technique.

Li Fan's avatar divine ability, which comprehended the transformation of true and false, was profound, but it had not yet reached the point where it could create infinite spirituality. He could not even allocate his own infinite spirituality. Therefore, to ignite the Mountains and Seas, he still needed to act personally. Now that a significant commotion had been made, he burned the residual divine consciousness, destroying the only clue that could track his true form. The avatar, according to plan, then fled rapidly towards the location of the Realm of Birth and Destruction.

"Although this move can expose the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation, the price is also a bit too high!" Ho Gan Immortal said somewhat regretfully, looking at the Mountains and Seas, which were now a sea of flames as far as the eye could see.

"To treat a serious illness, one needs drastic medicine. If this can eliminate the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation in one fell swoop, this price is absolutely worth it. Don't worry, this possibility is insignificant compared to the final outcome."

"Look, if not for this, how could the Shore have gone to such great lengths?"

Ho Gan Immortal saw Li Fan point his finger, but for some reason, his eyes were closed. Thinking that the other party was afraid of exposure after setting the fire, he didn't probe further. Following the direction Li Fan pointed, he saw a brilliant white ring, seemingly infinitely vast and immeasurable, descending as if from beyond the heavens of the Mountains and Seas, enveloping countless possibilities within them.

Within the white ring, several figures seemed to stand and flicker. However, hidden within the light, Ho Gan Immortal could not see them clearly. He only felt that merely by glancing at it, a feeling of heart-stopping dread and impending doom arose. He also felt as if all his inner secrets were exposed, as if he had been stripped naked in broad daylight for others to behold.

Where the white ring passed, the raging True Spirit Great Fire instantly subsided. The surging tide of Dao Annihilation, as if encountering an indestructible dam, could not breach it despite the churning waves. As the calamity subsided, new Mountains and Seas appeared from within the white ring, as if a clock had been turned back, and countless possibilities that had been destroyed by the True Spirit Fire and the tide of Dao Annihilation reappeared, filling the "blank" spaces. A simple wooden boat then sailed around within these Newly created Mountains and Seas, as if time had been reversed, and countless beings that had disappeared reappeared, as if returning to the state before this segment of Mountains and Seas was affected by the True Spirit Great Fire.

The anomaly was not yet over. A plain brush then flew out from the wooden boat, as if drawing in the void, and began to paint. A figure appeared under the brush, resembling Li Fan, or rather, the avatar Li Fan who set fire to the Mountains and Seas. A thin black line extended from the figure in the brush, connecting to a certain location within the Mountains and Seas – the Realm of Birth and Destruction! The white ring suddenly shrunk, descending upon that location.

Then... there was no earth-shattering battle as one might imagine. After only a moment, the white ring vanished from the Mountains and Seas. Along with it, the Realm of Birth and Destruction also seemed to disappear. Ho Gan Immortal was filled with doubt, gazing for a long time but unable to make a correct judgment. He only saw the Mountains and Seas recover, appearing vibrant and full of life. As if the calamity of fire and water had never happened.

"Is this... the might of a Saint?" Ho Gan Immortal had never personally witnessed a Saint act before. Seeing it today was truly earth-shattering and dazzling. With a mere gesture, they could reverse the power of collapsing Mountains and Seas. Such divine abilities were truly unimaginable! Recalling Li Fan's nonchalant demeanor when he set the fire earlier, Ho Gan Immortal's heart stirred. "Could it be that he had already anticipated that the Saints of the Shore would intervene?"

"What happened in the outside world?" Just as Ho Gan Immortal was deep in thought, Li Fan suddenly asked. Ho Gan Immortal froze. Under Li Fan's repeated questioning, he finally recounted everything he had just witnessed. Hearing that the Saints were no longer present, Li Fan slowly opened his eyes. Indeed, Li Fan, who had truly experienced the terror of the Saints, had not merely closed his eyes but had cut off all observation of the outside world, focusing solely on his inner self. He was afraid that his observations would be noticed by the Saints, even if they were merely illusory projections. At the same time, his vigilance was at its peak, using his intuition as a guide, ready to revert True Reversion at any moment if he sensed danger. He didn't dare to witness the grand spectacle of the Saints restoring the collapsing Mountains and Seas and instantly suppressing the Realm of Birth and Destruction. Only when the situation had completely calmed down did he return to normal and quickly ask Ho Gan Immortal for details.

"The white ring, the Mountains and Seas, the wooden boat, the brush..." Li Fan listened carefully, his eyes revealing a strange look. Ho Gan Immortal had indeed overestimated him. He truly did not expect that the Saints of the Shore would possess the means to reshape Mountains and Seas and reverse time and space! "Although it was the combined effort of the Saints, this action is almost equivalent to True Reversion. Especially that wooden boat..." Li Fan narrowed his eyes. He did not associate it with the names of Saints he had glimpsed in the past in the Shore. He was only pondering the Great Daos represented by these phenomena. "Illusory Mountains and Seas symbolize Mountains and Seas." "That wooden boat seems capable of reversing the time and space of Mountains and Seas, but it is clearly not on the same level as the ordinary 'Reverse' Dao, far surpassing it." "And that brush..." "It is definitely more than just tracking down the culprit. Li Fan had a premonition that his avatar's fate would not be good. "No wonder they remained indifferent and treated my threat of burning the Mountains and Seas as a joke." "Are the Saints' powers truly this terrifying?" "Moreover, this is only the power of the Saints' illusory projections. The true bodies of the Saints are not within this segment of Mountains and Seas." "The Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation, who were considered formidable enemies, couldn't even make a ripple before being suppressed like this..." While marveling, Li Fan's resolve to stick to his previous plan strengthened. Before finding a way to counter the Saints, he would never willingly expose himself to them, as doing so would be akin to suicide! It wasn't just Li Fan's thoughts that were racing. Ho Gan Immortal, and even all the transcendent cultivators in the Mountains and Seas who were fortunate enough to witness the Saints' illusory projections in action, fell into enlightenment, eagerly savoring the profound mysteries of the Saints' phenomena. Saints were almost legendary beings. It was difficult enough to even see a Saint, let alone witness them personally acting. Such an opportunity was truly rare! All thanks to Li Fan! Unfortunately, it seemed that the Heaven-Deciding Plan could not yield any feedback on cultivation from this. Otherwise, it would be an unimaginable boost in power. "Virtue..." Ho Gan Immortal murmured. After seeing true Saints, he seemed to have gained a new understanding of the true meaning of Virtue. After a long while, he said to Li Fan, "Perhaps, without Fellow Daoist's help, I also have a chance to achieve Sainthood." "Of course, if I fail, I will still have to trouble Fellow Daoist." Ho Gan Immortal quickly added. "It seems you have gained quite a lot this time. It's easy to say," Li Fan readily agreed. "The Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation seem to have been suppressed by the Saints. Why don't we take this opportunity to explore the remnants of the Realm of Birth and Destruction?" Li Fan proposed. "There don't seem to be any remnants there anymore?" "Even residual power from the Saints is extremely valuable." Ho Gan Immortal found Li Fan's suggestion reasonable and agreed. The two traveled together. When they arrived at the original location of the Realm of Birth and Destruction, five figures were already standing there. They stood apart, silently observing the traces of the place. They saw the newly arrived Li Fan and Ho Gan Immortal as if they were invisible. "All transcendent experts." "I don't recognize any of them." Li Fan observed and said to himself internally. He noticed that more and more transcendent experts were arriving from various parts of the Mountains and Seas. Li Fan quickly examined the traces in the area. At this moment, Ho Gan Immortal quietly transmitted a message, pointing Li Fan in a certain direction. "My other self seems to have fallen here." Li Fan's heart stirred and he focused more of his attention on investigating. The Saints' illusory projections did not destroy the Realm of Birth and Destruction. Instead, they had relocated the possibility, like moving house. All the people, events, and objects within that possibility had vanished, leaving only a blank space to resist Dao Annihilation.

Chapter 1644: The Re-evolution of Ten Thousand Laws

The Void of Myriad Daos Re-emerges

Though said to be a void, it was not an emptiness devoid of all.

The possibility itself still existed.

If one were to draw an analogy, it was akin to the very beginning of the world, when chaos first opened.

"It is a pity that the Saints cleansed it thoroughly; not even a blurry image can be sensed now," Ho Gan Immortal observed for a long time, expressing his regret.

"I can only faintly sense that my other self seems to have died by the hands of such power..."

As he spoke, Ho Gan Immortal transmitted a wisp of his Dao resonance. This Dao was utterly novel, something Li Fan had never encountered in other possibilities of the Mountains and Seas. It was so rare that finding words to describe it was difficult.

"It vaguely represents the tribulation of consciousness sinking, trapped in the Great Silence. When consciousness ceases to exist, all other existences lose their meaning. Let alone morality; even the Mountains and Seas are the same. No wonder it could destroy the Faceless Immortal..."

Li Fan savored this wisp of residual Dao resonance left by the Five Sovereigns of the Same Tribulation, feeling surprised in his heart.

The ruins of the Realm of Birth and Destruction did not remain blank for long.

Suddenly, a rainbow light, originating from the depths of the Mountains and Seas, arrived.

In an instant, it rode the wind and waves, passing through the Dao Annihilation, and fiercely pierced into this blankness.

Observing its origin, it was from the Shore!

The Transcended experts present all turned their attention to the descending rainbow light.

It was revealed to be a small, seven-colored flag!

"The Saints have acted again!"

Amidst exclamations, the rainbow light of the flag exploded, revealing a blurry silhouette.

The figure surveyed the blankness with a condescending gaze.

Then, it merged into it.

The illusory projection of the Saint disappeared, and this blank possibility, like the surface of water about to boil, became calm yet brimming with power.

"The Saints' divine abilities are truly marvelous! This is a method to catalyze the re-emerguration of the Great Daos! In no time, new Great Daos should be born and nurtured here. Such a spectacle is rare in the Mountains and Seas; we are fortunate to witness it today and may greatly benefit." Ho Gan Immortal’s eyes gleamed, praising with a 'tsk tsk'.

As if to confirm Ho Gan Immortal's words, the originally blank possibility began to show subtle color variations. Like wisps of faint smoke, they rippled and rose.

It was as if a pebble had dropped into a calm lake, causing ripples.

In an instant, one became a hundred, and a hundred became ten thousand variations!

The speed at which the Great Daos were reborn here was even faster than the two had anticipated!

From the moment the activity began, only a few breaths passed before the Great Daos here became as unfathomable as the starry sky.

Phantoms of mountains and seas emerged from the depths.

The mountains were the Upper Mountains, and the seas were the Infinite Seas.

Mountains and seas connected, and the Immortal Realm was born!

A stream of light burst forth from the darkness.

Then, it continuously leaped within the darkness, as if shaping islands in the darkness with every place it passed.

Vibrant star seas were born one after another.

The points of light leaped and self-replicated, and in a flash, they transformed into a sky full of twinkling stars.

The vast and boundless Immortal Realm thus took shape before everyone's observant eyes.

"This is..."

Li Fan stared intently at the light points that gradually dissipated after completing their mission, a realization dawning upon him: "The Profound Origin Primordial Spirit Array?"

These brilliant light points, which had reshaped the Mountains and Seas, contained the aura of the Profound Origin Primordial Spirit Array.

However, the complete version of the Profound Origin Primordial Spirit Array seemed to have transcended the level of an 'array' and reached the realm of 'Dao.'

And the scene of re-creating the Immortal Realm was simply too swift.

Although Li Fan had sensed something, he couldn't see it too clearly.

He couldn't help but feel regret.

As for the Transcended experts who arrived late, having missed the grand spectacle of the world's reopening, they all wrung their hands and sighed incessantly.

"The Saints acted, clearing away everything, and re-establishing the fundamental elements of existence. Such a grand scene, missed today, who knows when we will encounter it again!" lamented an old man holding a wooden staff.

"It all happened too suddenly; the tribulation and the Saints' arrival came and went quickly. And those who could react immediately and observe the 'Manifestation of Dao' in the blank Dao were either experienced elders or those with extraordinary spiritual senses. It was a rare few," said a middle-aged woman in a fitted long dress beside the old man, speaking calmly, though regret lingered in her eyes.

The old man and the middle-aged woman looked at Li Fan and the earlier arrivals with envy.

As their gazes met Li Fan's, even without recognition, they nodded slightly in greeting.

Li Fan's heart stirred, and he transmitted a message to Ho Gan Immortal: "Did you gain anything?"

If it were an ordinary opportunity, the surrounding Transcended experts would not have shown such expressions. Yet, Li Fan had no particular enlightenment, so he asked Ho Gan Immortal.

Ho Gan Immortal’s eyes were closed, seemingly still immersed in his enlightenment.

However, he did not forget to reply to Li Fan: "The phenomenon of the rebirth of Myriad Daos is like a mirror, capable of reflecting one's own cultivated path. This manifestation is the initial state of the Great Dao, its purest form. For cultivators like us, it has extremely important validation effects..."

"Furthermore, the new Dao corresponding to oneself in this reborn possibility, before it is fully formed, can be directly captured to strengthen oneself. Under normal circumstances, to absorb a Dao path, one needs one's other self in that possibility to have cultivated to at least the Nameless Realm. This is a rare and unrepeatable opportunity! Therefore, even for Transcended experts, this re-emergence of Myriad Daos is an extremely rare opportunity."

"How was your enlightenment?" Ho Gan Immortal did not forget to inquire.

Li Fan smiled: "My Great Dao does not lie here; therefore, I gained nothing."

Ho Gan Immortal’s body trembled upon hearing this. His eyelids flickered, almost unable to resist opening his eyes.

The blank possibility, with the rebirth of Myriad Daos. If, in that blank mirror, one did not see the Dao path they cultivated...

It meant either their talent was too poor, their eyes were blind, and they could not perceive the truth.

Or, the Dao path they cultivated was too high in level, having already surpassed the scope that ordinary possibilities of the Mountains and Seas could touch!

Seeing Li Fan’s nonchalant demeanor, it was unlikely he was speaking falsely.

Thus, Ho Gan Immortal further believed Li Fan's identity as coming from another segment of the Mountains and Seas.

In fact, on this matter, Li Fan had not lied to Ho Gan Immortal.

He truly did not see any trace of the evolution of the 'Transformation of True and False' in this possibility's rebirth of Myriad Daos.

Or rather, the Transformation of True and False did not exist within the mundane Mountains and Seas.

If it wasn't visible on the macro level of the Mountains and Seas, it was even less likely to be perceived on the micro level of possibilities.

"The Transformation of True and False only exists in the instant when True Reversion is activated and the Mountains and Seas are reset. At ordinary times, it is extremely difficult to detect. Otherwise, my comprehension and cultivation of it would not be so slow."

However, it wasn't as if Li Fan gained nothing from observing this spectacle.

If Myriad Daos’ rebirth served as a mirror, where ordinary Transcended cultivators could encounter their own paths of cultivation, then the Transformation of True and False was another mirror.

What it reflected was the Great Daos themselves!

But the evolution of Great Daos from nothingness to existence was too rapid. With Li Fan's current talent, it was difficult to comprehend all these myriad Daos within this short period.

"Perhaps if my aunt's spiritual essence were to be superimposed thousands of times, it might be possible," Li Fan did not force it.

After the world's reopening and the re-emerguration of Great Daos, it would take a considerable amount of time for new life to be nurtured, unless external forces were to introduce life.

The Transcended experts present did not have the patience for this.

They all dispersed one after another.

Even though Li Fan had nothing to do, he still waited for Ho Gan Immortal to finish his enlightenment.

Ho Gan Immortal’s enlightenment took longer than that of the other Transcended experts.

Only when they were the last two remaining in this place did Ho Gan Immortal slowly open his eyes.

"I have recaptured a wisp of Virtue’s resonance here. As long as I refine it carefully, I might be able to undertake the separation of Dao and Virtue again," Seeing that no one else was around, Ho Gan Immortal said to Li Fan with great joy.

"Oh?"

"After my other self died, my method of practicing Dao and Virtue separation, though it failed, originally required me to spend hundreds of thousands of years to re-nurture the balance of Dao and Virtue, and then wait for an opportune moment to separate. However, today, with the Saints’ intervention, I was fortunate to capture a wisp of nascent Virtue."

"This pure Great Dao, ignorant and unconscious, and without a master. Once refined, it can directly transform into my own strength."

Li Fan understood Ho Gan Immortal's words.

The re-emerged nascent Great Daos had not yet intertwined and integrated into the workings of heaven and earth; they remained distinct.

Although this state only lasted for a fleeting moment at the beginning of creation, if captured, it would be equivalent to tens of thousands of years of diligent cultivation and purification for a cultivator.

It might even be superior.

Ho Gan Immortal's ability to seize this fleeting opportunity demonstrated his extraordinary talent.

"How long will your refinement take?"

"A hundred years."

"Good, may I have the honor of witnessing the secret technique of Dao and Virtue separation?" Li Fan asked with a smile.

Ho Gan Immortal acted magnanimously: "The Great Dao of Virtue can be revealed to people. If Fellow Daoist wishes to observe it, I will certainly prepare a seat for you!"

"Then I shall gratefully accept!" Li Fan laughed heartily.

He discovered that since the fall of the Faceless Immortal and the failure of the Dao and Virtue separation, Ho Gan Immortal had been gradually losing the characteristics that originally belonged to him, and was slowly regressing towards the original 'True Immortal of Virtue.'

"The Great Dao of Virtue indeed possesses some profundity. I wish to see what it is truly about," Li Fan mused inwardly.

"However, the separation of Dao and Virtue requires the interaction of Heaven and Man, and a suitable location is needed."

Ho Gan Immortal glanced around the surrounding Mountains and Seas, shaking his head slightly: "There is no suitable place nearby."

"What conditions are needed?"

"A critical moment when facing imminent tribulation, necessitating a decisive choice," Ho Gan Immortal said, looking at Li Fan.

"This is an easy matter!" Li Fan immediately understood why Ho Gan Immortal had said this to him.

"However, having just burned the mountains and boiled the seas not long ago, it's not easy to cause a particularly large disturbance again. But to simply aid you in pushing yourself to a desperate situation... it wouldn't require the Mountains and Seas..." Li Fan said, and a wisp of flame appeared in his hand.

The flames, like dragons, surged forth.

In a mere breath, they surrounded Ho Gan Immortal.

Ho Gan Immortal stared intently at the True Spirit flames surrounding him, inwardly gasping in astonishment.

If the previous conflagration that engulfed the Mountains and Seas relied on the countless possibilities within the Mountains and Seas as fuel, then the flames before him were purely supported by Li Fan's spiritual essence as fuel.

Most crucially...

Ho Gan Immortal vaguely sensed that this cluster of flames seemed capable of burning indefinitely!

After absorbing that wisp of nascent Virtue, Ho Gan Immortal's own intuition had grown stronger.

He had great confidence in his premonitions.

"It is absolutely necessary to traverse the Eternal Void to possess such an abundance of incredible spiritual essence."

"And it is precisely because this spiritual essence does not belong to him that he cannot transform it into his own cultivation talent..." Ho Gan Immortal understood.

Li Fan had not mentioned the true extent of his natural talent in front of Ho Gan Immortal.

He had not even engaged in secluded cultivation.

Yet, Ho Gan Immortal could discern some clues from their interactions.

For example, the scene of the world's reopening and the re-emerguration of Myriad Daos earlier.

Although Li Fan claimed his cultivated Dao was not present, if one's cultivation talent truly reached a certain level, even without cultivating Myriad Daos, mere observation would lead to enlightenment.

And Li Fan had 'awakened' too quickly.

Although he saw this, Ho Gan Immortal did not belittle him.

On the contrary, he treated him with even greater seriousness.

Cultivation talent and realm were never the same thing.

In other words, to reach the same Transcended realm with lower talent only further proved his exceptional nature.

Moreover, Li Fan had implicitly crossed the Eternal Void from another segment of the Mountains and Seas!

"I suddenly understand, it is not only those who have reached the Saint realm who can traverse the Eternal Void."

"But in our perception, only by reaching the Saint realm and possessing the strength of a 'Saint' can one survive and travel in the Eternal Void, where even concepts of existence cease to be."

"So, we developed that illusion."

"And if there were some special, unknown method that allowed Transcended beings below the Saint realm to traverse the Eternal Void?"

After Ho Gan Immortal slowly regressed to become True Immortal of Virtue, his thoughts became less extreme.

He considered all aspects more thoroughly.

"Furthermore, this person’s statement that he could help me achieve Sainthood was made with such conviction; it should not be false..."

"Regardless of the reason, this person is worthy of deep friendship."

Encased by the True Spirit flames, countless thoughts flashed through the True Immortal of Virtue's mind.

He remained unfazed, feeling the power of the True Spirit flames.

He shook his head slightly: "Although these flames are powerful, they cannot force me into a desperate situation. Even if I were surrounded, I could still break a path out by sacrificing spiritual essence."

"Then what about adding the Dao Annihilation?"

"Still not enough. Unless it is the power of the world’s destruction." The True Immortal of Virtue continued to shake his head.

This time, it was Li Fan’s turn to frown deeply.

"Now, my strength is not what it used to be. To separate Dao and Virtue again..."

"Requires the desperation of traversing the Eternal Void!"

Upon hearing the words "Eternal Void," Li Fan’s eyes narrowed instantly, and he scrutinized the True Immortal of Virtue within the flames.

The True Immortal of Virtue's expression was calm as he met Li Fan's gaze.

"Fellow Daoist, do you know the technique of 'Reverse'?" Li Fan suddenly asked after a long silence.

"I know a little bit. I learned it to aid my travels in the Mountains and Seas," the True Immortal of Virtue replied lightly.

"Then, at the end of the Mountains and Seas, at the beginning of time, we shall meet before the Eternal Void!"

With that, Li Fan leaped, falling back into the Mountains and Seas.

However, this time, it was not a crossing through the Dao Annihilation.

Instead, he moved against the direction of the river of time, heading towards the earliest moments of this surviving segment of the Mountains and Seas at extreme speed.

Compared to the initial panic of falling into the river of time, Li Fan was now quite adept.

But the True Immortal of Virtue was no weaker than him!

Following closely behind!

Chapter 1645: Enlightenment Before the Void Realm

"Does this fit the description of 'true virtue'?" Ho Gan Immortal's face showed a stark contrast, with his left side furrowed in worry and his right side splitting open with a smile of enlightenment.

But in the next instant, the expressions on the left and right halves swapped.

Then, in the next moment, the expressions on both sides swapped again.

This cycle continued, with the speed of expression changes increasing until, finally, the expressions on both sides seemed to blend together, settling on a single calm face.

The change in facial expression was merely the first step in splitting Virtue.

It seemed that a wisp of True Virtue was being constantly rotated amidst the changes, gradually differentiating into two streams of energy: black and white.

However, looking from afar, these black and white energies did not seem pure.

They were still intertwined, with you in me and me in you, inseparable.

The black and white energies coiled around each other, constantly rotating, forming a Taiji diagram.

And from all parts of the Mountains and Seas, it seemed as if traces of the Great Dao of Virtue were being drawn towards it, ignoring the blockade of the True Spirit Flames, and merging into the Taiji diagram!

"This is..."

Li Fan, hidden within the True Spirit Flames, maintained his output of spirituality and the transformation of true and false, carefully observing the Taiji diagram on Ho Gan Immortal.

The great terror that Ho Gan Immortal felt was naturally the transformation of true and false.

Or, to be precise, the transformation of "truth into falsehood."

After more than thirty cycles of enlightenment, compared to the initial blade that diminished spirituality, the "truth into falsehood" divine ability now was dozens of times more powerful.

It was no longer a simple matter of reducing spirituality.

Even a transcendent expert like True Immortal of Virtue, Li Fan was confident that he could slowly erase his existence and turn him into nothingness!

However... it would take some time.

Ho Gan Immortal's premonition was not wrong.

The True Spirit Flames, combined with the "truth into falsehood" technique, would indeed, like the Eternal Void, erase his existence.

But Li Fan could not be compared to the Eternal Void.

If the Eternal Void was a vast swamp that could instantly swallow True Immortal of Virtue.

Then Li Fan was merely a black paste, capable of slowly consuming only the localized areas it touched.

Although the effects they could achieve were somewhat similar.

The efficiency of swallowing was vastly different.

The reason Ho Gan Immortal had the illusion of being truly in a desperate situation was due to the grand posture created by the True Spirit Flames and his complete ignorance of the "truth into falsehood" technique.

If he had truly disregarded everything and charged into the True Spirit Flames, he could have certainly escaped, only suffering some injuries.

But Ho Gan Immortal had come precisely to seek enlightenment in a desperate situation, and thus did not act rashly.

"Virtue flows, approaching change."

"It has formed an atmosphere that seems like transcendence. Hence, it could attract similar Daos of Virtue from the Mountains and Seas, coming from afar, to gather here."

Li Fan, hidden within the True Spirit Flames, quietly observed the Taiji diagram, deep in thought.

It was similar to Emperor Tian Luo's plan to transcend the Immortal Realm, which attracted many followers to aid him.

The mysterious Taiji diagram currently manifested by True Immortal of Virtue also constructed a scenario of transcending the Mountains and Seas.

However, it was merely a scenario.

"If True Immortal of Virtue's understanding of Virtue truly reached the limit of the Mountains and Seas, perhaps he could indeed turn the scenario into reality!"

"Virtue flows on its own, Taiji gives birth to all things. This is a Dao path comparable to the Great Dao of Longevity, able to rival the Mountains and Seas..."

"However, True Immortal of Virtue is merely at the transcendent realm, far from completely comprehending its true meaning. He hasn't even fully grasped Virtue, let alone Taiji."

As if confirming Li Fan's speculation.

The Daos of Virtue that came from afar across the Mountains and Seas, upon discovering that the Taiji diagram before them was merely an illusory scene woven from thin air, mostly lost interest.

Soon, they disappeared again.

However, a tiny fraction seemed to have seen the potential of True Immortal of Virtue and chose to remain.

With the replenished Daos of Virtue from nowhere, True Immortal of Virtue's aura became more solid.

The strength lost from approaching the edge of the Eternal Void had also been largely recovered.

Most importantly...

This choice of staying and leaving, two different paths.

Generated the initial impetus for the splitting of Virtue!

"Can you still keep up?" Li Fan asked, looking back, without revealing any flaws, his expression calm and composed.

True Immortal of Virtue's expression was grave: "Even though I knew the danger of the Eternal Void beforehand, only by arriving personally can one truly understand its meaning. If one accidentally falls into it, indeed, even the concept of Virtue will vanish instantly."

"However... I can still try one last time."

"Isn't this precisely the 'desperate situation' you need?" Li Fan smiled and continued forward without changing his posture.

On the surface, he remained calm, but internally, he was already drenched in sweat.

Every cell in his body was frantically warning him, desperately resisting the approaching Eternal Void.

And Li Fan's own spiritual sense was constantly warning him that the crisis ahead was extreme.

The only thing that comforted Li Fan was that True Reversion seemed to have no reaction to his attempt to approach the Eternal Void.

"It's just observing from afar, not truly entering, so it should be fine."

Thinking this, Li Fan overcame his instincts and continued to step forward.

Absolute void darkness began to rise in his vision, presenting an utterly oppressive power. The closer he got, the more suffocating it became.

Li Fan even felt that his Dao path and cultivation had become somewhat unstable.

As if sensing its impending doom, "Dao" itself instinctively sought to dissipate.

Like ink drops in water, scattering into countless threads!

To survive and circulate was also an inherent instinct of Dao, hence Li Fan could hardly prevent its self-dissipation at this moment.

"And this dissipation process is irreversible. Once lost, it is lost forever. Even if he returned to the normal time point of the Mountains and Seas, the dissipated cultivation would not return, and he would have to re-cultivate it himself."

However, relying on the advantage of True Reversion, Li Fan was unconcerned about the dissipation of his cultivation. After all, even if he were reduced to a mortal, as long as he returned to the saved anchor point, he could recover to his original state.

But as his cultivation decreased, his situation at the beginning of time became increasingly dangerous. Li Fan became more cautious, ready to activate True Reversion at any moment.

On the contrary, True Immortal of Virtue was far less indifferent than Li Fan.

His cultivation was the result of painstaking effort accumulated over years. Every step forward, hundreds, even thousands of years of arduous cultivation, would be wasted.

He had not yet become a Saint, so how could he not feel heartache?

Coupled with the increasingly intense sense of inner crisis, True Immortal of Virtue's progress became even slower.

At times, he almost came to a standstill, moving only one step after a long while.

Looking at Li Fan's receding back, whose speed did not decrease and whose posture was elegant and free, True Immortal of Virtue's respect for Li Fan grew spontaneously.

"It seems my previous guess was indeed correct! Perhaps only those who have traversed the Eternal Void can stroll leisurely at the beginning of time like this!"

The further they went, the faster their cultivation and Dao dissipated, and the lower their strength became.

The weaker they became, the less courage they had to continue forward.

Under this vicious cycle, True Immortal of Virtue ultimately could not truly reach the limit of this segment of Mountains and Seas.

However, he had managed to get within one step of it.

"Another half a year forward, and it will be the initial time point of this segment of Mountains and Seas."

"Approximately..."

"Sixty-eight thousand four hundred and thirty-seven years before anchoring."

The void of the Eternal Void stretched across the horizon, almost within reach.

Darkness covered their heads, almost enveloping their entire bodies.

It felt as if if they reached out their hands, they would sink into that deep darkness.

Every thought Li Fan pondered required a thousand times more effort to suppress the innate fear welling up from the depths of his soul.

This had nothing to do with his state of mind, but was the innate fear of a living being towards the tribulation of "concept disappearance."

Thoughts were like this, and actions were even more so.

True Immortal of Virtue was covered in sweat, his expression contorted.

He wanted to move his feet.

After several attempts, he still could not do it.

Finally, he let out a long sigh and gave up.

"This is my limit."

True Immortal of Virtue closed his eyes and said with great difficulty: "I have a premonition that if I insist on going further, I will not need to fall into the Eternal Void; my own existence will disintegrate first."

"From my perspective, this is a desperate situation."

Li Fan stood before True Immortal of Virtue, his hands behind his back, leaving behind an unforgettable back view for the other party.

He said slowly: "A pity. Every step further here reveals scenery that overturns the heavens and earth. What I see now, you cannot perceive."

Having said that, Li Fan shook his head and retreated from his forward position.

Even though his heart had not yet escaped the state of extreme fear, and he occasionally felt a sharp tearing pain, it did not affect Li Fan's calm demeanor, appearing as if he were still unsatisfied.

"Actually, what lies further ahead is a hundred times more wondrous than here. It's a pity..." Li Fan sighed lightly, stopping short of finishing his sentence.

He did not explicitly state where "ahead" was, but to True Immortal of Virtue, it clearly referred to the Eternal Void!

"Is it because of traversing [the Eternal Void] that his cultivation has been damaged, and he is no longer at the Saint realm?"

True Immortal of Virtue thought to himself.

The loss of cultivation during the crossing was already severe, let alone within the Eternal Void itself?

The fact that his traversal caused him to fall from his realm was logical.

All his previous guesses about Li Fan now formed a closed loop. True Immortal of Virtue solemnly said: "I hope Fellow Daoist can lend me a helping hand!"

"Good!"

A glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes.

The True Spirit Flames reappeared.

The flames blazed fiercely, forming an arc that sealed off True Immortal of Virtue.

At this moment, from True Immortal of Virtue's perspective, moving forward meant facing the terrifying Eternal Void.

Moving backward meant facing the blazing True Spirit Flames.

Although the True Spirit Flames were also extremely dangerous, they were still less threatening than the Eternal Void.

Therefore, in a life-or-death situation, if he had to choose, he would definitely choose to break through the blockade of the True Spirit Flames.

Just as True Immortal of Virtue had said earlier, even with the True Spirit Flames plus Dao Annihilation, it was far from a desperate situation!

But Li Fan was not done yet.

Li Fan looked at True Immortal of Virtue, who was meditating within the flames, and his expression suddenly turned cold.

It was a look that was incompatible with all beings in the Mountains and Seas, a condescending gaze that looked down upon all living beings.

True Immortal of Virtue met Li Fan's gaze and couldn't help but tremble.

He felt as if he were facing a Saint again!

"Perhaps, it's not an illusion?"

Thinking this, True Immortal of Virtue suddenly felt a great terror descending from the True Spirit Flames!

The threat of the True Spirit Flames increased tenfold instantly.

Moreover, it felt strangely similar to the Eternal Void!

"Falling into it means utter annihilation of body and soul..."

One moment, there was still a way out.

The next second, there was no escape!

True Immortal of Virtue's hair stood on end, cold sweat drenching his forehead.

"Are you satisfied with this desperate situation?"

Li Fan's voice, extremely cold, cut through the flickering flames and reached True Immortal of Virtue's ears.

"Please quickly split your Dao and Virtue."

"Do not attempt to escape, otherwise..."

"There might no longer be a True Immortal of Virtue in this world."

The flames suddenly surged, completely obscuring True Immortal of Virtue's vision.

He naturally understood that Li Fan's words were not a joke.

If he tried to force his way out, the other party would likely show no mercy!

Desperation was something he had sought for countless years by traversing time and space, tirelessly pursuing the divine ability of splitting Dao and Virtue.

But now that he had truly fallen into a desperate situation, True Immortal of Virtue felt a sense of regret.

However, now was not the time for regret.

Seeing that True Immortal of Virtue remained inactive,

The True Spirit Flames began to slowly advance!

True Immortal of Virtue's heart pounded, and he shouted: "Fellow Daoist, wait!"

However, Li Fan seemed not to hear him, continuing to push the True Spirit Flames forward relentlessly.

At this moment, True Immortal of Virtue was truly trapped in a desperate situation.

Moving forward meant facing the pressure of the Eternal Void, which would disintegrate him.

Moving backward...

The True Spirit Flames, and the terrifying power within the flames, would also cause his body and soul to vanish.

True Immortal of Virtue could only force himself to calm down first.

"At this moment, it is exactly like when the Immortal Realm was destroyed and Dao Annihilation descended."

"Finding oneself in a desperate situation, a divine technique was born out of necessity."

"They say that when one is穷 (qióng - poor/desperate), one must change; when one changes, one attains通 (tōng - understanding/success)!"

True Immortal of Virtue's face now showed two completely different expressions.

The left half was furrowed, as if worried.

The right half seemed to have attained enlightenment, a look of joy.

But in the next moment, the expressions on the left and right halves swapped.

Then, in the next moment, the expressions on both sides swapped again.

This cycle continued, with the speed of expression changes increasing until, finally, the expressions on both sides seemed to blend together, settling on a single calm face.

The change in facial expression was merely the first step in splitting Virtue.

It seemed that a wisp of True Virtue was being constantly rotated amidst the changes, gradually differentiating into two streams of energy: black and white.

However, looking from afar, these black and white energies did not seem pure.

They were still intertwined, with you in me and me in you, inseparable.

The black and white energies coiled around each other, constantly rotating, forming a Taiji diagram.

And from all parts of the Mountains and Seas, it seemed as if traces of the Great Dao of Virtue were being drawn towards it, ignoring the blockade of the True Spirit Flames, and merging into the Taiji diagram!

"This is..."

Li Fan, hidden within the True Spirit Flames, maintained his output of spirituality and the transformation of true and false, carefully observing the Taiji diagram on Ho Gan Immortal.

The great terror that Ho Gan Immortal felt was naturally the transformation of true and false.

Or, to be precise, the transformation of "truth into falsehood."

After more than thirty cycles of enlightenment, compared to the initial blade that diminished spirituality, the "truth into falsehood" divine ability now was dozens of times more powerful.

It was no longer a simple matter of reducing spirituality.

Even a transcendent expert like True Immortal of Virtue, Li Fan was confident that he could slowly erase his existence and turn him into nothingness!

However... it would take some time.

Ho Gan Immortal's premonition was not wrong.

The True Spirit Flames, combined with the "truth into falsehood" technique, would indeed, like the Eternal Void, erase his existence.
