But Li Fan could not be compared to the Eternal Void.

If the Eternal Void was a vast swamp that could instantly swallow True Immortal of Virtue.

Then Li Fan was merely a black paste, capable of slowly consuming only the localized areas it touched.

Although the effects they could achieve were somewhat similar.

The efficiency of swallowing was vastly different.

The reason Ho Gan Immortal had the illusion of being truly in a desperate situation was due to the grand posture created by the True Spirit Flames and his complete ignorance of the "truth into falsehood" technique.

If he had truly disregarded everything and charged into the True Spirit Flames, he could have certainly escaped, only suffering some injuries.

But Ho Gan Immortal had come precisely to seek enlightenment in a desperate situation, and thus did not act rashly.

Chapter 1646: Illusory Realm Hinders Return to Truth

Between the two illusory figures, a vortex seemed to spin.

A blurred Taiji diagram, with the two separated forms of the True Immortal of Virtue as yin and yang fish eyes, appeared to be moving and still, stopping and rotating, separating and merging!

"The separation of Virtue and the Dao..."

Li Fan stared intently at the wondrous phenomenon unfolding before him, where the form was splitting into two.

As the black and white Taiji rotated to a certain speed, it instantly vanished from Li Fan's sight.

Concurrently, the True Immortal of Virtue also disappeared from the world.

In their place stood two transcended beings, one representing the Dao and the other representing Virtue!

At this moment, they had not yet awakened, still seated with their eyes closed.

However, after the separation, the conditions of the two True Immortals were vastly different!

Temporarily, the previous appellations would still be used.

He Gan Immortal's aura was stable, with no significant fluctuations in strength. In fact, his strength seemed to have subtly improved.

Conversely, Wu Mian Immortal's realm appeared to have plummeted. His face also slowly became transparent.

Yet, to Li Fan's senses...

Wu Mian Immortal still posed a greater threat!

"The separation of Virtue and the Dao ultimately seeks to completely discard one aspect, leaving only the other in its pure form."

"The Dao and Virtue are inherently difficult to separate. This process of continuous division..."

"Also represents a form of convergence!"

Before Li Fan's eyes, the vanished Taiji diagram seemed to reappear.

And as it spun rapidly, the black and white colors were separating from their amalgamation. However, outside the original Taiji, a larger, new Taiji diagram was being nurtured.

Or rather, that magnificent Taiji diagram had transcended the concept of "Taiji" and resembled a brand new world. It was precisely as Li Fan and He Gan Immortal had glimpsed before – the unfolding scenery of the Rebirth of Myriad Daos!

"Once the separation and recombination are complete, it will be the shedding of the old and the embracing of the new, with Taiji giving birth to all phenomena. The separation of Virtue and the Dao is essentially breaking free from the inherent constraints of one's own Dao nature! No wonder one can become a Saint just by standing still!"

Li Fan dimly understood the mechanism behind Virtue's attainment of Sainthood in his previous life.

In simple terms, it was through the divine art of splitting Virtue and the Dao that one broke free from the inherent nature of the 'Virtue and Dao' Great Dao.

Because it is nothing, it contains everything and encompasses everything.

It was as if, in a rigid feudal dynasty with a strict bureaucratic hierarchy, no matter how diligent and meritorious one was, in terms of promotion and reward, the Prime Minister, First Assistant, Grand Tutor, or the King with Shoulder-to-Shoulder Reigns were already at the pinnacle of human subjects.

To advance further...

One could either conspire against the sovereign and usurp the throne, or traverse all the imperial roads, destroying all officials and rebuilding anew.

Or, one could establish a kingdom in a foreign land and lay the foundation for a new system.

If normal methods of achieving Sainthood were like options one and two, then the method of Virtue's attainment of Sainthood adopted the third approach.

Finding a different path!

"It's a small nation with a sparse population. No wonder the 'Virtue' I saw in my previous life was far less powerful than the Saints of the Shore."

"I had previously thought that even among Saints, there was such a significant difference in strength."

Observing the secret of Virtue's attainment of Sainthood up close, Li Fan finally understood why he could escape from the presence of a Saint in his previous life.

"However, in ancient times, strength and weakness had no fixed rules. Although weak during the process of attaining the Dao, it does not mean one remains weak forever. As long as one becomes a Saint first, there will always be opportunities to become stronger later." Having witnessed countless examples of small nations rising from insignificance, Li Fan was confident in the potential of this method of achieving Sainthood through Virtue.

"It's a shame, though, that it seems applicable only to the path of 'Virtue and Dao' and does not possess universal applicability. Or perhaps, my comprehension is insufficient..."

While Li Fan was contemplating, the new He Gan Immortal and Wu Mian Immortal finally awoke from their enlightenment.

They both looked towards Li Fan simultaneously. Although they cupped their hands in greeting, one's eyes showed gratitude, while the other's glinted with vigilance.

Li Fan laughed heartily and waved his hand, dispelling the True Spirit Flames and the "Truth into Falsehood" divine ability that was maintaining the circumstances. "The separation of Virtue and the Dao is indeed profoundly mysterious."

"Far inferior to Fellow Daoist's divine ability!" Wu Mian Immortal chuckled sinisterly.

"This 'me' is not the 'me' from before. The memories and emotions before the separation into two are identical. As for afterward... we can now be considered two different people," He Gan Immortal explained from the side.

"With the initial separation of Virtue and the Dao, we need to reaccumulate our foundations. Perhaps, we will have the opportunity to attain the Dao on our own."

"But if not, we may still need Fellow Daoist's help."

He Gan and Wu Mian, at this moment, still seemed to be of one mind, speaking sequentially.

Li Fan readily agreed: "Easy to say. I also sincerely hope that another Saint will emerge from this segment of Mountains and Seas."

"If you need anything in the future, use this item to contact me."

With that, Li Fan flicked two beams of light, heading straight for the two Immortals.

After receiving them, the two found they each held a black and a white, two different chess pieces.

The aura of this token bore a slight resemblance to their own Great Dao of Virtue.

Even Wu Mian Immortal accepted it solemnly.

After all, it represented the hope of attaining Sainthood!

As for who would be the final winner, Dao or Virtue, that would depend on their individual capabilities!

"You may go now! I still have scenery to behold ahead."

Without waiting for the two Immortals to respond, Li Fan's figure elegantly moved forward, continuing towards the Eternal Void, vanishing from the realm of time.

Although inwardly they wished to follow and see what this "scenery" entailed,

The instinctive fear of the Eternal Void made it difficult for the two Immortals to keep up.

They could only sigh and give up.

He Gan Immortal and Wu Mian Immortal exchanged glances, then each let out a soft snort and parted ways.

This was precisely...

Different paths, different plans!

And what they did not know was that Li Fan had not taken many steps forward before he could no longer sustain himself.

Without any regard for his previous promise to the two Virtuous Immortals, Li Fan simply focused his gaze on the utterly void and dark area ahead.

Then, he silently uttered,

True Reversion!

His aunt had already perished in this lifetime; the reason he had lingered was to observe the secret of Virtue's attainment of Sainthood. Now that his objective had been achieved, why should he continue to stay?

Could it be that he was going to wait for hundreds of thousands of years as a kind person, assisting Virtue in attaining Sainthood?

Li Fan was not that kind.

Therefore, when activating True Reversion, he did not hesitate in the slightest.

And the reason he ventured forward into the Eternal Void at great risk...

Was because Li Fan wanted to see clearly whether activating True Reversion would affect the segment of Mountains and Seas outside the current one!

"If it can, then even the Eternal Void will undergo corresponding changes."

"If not..."

The familiar hazy mist enveloped everything around them.

Li Fan's vision struggled to penetrate the white fog, looking outward.

The initial end of time, like a very obvious dividing line.

The pitch-black Eternal Void was not stained with white.

Even though this side had already become like the moon in the mirror, the flower in the water, the Eternal Void remained eternally silent and unchanging.

"Could it be, as I suspected, that True Reversion only covers the current segment of Mountains and Seas?"

"The Saints in the Eternal Void and other Mountains and Seas are not within the scope of True Reversion?"

Observing the clear demarcation before him, Li Fan's heart suddenly leaped.

Then, he recalled the various encounters with Shou Qiu in his past reincarnations.

"Doesn't that mean that as long as I meet Shou Qiu, my possession of True Reversion will be exposed?"

The hazy mist was about to completely obscure all scenery before Li Fan.

Just as he was about to fall into complete darkness, Li Fan suddenly looked up again.

Within the Eternal Void, something seemed to be targeting him.

Or more accurately, it was targeting True Reversion.

It was as if something was about to emerge from the bottom of the water.

The darkness seemed to be fading.

Even while undergoing the process of True Reversion, this moment felt exceptionally long.

Cold sweat dripped uncontrollably from Li Fan's forehead.

As if he had completely fallen into the Eternal Void, his entire body trembled violently with extreme fear.

It felt as if in the next second, he would fall into the grasp of that unknown existence.

Fortunately, the white fog of True Reversion timely obscured his vision.

As if subjected to a violent impact, the white fog shook unstoppably, vibrating ceaselessly!

"True Reversion, True Reversion, True Reversion!"

Still not returning to the predetermined anchor point, Li Fan, within the white fog, was like an infant swaddled in a blanket, helpless to make any response.

He could only instinctively call out repeatedly.

Attempting to break free from this terrifying predicament.

This was the first time Li Fan had experienced a situation where True Reversion had almost failed!

This was enough to show the terrifying nature of the unknown existence within the Eternal Void.

It was even superior to the Saints of the Mountains and Seas.

Most crucially...

Neither True Reversion nor Li Fan's intuition had issued any warning about its arrival.

This seemed to indicate that its existence had already surpassed the existing scope of cognition.

All of Li Fan's life-saving methods were almost rendered useless!

His heart stopped, and Li Fan looked fearfully at the distorted and warped white fog, regretting his reckless actions just now.

The distorted part of the white fog drew closer and closer to Li Fan.

Li Fan could only watch helplessly, unable to do anything.

The cultivation gained through hundreds of reincarnations seemed like a joke in the face of such terror!

"True Reversion!"

Li Fan roared in his heart again.

Finally, as if hearing his call.

The white fog instantly subsided.

The collision and distortion disappeared.

In the misty haze, Li Fan slowly fell into a deep sleep.

Anchor point: 1 Year!

Upon regaining consciousness, Li Fan seemed unable to shake off the horrifying scene of his previous life.

Still drenched in cold sweat, fear lingered in his heart.

He nervously looked up at the sky, towards the area beyond the Mountains and Seas, fearing that the unknown existence from the Eternal Void would track him here.

But after waiting for a good while, the Great Profound Minor World remained silent and still.

There was no difference from the previous anchor point of 1 year.

Only then did Li Fan heave a long sigh of relief.

"I'm alive."

His face regained the demeanor of a transcendent expert, and Li Fan began to ponder the bizarre events that had occurred during True Reversion in his previous life.

"The Eternal Void is a place of absolute nothingness where the concept of existence ceases to be. Then, what was that I sensed just now..."

"Even without revealing itself, the threat it posed far surpassed that of the Saints of the Shore."

Recalling that the annihilation tide of Dao Annihilation was, after all, part of the Mountains and Seas' connection to [Stars],

Li Fan almost instinctively thought of the "Creator God" mentioned in the prophetic texts left by Sun Piaomiao.

Previously, he had only glimpsed its existence in the simple writings left by Sun Piaomiao. He had no concrete understanding of the 'Creator God's' power.

After this ordeal, Li Fan had gained a preliminary understanding.

The pressure it exerted surpassed anything Li Fan had experienced in his countless reincarnations.

So much so that for the following year, when he was alone, Li Fan would still occasionally look up at the sky, fearing that disaster would suddenly descend.

As for Li Fan's aunt, Bai Shuyue, she was also not faring well.

Everyone, at each stage, had their own fears.

Li Fan was terrified of [Stars], while Bai Shuyue, on the other hand, was haunted by the vision of the cataclysmic Dao Annihilation that had engulfed her in her previous life.

Bai Shuyue did not blame the Boundless Wall excessively for inexplicably attracting disaster.

She was merely horrified by the legendary tribulation of the destruction of the Immortal Realm.

"What level of cultivation must one possess to survive such a great tribulation? Transcendence?" Bai Shuyue felt a sense of melancholy.

Knowing that the experience of her previous life should not become a mental obstacle, Bai Shuyue, with her spiritual essence accumulated nearly thirty times, did not choose to evade.

Instead, she closed her eyes, concentrated her mind, and constantly recalled the sensation of being engulfed by Dao Annihilation in her previous life.

After choosing to confront the fear in her heart.

The fear within her heart gradually subsided.

In just over a month, Bai Shuyue's expression became completely serene.

"Dao Annihilation..."

"Is nothing more than this."

"Even if I were to be engulfed by it again in this lifetime, I would no longer be this terrified." Bai Shuyue was very confident.

Having escaped the inner demons, Bai Shuyue restarted her cultivation journey.

Almost habitually, she wanted to cultivate using the method from her previous life.

But then she stopped.

"Without [Wuji], it's indeed a little unaccustomed."

"The rules and restrictions pressing down on me are too numerous and too heavy."

There was no alternative, so Bai Shuyue had to go find the Boundless Wall again and plot the matter of Wuji.

After some preparation and planning, they ultimately managed to suppress Wuji again, without any major incidents.

The Boundless Wall praised, "As expected of someone with transcendent potential! I was worried you might fail at the crucial moment, but I never expected you to be so composed!"

Bai Shuyue simply smiled and did not reply.

Possession was the best method of demystification. Now that she was accustomed to using Wuji as a convenient tool for cultivation, why would she fear it? It was simply a matter of time.

It took a total of one year, back and forth, to finally restore her peak cultivation from her previous life.

At this point, to ascend to immortality, the Boundless Wall once again proposed the plan of continuously searching for True Immortals to suppress, paving the path to immortality.

It also suggested practicing with the remaining immortal artifacts within the Xuanhuang Realm first.

"I think it’s unnecessary."

"Let's directly target Immortals as enemies." Bai Shuyue said domineeringly.

"If there are no suitable opponents in this realm, we shall go beyond the Star Sea."

"There's no need to waste time here anymore."

Bai Shuyue was resolute, and the Boundless Wall had no choice but to follow.

"True Immortals also have their strengths and weaknesses. Let's proceed step by step."

Passing through the high walls, Bai Shuyue and the Boundless Wall arrived outside the Star Sea and suddenly stopped.

"If I recall correctly, in one lifetime, upon entering the Star Sea ahead, I was captured and suppressed by a single palm."

"Let's see how this one fares now."

With such a thought, a cold glint flashed in Bai Shuyue's eyes as she charged into the Dao Net.

Chapter 1647: The Holy Dao Descends Upon the Body

Just like the previous time they intruded upon the Dao Net, countless interlacing fine threads instantly appeared around them, like a giant net, enveloping Bai Shuyue.

Furthermore, a pair of translucent giant hands materialized, filled with immense rage, pressing down upon the person and the wall: "How dare you!"

However, this time, Bai Shuyue was no longer as defenseless as before.

The rhythm of Wuji surged around her body, transforming into an armor impervious to all laws. The moment the translucent hands collided, they were distorted and repelled.

"Oh?"

While still wondering in surprise, Bai Shuyue, holding her jade staff, arrived in an instant.

With the power to overturn heaven and earth, the translucent hand was pulverized in moments. Even the Dao Net within a large radius of the star field was shattered and distorted!

This directly revealed a path leading to the core within.

The fragility of the Dao Net was truly beyond Bai Shuyue's expectations. However, her reaction was swift, and without fear, she charged straight in.

Occasionally, threads of restoration, like tentacles, extended out, attempting to obstruct Bai Shuyue's charge. But the Great Dao of Wuji's ability to overcome all laws was too prominent, causing these Dao strings, each possessing power comparable to a True Immortal, to shatter upon contact!

Seeing Bai Shuyue advancing like a bamboo shoot breaking through the ground, the Boundless Wall excitedly shouted: "Go this way! I can sense a strong True Immortal aura from here! Although their Dao is flourishing, their momentum is weak, they must have been suppressed for a long time..."

Following the Boundless Wall's guidance, Bai Shuyue continued to speed through the depths of the Dao Net.

Gradually, groups of figures began to appear, blocking Bai Shuyue's path.

"Those who block my way shall die!"

Facing these mortal interferers, Bai Shuyue merely snorted coldly, her speed unwavering.

The Heaven-Overturning Staff Technique unleashed waves of sweeping cyan light, and in mere moments, the vast majority of the enemies before her were engulfed.

Yet, there was one figure who, astonishingly, blocked Bai Shuyue's staff strike!

Bai Shuyue's surging momentum was instantly halted.

She narrowed her eyes and scrutinized the person blocking her.

A refined middle-aged man, dressed in white, with a scholar's cap. As he met Bai Shuyue's gaze, a hint of anger flickered beneath his calm eyes.

Without further ado, they began to fight.

"Nangong Fusheng, receive the Dao Net's blessing!"

As a light shout echoed, Bai Shuyue seemed to see threads of light crisscrossing the sky. It was as if a gentle palm strike had caused a light fragment to disconnect and fall.

Slowly drifting down, it imprinted itself upon Nangong Fusheng's body.

His aura began to ascend and expand boundlessly.

Initially, like Bai Shuyue, he was at the pinnacle of mortality. But in a moment, he became a powerful True Immortal.

Then, his body became comparable to the Nameless.

And this was not his limit.

It was as if all the Daos of the heavens were engraved on him. Nangong Fusheng stood there alone, and Bai Shuyue felt as though she were facing the Great Dao itself!

In an instant, Nangong Fusheng completed his transformation from an ant to a giant.

Fiercely glaring at Bai Shuyue, who dared to intrude upon the Dao Net, Nangong Fusheng held nothing back.

"Universe in a Palm!"

A palm as immense as a mountain descended from above.

In Bai Shuyue's vision, everything else disappeared, leaving only the palm lines that protruded like mountain ranges.

Mountains and rivers within the palm, stretching endlessly; ascending to the heavens and descending to the earth, there was nowhere to escape!

"Turn it over for me!"

Bai Shuyue remained composed, continuously stirring her jade staff, trying to overturn this collapsing sky.

Waves of cyan light rose, attempting to support the descending giant palm.

But the moment they touched, Bai Shuyue sensed the vast difference in strength between them.

She could perhaps hold on for a while with her divine abilities and treasures, but there was absolutely no possibility of pushing it away or overturning it.

"Great Dao of Wuji!"

Bai Shuyue instinctively wanted to use the nature of Wuji to break all laws and resolve the opponent's attack.

However, for some unknown reason, the Wuji rhythm, which had always been effective, failed against Nangong Fusheng!

The Dao patterns transformed into markings. Although they sensed the aura of Wuji, they remained condensed and did not disperse.

"This is bad, it's the Dao Imprinting the Body, using the laws for oneself!"

It was the knowledgeable Boundless Wall that noticed the anomaly and urgently reminded her.

"Dao Imprinting the Body?"

"Although Wuji can break all laws, the opponent is not directly using various Great Dao laws to attack. Instead, they are engraving the entire Dao Net onto themselves, thereby increasing the toughness of their physical body."

"It does not directly confront Wuji, adding a layer of obstruction, thus allowing itself to persist. Strictly speaking, the opponent is a body cultivator, not using divine abilities or techniques to fight, but purely relying on physical strength to suppress people! We must first break the Dao Net Imprinted on his body!"

In a flash, Bai Shuyue and the Boundless Wall exchanged information.

And Nangong Fusheng's giant palm was already right above their heads.

"No need to worry, I'll help you!"

The Boundless Wall produced the Eternal Straw Cloak and promptly covered Bai Shuyue's entire body.

As if pressing down on a hard pebble, Nangong Fusheng's palm, though it had already descended, only pricked his palm, causing it to bleed. He painfully withdrew his hand.

Bai Shuyue seized the opportunity to escape, getting out of the palm's coverage. Her jade staff, imbued with the Great Dao of Wuji, smashed towards the Dao markings engraved on Nangong Fusheng's body.

Where Wuji went, all Daos dispersed.

Nangong Fusheng's originally flawless Dao inscriptions thus developed a gap.

However, he did not show the slightest sign of panic. Gazing at Bai Shuyue, who was darting around, he sneered: "The Dao gives birth to the world!"

Every Dao marking on his body erupted with an intensely blinding light. Following this, figures emerged from the light.

In just a moment, they filled the sky, dense as brushwood, obscuring the sun and moon.

Nangong Fusheng's colossal body instantly vanished, replaced by countless heavenly soldiers and generals!

And without exception, all of them were body cultivators!

The Boundless Wall gasped in admiration: "This brat has refined all his vital energy into avatars. Although the power of the Dao Net Imprinting the Body is dispersed among each avatar, his overall strength has decreased. However, for us, it is even more difficult to deal with!"

"He saw through our reliance on the Great Dao of Wuji and devised a countermeasure!"

Under the siege of countless body cultivators, Bai Shuyue found herself in a bitter struggle.

Even though each swing of her staff could eliminate dozens of figures, Nangong Fusheng's vital energy surged as if inexhaustible.

The rate at which he generated them far outstripped the rate at which they were eliminated.

Slowly, the figures surrounding them grew more numerous, like ropes, attempting to bind Bai Shuyue firmly.

Even with the protection of the Eternal Straw Cloak, Nangong Fusheng could not harm Bai Shuyue in a short period. However, Bai Shuyue felt her movements becoming slower and slower, her actions becoming increasingly restricted.

"This situation is not good!" the Boundless Wall exclaimed with great concern.

Bai Shuyue also felt quite frustrated in her heart.

She had intended to dominate with the Great Dao of Wuji, supplemented by the Boundless Wall's various treasures. How could she have expected to be defeated so easily?

Could it be that the plan to create an immortal path by slaying Immortals was doomed to fail before it even began?

Bai Shuyue's expression darkened. The Boundless Wall, sensing that the Dao Net, previously broken by the Great Dao of Wuji, was slowly recovering, urged ceaselessly: "Temporarily retreat and consider a countermeasure!"

Bai Shuyue was not foolhardy. She immediately ceased her engagement with Nangong Fusheng. Opening a path with the Great Dao of Wuji, she broke out from the depths of the Dao Net.

Temporarily escaping the Star Sea, she returned within the high walls.

Retracting his countless avatars, Nangong Fusheng, clad in white, calmly gazed in the direction Bai Shuyue had disappeared.

Beneath his white robe, the Dao markings remained clearly visible, like searing brands covering his entire body, startling and shocking.

Furthermore, Nangong Fusheng coughed a few times, and a trace of blood appeared at the corner of his mouth.

...

"Are the cultivators in the lower realms generally this strong now?"

The two, their first attempt having failed, fell into self-doubt.

"That Dao Imprinting the Body technique is indeed difficult to deal with. It's almost like confronting the power of the Dao Net in the Star Sea, just converted to the physical aspect."

"Without the advantage of Wuji breaking all laws, it was already fortunate that we could retreat safely. It was no easy feat." After a long while, the Boundless Wall spoke, trying to comfort itself.

Bai Shuyue looked up at the Immortal Ruins outside the Xuanhuang Realm: "Why don't we find a different opponent?"

The Boundless Wall pondered carefully and shook its head: "The Star Sea Dao Net is on our necessary path. We will have to face it sooner or later. If we are to create an immortal path, relying on just one or two True Immortals is far from enough..."

Hearing this, Bai Shuyue's eyes narrowed, and she slowly nodded.

"However, it's not that we must necessarily oppose the Dao Net." The Boundless Wall suddenly changed its tone.

"During the previous battle, I vaguely sensed that beneath the Dao Net, many True Immortals are suppressed. Thinking about it now, if they could weave such a vast net in the Star Sea, it is likely because they are imprisoning and utilizing these True Immortals..."

"You mean?"

"Based on my understanding of True Immortals in the Immortal Realm, such capture is something they would definitely not passively accept. Therefore, this Dao Net force is likely in opposition to the masses of Immortals. In other words, we might be able to cooperate." The Boundless Wall whispered.

"However, the prerequisite is that they have not captured all the True Immortals in this realm."

Once again outside the high walls, facing the Star Sea, the Boundless Wall shot out strands of ethereal light: "Let me first investigate secretly!"

The Dao Net was densely interwoven, and the Boundless Wall's investigation seemed extremely difficult.

It was only after a full three years that it achieved success and returned.

"As I predicted. There are 'Immortal Hunters' in the Star Sea, hunting down True Immortals to sculpt the Dao Net."

"The Nangong Fusheng who fought us that day was one of the founders of the Dao Net."

"However, the true owner of the Dao Net is called [The Great Net]. Extremely mysterious, usually appearing only as a pair of blue giant hands. Even when we intruded into the Dao Net that day, it did not take action..." The Boundless Wall recounted the intelligence it had gathered — Feng.

In Bai Shuyue's mind, however, she recalled the Boundless Wall being suppressed in her previous two lifetimes.

"Those giant hands felt even stronger than Nangong Fusheng."

With the intention of cooperation, Bai Shuyue once again arrived within the Star Sea Dao Net.

However, this time, she did not intrude. Instead, she quietly waited.

As expected, the Dao Net faction soon noticed the arrival of the previous intruder.

Figures one after another appeared, confronting them from afar.

Bai Shuyue scanned the surroundings but did not find Nangong Fusheng.

"Chaos, Divine Thought?..." The Boundless Wall quietly informed her of their identities.

"You have returned, Senior. What is your intention this time?" Chaos asked expressionlessly.

Even though the opponent was a mortal, they, as True Immortals, dared not underestimate them in the slightest.

Especially after learning that she possessed the Great Dao of Wuji.

Although Nangong Fusheng had acted last time, stopping her, the Dao Imprinting the Body, especially the reinforcement of the entire Dao Net's power, had caused considerable damage to Nangong Fusheng's physique.

However, fortune and misfortune are intertwined. He also broke through a long-standing bottleneck and glimpsed an opportunity for breakthrough. He was currently in seclusion in enlightenment, hence his absence.

Bai Shuyue cut to the chase: "The Immortal Hunters capture Immortals, and I also wish to hunt Immortals. Perhaps, we can assist each other."

"Hmm?"

The True Immortals of the Dao Net all looked at Bai Shuyue with suspicion.

Bai Shuyue also felt somewhat helpless, and had to explain again: "There is no path forward, and to prove the path to becoming an Immortal, one must resort to this method."

The True Immortals of the Dao Net were once again silent. Looking at Bai Shuyue, their expressions were complex.

"So it was a misunderstanding earlier. That's excellent!"

"Indeed, we can discuss further."

A pair of blue giant hands suddenly appeared in the field.

Chaos and others were slightly surprised and nodded in greeting.

Bai Shuyue's heart also became vigilant subconsciously.

"Fellow Daoist, there's no need to be nervous. I am simply very interested in your 'Slaying Immortals to Prove the Dao' path."

"Of course, if you merely wish to transform from mortal to immortal, I have several other methods. If you are interested, I can explain them one by one." The blue giant hands said with a smile.

"Several methods of achieving immortality?" Hearing this, Bai Shuyue's brows furrowed, and her first reaction was disbelief.

However, the other True Immortals of the Dao Net all looked as if it were a matter of course.

What the blue giant hands said did not seem like a lie.

In an instant, Bai Shuyue suddenly understood the meaning behind the complex expressions on the faces of the Dao Net True Immortals just now.

It was probably: "It's just about becoming an Immortal, why make such a fuss?"

She had never expected that what she had been desperately seeking seemed so easily attainable in the eyes of the other party.

Even with Bai Shuyue's state of mind, which had undergone more than thirty lifetimes of reincarnation, she couldn't help but feel a ripple of emotion.

She then said solemnly: "I wish to hear your explanation."

"Hahaha!"

The blue giant hands let out a hearty laugh, and light erupted, instantly enveloping Bai Shuyue.

Bai Shuyue did not resist, allowing them to act.

As light and shadow shifted, Bai Shuyue's vision flickered, and the next moment, she found herself in a pavilion on a mountaintop.

A thin but spirited old man was waiting for her.

"Bai Shuyue!" She reported her name.

"This old man... is Cheng Dao."

Cheng Dao looked Bai Shuyue up and down, and a hint of joy flashed in his eyes.

"I never expected such a talent to emerge from such a desolate realm," Cheng Dao praised without reservation.

Bai Shuyue's heart leaped. Although she didn't understand what specific realm he was referring to, she assumed it was related to her heaven-defying talent.

Unsure how to respond, she remained silent.

Cheng Dao, however, did not mind. He spoke kindly and asked about the path of Slaying Immortals to Prove the Dao.

Bai Shuyue showed a look of shame: "It's just a desperate measure due to the lack of a path to immortality. One Immortal, one step. Though the divide between Immortals and mortals is vast, one can still complete the Immortal path."

Chapter 1648: The Ambitions of Cheng Dao

"Becoming an Immortal..."

"Why bother becoming an Immortal? If my estimations are correct, if you truly complete this path, you will be not far from the Nameless realm," Cheng Dao stroked his beard and chuckled approvingly.

"Uh? Is that really true?" Bai Shuyue was somewhat perplexed.

Although her talent was extraordinary, she was still completely ignorant of the specific methods of ascending to Immortality. This path of Slaying Immortals to Prove the Dao was, after all, a suggestion from the Boundless Wall.

However, since Cheng Dao's appearance, the usually arrogant and overbearing Boundless Wall had become uncharacteristically quiet, not daring to make a sound.

Cheng Dao patiently explained to Bai Shuyue: "Immortals are those who ascend a mountain; this mountain is the '[Above]'. To gain the momentum from Above, one obtains the might of an Immortal."

"However, this is not enough. One must also venture into the Infinite Sea to gain its peculiar characteristics on the '[Infinite]'. With the power of both Mountains and Seas, one can then become a True Immortal."

"The Mountain Above, the Infinite Sea..." Bai Shuyue had certainly heard of the names of Mountains and Seas before, but this was the first time she clearly understood the relationship between their power and True Immortals.

"Then what about climbing the mountain and traversing the sea?" Bai Shuyue asked again.

"It was precisely with this question in mind that the two Saint Monarchs, Lian Shan and Gui Hai, achieved their accomplishments!" Cheng Dao lamented, slowly recounting the deeds of the two Saints.

Lian Shan, the first Immortal in the world.

Gui Hai, who opened the Infinite Spring.

The supreme divine abilities of the Saints, the legends of creating heaven and earth, listening to them made Bai Shuyue's heart yearn.

"We mortals, like myself, do not possess the abilities of Saints to directly draw power from Mountains and Seas. Therefore, we must borrow the great power of the two Saints."

"In the past, mortals who ascended had to undergo a baptism on the Ascension Platform to truly become True Immortals. Even beings born in the Immortal Realm who wished to attain Immortal status needed the Imperial Decree of the Immortal Emperor for ennoblement..."

Bai Shuyue gradually understood: "Are the Ascension Platform baptism and the Immortal Emperor's ennoblement merely manifestations of the two Saints' authority? Doesn't this mean that all True Immortals in the world stand on the shoulders of the two Saints, Lian Shan and Gui Hai, to venture into Mountains and Seas? If, one day, the two Saints were to fall..."

The word "fall" could not be uttered before Cheng Dao gently raised a finger, silencing the sound.

"Only those like you, who have not yet entered the Immortal path, would dare to make such a statement. With Saint Monarchs above, some words are best left unsaid. Although Saints may not care, but..." Cheng Dao cast a glance at Bai Shuyue.

Instantly, she felt as if she were bearing a thousand pounds, and cold sweat dripped from her forehead.

Her heart filled with horror and she gained a preliminary understanding of the old man's power. She repeatedly nodded, indicating that she had learned her lesson.

Cheng Dao's expression softened again, correcting Bai Shuyue's previous understanding: "The assistance of the two Saints is not mandatory, but merely provides a smoother path. If you truly possess peerless talent, you can naturally climb the mountain and traverse the sea on your own. However..."

"Without the protection of Saint Monarchs, ordinary people, even if they can touch Mountains and Seas themselves, likely wouldn't be able to endure for long before being assimilated and swallowed by them."

"As for your concerns..." Cheng Dao chuckled, "Saints would definitely consider them more thoroughly than us."

His words stopped abruptly, not elaborating on the specifics of their thoroughness.

Bai Shuyue, being sensible, did not press further.

Instead, she shifted the conversation to the specific method of ascending to Immortality: "Senior Cheng Dao, the Immortal Realm has long since collapsed, the Immortal Emperor is no more, and Saints are nowhere to be seen. For mortals like us, how can we seek Immortality and cultivate the Dao?"

"The simplest method..."

"I shall write an Imperial Decree." Cheng Dao's tone was calm, uttered tonelessly.

Such an answer was completely beyond Bai Shuyue's expectations, and she was momentarily stunned.

Then, she looked at Cheng Dao with disbelief.

Even though she had already estimated the old man's power to some extent in her heart, when he uttered this remark so casually, Bai Shuyue was still profoundly shaken.

"To be able to decree True Immortals, could this person before me have been an Immortal Emperor of the Immortal Realm?"

"No wonder the Boundless Wall became so well-behaved, as if fearing discovery." Bai Shuyue couldn't help but have such thoughts.

Following this, a sense of unease arose in her heart.

"His status and power are unimaginable. Why does he look upon me with such favor? Could it be merely because of my talent? Or is it related to the secret of my continuous reincarnation?"

If Bai Shuyue were merely exceptionally talented, she would naturally not have such hidden worries. But precisely because she harbored a great secret, her state of mind became gradually unsettled.

Although Cheng Dao could not fully comprehend Bai Shuyue's inner thoughts, he did sense the turmoil in her heart. However, he merely assumed that Bai Shuyue was shocked by his words about decreeing Immortals and did not think further in other directions.

"This Imperial Decree can only be used once. It is considered a separate path connecting you to Mountains and Seas. Your accumulated realm is already sufficient. Upon receiving the decree, you will instantly glimpse the phenomena of Mountains and Seas and achieve True Immortality! However, I do not recommend you choose this path."

Bai Shuyue composed herself and asked solemnly: "And why is that? I hope Senior can provide some guidance."

"Because with your talent... it would be a waste to take this path. You are different from those vulgar individuals; you have the potential to forge a path that reaches the heavens." Cheng Dao did not explicitly state the realm, but used the words "path that reaches the heavens" as a substitute.

"Climbing the mountain and traversing the sea involves great peril, but also great opportunity! Lian Shan and Gui Hai became Saints precisely because of this. While external protection may ensure safety, it also eliminates the invaluable opportunity to personally comprehend Mountains and Seas. And the first glimpse of Mountains and Seas, which inspires insight, is the most crucial..."

"When I attained Immortality, I did so by observing Mountains and Seas myself, which is why my progress after becoming an Immortal was like a thousand miles in a day," Cheng Dao said with a pleased expression.

Bai Shuyue was slightly surprised, then gave a wry smile: "Although I possess some talent, I am also self-aware. I certainly cannot achieve what Senior did, experiencing Mountains and Seas personally."

"Alas..." Cheng Dao waved his hand, "You need not be so modest. In fact, your talent is not much weaker than mine."

Bai Shuyue was stunned.

"With the strength we had before becoming Immortals, we certainly could not face Mountains and Seas directly. However..."

Cheng Dao paused, then slowly said, "With the protection of a mentor, one can naturally ignore the risks involved."

Bai Shuyue was completely dumbfounded this time.

"Mentor?"

"Precisely! Unlike the protection of the two Saints, a mentor will not block all the incursions from Mountains and Seas. Instead, they will only filter out the parts that exceed your limit of endurance. This way, you can personally experience Mountains and Seas without worrying about your own life!"

"Furthermore, at that time, the mentor can offer guidance at crucial moments. It will not affect your comprehension of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, but will only clear the fog ahead for you. The efficiency of comprehension is hundreds of times higher than comprehending alone!" Regarding his mentor, Cheng Dao's expression became solemn, slowly explaining the subtleties involved.

Since embarking on the path of cultivation, Bai Shuyue had always explored on her own, never having formally apprenticed under anyone.

Hearing Cheng Dao speak of the convenience of having a mentor, she couldn't help but feel a sense of longing.

At the same time, her heart stirred, and she vaguely guessed the reason why he had looked upon her with special favor.

However, she did not state this directly and continued to feign ignorance, saying helplessly: "Having such a renowned mentor is truly a blessing from heaven. However, Senior, you may not know that I have always been alone since I began cultivating..."

Cheng Dao's eyebrows slightly raised, his joy becoming more pronounced, finally reaching the main point: "My Master is named [Shou Qiu]. I received his grace, which is why I have achieved my current cultivation. Since I learned my Master's Dao, I ought to carry it on and fulfill his aspirations."

"Alas, due to various reasons, I am still trapped here, failing to live up to my Master's expectations."

Cheng Dao stared intently at Bai Shuyue: "In the past, to save the Star Sea, I wove a Dao Net to bear the Dao Annihilation. This is an act of fulfilling my Master's teachings, but it has taken too long, and has now become a burden to me."

Saying this, Cheng Dao waved his hand, and an image of the Star Sea Dao Net appeared before Bai Shuyue.

Threads of Dao, crisscrossing horizontally and vertically. Mysterious and magnificent.

And as Cheng Dao's words continued, the image of the Dao Net gradually magnified, revealing its depths.

Four figures, like prisoners, were suppressed within the Dao Net.

The aura emanating from each of them sent shivers down Bai Shuyue's spine.

"Nameless True Immortals."

While her expression was solemn, Bai Shuyue's gaze fell upon the figure in the very center of the Dao Net.

Gaunt in appearance, with a thin build.

If she was not mistaken, his features were exactly the same as Cheng Dao's before her.

As if sensing Bai Shuyue's astonishment, Cheng Dao frankly admitted: "Yes, that is me!"

"In the past, in order to persuade the various Immortals, I was the first to enter the fray. Although I protected this star sea for tens of thousands of years, however..."

"This Dao Net has trapped me," Cheng Dao's expression became somewhat peculiar.

Bai Shuyue suddenly felt that her previous assumptions might have been somewhat incorrect.

"Over the years, I have pondered constantly and realized the difference between my actions and my Master's."

"The key to Mountains and Seas lies externally, not within. As the saying goes, 'irrelevant to the final outcome'."

"Therefore, my Master, who repeatedly intervened to save the Immortal Realm in the past, left behind an illusory form, Cheng Dao, after understanding this."

"My Master used an illusory form to resist the Dao Annihilation. But I used my own body as a pillar... this is the biggest difference!"

Cheng Dao sighed: "Trapped here, how can I truly carry on my Master's work and save the Mountains and Seas? At that time, I had no transcendent power but forced myself to transcend, which was a grave mistake!"

"If I had only focused on cultivation and ignored worldly affairs, perhaps I would have already reached the transcendent realm by now."

"Although my Master did not explicitly say so, I could vaguely sense his disappointment in me from our few communications."

After Cheng Dao finished speaking, he stared intently at Bai Shuyue.

"I have long had the idea of freeing myself, but the mistake has already been made. If I were to forcibly escape now, it would cause the Dao Net to collapse and this realm to be destroyed, which still goes against my Dao path..."

"So, Senior's meaning is?" Bai Shuyue asked cautiously.

"In the past, I searched the entire Star Sea, looking for someone qualified to guard the Star Sea in my stead. However, I found that they were all vulgar individuals, unworthy of the task. Now..."

"You are qualified!" Cheng Dao said resolutely.

"Are you willing to share my burden?"

Bai Shuyue hesitated and had not yet replied when the Boundless Wall, which had been silent until now, suddenly transmitted a message.

It frantically urged: "Agree! Agree! If you say no, we will all die!"

As if sensing the Boundless Wall's transmission, Cheng Dao glanced nonchalantly towards the place where the Boundless Wall was hidden.

Bai Shuyue's heart tightened.

Although she had the ability of infinite rebirth, she was unwilling to casually sacrifice her life if she was not in a desperate situation.

She could only steel herself and agree: "How could I refuse Senior's request."

"Good!" Cheng Dao laughed heartily, overjoyed at the prospect of shedding his burden.

From his previous image of a frail old man, he instantly transformed into a robust and steady middle-aged man.

"Rest assured, you are not helping me for naught. Know that many people in this realm wished to take my place but could not. Now..." Cheng Dao said with great delight, explaining to Bai Shuyue.

"To become a pillar of flesh and blood, supporting the Dao Annihilation. The core operation of the Dao Net is based on the 'Illusory Form Cheng Dao Technique' created by my Master. However, my power was limited at the time, and the illusory form was insufficient to bear the weight of the Dao Annihilation. Hence, I had to use my own body as a substitute."

"If you replace me, I will naturally pass on this Illusory Form Cheng Dao Technique to you. Although I am not qualified to accept you as a disciple on behalf of my Master, after receiving this Illusory Form Cheng Dao Technique, you can barely be considered a disciple of Shou Qiu. When I inform my Master later, you may have the opportunity to truly become his disciple."

Facing Cheng Dao's empty promises, Bai Shuyue did not hold much hope.

More importantly, regarding who Shou Qiu was and what deeds he had accomplished, Bai Shuyue knew very little.

She only knew that he had once resisted a devastating Dao Annihilation tribulation for the Immortal Realm.

Therefore, she was not particularly excited.

"There is another benefit to managing the Dao Net," Cheng Dao continued, waving his hand. Countless Dao string images transformed from the illusory to the real, as if truly delving into the core of the Dao Net.

Cheng Dao led Bai Shuyue and pointed to the countless clearly visible Dao strings surrounding them, slowly saying.

With Bai Shuyue's comprehension, she now knew that Cheng Dao's words were not false.

The enlightenment opportunities here were more than a hundred times better than exploring elsewhere.

Although the Daos within the Dao Net were somewhat lacking compared to the Star Sea, for Bai Shuyue, it was already enough for her to comprehend for a considerable period.

"Not only that, but the expansion of the Dao Net also coincides with your path of Slaying Immortals to Prove the Dao!"

"Please impart your knowledge, Senior." Bai Shuyue said solemnly.

"Know that in this Star Sea, there are still some wandering True Immortals. You can use the power of the Dao Net to defeat and suppress them one by one. While expanding the Dao Net, you can also increase your own foundation."

"When the accumulation is sufficient..."

Cheng Dao bent slightly, even summoning an illusory form.

"With the protection of your Master, I can help you ascend to the Immortal realm!"

Chapter 1649: A Thousand Years Pass Swiftly

"Shou Qiu..."

Bai Shuyue gazed at the illusory figure standing quietly before Cheng Dao.

Perhaps due to the vast difference in their power, Bai Shuyue did not sense how extraordinary this Shou Qiu figure was.

But since Cheng Dao spoke so solemnly, it must be exceptionally effective.

Cheng Dao began to share his feelings at the moment he attained Immortality: "The sea is deep, the mountains are boundless. However, Mountains and Seas cannot be blasphemed and are difficult to observe up close. Those who enter Mountains and Seas will inevitably be submerged within, losing their senses, their souls, and themselves. But if one receives the protection of a mentor, they can closely observe the secrets of Mountains and Seas. The Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, which others will spend lifetimes pondering and comprehending, you will have already glimpsed the moment you ascend to Immortality."

"From then on, until the transcendent realm, the path will be smooth sailing!"

In Cheng Dao's narration, Bai Shuyue seemed to truly see the magnificent scene of continuous mountains and seas, where all the principles of the world converged.

"You have amassed considerable fortune through your path of Slaying Immortals to Prove the Dao. If you can comprehend the changes in Mountains and Seas at the moment of ascending to Immortality, perhaps at the moment of becoming an Immortal, you will also achieve Transcendence!"

Although Bai Shuyue did not know how much truth there was in Cheng Dao's words, the other party had patiently explained so much to her, and Cheng Dao did not seem like a simple person.

If she refused, she might not be able to leave the core of the Dao Net.

However, Bai Shuyue had left the high walls precisely to find a suitable cultivation method. She could sense that cultivating in the Star Sea with the aid of the Dao Net might bring her immense benefits.

Therefore, she agreed: "I am willing to undertake Senior's task and guard the Dao Net."

Bai Shuyue agreed readily, and Cheng Dao's mood became even better.

"However, your current physical body is still too weak. It needs some modification..."

"Come out!" Cheng Dao glanced at the Boundless Wall hidden on Bai Shuyue and said lightly.

The Boundless Wall, always so arrogant, was now remarkably obedient. It did not pretend not to hear but immediately jumped out.

"You and I are, in a sense, of the same clan. Since we meet today, it is fate. My Master once depicted me, and I..."

"Today, I shall bestow upon you a great fortune!"

Saying this, Cheng Dao instantly vanished from their presence.

It was as if a gust of wind had blown, and the crisscrossing Dao Net suddenly rippled.

The Dao strings twisted and bent, forming a void that directly exposed the deepest core.

Bai Shuyue and the Boundless Wall plunged directly into the vacant circular space.

It was completely dark, with nothing visible. Even the Dao strings emitting a faint blue light within the Dao Net seemed to be high up in the heavens, extremely far from this place.

But as the wind grew stronger, the darkness was gradually illuminated by clusters of light.

Bai Shuyue looked at the lights and shadows flashing around and discovered that they seemed to be the phenomena of Mountains and Seas!

And not just illusory images, she could even comprehend the various Daos of Mountains and Seas from them!

"Jade that is not carved will not become a vessel."

"You have served before Saint Monarchs, but ultimately you are still a [thing]. To go further in this Mountains and Seas, you must transform from a thing into a person!" Cheng Dao said with deep emotion.

At the same time, continuous mountain shadows pressed down towards the Boundless Wall.

"Senior, spare me..."

"Stop your noise! If you cannot withstand this small hardship, how can you truly transform!" Before the Boundless Wall could even cry out, Cheng Dao interrupted it roughly with a cold snort.

"Mountain, come!"

Cheng Dao let out a low roar, and the continuous mountain shadows before them rapidly converged and compressed, eventually forming a seemingly solid black mountain that fiercely suppressed the Boundless Wall.

The Boundless Wall could not even utter a single whimper.

"Water, come!"

The boundless sea above also gradually gathered under Cheng Dao's guidance. It transformed into a white ribbon and plummeted down from the summit of the black mountain, like a torrential downpour. The mountain and water expanded, but unexpectedly, there was not much sound.

It was merely like a mountain stream, tinkling and flowing, refreshing the heart and mind.

The mountain and water formed a self-contained entity, endlessly circulating.

The water flowed to the bottom of the mountain, suddenly disappearing. The next moment, it reappeared hundreds of feet above the mountain summit, continuing its downward flow.

As the mountain and water circulated, they generated endless life.

"When the water is exhausted and the mountain collapses one day, that will be when you transform from a thing into a person!"

Saying these words, Cheng Dao finally revealed his true form.

Creating this scene of mountain and water seemed to have consumed a considerable amount of energy from Cheng Dao.

He reverted to his previous appearance of a frail old man.

He pointed to the black mountain and white water before him and said to Bai Shuyue: "You only need to sit amidst this mountain and water to borrow its power to resist the pressure from the core of the Dao Net."

"This creation of mountain and water contains many of my insights from these years. Not only will it enlighten the Boundless Wall, but it will also greatly benefit you. While you guard the Dao Net, you may also study it together."

"The stronger you become, the less pressure the Dao Net will exert on you. And the more powerful the strength of the Dao Net you can wield."

"Guarding the Dao Net is beneficial to you in every way. If not for your extraordinary talent, I would not entrust such a heavy responsibility to you."

"However, until you achieve transcendence and can split off an illusory form of Cheng Dao to replace you in bearing the Dao Net's burden, you absolutely cannot leave this place."

Bai Shuyue saw that the distorted Dao strings above her head were slowly returning to normal. The circular gap gradually disappeared. In the endless darkness, only the black mountain and white water stood firm.

"Next, I will teach you the 'Illusory Form Cheng Dao Technique'."

Cheng Dao's illusory form also vanished completely, leaving only echoing sounds.

Bai Shuyue listened intently.

This technique of Illusory Form Cheng Dao was indeed extraordinary.

Bai Shuyue seemed to see Shou Qiu, his back to all living beings, gazing at the sea, holding up the collapsing heavens alone.

When she emerged from the profound enlightenment of this divine technique, Cheng Dao had already completely disappeared.

Neither in the depths of the Dao Net's core, nor within the Dao Net itself.

His whereabouts were unknown, seemingly having escaped the cage like a bird breaking free from its bonds, leaving so swiftly and decisively.

Fortunately, several transmission scrolls remained: "There are still remaining Star Seas in the lower realms, but they are isolated by Dao Annihilation, like scattered islands in a vast ocean. The only thing you need to pay attention to is the Guangwu Star Sea, which is closest to the Star Sea."

"Although there are still True Immortals opposing each other within the Star Sea, they are few and far between, not worth fearing..."

Bai Shuyue carefully read Cheng Dao's instructions and then fell into a long silence.

She tried to move, but the dense darkness felt like shackles. Residing in the core of the Dao Net, she felt as if the weight of the entire Dao Net had descended upon her. If she were not sitting on the white water and black mountain at this moment, she would likely have been crushed to pieces on the spot.

"Apart from the constraints of the Dao Net itself, there are also some restrictions left by Cheng Dao... It seems that until a certain realm is reached, escape is impossible." Bai Shuyue shook her head slightly, but her heart was not particularly concerned.

Although this place was like a prison, for her, as long as she chose to end her life and start the next reincarnation, she could leave at any time.

"Indeed, it is a good place for enlightenment and cultivation."

Without the constraints of rules and regulations, with a single thought, she could observe all the Dao principles within the Dao Net.

Compared to the nameless beings like Fugui and Yanjian, who could occasionally chat and listen to ancient Immortal Realm secrets,

Moreover, there were Cheng Dao's insights into Mountains and Seas to study.

Compared to the Xuanhuang Realm, this place was truly a rare cultivation paradise.

Bai Shuyue immersed herself in it and diligently cultivated.

In fact, the Dao Net had its own operational system. Even if she did not intervene, the Dao Net could expand and develop on its own.

Organizations such as the Shuoxinghai Management Association and the Immortal Hunters hunted True Immortals surviving in the Star Sea, strengthening themselves.

Only when they encountered truly insurmountable Nameless True Immortals would they trigger the large-scale power of the Dao Net for intervention.

This was the time when Bai Shuyue needed to exert her strength.

Fortunately, such opportunities were few, and for Bai Shuyue, it was not a difficult task.

Although the Immortal Hunters were mostly mortals, their cultivation of special techniques and their research and utilization of the Dao Net had reached an astonishing level.

Bai Shuyue, as the coordinator, engraved the power of the Dao Net into their bodies.

Within the area covered by the Dao Net, their power was almost equivalent to that of Nameless True Immortals.

During her thousand years of guarding the Dao Net's core, there were only three instances of confronting Nameless True Immortals.

In all cases, the Dao Net emerged victorious.

Bai Shuyue finally understood why Cheng Dao had said that the True Immortals were not to be feared.

The path to becoming an Immortal in this world was broken, and the number of residual True Immortals was limited. Every time one was captured by the Star Sea, their own vital force diminished.

Conversely, the Dao Net could turn captured True Immortals into sources of power for itself. As for the losses incurred during battles with True Immortals...

Mortals were endless, and the Shuoxinghai Management Association had a sound system for selecting talent.

With this disparity, the defeat of the True Immortals was already a foregone conclusion.

As for the Guangwu Star Sea outside the Star Sea...

Taking Cheng Dao's warning very seriously, Bai Shuyue ultimately decided not to interact with them, despite their repeated attempts to communicate.

Controlling the core power of the Dao Net, although some factions within the Star Sea held differing opinions, they could not disobey.

Another seven hundred years passed, and the Star Sea had no more Immortals to capture.

Several Nameless individuals had all been captured and suppressed.

The Star Sea became peaceful from then on.

On this day.

"Damn it, I've been tricked."

Bai Shuyue stood upon the black mountain and white water, unable to refrain from cursing.

Nearly a thousand years had passed, but for her, it seemed like only an instant.

The scene of Cheng Dao's grandiose promises from the past was still vivid in her memory.

But after a thousand years of worldly changes, Bai Shuyue finally understood why Cheng Dao had been so eager to leave.

"The Star Sea is an isolated island. All the resources that can be observed and collected here are insufficient to give birth to a single transcendent being."

This was the conclusion Bai Shuyue reached after a thousand years of contemplation.

Her thirty reincarnations stacked together had truly given her extraordinary nature.

Coupled with the unique cultivation environment at the core of the Dao Net.

It could be said that if there was even a one percent chance, she could have painstakingly achieved it step by step.

But in reality...

At a certain point, her cultivation hit a bottleneck.

If comprehending ten Great Daos yielded a harvest of ten, then comprehending a hundred Great Daos yielded only twenty. And even with further comprehension, it would not exceed thirty.

"This is also why most True Immortals first attain the Nameless realm, then seek Transcendence."

"The path of Slaying Immortals to Prove the Dao, as proposed by the Boundless Wall, is indeed correct. But..."

Bai Shuyue shook her head slightly: "It is based on the premise that there are enough Immortals for me to slay."

"If the Immortal Realm still existed, perhaps it could have been easily achieved. But now..."

"True Immortals are still too rare."

Bai Shuyue looked down at the Boundless Wall, suppressed beneath the black mountain.

If Cheng Dao had deceived her in some aspects, then Cheng Dao had been exceptionally good to the Boundless Wall.

Over a thousand years, the black mountain and white water had benefited her immensely, perhaps even more than the harvest from the Dao Net.

However, compared to the Boundless Wall's changes, hers were like a drop in the ocean.

Initially, the Boundless Wall could not utter a single word after being suppressed.

But after five hundred years, it could manage a few faint grunts.

After a thousand years, it could occasionally utter a complete sentence or two.

"Don't worry, even though there are no True Immortals in the Star Sea, there are still other Star Seas. After I break free, I'll take you on a rampage!"

Throughout the thousand years, Bai Shuyue had heard this promise from the Boundless Wall no less than a hundred times.

At this moment, she asked helplessly: "Last time I asked you when you would be free, you said soon. But after so much time has passed, why do I see no change in you?"

Her gaze could vaguely penetrate the black mountain and white water, seeing the Boundless Wall suppressed within.

Compared to a thousand years ago, the change was indeed immense.

The flowing water, like a carving knife, incessantly sculpted day and night, creating a human embryo within.

But after so many years, only a rough outline had been formed.

Not to mention facial features, even limbs had yet to take shape.

Facing Bai Shuyue's questioning, the Boundless Wall finally managed to utter another sentence after a long while: "Only a thousand years have passed. It's already astonishing that I've achieved this much change!"

"Do you know how long Cheng Dao used to transform from a stone into a human? Tens of thousands of years! Compared to that, I am already a genius among geniuses!"

Ignoring the Boundless Wall's defense, Bai Shuyue stomped lightly on the black mountain.

The flow speed of the white water seemed to increase slightly as a result.

"Ahhhhh..."

"I can't take it anymore, I can't take it anymore!"

Ignoring the Boundless Wall's wails, Bai Shuyue continued to accelerate the circulation of the black mountain and white water.

After a thousand years of contemplation here, she might not have fully grasped the true essence of Mountains and Seas, but she could at least manipulate it to this extent.

Only when the Boundless Wall completely fell silent, and passively accepted its modification, did Bai Shuyue sigh.

Sitting for a thousand years, this was the only solace she could find.

To be honest, after being imprisoned in the Dao Net for a thousand years, she was getting restless.

After all, even the combined time of her thirty reincarnations did not amount to this period of solitary cultivation.

Moreover, during her reincarnations, she could still witness various sceneries, people, and events.

But within this Dao Net, there was only endless darkness. And the faintly glowing blue Dao strings seemed eternal and unchanging.

The myriad beings within the Star Sea also seemed unrelated to her.

She had no sense of belonging whatsoever.

Most importantly...

She missed her nephew.

"Little Fan, I'm afraid you've long since turned to dust."

Even after a thousand years, Li Fan's appearance had not faded. Instead, it had become more enduring with time, appearing in Bai Shuyue's mind from time to time.

"If it weren't for the fact that I still wanted to see what the Boundless Wall would look like after transforming into a human, I would have ended this lifetime's reincarnation long ago." Bai Shuyue thought helplessly.

However, the matter had only just begun, and abandoning it halfway was not her style.

"Besides, I still need to find a way to break through."

"Could it be that we really have to advance towards the Guangwu Star Sea?"

"But with Dao Annihilation blocking the way, what should we do?"

Chapter 1650: The Annihilation of the Dao Ends Everything

The Annihilation of the Dao Ultimately Consumes Everything

However, Bai Shuyue did not need to make a choice.

Not long after, an event occurred that stirred up the tranquility of the Shuoxing Sea, which had remained peaceful for a thousand years.

Initially, Bai Shuyue felt the entire Shuoxing Sea shaking violently, as if it were constantly vibrating.

The Dao Net trembled, and the star river boiled.

If not for the Shuoxing Sea’s Dao Net having been significantly reinforced over the past millennium, such a level of vibration would undoubtedly have been a terrifying calamity. It might not have collapsed immediately, but the Dao Net would have been torn apart, and a third of its inhabitants would have perished instantly.

“The direction of this vibration…”

“Guangwu Star Sea? What on earth has happened?”

Bai Shuyue’s gaze shifted across the Shuoxing Sea. Standing on the Dao Net, she gazed into the distant void of darkness. A strong sense of unease suddenly welled up in her heart.

This feeling was exactly the same as when she was engulfed by the magnificent Dao Annihilation in her previous life!

“Not good, the Dao Annihilation tide is coming!” Bai Shuyue instantly understood.

She immediately used her divine sense to contact the various organizations of the Shuoxing Sea Management Association, instructing them to be vigilant.

In fact, without Bai Shuyue’s reminder, the Dao Net had already become busy.

One group of a thousand people collectively used the Great Dao Manifestation Technique to share the pressure on the Dao Net, connecting themselves to it.

Four Nameless True Immortals were stationed at the four corners of the Dao Net, complementing the four pillars that suppressed the core of the Dao Net, further reinforcing its stability.

Tens of thousands of flags of various colors rose into the sky, flying to every corner of the Shuoxing Sea. The angles and speeds at which the flags fluttered varied dramatically, precisely the artifact developed by the Shuoxing Sea over the past thousand years to monitor the arrival of Dao Annihilation.

Dao Annihilation was imperceptible and invisible, but its destruction to the real world could be observed. This artifact was based on this principle.

At this moment, all the flags were rustling, and many even crumbled under the Daoic pressure, disintegrating on the spot. This indicated the intensity of the approaching Dao Annihilation tide.

“Activate the Myriad Immortals Formation!”

As the core controller of the Dao Net, Bai Shuyue decisively issued the command.

In just a few breaths, it was as if tens of thousands of stars were rising from various locations in the Shuoxing Sea.

Upon closer inspection, although the true forms of these stars were mortal beings, the aura emanating from them was akin to that of True Immortals!

Myriad Immortals stood in formation, ascending above the Dao Net.

They formed numerous small pillars.

As if they had practiced countless times, in an instant, the Star Sea in the Shuoxing Sea, which had been somewhat shaky under the impact of the Dao Annihilation tide, finally began to stabilize slowly under the concerted efforts of multiple parties.

However, Bai Shuyue knew that it was far from time to relax.

The truly terrifying tide had yet to arrive; what was reaching them now was merely the aftermath!

“All units maintain your positions. No one moves without my command!”

The so-called Myriad Immortals Formation was an attempt by Bai Shuyue during her thousand years of Dao comprehension, a sudden inspiration.

She had observed the principles of the black mountain and white water left by Cheng Dao, and had vaguely understood the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas.

The lofty momentum of the mountains, the infinitude of the seas.

Possessing both, one could become a True Immortal.

During her thousand years of Dao comprehension and cultivation, although Bai Shuyue had not truly stepped across that threshold, she was infinitely close, just one step away.

If Bai Shuyue wished, or rather, if she could break free from the suppression at the core of the Dao Net and touch the divine power of Mountains and Seas, directly ascending to the realm of True Immortality would not be difficult for her.

Of course, without the protection of Saints, it was hard to say how long one could survive after becoming an Immortal.

Although Bai Shuyue had no protection from Saints, she could protect others herself.

She publicly shared her insights into Mountains and Seas from these years.

All cultivators within the Shuoxing Sea were welcome to observe and learn.

In this world, there would never be a lack of geniuses, especially when the definition of genius included the opportunity to cultivate into a True Immortal. In just over three years since Bai Shuyue publicized her insights into Mountains and Seas,

In the Shuoxing Sea, there were already over ten thousand individuals who had achieved minor success.

Minor success, in simple terms, meant being able to touch the boundaries of the power of Mountains and Seas solely through one’s own strength. However, due to the lack of protection and guidance, they had always been unable to convert the power of Mountains and Seas into their own use and did not possess the authority of True Immortals.

They could perhaps be called Half-Immortals.

However, with the enhancement of the Dao Net, especially the black mountain and white water left by Cheng Dao, these over ten thousand Half-Immortals could temporarily elevate themselves to the realm of pseudo-True Immortals.

If ordinary True Immortals could easily wield infinite power on their own, then these pseudo-Immortals often needed to work in groups of ten, assisting each other, to barely manipulate infinite power.

But after all, they had truly touched upon the word "Immortal"!

With the Myriad Immortals Formation activated, it was as if over a thousand True Immortals were present, providing their support.

The Shuoxing Sea’s Dao Net had also reached its most robust state ever.

But…

When the terrifying Dao Annihilation tide truly arrived from the darkness beyond,

The seemingly indestructible Dao Net was instantly like a thin piece of white paper, rustling and falling apart in the wind!

Buzzing!

Bai Shuyue personally witnessed more than half of the Dao strings vanishing amidst the fierce onslaught of Dao Annihilation.

And the remaining Dao strings were mostly bent to their limit, seemingly on the verge of complete collapse at any moment, disappearing into the Dao Annihilation.

With a single sweep of her divine sense, Bai Shuyue estimated the number of casualties among the Shuoxing Sea’s inhabitants.

Nearly ninety percent of the beings were annihilated.

Such a tragic situation made the remaining inhabitants of the Shuoxing Sea almost lose the will to resist.

Fear occupied their minds, and their brains went blank.

But Bai Shuyue did not panic; she continued to issue commands with extreme calmness.

“Shrink the Dao Net, cut off the tail to save the body.”

“Within a hundred breaths, those who have not reached the central area will be abandoned.”

A cold command was issued, meaning that countless more lives had lost their hope of survival.

But when everyone was almost at a loss, Bai Shuyue’s calm demeanor, as if nothing had happened, immediately gave the Shuoxing Sea’s inhabitants a backbone once again.

Upon regaining their senses, they quickly started acting again.

The shrinking of the Dao Net was something they had anticipated over the millennia. It was just that it had always been theoretically implemented and never truly practiced. In past simulations, facing the fate of being abandoned, the cultivators often faced it with laughter, but now, in the face of true abandonment, they cursed in despair.

But no matter what, they were destined not to influence the Dao Net’s act of cutting off the tail to save the body.

A hundred breaths passed, and the Dao Net, which had originally covered almost the entire Shuoxing Sea, was reduced to one percent of its size.

The number of surviving beings within it was also reduced to one in a thousand.

But the ability to resist the Dao Annihilation tide increased instead of decreased!

The True Immortals and Nameless True Immortals supported by the Dao Net were mostly unharmed.

And the core strength of the Immortal Hunters was also largely preserved.

The overall strength was not significantly diminished, but the area that needed protection had shrunk a hundredfold.

The Dao Net’s ability to resist Dao Annihilation naturally increased rapidly.

However, it could only protect this small area.

And even that was temporary.

Bai Shuyue personally witnessed the Shuoxing Sea, devoid of the Dao Net’s protection, disappearing into the Dao Annihilation.

But her homeland, the Uttermost Darkness Star Sea, unexpectedly survived.

It was as if there was a similar force within it, similar to the Dao Net, supporting its resistance against the Dao Annihilation.

Bai Shuyue gazed into the distance, her expression solemn: “It seems there are still secrets hidden there.”

The Dao Annihilation surged, sweeping away everything.

The remaining Dao Net could only drift with the currents, and soon, the Uttermost Darkness Star Sea could no longer be observed.

In the silent space, it was as if countless cracks had been torn open.

Some were pitch black, while others allowed a glimpse of continuous mountain and sea scenery!

The mountains and seas were magnificent and majestic, but they were also accompanied by fatal dangers.

“The world has been completely swallowed by Dao Annihilation, torn into pieces.”

“We are completely exposed to the Mountains and Seas.”

Bai Shuyue sighed.

“The destruction of this lifetime was caused by the Guangwu Star Sea, and then spread, even leading to the destruction of the entire possibility.”

Although she did not know what had happened in the Guangwu Star Sea, Bai Shuyue vaguely suspected that it had something to do with the celestial coffin that they had been trying to contact.

“Although I refused them and sealed off the Star Sea, I still could not prevent the final doom.”

Bai Shuyue slowly began to understand the meaning of Cheng Dao’s words, “irrelevant to the final outcome.”

The encroachment of Dao Annihilation around the Dao Net seemed to be slowly subsiding.

But Bai Shuyue knew that soon, Dao Annihilation would launch wave after wave of attacks, seemingly endless.

And the Dao Net would likely ultimately be unable to escape being swallowed.

“Unless we can successfully find another habitat before our strength is exhausted,” Xuanyuan Fusheng said with a bitter smile.

Of the Xuanyuan family, only a few core members survived this calamity.

What hurt Xuanyuan Fusheng even more was that the thousand-person Great Dao Manifestation team he led had also suffered heavy losses in this battle.

The Great Dao Manifestation team used their physical bodies to shoulder the pressure of the Dao Net. At the time of the disaster, they were the first to be impacted.

Out of a thousand people, only nine were fortunate enough to survive.

And these individuals were all personally taught by Xuanyuan Fusheng.

They were both his disciples and his sons.

Seeing his once lively and jovial disciples reduced to mere handfuls, Xuanyuan Fusheng was almost heartbroken.

Bai Shuyue watched his tragic state and remained silent for a long time.

Looking at the Myriad Immortals Formation, which had also lost more than half of its members, she said slowly, “We can hold on for a while, that’s all.”

“Perhaps a miracle will happen?”

However, a miracle ultimately did not happen.

Surviving in the Dao Annihilation seemed to have exhausted their good fortune.

Next, the beings within the Dao Net entered a period of lonely and desperate wandering, and the end finally arrived.

And before the end arrived, the Dao Net organization had already collapsed.

In despair, they went mad, turned on each other…

Even Bai Shuyue could no longer control the chaotic situation.

Bai Shuyue had also attempted a final struggle, which was to seek help from Cheng Dao.

But until the black mountain and white water also disappeared into the Dao Annihilation, Cheng Dao did not respond.

“The Mountains and Seas are vast, and the Dao Annihilation is profound.”

“There is no hope left.”

Silently, after another thirty-six years, the remnants of the Shuoxing Sea’s Dao Net finally shattered.

Only Bai Shuyue and the Boundless Wall, under the protection of the Eternal Straw Cloak, barely survived.

“Why am I so unlucky? I haven’t even transformed yet, and I’ve encountered the Dao Annihilation tribulation again?”

“My fortune!” The Boundless Wall cried with tears.

“Are you still thinking about your opportunities? Your life is at stake right now,” Bai Shuyue said speechlessly.

Without the protection of the Dao Net, directly exposed to Dao Annihilation and the Mountains and Seas.

Bai Shuyue felt an inexplicable darkness, encroaching from all directions.

Her soul, her thoughts, seemed to be frozen by this biting darkness.

She could barely breathe or think, relying only on banter with the Boundless Wall to barely maintain her focus.

“I refuse to accept this! If I could transform, I would surely be able to roam within Dao Annihilation…”

The Boundless Wall’s voice gradually faded.

And Bai Shuyue’s consciousness became increasingly blurry.

At the critical moment of her life, Bai Shuyue seemed to see a celestial coffin floating in the distance.

Her heart stirred, and she struggled to approach it.

But just as she was about to get close to the celestial coffin, the Eternal Straw Cloak shattered inch by inch.

Bai Shuyue perished in the Dao Annihilation.

…

A figure inexplicably appeared near Bai Shuyue’s place of death.

The surrounding Dao Annihilation ravaged, but it could not harm him in the slightest.

It was Li Fan!
