With a wave of his hand, he summoned the celestial coffin from afar and opened it.

To his surprise, it was empty.

“It’s not the same one that carried Emperor Shuosuo.”

“It’s another intact celestial coffin…”

After some observation, Li Fan concluded.

“Neither know its origin nor its destination.”

“But the material of this celestial coffin is truly extraordinary. If my aunt had persisted a little longer and hidden inside…”

“She should have been able to extend her lifespan considerably.”

“Unfortunately, it was just a bit short. Tsk tsk…”

“However, without a clear target, purely drifting with the currents. The probability of reaching a safe area is too low. Not to mention reaching the other shore.”

“Garbage time, let’s skip it.”

Li Fan closed the celestial coffin again and re-buried it in the Dao Annihilation.

“My aunt in this lifetime could have touched the threshold of transcendence. She is getting closer to my goal. I just don’t know how she will break through in the end?”

Li Fan smiled, his gaze deep.

He stood still, contemplating something.

After a long while, he mentally uttered.

“True Reversion!”

Another lifetime in the ‘Create Saint Plan’.

Upon waking up, Bai Shuyue looked around in confusion. It took her a long time to realize that she had been reborn.

The layout of the room was both unfamiliar and familiar.

A sudden impulse surged in her heart, and she hurried to Li Fan’s room.

She hugged Li Fan, who looked bewildered, into her arms.

Then, she quietly wept.

“Auntie, what’s wrong?” Li Fan asked cautiously.

Bai Shuyue just wept silently, not speaking.

After a long while, when her tears had dried, she finally let go.

She smiled with difficulty: “It’s nothing, Auntie is just tired.”

Li Fan asked with concern: “Are you worried that the village chief will annex our family’s property? Don’t worry, even if I have to give my life, I won’t let him succeed!”

Seeing Li Fan’s determined look, Bai Shuyue finally smiled happily.

Then she paused slightly.

She had been reincarnating for so long.

What had been impossible to solve with all her efforts before, now seemed like a joke.

But…

What was the meaning of her reincarnation?

What was she reincarnating for, time and time again?

When would the endpoint arrive?

Bai Shuyue had almost forgotten her original goal.

Chapter 1651: Aunt and Nephew Play a Different Tune

"That's right, before long, Fan'er will contract some strange illness and die young. It was precisely to save him that I embarked on this path of cultivation."

"And my later desperate cultivation and deduction of new methods were also largely for the sake of prolonging his life, since he couldn't cultivate."

In an instant, Bai Shuyue's mind rapidly swept through the scenes she had experienced in her reincarnations, and a myriad of emotions surged in her heart.

"Time flies, yet things remain the same..."

She stared at her nephew, who looked somewhat bewildered, and her mind suddenly recalled another young man she had met in her reincarnations, named Ou Shangtian.

She and the Boundless Wall had unintentionally caused the death of Ou Shangtian's father, Ou Daozi. This young man, in revenge for his father, had not even spared his own life.

"Kill me or torture me as you please! Do you think I'm afraid of you two wicked thieves?" Ou Shangtian's roar seemed to echo in her ears again.

Bai Shuyue then had a sudden thought: "If I were to be harmed, what lengths would Fan'er go to for me?"

The thought, once ignited, spread like wildfire, rapidly growing and consuming her heart, making it impossible to suppress.

Bai Shuyue was somewhat eager to know the answer.

But at the same time, she felt a vague sense of fear.

She was afraid that if Fan'er's performance disappointed her, what would she do in the future?

Bai Shuyue firmly believed that Li Fan was a good child.

But...

She subconsciously closed her eyes, unwilling to think about that terrible outcome.

However, the thought did not disappear with this momentary evasion but continued to entangle Bai Shuyue like a inner demon.

"Aunt, are you feeling unwell? Why don't you go back to your room and rest first? I'll cook for you."

Seeing Bai Shuyue's unusual behavior, Li Fan said with great concern.

Bai Shuyue nodded and walked into the room with rather heavy steps.

After the door was closed, Bai Shuyue, deeply conflicted, pondered for a long time before finally making up her mind.

"It seems Aunt wants to play a role-playing game with me. In that case, I'll cooperate with her well."

"Consider it an appetizer before becoming a Saint." On the surface, her actions, demeanor, and expressions perfectly matched that of an honest nephew, but Li Fan chuckled inwardly.

That evening, the aunt and nephew ate a meal, each harboring their own thoughts.

The next morning, while Li Fan was still asleep, a group of fierce-looking constables burst in and rudely dragged him out of bed.

"Who are you?" Li Fan exclaimed, shocked and angry.

"Behave yourself! Scholar Li, you've been found out!" The leading constable sneered, forcibly placing a wooden yoke on Li Fan.

"This is outrageous! I spend all day at home reading and writing, how could I have committed any crime? You must have the wrong person?" Li Fan shouted indignantly, trying to prove his innocence. He instinctively wanted to struggle.

However, as a mere scholar, he was extremely weak. After taking a couple of blows, he hunched over and coughed violently, finally complying.

"Wrong person? Scholar Li, you think too little of us, don't you? Reading and writing... Hmph, the most hateful people are scholars like you! On the surface, you pretend to be ignorant of worldly affairs, but in reality, you are plotting unspeakable schemes all day long."

"Boss, we found it!"

As he was speaking, a constable emerged from Li Fan's study, holding a stack of papers.

"Is this your handwriting?"

The constable leader waved the papers in front of Li Fan.

Li Fan naturally recognized his own handwriting and nodded subconsciously. But upon seeing the content on the first page of the stack, cold sweat broke out on his forehead.

"No! I didn't write this! Someone is framing me!"

Before he could finish speaking, a messy wad of cloth was stuffed into his mouth, silencing him.

The constable leader narrowed his eyes and read the content of the papers in a cold voice.

"Cold stars illuminate the misty path, turbulent waves crash, concealing a jade flute. Ten years of wind and frost have honed the sword's edge, a lifetime of loyalty entrusted to fishermen and woodcutters. The Cloud Terrace sees no unicorn's horn, yet the wild grass breeds a proud steed. When thunder and wind arise from the ground, we shall rewrite history and speak of former dynasties!"

"Hehehe, well said, 'rewrite history and speak of former dynasties.' You dare to plot a rebellion that warrants the extermination of your clan. Take him away!"

"Mmmph..."

Li Fan was quickly apprehended.

Not only himself, but even his aunt was implicated.

The constables showed no regard for her being a woman, their actions equally rough.

"Mmmph mmmph mmmph..."

In such a scene, Li Fan and his aunt met again. Li Fan seemed to have a thousand words to say, but could only make muffled sounds.

Bai Shuyue seemed to be weeping from fear, trembling all over.

Soon, the two were separated and imprisoned.

The verdict was also quickly delivered: intentional rebellion, unforgivable guilt.

Sentenced to death row, to be executed after the autumn.

Upon hearing the verdict, Li Fan immediately collapsed. He roared like a madman, proclaiming his innocence.

After receiving a few blows, he could no longer make any sound.

He was dragged into death row.

Completely losing hope of survival, Li Fan's expression was dejected, and he sat limply on the ground, waiting to die.

"I don't think you seem like a heinous criminal. Why are you locked up here?"

Half a month later, one night, a faint voice came from the adjacent cell.

Li Fan was startled by the sound and looked towards the direction of the voice. He saw a skeleton-like being, only skin and bones.

He was immediately frightened and retreated backward repeatedly.

"So timid, it seems you were indeed wronged," the voice chuckled.

Perhaps it was this sentence that resonated with Li Fan's inner feelings. After a long while, Li Fan, mustering his courage, approached the other person again. He honestly recounted his suffering of injustice.

"I swear to heaven, I never wrote this seditious poem!" Li Fan gritted his teeth and said.

"Have you offended anyone in your daily life?"

Li Fan looked bewildered: "I stay at home all day, never going out, how could I have offended anyone..."

Suddenly, Li Fan seemed to recall his aunt's strange behavior before, and trembled violently: "Could it be..."

So he quickly told about the village chief's coveting of his family's land.

"..."

"A mere village chief possesses such means?" The voice on the other side was skeptical.

"It must be him! I heard that the village chief's son is also quite talented in literature. This seditious poem must have been written by him!" Li Fan said fiercely.

The other side fell into an eerie silence.

In the darkness, only Li Fan's curses could be heard continuously.

A few days later, for no apparent reason, Li Fan suddenly burst into tears.

"A true man faces death with dignity. Crying and sobbing, what sort of image is that!" the voice next door reprimanded in a low voice.

"These past few days, I've thought it through. My own life is cheap, and being beheaded is nothing. It's just a pity about my aunt, who was implicated by me. At her age, she still has to suffer such hardship."

"I lost my parents when I was young. It was my aunt who raised me tirelessly. Although we are not related by blood, I have already regarded her as my mother..." Li Fan wailed in despair, unable to stop.

Only when he completely lost his strength did he finally stop.

One night, a quiet whispering voice came from the adjacent cell again: "Filial piety is the first of all virtues. To have such feelings for your aunt, you are not entirely without merit."

Li Fan lay limp on the ground, seeming not to hear.

Then, he suddenly sat up in horror.

Because in the darkness, a viscous, damp snake seemed to coil around him.

"What is this thing..."

"Hush, it's me!"

Li Fan focused his gaze and saw that the long python coiled around his leg actually had a human head!

"Am I a ghost? Have I been beheaded?"

Li Fan, startled, quickly touched his neck, thinking he had already been beheaded and was seeing a ghost.

The python's head was almost angered to laugh. It exerted a slight force, constricting Li Fan and stopping his suspicious movements.

"This is the Myriad Transformations of the Dragon technique! What ghost or god are you talking about!"

"Senior, who exactly are you?" After a long time, Li Fan slowly accepted this rather terrifying existence and asked cautiously.

"You don't need to know my name. You just need to know that I can save you from this dire situation!"

"Is that true?" Li Fan's voice suddenly became louder, but he quickly realized and lowered his voice.

"No, if you had that ability, you would have escaped long ago. How would you still be trapped here?"

"Once I escape, I will probably be irrevocably branded a rebel, and I will never be able to clear my name in this lifetime..."

"If you die, you won't be able to clear your name either. Moreover, your aunt is old, and she probably won't last many days in this prison. She might pass away before being beheaded," the other party taunted.

Li Fan's expression shifted: "Alright, I'll learn!"

Seven days later: "Why are you so useless? You still can't learn such a simple technique!"

Thirty days later: "You've finally got the basics. It's only because I've passed on all my internal energy to you. Alas, I didn't expect to find such a useless disciple."

One hundred and three days later, with only seven days left until his execution.

Li Fan could finally fully transform into a swimming dragon and escape from death row.

Before leaving, he paid a deep respectful gaze to his master, who had already turned into a skeleton, whose name he didn't even know.

Then, he quietly slipped away.

The first thing Li Fan did after escaping was to search for his aunt's whereabouts.

However, the news he received struck him like lightning.

It turned out that just three days ago, his aunt had died from the harsh environment in the prison, unable to bear it any longer.

"Impossible! Impossible!"

Li Fan went mad, and it wasn't until he saw his aunt's corpse with his own eyes that he finally believed and was completely stunned.

"Ahhhhhh!"

Tears streamed down his face, filled with regret: "If only I had learned faster, wouldn't I have been able to save my aunt?"

"Why am I so foolish? I truly deserve to die!"

Li Fan was so grief-stricken that he could barely breathe, only wailing while holding his aunt's corpse until his tears ran dry and his throat was hoarse.

Only then did he slowly recover.

With a heart full of grief and despair, Li Fan buried his aunt's body.

Then, a blazing flame of revenge ignited in his eyes.

"Aunt, if you can see this in the afterlife, watch as I make them all pay for your life!"

In the darkness, a menacing coiled dragon moved rapidly across the land.

With supreme divine skill, Li Fan captured the county magistrate and the entire village chief's family without much effort.

After intense interrogation, it was indeed the village chief who coveted his family's land and maliciously framed him. He also bribed the county magistrate to quickly confirm the false charges.

"Little Fan, spare me, Little Fan, spare me! Uncle knows he was wrong..."

The village chief wept and begged for mercy, continuously.

Because of the unfathomable power Li Fan displayed, he was already scared out of his wits.

Li Fan glared with rage, his eyes showing no mercy, still burning with boundless anger: "It's easy to spare you..."

"Give me back my aunt's life!"

With a palm strike, the village chief's head was crushed into pieces.

Blood and gore splattered. This was Li Fan's first time killing, and his anger was not appeased as he slaughtered all the sinners present.

The village chief was one thing, but the county magistrate was an official of the court.

In his rage, Li Fan killing the county magistrate made him no different from a rebel.

"Since that's the case, let's oppose the heavens!"

With his emotions surging, Li Fan used the blood splattered all over the ground to write his seditious poem on the wall.

"Today, as thunder and wind arise from the ground, we shall rewrite history and speak of former dynasties!"

Then he inscribed: "The killer is Li Fan!"

Without looking back, he flicked his sleeves and left.

In the Great Xuan Dynasty, it was common for the common people to be oppressed by corrupt officials.

But the empire had enjoyed peace for too long, and unless they were driven to desperation, the common people would not rebel.

Li Fan led his followers to raise the banner of rebellion, but the response was sparse.

The government quickly sent troops to suppress them, but Li Fan, relying on his Myriad Transformations of the Dragon technique, repeatedly repelled the government soldiers.

Then he occupied a mountain stronghold, erected a banner of "Acting on Heaven's Behalf," recruited talents, accumulated grain, and awaited the opportune moment.

Years later, during a severe drought and locust plague in Jiangnan.

Famine spread everywhere, and the people had no means to live.

Li Fan seized the opportunity, igniting the flames of rebellion.

This time, responses came from all over the Great Xuan.

Ten years later, Li Fan finally led his troops to attack Xuanjing.

He overthrew the old dynasty, donned the imperial yellow robe, and ascended the throne.

"This Emperor wishes to posthumously bestow the title of Empress Dowager upon my aunt. What do you all think, my ministers?"

One day, in the imperial court, Li Fan suddenly asked this question.

The officials looked at each other.

However, there were those who knew Li Fan's story, so one of them immediately spoke, "Your Majesty's suggestion is most wise!"

"As everyone knows, His Majesty was raised entirely by his aunt in his early years."

"Her upbringing in childhood was as nurturing as a biological mother..."

After a lengthy explanation, most of the officials were stunned.

Seeing Li Fan's very satisfied expression, everyone else regretted not speaking up sooner.

Ultimately, Li Fan posthumously honored Bai Shuyue as the "Empress Dowager Zhaohui Cishang," and reported to the ancestral temple with the ceremony of the highest state funeral. He bestowed upon her a golden edict and jade seal, and all officials performed the four bows of obeisance.

Li Fan personally penned the "Ode to the Virtuous Mother," built an altar in the suburbs of Xuanjing, and burned a memorial to the heavens.

He then ordered the construction of a grand mausoleum and the relocation of Bai Shuyue's remains.

Li Fan reigned for more than seventy years, and only after reaching the age of one hundred did he pass away.

He governed with non-interference and imposed light taxes, and the people all praised his benevolent rule.

On the day of his death, the entire nation mourned.

Li Fan's imperial tomb was adjacent to Bai Shuyue's tomb.

At this moment, a figure quietly appeared.

Floating in the sky, looking at the two imperial tombs below.

It was Bai Shuyue!

"Fan'er..."

Her expression was complex, and at the same time, as if she had completely resolved something in her heart,

Her gaze gradually became resolute.

Chapter 1652: Luring with the Intent of Transcendence

"He Fan is a good child."

At this point, Bai Shuyue had no more doubts in her heart.

Since this point had been verified, she should do her best to support him, both in reason and in emotion.

"Rather than being bound by each lifetime, perhaps I can first find the optimal solution."

"Either, I walk far enough. Reach the Nameless, Transcendent realm, or even go further! With my care, even if Fan'er is in a mortal body, he will not need to worry about the tribulation of Dao Annihilation."

"Alternatively, I can find a cultivation path suitable for him. But..."

Thinking of this, Bai Shuyue couldn't help but shake her head slightly.

"Fan'er's cultivation talent is truly too poor. Even with my secret help, even the simplest technique like the Myriad Transformations of the Dragon Technique is so difficult for him to learn. Relying on him alone, to achieve success in cultivation..."

In this lifetime, although Li Fan had already passed away.

To complete the path of transcendence that she had not achieved last time.

What followed was a mechanical repetition of operations.

Cultivate, restore a certain realm; find the Boundless Wall, and conspire to scheme for the Great Dao of Wuji.

Before preparing to leave the Xuanhuang Realm and head to the Shuoxing Sea, Bai Shuyue did not forget to set up layers of restrictions again, completely sealing off the Great Xuan Minor World.

To prevent cultivators from accidentally entering again and disturbing the peace of Li Fan's soul.

"Since you value it so much, why not just take this small world with you?"

She recalled the scene from her previous life when the tribulation of Dao Annihilation descended and Shuoxing and Guangwu were swallowed by Dao Annihilation, yet the Uttermost Darkness Star Sea still existed.

The Boundless Wall could not spy on all the secrets within the Lan Ke Dojo, and Bai Shuyue had no intention of delving deeper.

After bowing from a distance to the several illusory figures standing in the dojo.

The story continues.

Taking over from Cheng Dao, guarding the core of the Dao Net.

Hunting Immortals and comprehending the Dao, promoting the growth of Shuoxing Sea civilization.

With the experience of the previous lifetime of a thousand years, Bai Shuyue displayed astonishing control over the Dao Net.

Avoiding many unnecessary detours.

In just a hundred years, she cleared all the remaining True Immortals in the Shuoxing Sea.

After another fifty years, the various departments of the Immortal Hunters, after rapid development, had also basically recovered to their peak levels of the previous lifetime.

At this opportune moment, Guangwu Star Sea sent scouts to make contact again.

The Guangwu Star Sea side had heard about the drastic changes in the Shuoxing Sea in the past century. They held an attitude of curiosity and caution towards Bai Shuyue, this mysterious mortal of unknown origin.

"I am here on behalf of myself to seek cooperation."

...

Guangwu Star Sea was powerful, and if they joined forces, their chances of winning would be even greater.

Bai Shuyue, however, was one of the few in the group who remained absolutely clear-headed.

Recalling the terrifying Dao Annihilation tribulation she had witnessed at the end of her previous lifetime.

Bai Shuyue's icy voice brought a sobering effect to the Shuoxing Sea group.

This corpse of transcendence has endured Dao Annihilation for tens of thousands of years without deteriorating. The degree of attention Dao Annihilation pays to it has long reached a terrifying level. If it remains in the star sea for a long time, it will inevitably lead to the erosion of Dao Annihilation."

Wan Sheng's expression became somewhat solemn: "Recently, the impact of Dao Annihilation on our probability has gradually increased."

"We suspect that Dao Annihilation may have discovered the connection between us and that corpse of transcendence."

The Shuoxing Sea group looked at each other in dismay.

They could never have imagined that Dao Annihilation would think and even seem to have wisdom like living beings?

"Then, according to this, if we abandon the corpse of transcendence and let it drift into the depths of mountains and seas, the tribulation will naturally be lifted?" Bai Shuyue, among the crowd, was the only one who quickly grasped the key point.

Wan Sheng was speechless and could only nod helplessly.

Bai Shuyue finally understood the specific reason for the demise of the Guangwu Star Sea in her previous lifetime.

But please rest assured, we have already researched a method to make Dao Annihilation ignore us and the corpse of transcendence. It's just..."

Wan Sheng paused, then said in a low voice: "Besides the corpse of transcendence, other Immortal Coffin baits have also been marked as targets by Dao Annihilation. If we have to deal with multiple pressures simultaneously, it will be somewhat strenuous."

"Then just throw away the other Immortal Coffins. You won't be reluctant to part with them, will you?" Chaos said irritably.

Wan Sheng sighed: "This is the fundamental reason why we need your cooperation."

Chapter 1653: Transferring the Dao and Exchanging the Shed Skin

"If we consider fishing in the Great Tribulation of Dao Annihilation as a struggle between strength, then we are the ones holding the fishing rod, and Dao Annihilation is the unknown fierce beast beneath the water. The current situation is that the force coming from underwater is too great, and it is highly possible that we will not be able to pull the rod but will be dragged into the water instead."

Wan Sheng, from the Guangwu Star Sea, said with a solemn expression: "The remnants of transcendence, and even other immortal coffins, are all part of this bait. Ordinary treasures, we naturally do not value them so much. But this remnant of transcendence..."

Wan Sheng sighed deeply: "To be honest with you all, according to our estimations, the number of remnants of transcendence drifting in the mountains and seas should be extremely rare. It is already a stroke of luck for us to salvage one. If we were to return it this time, I am afraid we would never have the chance to encounter a new one."

After his words, the Shuoxing Sea side also fell into silence.

If they were in their position, they probably could not give up so easily. Let alone them, perhaps even the Immortal Emperors of the complete Immortal Realm in the past, if they controlled such treasures, would not let go easily.

"We will not give up until we are forced into a corner. In recent years, we have been actively seeking solutions. And coming here from afar to invite everyone to cooperate is an important part of that."

Bai Shuyue, who had been listening for a long time, finally spoke: "Fellow Daoist, stop beating around the bush and explain in detail."

"Alright, I'll make a long story short. The targets locked onto by Dao Annihilation are the baits we have continuously invested in the mountains and seas over the long years. Immortal coffins and remnants of transcendence are all part of the bait."

"Although we are reluctant to abandon them now, we can destroy some of the bait ourselves. With the loss of the locked targets, the pressure of Dao Annihilation's descent will also be reduced accordingly."

"After calculation, we only need to reduce the number of existing baits to one-third, and we can be safe and sound."

Wan Sheng's words were very clear, and the Shuoxing Sea group had already understood: "Your so-called cooperation is to use the power of the Dao Net to eliminate the baits? Things that can be used as bait and can float in Dao Annihilation are probably not easy to deal with, right?"

"It's not just about borrowing your strength. In fact, the strength of our Guangwu Star Sea is enough to trim the excess bait one by one. More importantly, it's to borrow this treasure land." Wan Sheng pointed to the surrounding, vibrant Shuoxing Sea.

"Although most of the things sealed in the immortal coffins have lost their vitality, even the remnants, their strength is not comparable to ordinary Nameless beings. When fighting, it will inevitably cause damage to the structure of the lower star sea itself. Once or twice, it can still be barely supported. If it happens many times..."

Wan Sheng said helplessly: "Therefore, we need to fight separately. The Shuoxing Sea has the support of the Dao Net, and even if it is damaged, its recovery will be much faster than ordinary star seas, making it the most suitable place for combat."

"And we will never treat you poorly. Not only the remnants of transcendence, but also rare treasures like the Dao Sword and Dao Blade that we have salvaged over the years, we can provide five of them as compensation." After explaining the cooperation matters in detail, Wan Sheng also offered substantial rewards.

Even though the reward was truly tempting, the Shuoxing Sea immortals did not lose their minds and directly agreed.

Bai Shuyue said: "This is a matter of great importance. We need to discuss it carefully before giving an answer."

"We look forward to it!" Wan Sheng nodded and, piloting the wooden boat, drifted away and disappeared from everyone's sight.

"Traversing Dao Annihilation, such skill is truly enviable. If we also mastered such divine abilities, we would not be confined to the corner of Shuoxing." The immortals of the Shuoxing Sea had mixed feelings.

It was definitely a lie for cultivators at the Nameless realm to say they had no longing for transcendence.

Bai Shuyue could see the desire in the hearts of all the immortals.

She calmly reminded them: "In my opinion, what the Guangwu Star Sea says may still have inaccuracies. Of course, we haven't agreed to cooperate yet, so it's normal for them to conceal something. What I worry about is the huge gap in strength between Shuoxing and Guangwu. It was different when Dao Annihilation isolated us, but if they habitually communicate..."

"Opening the door to welcome bandits, inviting a wolf into the house."

Judging from the treasures like Dao Sword and Dao Blade that the Guangwu Star Sea could casually produce, their strength undoubtedly far surpassed that of the Shuoxing Sea.

Realizing this deeply, everyone did not speak in rebuttal.

"Moreover, fighting against immortal coffins and remnants is also extremely dangerous. It is inevitable that everyone present will be injured."

"Conversely, if we refuse to cooperate, although we will lose the opportunity to touch the remnants of transcendence, we will also avoid immense risks. Even if Dao Annihilation is approaching, as long as our Shuoxing Sea joins forces with all parties, we may be able to build a wooden boat to traverse Dao Annihilation." Bai Shuyue thought of the scene in her previous life when the core area of the Dao Net survived the world-ending tribulation, and could not help but say so.

Relying on the experience of her previous life, she was confident that she could increase the overall Dao Net to a level that could resist that degree of Dao Annihilation before the tribulation arrived.

Therefore, in Bai Shuyue's heart, she did not want to get involved in the affairs of the Guangwu Star Sea.

Even with the temptation of the remnants of transcendence.

However, she did not act unilaterally. Instead, after analyzing the pros and cons in detail, she let everyone vote.

In the end, they could not resist the greed in the hearts of the immortals.

The vast majority chose to agree to cooperate with the Guangwu Star Sea to resist Dao Annihilation together.

"Fine, let's see."

Bai Shuyue was indifferent. After all, even if it failed, she could still be reborn.

Once the opinions were unified, they quickly contacted the Guangwu Star Sea again.

The progress of cooperation between the two parties was very rapid.

When the Guangwu Star Sea sent people for the second time, the scale was even larger.

The tool for traversing was no longer a wooden boat.

But the skeletal remains of a monstrous beast!

It was impossible to tell the specific appearance of the beast when it was alive. Its flesh and blood were almost completely eroded. Two-thirds of its body was all white bones.

But the remaining one-third of its flesh and blood was enough to serve as a temporary refuge from Dao Annihilation.

After the beast's remains arrived, a hundred True Immortals and four Nameless beings emerged one after another.

Such a large lineup made the Shuoxing Sea side instantly feel immense pressure, and their spirits became instantly tense.

If not for the other party's casual demeanor and lack of malice, they would almost have thought that the Guangwu Star Sea had come to attack them directly.

"One should guard against others." Bai Shuyue reminded them.

The Myriad Immortals Formation had already been activated, and the Dao Net was operating at maximum power, in a state of highest readiness.

The first formal negotiation between the Shuoxing Sea and the Guangwu Star Sea began.

Although they had decided to cooperate, in the current situation, they could not agree so easily. At the very least, the matter of compensation needed to be discussed in detail.

Having witnessed the generosity of the Guangwu Star Sea, the Shuoxing Sea group decisively chose to increase their demands.

They thought their appetite was already big enough, but when Bai Shuyue spoke, everyone couldn't help but be shocked.

"These are all minor details. I think whether it's one more or one less immortal treasure, it doesn't really matter to you. As long as you can survive this tribulation, you will be able to continuously fish for treasures from Dao Annihilation."

"We, the Shuoxing Sea, need the method of fishing in Dao Annihilation!"

As soon as these words were spoken, the expression of Yuan Shu, the leader of the Guangwu Star Sea delegation, changed slightly.

Just as he was about to refuse, Bai Shuyue directly showed him the powerful imagery of the Dao Net.

She laid her cards on the table: "Our cooperation this time involves taking considerable, unnecessary risks. The Dao Net as a boat, we could have simply watched from the sidelines..."

Yuan Shu carefully examined the Dao Net, a trace of surprise flashing in his eyes. However, he did not back down, saying with a cold smile: "This Dao Annihilation tribulation is different from the past. It may not be weaker than the one that destroyed the Immortal Realm back then. Where does your confidence come from?"

"Even if the power of Dao Annihilation is the same as back then, we can still safely overcome this tribulation." Bai Shuyue said firmly.

The rest of the Shuoxing Sea group was secretly surprised.

When did the Dao Net become so powerful?

"If you don't believe me, just watch."

Saying that, Bai Shuyue clapped her hands.

Outside the Shuoxing Sea, in the dark void, it seemed as if true Dao Annihilation was approaching.

Yuan Shu's expression suddenly changed, and then he realized: "It's not real Dao Annihilation. It's using the power of the Dao Net itself to simulate the pressure that would be borne during the descent of Dao Annihilation..."

As if the scene of Dao Annihilation's descent in the previous life was re-enacted, the center of the Dao Net, thousands of Dao strings twisted and distorted, almost collapsing.

However, with the appearance of the Myriad Immortals Formation and the Great Dao Manifestation team, the Dao Net finally bore this terrifying pressure safely.

Bai Shuyue did not hold back in the simulation, weakening the pressure that the Dao Net needed to bear.

The reason the Dao Net could withstand it this time was largely due to the Dao Sword and Dao Blade that the Guangwu Star Sea had given them before.

Just this one treasure could be equivalent to the support of two or three Nameless beings.

With the method of the 'Illusory Form Dao Bearing Technique' from the Shou Qiu inheritance, the Shuoxing Sea's level of resisting Dao Annihilation was far superior to that of the Guangwu Star Sea.

Although the Guangwu Star Sea carried many rare treasures, they could at most exert the power of the treasures themselves.

They were unable to use these treasures to resist the calamity of Dao Annihilation.

"How about it?" Bai Shuyue said calmly, ending the "performance."

Yuan Shu, being a Nameless True Immortal, had excellent eyesight and could see the differences between the Shuoxing Sea and their own side.

"It's not impossible for you to have the method of fishing in Dao Annihilation."

He pretended to ponder for a moment, then revealed his true intentions: "But it requires the technique of 'Dao Bearing in Illusory Form' as an exchange!"

Bai Shuyue's expression slowly turned cold.

"Absolutely not!"

"No need to mention it further, show them out!"

Unexpectedly, with no preamble, she directly kicked the Guangwu Star Sea group out.

This sudden change caught both sides off guard.

Chaos, who was in a hurry, spoke to persuade her.

The other immortals also looked regretful, and one after another, they subtly tried to persuade her to see if there was any room for maneuver.

Bai Shuyue merely smiled slightly: "Who said I was truly refusing them? I just want to ask for more benefits. Don't worry, they will definitely come back."

Bai Shuyue's acting skills even deceived her own people.

The crowd breathed a sigh of relief, and could not help but sigh inwardly, "The hearts of women are truly unfathomable."

On the other side, as Bai Shuyue had predicted, the Guangwu Star Sea had not given up on cooperation.

In fact, their contacts became even more frequent.

Their bottom line also kept lowering.

The 'Illusory Form Dao Bearing Technique' held too much significance for the Guangwu Star Sea.

If they could master this divine technique...

With their accumulated resources over the years, they could then build a high dam and completely ignore the threat of Dao Annihilation.

In fact, if Bai Shuyue had not demonstrated the Dao Net's pressure-bearing capacity in the previous simulation, and if she hadn't worried that if the two sides fought to the death, the Shuoxing Sea might be destroyed and the 'Illusory Form Dao Bearing Technique' lost forever. The Guangwu Star Sea would have already sent out their elites to attack.

But now, although the price to pay was greater, it was still acceptable.

Finally, after several negotiations between the two sides.

The Guangwu Star Sea and the Shuoxing Sea finally reached a cooperation agreement.

The number of fishing immortal treasures equivalent to Dao Sword and Dao Blade that the Guangwu Star Sea had to pay, increased from five to thirteen, not including the opportunity to observe the remnants of transcendence after the mission was completed.

The Shuoxing Sea, on the other hand, needed to help eliminate the fishing immortal baits and provide the area of the Dao Net as the battlefield.

And the 'Illusory Form Dao Bearing Technique'.

The outcome was satisfactory for both parties.

"There is no time to delay. We have observed that the pressure of Dao Annihilation's waves has been increasing recently."

"The first immortal bait will be sent in three years. Please make preparations. At that time, we will send fifty True Immortals and two Nameless beings to assist in the operation."

Bai Shuyue nodded in agreement.

The Guangwu Star Sea delegation left in a hurry. The various immortal treasures they left behind were carefully scanned by the Dao Net to ensure there were no hidden surveillance methods. Bai Shuyue then placed them all within the Dao Net using the 'Illusory Form Dao Bearing Technique'.

Under normal circumstances, they could serve as pillars supporting the sky.

They could also be withdrawn and used at any time.

"This technique is truly miraculous."

"Old Man Shou Qiu is indeed an unparalleled genius."

Not only did the Shuoxing Sea immortals marvel, but Bai Shuyue herself, who had completed it, could not help but sigh in admiration.

After more than thirty reincarnations, Bai Shuyue considered her own aptitude to be extremely strong.

But compared to Old Man Shou Qiu, she was eclipsed.

Bai Shuyue pondered inwardly: "The Guangwu Star Sea was willing to pay such a high price, so the preciousness of this technique is self-evident. When Cheng Dao passed it to me, he didn't explicitly say whether it could be passed on externally."

"If I tell the Guangwu Star Sea, I might be punished."

"However, no matter what method I use, I can't contact Cheng Dao anymore. Perhaps I can use this opportunity to lure him out again."

Even though she obtained more than ten fishing immortal treasures, greatly enhancing the strength of the Dao Net, Bai Shuyue did not relax her vigilance. She ordered all departments of the Dao Net to intensify their cultivation.

In addition to preparing for the immortal bait three years later, Bai Shuyue also worried that the Guangwu Star Sea might make a move when the Dao Net was weakened after the great battle.

Therefore, she needed to make more preparations.

"Besides Fan'er, there is no one in this world worth truly trusting." Bai Shuyue secretly warned herself.

"Or, perhaps, including it?"

Bai Shuyue looked again at the Boundless Wall, which was quietly cultivating under the black mountain and white water.

Although the Boundless Wall was a bit slippery, based on their interactions in this reincarnation, it was generally reliable.

"Hungry... Hungry."

"This great master wants to eat that!"

Just as Bai Shuyue was contemplating, the Boundless Wall's voice, weak yet arrogant, echoed faintly from below.

Chapter 1654: The Boundless Green of Mountains and Seas

Following the direction pointed by the Boundless Wall, Bai Shuyue saw it was pointing at one of the Immortal Treasures salvaged from the Vast Light Star Sea.

"This isn't something you can eat," Bai Shuyue said helplessly.

With that, she roughly explained the current situation of the Shuoxing Sea.

"So you're saying the Vast Light Star Sea has many more delicious things like this?"

The Boundless Wall immediately became restless, its suppressive black mountain and white water even showing signs of halting their self-circulation.

The Boundless Wall then continued, "Of course! With my talent, after being suppressed for so long, how could I gain no benefit? Of course, there's still a gap compared to Senior Cheng Dao, who truly transformed into a human." The Boundless Wall spoke ambiguously and shifted the topic back to the Vast Light Star Sea, "Be careful, I always feel like they are up to no good. If you encounter danger and can't win, escape is the best strategy. Everything will be discussed after I finish my cultivation and wake up! By then, no matter what tricks those scoundrels have, I'll suppress them all!"

"Heh heh, didn't expect this. I originally planned to rely on you for support after your transcendence, but now it seems I'll be guiding you."

Bai Shuyue did not get angry upon hearing this, but merely smiled, "Then let's see who transcends first."

"With Senior Cheng Dao's help in my enlightenment, most of the stockpiled knowledge within me is now useless. I'll give you these treasures for self-preservation! I hope you can safely survive this tribulation."

Saying this, the Boundless Wall spat out a collection of items, including the Eternal Straw Cloak, and handed them all to Bai Shuyue.

"Remember, be careful of the Vast Light Star Sea!" the Boundless Wall reiterated.

Then, the black mountain and white water began to flow again, and the Boundless Wall fell silent once more.

"The Vast Light Star Sea..."

Bai Shuyue looked towards the other end of the star sea, her eyes narrowing slightly.

"It seems I need to make more preparations."

Although she didn't know what the Boundless Wall had sensed, Bai Shuyue chose to believe its judgment.

Time flew by, and three years passed in a flash.

On that day, over a hundred True Immortals and two Nameless beings from the Vast Light Star Sea, surrounding a celestial coffin covered in bronze rust, traversed the void.

Leading them was Yuan Shu, who had been responsible for the negotiations before.

After exchanging pleasantries, under everyone's watchful eyes, the coffin was opened, and the Immortals were to be slain!

"Although I don't know what exactly is buried in this bronze celestial coffin. However, among all the immortal baits, the Dao Annihilation ripples it caused in Mountains and Seas are only second to that remnant of transcendence. Everyone, do not be careless!"

The Shuoxing Sea had demanded a steep price during the negotiations.

The Vast Light Star Sea would naturally have to share the increased pressure.

The immortals of the Shuoxing Sea stared intently at the bronze celestial coffin, their expressions grave.

As a faint crack appeared on the celestial coffin, the bronze rust clinging to its surface seemed to come alive, making a rustling sound as it flowed into the coffin.

Mysterious ancient chants from the desolate era echoed from within the celestial coffin.

Upon hearing this, everyone present instinctively felt a sense of sorrow and desolation.

"Be careful!"

A True Immortal from the Vast Light Star Sea, perhaps too engrossed in listening, was unknowingly contaminated by some dark green bronze rust that appeared out of nowhere.

In an instant, he transformed into a bronze statue.

His eyes were hollowed out by the corrosion, revealing a profound darkness within.

It looked extremely terrifying.

More importantly, after being transformed into a bronze statue, this True Immortal also began to chant that mysterious and ancient melody.

Like a virus, the bronze transformation rapidly spread.

Ordinary True Immortals were truly infected upon contact, with no ability to resist.

Only the Nameless True Immortals fared better, as their control over a single Dao path provided strong resistance against this external bronze transformation.

However, this was limited to self-preservation.

Even the densely interwoven Dao Net could not completely prevent the spread of the bronze melody; it could only slow it down slightly.

The mysterious song gradually echoed throughout the Shuoxing Sea as the bronze celestial coffin opened.

Around the celestial coffin, a continuous army of bronze figures began to assemble.

This bizarre scene caught both the Vast Light and Shuoxing Sea off guard.

"Is this the power close to transcendence?"

"What exactly is buried in that bronze celestial coffin?"

After the initial shock, they slowly reacted.

They retracted the power of the Dao Net, forming a protective barrier with the Nameless beings at the center to prevent the spread of the bronze transformation.

The strange power of the bronze melody was completely outside their realm of cultivation knowledge.

It would take some time to analyze and respond.

"We cannot attend to the entire star sea; that area can only be abandoned." Bai Shuyue sighed.

As she spoke, the Shuoxing Sea had already been divided into two distinct halves.

One was the Dao Net, where blue light occasionally flickered, and the other was the celestial coffin, surrounded by dense green shadows and countless bronze armies.

In the stalemate, perhaps due to gathering enough strength, the bronze celestial coffin underwent further changes.

The dark green bronze rust on the coffin completely disappeared.

The coffin opened completely.

With a clinking sound, a solemn and majestic bronze chariot slowly emerged from the celestial coffin.

Eight ferocious ancient beasts of various shapes led the way. On the chariot, there was not a person, but an extremely complex bronze ancient tree!

Although it was no taller than a hundred feet, it seemed to encompass countless transformations, making it impossible to clearly discern the true appearance of the ancient tree.

On the bronze ancient tree, every branch and leaf seemed to record the rise and fall of an ancient bronze dynasty.

On the hundred-foot bronze tree, a dense accumulation of history, incredibly heavy.

"Xuan Yue dances, wind and thunder split."

"Turtle shell cracks, blood-red sun appears..."

The billions of transformed bronze soldiers chanted loudly in unison.

Amidst the sorrowful melody, more past shadows were projected from the bronze ancient tree.

These were countless ancient bronze civilizations, each developed to its peak prosperity.

But without exception, each was destroyed by a terrifying calamity at the final moment.

That scene of world-ending destruction was precisely the tribulation of Dao Annihilation!

The bronze civilization possessed an unimaginable resilience. Even under the threat of Dao Annihilation, it could maintain a sliver of life, a sprout for the next civilization's inspiration.

Through countless cycles, the branches and leaves on the bronze ancient tree grew more luxuriant, and the number of bronze civilizations that had existed increased.

However, without exception, none could truly escape the fate of being devoured by Dao Annihilation.

Endless cycles, with no hope of victory.

Thus, the last king of the bronze civilization chose not to continue an endless cycle.

He sealed himself and buried himself within a coffin, carrying all the traces of the bronze civilization's existence. After drifting in Dao Annihilation for countless years, he was finally salvaged by the Vast Light Star Sea.

"Emerging from the darkness and reawakening, this is the will of the ancient sages."

"Today, I shall commemorate my awakening with your fresh blood."

From the perspective of the bronze civilization, the immortals of the Vast Light and Shuoxing Seas were undoubtedly outsiders.

There was no need for communication; a battle immediately commenced.

Although the individual strength of the bronze civilization army was relatively weak, their numbers were practically endless.

From the bronze ancient tree, less than a hundred feet tall, it seemed that beings that had existed in Mountains and Seas could be summoned at any time.

And they did not truly experience life and death.

Even if defeated by the immortals of the Shuoxing Sea, they would only turn into bronze rust, flow back onto the bronze tree, and condense into branches and leaves again.

Bai Shuyue and the others had not considered blocking this endless cycle of transformation.

However, to completely eradicate it would require much more effort than defeating them. It would take the combined efforts of several Nameless beings to completely dispel the strange power of "bronze transformation."

It was a thankless task.

After a brief period of frustration, Bai Shuyue's side decisively changed their strategy.

Instead of trying to erase the bronze transformations, they focused on eliminating the transformed bronze armies and gradually weakening the bronze ancient tree's power.

Transforming bronze armies was not without cost to the ancient tree standing on the chariot.

At the very least, after half a year of war, Bai Shuyue noticed that it had visibly diminished.

Although the bronze civilization was mysterious, the people of the Shuoxing and Vast Light Seas had also survived the tribulation of Dao Annihilation with great difficulty.

Their foundation was not much weaker.

Moreover, they were fighting on their home turf.

As the battle stalemated, the bronze ancient tree underwent another change.

Leaves of bronze began to wither and fall from the branches along with the trunk.

Each fall transformed into a blurry, colossal figure.

These were seemingly the "kings" of past bronze civilizations.

Ten million of them stood side-by-side, advancing towards the Dao Net.

Compared to the bronze armies, the bronze ancient kings were significantly more difficult to deal with.

These bronze figures all possessed their own unique divine abilities, all based on "bronze transformation" and developing into various strange evolutions.

Some were almost identical to the Great Dao of the current era.

For example, one could flatten its palm, and upon being struck, the victim's body and soul would instantly freeze, as if trapped in the past.

Another could chant golden scripture, and countless twisted words would swarm the enemy like insects. Those affected would have their memories distorted, believing they were from the Shuoxing Sea side, and would end up helping the bronze ancient tree slaughter the immortals.

The bronze kings, while not comparable to Nameless beings, were still much stronger than True Immortals.

With all of them appearing at once, Bai Shuyue's side began to struggle.

More critically, the eight ferocious beasts pulling the bronze chariot had remained motionless from the beginning, merely observing the battlefield with indifference.

"Let's use the Immortal Treasures."

After some deliberation, everyone made their decision.

The Dao Sword and Dao Blade.

Two streaks of bright light appeared one after another.

The phantom images of the sword and blade covered countless bronze phantoms, destroying them. Simultaneously, the bronze rust they transformed into after being destroyed was all absorbed.

The Dao Sword and Dao Blade became stained with bronze rust.

However, their inherent power was not lost, but instead gained a touch of mysterious charm.

The bronze ancient tree's army was instantly cleared, leaving only over a hundred "kings" surviving.

The eight ancient beasts, who had been observing the entire time, finally made their move.

If the Dao Sword and Dao Blade were relics of other civilizations salvaged from Dao Annihilation by the Vast Light Star Sea, then these ancient beasts were relics of Mountains and Seas collected by the bronze civilization.

Compared to the current Great Dao, these survivors from ancient Mountains and Seas resisted Dao Annihilation solely through their bodies.

Even with the reinforcement of the Dao Net, the divine abilities and techniques of the immortals landed on them as if they were tickling.

Under the rampage of the ancient beasts, the Dao Net almost snapped.

Fortunately, over the past few years, under Bai Shuyue's direction, all departments of the Dao Net had been training to their limits in preparation.

Thus, it was not immediately destroyed.

The immortals could only summon more salvaged Immortal Treasures to fight against them.

The ancient civilizations from Mountains and Seas, and the surviving star sea civilization from the lower realms, engaged in a stalemate on the battlefield.

The bronze civilization did not connect to Mountains and Seas; it continuously regenerated through its own peculiar nature.

While the Vast Light and Shuoxing Seas relied on the power of Infinite Mountains and Seas for support.

With back-and-forth exchanges, Infinite Mountains and Seas ultimately proved superior.

Leaves began to wither and fall from the bronze ancient tree, leaving only a bare trunk.

The last bronze king, with a calm expression, tightly gripped the bronze trunk. He then surprisingly thrust it fiercely into his own chest!

The bronze ancient tree transformed into simple bronze rust, flowing into the bronze king's body through the wound in his chest. A vibrant new tree then appeared.

However, unlike the bronze ancient tree that carried the past, this one representing abandonment and rebirth...

The bronze king's features gradually became clear, while the bronze transformations on the battlefield, having lost their power source, slowly dissipated.

The kings, the ancient beasts. All of them vanished.

The immense pressure on the immortals of the star seas instantly disappeared.

But Bai Shuyue and the others were more alarmed than pleased.

They stared at the last bronze king, on the verge of a world-shattering transformation, and a sense of foreboding arose in their hearts.

"Not good! This is a sign of achieving transcendence!" Yuan Shu was the first to react, screaming, "If this damned thing truly transcends, we will all die!"

Upon hearing this, the immortals' hearts trembled.

Understanding the seriousness of the situation, they no longer held back, unleashing all their trump cards, divine abilities, techniques, and treasures.

They hurled them towards the last bronze king.

Bai Shuyue, acting instinctively, was about to activate the Dao Net to its maximum power.

But suddenly, she remembered the Boundless Wall's reminder from earlier.

Her heart stirred, and she held back, not unleashing her prepared techniques.

Having abandoned past glories and memories, integrating all the memories of the bronze civilization into himself.

The last bronze king was only one step away from transcendence.

Even the Dao Annihilation outside the Shuoxing Sea seemed to sense it.

Waves surged, becoming increasingly turbulent.

Although the immortals tried their best to stop him, they were ultimately unable to harm him in the slightest.

As the patterns on the bronze king's body grew more luxuriant, it seemed that a new transcendent powerhouse was truly about to be born.

The immortals looked on in despair.

Instinctively, some had already started thinking of escape.

At this critical moment, Yuan Shu from the Vast Light Star Sea gritted his teeth and threw an ordinary-looking pearl towards the bronze king.

Radiance bloomed, and countless light images erupted, precisely the Dao Chronicle Projection Pearl!

Chapter 1655: Wash Moon Finally Transcends

The last Bronze King was the culmination of all ancient Bronze Civilizations from the Mountains and Seas of the past.

The Dao Chronicle Projection Pearl, on the other hand, was a replication of all divine abilities, arts, and techniques that had ever existed, from nothingness to their formation, within a single possibility.

A confrontation between equals, a perfect match!

Boom, boom, boom, boom!

Infinite light and infinite heat erupted in the Shuoxing Sea at the moment of collision.

Even though they were merely affected and not the main participants in the collision, Qianye and the remaining inhabitants of the Shuoxing Sea were all aghast.

"Everyone, work together to withstand this wave!"

Bai Shuyue roared.

The Eternal Straw Cloak was quietly donned. From the depths of the Dao Net's core, beneath the black mountain and white water that suppressed the Boundless Wall, Bai Shuyue leaped out.

Unlike the True Immortals who had already begun to flee, the remaining departments of the Dao Net held their positions, cooperating with Bai Shuyue's commands.

"Dao Net, merge with me!" Bai Shuyue chanted softly.

As if an extension of her arm, the Shuoxing Sea's Dao Net once again contracted, becoming smaller and smaller.

Ultimately, it transformed into a shimmering veil of ethereal, dreamlike luster that enveloped Bai Shuyue's body.

Bai Shuyue did not break the restrictions left by Cheng Dao, to leave the core of the Dao Net. Instead, she wore the Dao Net like a garment.

In this manner, she manifested herself in the Star Sea!

Even after meditating for a thousand years, with her current strength, she was indeed unable to support the entire Dao Net. Even though the Dao Net had suffered some damage during the great battle.

However, the Great Dao Manifestation Department, led by Nangong Fusheng, shared most of the pressure for her.

And every member of the Myriad Immortals Formation was like her arm, assisting her in manipulating the Dao Net with extreme precision.

"Is this what it feels like to be a true powerhouse?"

At this moment, Bai Shuyue had channeled all the power of the Dao Net onto herself, surpassing the strength limit of an ordinary Nameless True Immortal, subtly touching the threshold of Transcendence.

When one stood at such a realm, everything perceived, contemplated, thought, and seen was vastly different from before.

Coupled with Bai Shuyue's heaven-defying talent, her insights surged like an endless storm every moment.

While meditating, Bai Shuyue also did her utmost to resist the impact of the collision between the Dao Chronicle Projection and the last Bronze King.

It was as if facing the combined forces of two peerless experts, under this immense pressure, Bai Shuyue transformed her insights into practical power every second.

Constantly on the brink of life and death, theoretically, she could not have maintained such calmness.

But Bai Shuyue possessed the ability to repeatedly reincarnate and be reborn. Facing the threat of annihilation, she had been utterly calm from beginning to end.

When the True Immortals who attempted to flee were annihilated in the impact; when the Nameless beings in the Dao Net hysterically contributed their energy under the pressure of death; when Yuan Shu of the Vast Light Star Sea was lost in thought from the massive collision of the Dao Chronicle Projection Pearl and the Bronze King...

Bai Shuyue silently observed, her mind devoid of distractions. She did her best to resolve the impending impact.

The projections from time and space seemed endless.

The Bronze Civilization had once flourished across mountains and seas.

Time seemed to have lost all meaning in the face of this violent collision and explosion.

However, the infinite light finally began to dim.

The entire Shuoxing Sea was almost destroyed.

The tide of Dao Annihilation seized the opportunity, engulfing it.

Only the high walls and the Dao Net remained.

Under the protection of Shou Qiu's illusory form, though the high walls suffered impact, they remained relatively intact.

However, there was clearly significant damage, as if Dao Annihilation had discovered a weakness and was gleefully attacking.

Under Bai Shuyue's direction, although the Dao Net was eighty percent damaged, it ultimately withstood this calamity.

And...

A mysterious regenerative power emerged from the core of the Dao Net, like a source, rapidly repairing the broken Dao strings.

The True Immortals and Nameless True Immortals, who had sacrificed themselves to support the Dao Net, seemed to have been resurrected.

Their Dao paths reappeared!

But looking at the direction from which these new Dao strings emerged, it was evident that they all originated from a single point.

Bai Shuyue!

Compared to before the collision between the Dao Chronicle Projection and the Bronze King, she was a completely different person.

During that time, which felt like both an instant and an eternity,

Bai Shuyue meticulously maintained the existence of the Dao Net while reflecting everything happening around her.

The changes in the True Immortals' Dao paths, the divine abilities recorded by the Dao Chronicle Projection, the ancient anecdotes of the Bronze Civilization.

And even the annihilation of possibility, the ripples of Dao Annihilation...

For everyone else, this was a catastrophe akin to the end of the world. But for Bai Shuyue, it was an excellent opportunity for enlightenment.

Her terrifying spiritual essence, accumulated over thirty lifetimes, was fully utilized in this scenario.

She had completely mastered the Dao paths of the True Immortals who had perished in the collision, thus she could easily recreate them.

The Dao Net lost eighty percent of its structure.

Compared to the Shuoxing Sea, the Vast Light Star Sea suffered even heavier losses.

Out of over a hundred True Immortals, only thirteen survived.

One of the two leading Nameless beings also perished in this calamity.

However, the divine abilities they displayed in their final moments of struggle became sustenance for Bai Shuyue's enlightenment.

"In a sense, I have also achieved the path of 'Slaying Immortals to Prove the Dao' in another way."

"But it was not me who personally slew them."

Bai Shuyue looked at Yuan Shu, who seemed somewhat lost in thought.

Although the Dao Chronicle Projection ultimately defeated the Bronze King, it was severely weakened.

The recorded light and shadow within it became dim and fragile, its ability to unleash further power uncertain.

"However, the initial objective has been somewhat achieved."

"It's just that the cost was far more severe than expected," Yuan Shu said with a wry smile.

Sizing up Bai Shuyue, who had appeared inexplicably with an unfathomable aura, he eventually could only leave dejectedly.

They had only managed to discuss the exchange of the [Illusory Form Dao Bearing] technique and the time to observe the remnant of Transcendence.

"The Vast Light Star Sea possesses such a powerful weapon, yet they didn't inform us beforehand! Their intentions are reprehensible!"

"If not for the Bronze King's underlying strength far exceeding expectations, forcing him to use it. Our outcome would likely have been even more dire," Chaos said coldly, his killing intent towards the Vast Light Star Sea unconcealed.

His old friends, Shan Hua and Wan Sheng, had both died in this calamity.

He had completely lost trust in the ill-intentioned Vast Light Star Sea.

As for their promise to let him view the remnant of Transcendence, he no longer believed it.

The other Nameless beings, also sobered by this tragic incident, shed their greed.

Among the surviving remnants of the Dao Net, only Bai Shuyue remained steadfast in her original intention.

"Everyone, there is no need for worry. After paying such a great price, how can we give up on the promised rewards from the other party?"

"I will embody the Dao Net and personally attend the meeting."

"In exchange for the opportunity to observe the remnant of Transcendence, I will use the [Illusory Form Dao Bearing] technique."

The emotions of the Dao Net's inhabitants varied.

Some urgently tried to dissuade her, others greedily yearned for the opportunity, and some were lost in contemplation, filled with excitement.

But regardless, Bai Shuyue's decision was made.

Given her performance in this calamity, where she almost single-handedly averted disaster, no one could object.

Two years later, without the attraction of immortal bait, the Dao Annihilation surrounding the Dao Net gradually subsided.

With the reconstruction of the Dao Net as its backbone, a new starry sky began to form.

Although it was also called the Shuoxing Sea, it was not the same as before.

And in the darkness ahead, in the direction of the Vast Light Star Sea.

Occasional fluctuations of Dao Annihilation could be sensed.

It was clear that the Vast Light Star Sea's actions of cutting off other immortal bait had not yet ended.

The agreed-upon time had passed, but Yuan Shu had still not appeared.

All the Immortals of the Dao Net believed that the other party had deliberately broken their promise and cursed endlessly.

But Bai Shuyue remained silent, gazing into the distance, waiting patiently.

"It seems the troubles faced by the Vast Light Star Sea are even greater than imagined."

As time flowed by, thirty-three years later.

The Dao Annihilation fluctuations from that direction finally subsided completely.

"It's time." A glint flashed in Bai Shuyue's eyes.

Without waiting for anyone from the Vast Light Star Sea to arrive, she took the initiative to go!

With a single thought, the Dao Net transformed into a shimmering veil once more, enveloping her body.

Bai Shuyue stepped lightly towards the Dao Annihilation ahead.

Like a dragonfly skimming the water's surface, she caused ripples in the Dao Annihilation.

Yet, Bai Shuyue was not swallowed by the Dao Annihilation.

Instead, she moved lightly across the waves, rapidly crossing towards the Vast Light Star Sea!

In her previous life, Bai Shuyue had survived by drifting in the Dao Annihilation with the Eternal Straw Cloak and the Dao Net.

This lifetime, after a thousand years of accumulation and enlightenment during the collision,

Bai Shuyue now possessed the strength to traverse the Dao Annihilation for a short period!

The inhabitants within the Dao Net were swept along by her, traversing the Dao Annihilation, filled with uncontrollable excitement. At the same time, they dared not be careless, each fulfilling their duties to maintain the stability of the Dao Net veil.

The journey was uneventful.

When they finally emerged from the Dao Annihilation and arrived in a brand new, vibrant starry sea,

Everyone felt as if they had gone through a lifetime, as if in a dream.

Bai Shuyue, clad in the Dao Net, had traversed from the Dao Annihilation.

Such a massive commotion naturally attracted the attention of the Vast Light Star Sea immediately.

Figures flew from all directions, surrounding them, all possessing the strength of Nameless beings, including Yuan Shu.

"It's you?! How can you traverse the Dao Annihilation? How is this possible?" Yuan Yuan, recognizing Bai Shuyue, was utterly astonished.

Bai Shuyue smiled: "If you can go, I can go too. The time has come, and I have come today as promised."

Facing the siege of a crowd of Nameless beings, Bai Shuyue, who had come alone, remained calm and fearless.

After a moment of deathly silence,

Following a round of discussion, the Vast Light Star Sea ultimately decided to treat her as an honored guest.

It was not that they truly feared Bai Shuyue. It was simply that the timing of her arrival was too opportune.

In the period of weakness following the great battle, if a fight truly broke out, their chances of winning were not high.

Moreover, the Vast Light Star Sea could not afford further turmoil in the short term.

Thus, surrounded by all the Immortals, Bai Shuyue was led to the fishing immortal platform.

The periphery was densely packed with over a hundred heavenly pillars, surrounding nine central pillars.

From weak to strong, forming a tiered embankment to attract Dao Annihilation.

"So this is the method of fishing for Dao Annihilation in the Vast Light Star Sea."

"The principle is simple, yet it is effective." Bai Shuyue saw through its mystery at a glance, nodding inwardly.

"Open!" The Immortals of the Vast Light Star Sea chanted in unison.

The central area surrounded by the hundred heavenly pillars began to churn with dark currents, and Dao Annihilation surged like waves.

It was as if something deep within the Dao Annihilation was being attracted.

Soon, a few faint points of light emerged from the abyss of Dao Annihilation in the center.

Initially, like countless stars.

As the chanting of the Vast Light Immortals grew more urgent, these points of light became brighter and brighter.

Even dazzling!

The brilliance was even greater than the collision of the Dao Chronicle Projection and the Bronze King.

The hundred heavenly pillars surrounding the immortal platform also suddenly shone brightly, shooting out threads of light, like ropes, entangling the starlight.

"Open!" The Immortals of the Vast Light Star Sea shouted in unison again.

A figure, appearing somewhat frail, was slowly pulled out from the vortex.

Although solitary, it seemed to carry the weight of mountains and seas!

All the Immortals of the Vast Light Star Sea seemed to be bearing immense pressure, their auras surging to their limits.

And the hundred heavenly pillars of the immortal platform also tilted to varying degrees.

The source of all this pressure came from the figure that emerged from the Dao Annihilation!

The veil of the Dao Net on Bai Shuyue's body rustled as if blown by a strong wind.

The Immortals within the Dao Net all stared intently at the remnant of transcendence, their hearts stirred.

"This is..."

"Transcendence?"

They stared intently for a long time, expecting to gain profound insights.

However...

Although they knew he was a transcendent being, the reason for his transcendence, the profound mysteries within,

Were impossible to discern.

"This?"

The Immortals looked at each other.

The gap between expectation and reality was too great. Some, unwilling to give up, continued to choose to observe.

But the result was no different.

The secret of Transcendence, even when right before their eyes, was beyond their grasp.

The Immortals of the Dao Net slowly began to understand why the Vast Light Star Sea only used this remnant of transcendence as immortal bait,

"Being in a treasure mountain but unable to recognize its true value."

"What a pity, what a lament, what hatred!"

The Immortals were crestfallen.

The inhabitants of the Vast Light Star Sea, looking at the state of the Dao Net Immortals, did not mock them.

Because...

They were the same.

Among everyone present, only Bai Shuyue was different.

While others saw only a semi-decayed corpse.

In Bai Shuyue's eyes, she saw a lone boat sailing across mountains and seas!

"Mountains and seas are boundless, a lone boat can cross..."

"This is Transcendence, this is true Transcendence."

Bai Shuyue murmured to herself, her joy overflowing.

The Dao in this remnant of transcendence was not her own Dao,

But it pointed the way for Bai Shuyue.

Since embarking on the path of cultivation, Bai Shuyue had always explored on her own.

Occasionally receiving guidance from the Boundless Wall and Cheng Dao, but they had never charted a clear path for her. Only now...

When Bai Shuyue saw a complete remnant of transcendence with her own eyes,

She finally saw the direction she should take.

"Crossing Dao Annihilation, we must all use our own abilities to cross."

"We must forge a unique Dao path..."

As if resonating with Bai Shuyue's thoughts, the solitary boat within the remnant of transcendence,

Suddenly surged!

In an instant, Bai Shuyue felt as if she were on that lone boat, on a wooden vessel.

What she saw around her was the vast boundless mountains and seas, the endless Dao Annihilation!

"Hmm?"

Bai Shuyue suddenly awoke from her ecstatic enlightenment.

Because she inexplicably discovered that on this lone boat, besides herself, there were other blurry figures.

And this figure was surprisingly familiar!

Chapter 1656: Crossing Intent with Home

"Fan'er?!"

Bai Shuyue was far too familiar with this figure. The moment she saw its blurry image, she blurted it out.

But quickly, Bai Shuyue reacted. This was the core of the Lone Sail Transcendence True Intent. How could Fan'er, a mere mortal, possibly be here!

Yet, the faint figure before her resembled Li Fan too closely. It held Bai Shuyue's gaze for a long time.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless; it is not impossible for such a degree of similarity to appear."

"This figure does not belong to the original owner of this Transcendence True Intent. It is..."

Bai Shuyue observed for a long time, then faintly understood.

"It is a True Immortal between the Mountains and Seas who also treads the path of the 'Lone Sail.' When the 'Lone Sail' perishes, True Immortals in the Mountains and Seas can naturally comprehend this path again. However, since the 'Lone Sail' has not completely dissipated, those who follow this path will appear here together."

"This Transcendence True Intent is like a bright mirror, reflecting all fellow travelers in the Mountains and Seas. If this figure before me truly takes that step of transcendence, the two will merge into one..."

Thinking this, Bai Shuyue couldn't help but breathe a sigh of relief. Clearly, the figure before her was not the "Li Fan" she knew.

"I heard that the Mountains and Seas are boundless, existing with infinite possibilities. Perhaps, he is Fan'er from another possibility. I just don't know what kind of life he has lived..."

But Bai Shuyue knew well that this Li Fan was not that Li Fan. She was also not the ignorant and innocent peasant woman from another possibility. Thus, after indulging in her thoughts for a while, Bai Shuyue refocused her attention on the True Intent of the 'Lone Sail.'

In a daze, Bai Shuyue seemed to fall into boundless Mountains and Seas. Looking around, there was no direction, no escape. All around were the surging tides of Dao Annihilation. In such a desperate situation, only a single Lone Sail hung high, resolutely traversing.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, only I am the boat."

"It is precisely with this belief that this Transcendence True Intent was forged. Therefore, transcendence does not merely refer to a realm above the Nameless, but also requires a state of mind and intention that matches one's strength."

"By what right can I transcend?"

Bai Shuyue's mind became one with the Lone Sail, immersed in its long memory of traversing the Mountains and Seas. Although Bai Shuyue subjectively only wanted to refer to the Lone Sail's True Intent and forge her own independent path, firstly, she could only touch the threshold of transcendence by relying on the Dao Net enveloping her; she was not a true transcendent expert herself. She could not completely shield herself from the influence of Transcendence True Intent. Secondly, her talent and comprehension were too high. Others might wish to observe but could not, while Bai Shuyue could experience it firsthand, almost fully comprehending the 'Lone Sail' in its prime. Thus, when she dedicated herself to its comprehension, she inevitably began to evolve towards the 'Lone Sail.'

"No, this is not the path I want to take!"

Only when the change was halfway through did Bai Shuyue suddenly awaken. Without the slightest hesitation, she directly severed her thoughts from the Transcendence True Intent before her, instantly withdrawing from the profound state of enlightenment. The comprehension progress, which had been halfway accumulated, vanished with Bai Shuyue's voluntary abandonment, leaving not even a trace. From beginning to end, it was as if it were just Bai Shuyue's illusion.

However, the boundless sense of loneliness that still lingered in her heart told Bai Shuyue that the experience just now was not a false dream. Even if she borrowed the Transcendence True Intent of past figures to enlighten herself, it would not prevent her from ultimately becoming a new transcendent being. Faced with such temptation before her, Bai Shuyue still resolutely gave it up. Because Bai Shuyue was confident enough. She absolutely could carve out a path that suited her best without walking the old path of others.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, I shall traverse them myself. My method of traversing need not be the same as yours."

With this thought, the True Intent of the Lone Sail held no more temptation in Bai Shuyue's eyes. She bowed respectfully, then no longer looked at the remnant of transcendence surrounded by the dam. Instead, she turned to face the Immortals of the Guangwu Star Sea.

"Since you have fulfilled your promise, I will not break mine."

"I will impart the method of 'Fishing for Immortal Treasures' transformed into a technique akin to celestial pillars, named '[Illusory Form Dao Bearing],' passed down from Master Shou Qiu!" Bai Shuyue declared proudly.

"Master Shou Qiu?!" The Immortals of the Guangwu Star Sea all exclaimed in unison. Although many years had passed, they still vividly remembered Master Shou Qiu's mighty display, blocking the Dao Annihilation alone. They never expected that the Star Sea Dao Net of the Shuoxing Sea would be a direct descendant of Shou Qiu!

Amidst their shock, they quickly focused their attention and listened intently to Bai Shuyue's divine ability and profound methods. They truly felt that every word was a pearl, profoundly mysterious. When they came back to their senses, Bai Shuyue had already gracefully departed, returning to the Shuoxing Sea.

Yuan Fu, the middle-aged man leading the Guangwu Star Sea Immortals, shook his head: "Forget it, let her go. After all, she is a disciple of Shou Qiu..."

"Moreover, we have obtained the method of '[Illusory Form Dao Bearing]'. With its assistance, the Guangwu Star Sea will no longer fear destruction. Even if the possibility is swallowed by Dao Annihilation, we can still float safely."

"The Shuoxing Sea is no longer important. Everyone, the urgent task is to transform all the fished immortal treasures into Dao Bearing Illusory Forms. Once we have enough support..."

"We can then accept the invitation and head to that realm of birth and death!" Yuan Fu's eyes were filled with fanaticism. As if seeing a brilliant future, the Guangwu Immortals were also stirred. They immediately worked with full vigor, pooling their efforts to transform the myriad fished immortal treasures.

Bai Shuyue was naturally unaware of what happened in the Guangwu Star Sea after she left. For her, at this moment, there was only one important matter. That was to enter seclusion and comprehend the Dao! Although her understanding of the Lone Sail's True Intent had faded like a tide, her comprehension of 'transcendence' itself still lingered in her heart.

"I must seize this opportune moment to take that final crucial step!" The light Dao Net draped over her body once again unfurled and resumed its normal form. Bai Shuyue leaped back into the depths of the Dao Net's core and sat quietly upon the black mountain and white water. The fragments of her thirty-plus reincarnations flashed before her eyes. Although her experiences were certainly rich and colorful, to reach the realm of transcendence with just this seemed to be lacking something.

"Transcendence True Intent is the core spiritual support of one's unique self. Even if one falls into Dao Annihilation, one can still rely on it to traverse safely."

"Along the way, why did I cultivate so arduelly?" Bai Shuyue pondered this question again. The answer remained the same. To protect her pitiful nephew, Li Fan. To create an eternal home, free from the interference of external storms and Dao Annihilation. To be able to, forever, live peacefully and stably.

"Mercy is easy to grant, but bring back my aunt's life!" Bai Shuyue's eyes once again saw the furious appearance of her nephew as he sought revenge for her, disregarding all risks. It was as if she had returned to the ancestral house of the Great Xuan Dynasty, where they lived dependently but harmoniously. The scene of the farmhouse, springing from Bai Shuyue's heart, gradually transformed from illusory to real, completely solidifying.

"This is the home for my nephew and me."

"I will not allow anyone to destroy it." Bai Shuyue slowly walked into the house, looking at the familiar furnishings and decorations within, her eyes gradually becoming calm and contented.
