Even if Li Fan was not present in this house at the moment, Bai Shuyue firmly believed that one day, she could bring Li Fan back, and they would live peacefully forever. Perhaps Fan'er would grow tired and want to see the world outside. Bai Shuyue would not restrict him; she would even support him as much as possible. But as long as Li Fan wished, he could always return. Bai Shuyue would always be waiting for him at home.

... Bai Shuyue returned to the dining table and sat down, as if Li Fan were sitting opposite her. Her mind was empty, calm, and contented. No other thoughts lingered. Even if storms raged outside and Dao Annihilation roared, it could not affect the warmth within the small house in the slightest. At this moment, this farmhouse, which carried all of Bai Shuyue's beautiful memories of "home," completely solidified. It transformed into a crystal clear, immortal thought, forever preserved in the world.

At the same moment, Bai Shuyue had a sudden realization, as if guided by fate.

"It's time."

She looked up towards the sky beyond, her gaze passing through layers of Dao Net, falling upon the Mountains and Seas. She took a light step forward. The restrictions left by Cheng Dao, like a faint gleam, perhaps sensing the aura surging from Bai Shuyue, did not truly obstruct her. Instead, they allowed her to leap out. This time, Bai Shuyue did not wear the Dao Net. Instead, she moved alone, arriving within the nascent star sea. The Mountains and Seas beyond possibility, Dao Annihilation, seemed within reach. Bai Shuyue leaped forward, breaking free from the origin, and fell into the Mountains and Seas, into Dao Annihilation! Cold, lonely, annihilating all. Dao Annihilation, all-pervasive, instantly enveloped Bai Shuyue. But simultaneously, Bai Shuyue truly felt the might of the Infinite Sea and the Above Mountains.

"The fusion of Mountains and Seas gives rise to Dao Annihilation."

A peculiar glint flashed in Bai Shuyue's eyes. Her aura, which was originally at the peak of the Combined Dao realm, upon connecting with the Mountains and Seas, began to climb boundlessly! If she were merely a cultivator at the Combined Dao realm, she would certainly not be able to handle such an exponential surge in cultivation. But Bai Shuyue had already touched the threshold of transcendence during her control of the Dao Net. Therefore, no matter how much her strength soared like a wild horse, she remained in control, mastering it with ease. As her strength and realm climbed towards the realm of transcendence, while facing the omnipresent threat of Dao Annihilation, Bai Shuyue remained completely composed.

She still sat in the house, at the dining table. Looking at the surging Dao Annihilation waves outside the window, she didn't even bother to get up. Outside, the wind howled, but the small home remained unshaken like a steadfast dam! Inside the house, the candlelight flickered. Bai Shuyue sat upright. Opposite her, a figure slowly took shape – it was Li Fan's likeness. This was a seat Bai Shuyue had reserved for Li Fan within her own Transcendence True Intent. Even as a mere mortal, he could sit here with ease. Or rather, it was only with Li Fan's inclusion that Bai Shuyue's Transcendence True Intent truly became complete.

When Li Fan's blurry figure also sat down, Bai Shuyue's Transcendence True Intent truly manifested. The surging aura reached its peak at this moment. A new transcendent expert descended upon the world. In an instant, the winds calmed and the waves subsided! Perhaps knowing they could not harm Bai Shuyue in a short time, Dao Annihilation temporarily retreated, accumulating more power to prepare for a future resurgence. But Bai Shuyue, who had attained Dao, remained emotionless. She merely felt that at such an激动 moment, it was truly regrettable that Li Fan was not here to witness it.

"It's alright, Fan'er."

"We will be able to meet again soon." Bai Shuyue looked into the boundless Mountains and Seas in the distance. Although the Mountains and Seas were vast, she could find no place for herself to reside. Only where she and Li Fan were was truly home. Even with the ability to sail across the sea, Bai Shuyue had no intention of venturing far. After all, her initial purpose for cultivating was to truly protect Li Fan. Now that the objective seemed to have been achieved, the desire for further advancement had largely vanished. "As long as in the next lifetime, I can first preserve Fan'er's life before seeking Dao attainment."

"Even if the threat of Dao Annihilation descends, we will be safe and sound." Bai Shuyue sighed deeply. Her thoughts were calm; she had no further desire to explore the boundless Mountains and Seas. Instead, Bai Shuyue returned to the Shuoxing Sea. The earth-shattering aura of her Dao attainment could hardly be hidden from the Immortals of the Dao Net. At this moment, they all knew Bai Shuyue had truly taken that step. While envious, they were also respectful before her, fearing to displease this newly emerged transcendent being. Although their past interactions showed Bai Shuyue to be approachable, who could guarantee that her temperament would not change after transcending? Moreover, for transcendent experts, killing ordinary Nameless beings was no more difficult than crushing an ant. Therefore, before Bai Shuyue, the Dao Net Immortals were all extremely cautious. Fortunately, Bai Shuyue's state of mind seemed unchanged.

"I have just attained Dao and have gained some insights."

"I can share them with you." Upon hearing this, the Dao Net Immortals were all stunned, looking at Bai Shuyue with disbelief. Then, immense joy surged. A transcendent expert lecturing was far more valuable than observing a remnant of transcendence. They had paid a heavy price to observe the remnant of transcendence, and now, they could freely listen to a transcendent expert personally lecture...

"Senior is merciful!" All the Immortals praised with gratitude, bowing respectfully. Bai Shuyue nodded slightly, then imparted all her insights from her Dao attainment process without any concealment.

"The Mountains and Seas are boundless, only I am the boat."

"Though Dao Annihilation is vast, my will can sail." Various profound aspects were heard by the Immortals as if they were entranced, as if they saw their own prospects of transcendence, and many even danced with excitement on the spot. When they finally calmed down, they found that Bai Shuyue had already disappeared, gone to an unknown location. The Immortals assumed Bai Shuyue had resolved her karma and had likely headed to the legendary other shore. However... Bai Shuyue had not left. Instead, she quietly returned to the deepest part of the Dao Net, awaiting the transformation and metamorphosis of the Boundless Wall. She did not emit any aura, deliberately displaying her breakthrough, but as usual, sat patiently waiting.

Chapter 1657: Really Mending the Sky's Defect

Under the black mountain and white water, the Boundless Wall was immersed in enlightenment and did not notice Bai Shuyue's changes for a long time.

Bai Shuyue did not reveal herself and silently observed it.

With her current transcendent perspective, she could see things she couldn't before upon closer inspection.

"Cheng Dao was originally a spiritual stone by the sea, enlightened by Shou Qiu and transformed into a human. This black mountain and white water are the crystallization of his transformation and his comprehension of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas."

"His enlightenment during transformation can indeed serve as a reference for the Boundless Wall. However, his comprehension of the Mountains and Seas..."

Bai Shuyue shook her head slightly.

Cheng Dao had not truly transcended yet. The black mountain and white water he left behind could never compare to the true Great Dao of Mountains and Seas.

If the Boundless Wall were to enlighten based on this flawed foundation, it would be even more misguided.

Bai Shuyue used her finger as a brush, embellishing the barren black mountain and white water.

Before long, the once desolate mountain and water scenery, which only possessed imposing majesty, began to teem with life.

Because of this diffused vitality, the mountain and water appeared even more vast and magnificent.

The higher the mountain, the deeper the water.

Just like the Mountains and Seas!

In the face of such earth-shattering changes, the Boundless Wall let out a surprised cry and finally awoke.

"What's happening? What's happening?"

The Boundless Wall was bewildered, looking left and right.

Naturally, it immediately discovered Bai Shuyue's smiling figure.

Because of its familiarity with Bai Shuyue, it didn't immediately suspect her as the cause of the anomaly.

It quietly asked, "Did Senior Cheng Dao return just now?"

Bai Shuyue's smile froze on her face, then she sighed.

She tapped the black mountain and white water below with her finger.

As if Dao Annihilation had descended, the mountain and water trembled violently, looking as if they could collapse at any moment.

The Boundless Wall was terrified, staring at Bai Shuyue with wide eyes.

After a long silence, it finally managed to exclaim, "No, you... you, you!"

It could only manage three "you"s before the complete sentence escaped.

Bai Shuyue finally felt satisfied and smiled as she asked, "You said before that when your cultivation was complete, you would take me along. Is it time now?"

"I was just worried about not having a way to go to the other shore."

Hearing her words, the Boundless Wall finally confirmed: Bai Shuyue had transcended!

The Boundless Wall was stunned for a moment, then asked blankly, "What year is it today?"

It had doubted if it had slept for too long during its enlightenment, and in this long period, Bai Shuyue had finally achieved transcendence!

"It seems you still haven't fully woken up."

Bai Shuyue continued to tap the black mountain and white water. Amidst the earth-shattering tremors, the Boundless Wall finally managed to calculate the correct time.

Since it was willing to face the danger of the collapsing mountain, it screamed in extreme shock, "How is this possible? How could you have transcended in such a short time?"

"Am I going crazy, or am I still dreaming?"

It was simply unable to accept this fact, and the Boundless Wall remained stunned for a while.

"When there are countless geniuses in the Mountains and Seas, and countless extraordinary individuals, although my cultivation speed is a bit faster, it's nothing compared to the three Saints. You, who were once a confidant of a Saint Monarch, should not be so surprised." Bai Shuyue teased.

"That's right... that makes sense." With this perspective, the Boundless Wall's shock slowly dissipated.

"Yes, yes, you are transcendent, and I am a confidant of a Saint. You are strong, but I am not afraid of you!" the Boundless Wall said, trying to maintain its composure.

However, it ultimately knew the terror of transcendence, and its tone was far less arrogant than before, filled with a sense of forced bravura.

Seeing this, Bai Shuyue suddenly felt a sense of weariness.

She knew that a regrettable and insurmountable barrier had formed between her and the Boundless Wall.

"If Fan'er were still here, he surely wouldn't be so afraid of me, right? No matter how strong I become, I'd still be the same aunt he knew."

No longer teasing the Boundless Wall, Bai Shuyue specifically explained her enlightenment regarding transcendence to it alone.

Like the immortals of the Dao Net, the Boundless Wall listened with rapt attention, utterly mesmerized. Then, it was filled with gratitude towards Bai Shuyue.

"I have reshaped the black mountain and white water for you. If you observe them day and night, your transformation and even transcendence are within reach."

After saying this, Bai Shuyue disappeared.

Although the Boundless Wall felt a sense of loss, it soon immersed itself in observation and comprehension again.

With a transcendent expert personally guiding it, this was truly a heaven-sent opportunity. Although the title of "Confidant of a Saint Monarch" was true, the Boundless Wall itself knew that the supreme Saint would never offer guidance in such matters.

"Transcendence is possible, transcendence is possible!" the Boundless Wall rejoiced, its thoughts gradually sinking into contemplation.

After fulfilling her promise to the Boundless Wall, Bai Shuyue stood in the starry sky, a sense of being out of place suddenly arising in her heart.

The possibility beneath her feet was too small; it could be seen at a glance.

Even a casual movement from her might overturn it.

"I finally understand why most transcendent beings eventually depart."

Bai Shuyue sighed wistfully, her thoughts subtly changing.

Originally, she had not intended to traverse the Mountains and Seas to explore the unknown depths.

However, her post-transcendence experiences made her unconsciously change her mind.

Out of boredom, she began to contemplate traveling far away.

But Bai Shuyue did not leave immediately.

She waited another hundred years.

This wait was because Bai Shuyue wanted to see Cheng Dao again.

However, even though Bai Shuyue had disseminated the method of [Illusory Form Cheng Dao], Cheng Dao did not seem particularly interested, never returning to investigate.

"It seems Cheng Dao will not return. I wonder where he is in the Mountains and Seas right now."

With nothing left to linger for in this place, Bai Shuyue leaped forward and floated away.

Within the Transcendance True Meaning of the Xuanhuang Household, Bai Shuyue quietly sat in her own seat, with Li Fan's illusory figure opposite her.

Regardless of the roaring Dao Annihilation outside, the interior of the house remained peaceful and serene.

The Xuanhuang Household, carrying Bai Shuyue, silently drifted towards the depths of the Mountains and Seas.

Completely disappearing from sight.

The Primal did not stop its self-operation just because someone disappeared.

Even because of Bai Shuyue's transcendent blessing, this possibility, which had been fragmented and encroached upon by Dao Annihilation, unexpectedly regained vitality from the Guangwu and Shuoxing Seas.

After an unknown period, a figure appeared like a ghost.

He first scanned the surroundings, then stared at the direction Bai Shuyue had disappeared, murmuring with an inscrutable smile: "I never expected that Aunt's condensed Transcendance True Meaning would be [Home]. And even have a place for me."

"It's truly somewhat moving. Hehehe..."

Li Fan chuckled lowly, but his expression held no trace of being moved.

"Finally, the step towards transcendence has been reached."

"What comes next..."

"Is beyond my control."

Li Fan had no intention of tracking Bai Shuyue.

In fact, when he sensed Bai Shuyue was about to achieve transcendence, he had stopped observing in secret. Instead, he actively distanced himself, only returning after Bai Shuyue had left.

Although Bai Shuyue's strength after transcendence was still weaker than his, their realms were within the same range.

If he had forcibly pursued her, he would have risked being discovered.

"After all, as long as I perform True Reversion, I can choose to inherit Aunt's memories. Then I will know what she encountered later."

"The only downside is that I have to wait for her to perish before I can activate True Reversion. Otherwise, it will inevitably expose flaws. Transcendent experts have almost infinite lifespans. Under normal circumstances, only when this segment of Mountains and Seas reaches its end will she possibly face a mortal danger. However..."

Li Fan smiled confidently: "Now that the 'Li Fan' in the Mountains and Seas no longer exists, for the sake of her beloved nephew, Aunt surely won't force herself to live that long. Perhaps she will even voluntarily end her life."

"And thanks to the place she left for me within her Transcendance True Meaning, as soon as she dies, I will sense it."

"All I need to do is wait patiently," Li Fan said confidently.

From the beginning to the present, Li Fan's plan to create a Saint had been flawless.

Even though Bai Shuyue had reached the transcendent realm, she had not discovered any flaws.

However, the step from transcendence to Saint was beyond Li Fan's control.

He could only hope that his aunt, after more than thirty reincarnations, would truly bring him some surprises.

"Considering that Aunt might have the opportunity to enter the Shore next, I need to prepare in advance."

"If my guess is correct, the moment she meets the illusory forms of the Nine Saints, Aunt's reincarnation memories will also be exposed, with nowhere to hide. The Nine Saints might connect it to True Reversion and then search the entire Mountains and Seas."

"I need to hide well."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, deducing the various possibilities that might occur after Bai Shuyue entered the Shore.

His greatest confidence was that Bai Shuyue's choice to inherit the memories of her previous life was still in his hands.

If, after True Reversion, he discovered that his secrets had been exposed in the Shore through the guidance of the illusory forms of the Nine Saints,

Then he would not let his aunt inherit the memories and would let her live as an ordinary peasant woman.

He would then find another way to contend with the Saints.

At most, it would be a waste of thirty-plus reincarnations' time.

For his infinite spiritual essence, the cost was negligible.

Recalling the Saint Creation plan, perhaps the only flaw was the figure of Li Fan that shouldn't have appeared on the [Eternal Sail]!

"I have calculated everything flawlessly and have already severed my connection to the Transcendance Path of the Eternal Sail. How could that small boat still reflect my image?"

Fortunately, the connection between that figure and Li Fan was not particularly obvious, and even though the Mountains and Seas were eroded by Dao Annihilation, there were still "infinite" possibilities. Therefore, Bai Shuyue mistook it for another "Li Fan" from a different possibility and did not investigate further, thus failing to expose the flaw.

However, Li Fan, the originator, would not think so simply.

A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan's eyes, and his figure disappeared.

When he reappeared, he was already within the Immortal Embankment of the Guangwu Star Sea.

Having learned the method of [Illusory Form Cheng Dao], compared to the appearance Li Fan had seen before, the Guangwu Immortal Embankment now had nearly three hundred new Heavenly Pillars.

All of them were built with fishing immortal treasures as the foundation. The might of the newly constructed pillars surpassed the old ones.

With so many supports added, the Guangwu Star Sea's ability to resist Dao Annihilation had increased manifold, even vaguely showing a trend similar to Li Fan's previous creation of the "Xuanhuang Immortal Boat" towards transcendence.

"Tsk tsk tsk, it has truly changed a lot."

"However, based on my experience, although it can traverse for a time, it is difficult to endure for a lifetime."

"After all, it is not true transcendence. No matter how high or firm the embankment is built, this immortal embankment will eventually be destroyed by the erosion of Dao Annihilation."

To prevent Bai Shuyue from returning, Li Fan did not alert the Guangwu immortals. He merely commented inwardly and then went to find his target for this trip.

He entered the remnant of the Eternal Sail and stared at the figure on the small boat ahead, his expression unreadable.

"Although it points to me, in reality..."

"It has nothing to do with me."

"I have indeed severed my connection with the Transcendance True Meaning of the Eternal Sail, and the reason my figure appears here is because..."

"True Reversion?!"

"What are you up to?"

Deep doubts arose in Li Fan's heart.

The True Meaning of the Eternal Sail was like a mirror, reflecting the Mountains and Seas.

It connected all beings who understood the Transcendance Path of the Eternal Sail.

Although Li Fan had severed his connection with the True Meaning of the Eternal Sail long ago, he had never imagined that True Reversion still had a faint connection to it.

"With True Reversion's ability, if one deliberately hides oneself, it's impossible to be discovered by a mere Transcendance True Meaning. The reason this figure appears here is perhaps to remind me of something?"

As if to confirm this.

The moment this thought entered Li Fan's mind, the figure resembling him on the Eternal Sail actually nodded slightly towards him.

Then, as if its mission was complete, its aura inexplicably changed.

It still existed, still pointing towards someone in the Mountains and Seas,

But it was no longer related to Li Fan or True Reversion.

"This... what exactly?"

Li Fan closely examined the transformed illusory form and discovered that it now reflected another "Li Fan" from a certain possibility!

Following the connection of fellow travelers in the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan tried to peer into the life of this illusory figure.

"I am certain that just now, he did not exist."

"It was only after I discovered True Reversion's hint that he sprang into existence out of thin air."

"His life, his cultivation path, his experiences, and even his location within the possibilities, were all created from nothing."

"If Aunt investigates later, she won't find anything amiss. It perfectly matches her previous guess. Perhaps she'll even sigh, 'Different lives for different people.'"

Li Fan stared intently at this other, newly born "Li Fan."

"Creation from nothing, this is indeed True Reversion's method. It perfectly compensates for the flaw I might have left."

"But the problem is, why?"

Li Fan frowned deeply.

"And, it could even take the initiative to make up for it. Does this mean True Reversion is slowly waking up from its slumber and even recovering more power?"

Li Fan couldn't help but think so.

Chapter 1658: The Ancient Immortal Reappears

Li Fan attempted to find more clues from the phantom body that had been created from scratch before him. However, it was clear that True Reversion's actions were far beyond what Li Fan could currently decipher. Ultimately, Li Fan could only helplessly give up. “Let’s not dwell on True Reversion’s intentions for now. It’s just compensating for the flaws in my Saint Creation plan. The fact that True Reversion’s power is gradually recovering warrants my vigilance.” The current Li Fan was no longer the past, when he simply regarded True Reversion as his personal cheat. All signs indicated that True Reversion possessed its own independent consciousness, and it was highly likely connected to the so-called “Creator Gods” of the Mountains and Seas. Li Fan vividly remembered the scene when he activated True Reversion at the edge of the Eternal Silence Void. It was as if a terrifying existence had awakened within the Eternal Silence Void, fiercely striking the white mist representing True Reversion. The transformation of true and false was bound, becoming motionless, which was truly terrifying and despairing. “The higher the level of power, the closer one gets to Saints and the Void Realm, the easier it is for True Reversion to be exposed. If not for the heaven-defying ability of [True-False Transformation], which could reverse the Mountains and Seas in an instant, I would have truly fallen into the sight of Saints long ago.” “It could have communicated with me directly, but it insisted on being a riddle-master, hinting indirectly through other methods. Now, it’s even bypassing me directly and influencing the creation of the Mountains and Seas…” “Indeed, only one’s own abilities are truly reliable.” Li Fan narrowed his eyes, suppressing his dissatisfaction with True Reversion. He patiently attempted to communicate with it again. However, True Reversion remained silent as before. Li Fan was helpless. Already feeling restless, he suddenly heard cheers from outside the Guangwu Immortal Embankment. “Thanks to everyone’s hard work, a total of three hundred and ninety-nine new Heavenly Pillars have been completed. After a brief period of rest, we can officially accept the invitation and head to the [Realm of Birth and Death]!” The four words “Realm of Birth and Death” quickly attracted Li Fan’s attention. “Hmm?” Previously, to prevent Bai Shuyue, who was about to transcend, from noticing, Li Fan was not in the original possibility but was hiding in the Mountains and Seas, observing from afar. Moreover, most of his attention was focused on Bai Shuyue, so he hadn’t paid much attention to the events happening in the Guangwu Star Sea. He didn’t expect them to be connected to the Realm of Birth and Death and the Five Lords of the Same Tribulation! “Accepting an invitation?” Li Fan coldly sneered: “They haven’t even reached the realm of transcendence, so how could they catch the eye of the Five Lords of the Same Tribulation? Traveling such a distance, it’s more likely they are walking into a tiger’s den and becoming their sustenance.” But soon, Li Fan realized something was wrong. He was relatively familiar with the people of the Guangwu Star Sea, as he had personally destroyed them once before. They were too weak and had no value for exploitation. Therefore, the Five Lords of the Same Tribulation would generally not take notice of them, let alone send an “invitation.” “But if the invitation is real…” Li Fan couldn’t help but think of the guess that Emperor Tian Luo had successfully led many people to transcendence. “If there is anything about the Guangwu Star Sea that is worthy of the Five Lords of the Same Tribulation’s special attention, perhaps it is their identity as remnant descendants of the Primordial Era.” “Transcending from the Primordial Immortal Realm has benefited later generations, greatly enhancing their potential and spiritual essence…” Li Fan secretly observed Xing Fu, the leader of the Guangwu Immortals, and an idea struck him. The Realm of Birth and Death was an unknown place of extreme danger. Even the Immortal Dao Master had gone in and never returned. As for the Faceless Immortals after the split of Morality, they had tragically died within. Although they were swept away with no resistance under the might of the Saints, for ordinary transcendent experts, it was indeed a dangerous place. Under normal circumstances, Li Fan would not have ventured there without reason. But now, a god-sent opportunity with little risk was laid before him. Furthermore, he was indeed bored waiting for Bai Shuyue’s demise. Since he had nothing else to do, why not go to the Realm of Birth and Death to investigate! “Perhaps I can even figure out why the Faceless Immortal died mysteriously before.” Having made up his mind, Li Fan lightly blew a breath. A smoke-like figure appeared. It had no fixed form, and upon receiving Li Fan’s instructions, it silently drilled into Xing Fu’s body. Xing Fu was merely in the Nameless realm and had no room for resistance against Li Fan’s unfathomable power. The smoke-like figure covered Xing Fu’s soul. “When true becomes false, false also becomes true!” Li Fan chanted leisurely, and the smoke-like figure, originally blank, officially took on Xing Fu’s appearance, like a copied duplicate! The real Xing Fu struggled in vain, utterly unable to resist! He was replaced! From beginning to end, Xing Fu’s external body showed no abnormality. The Guangwu Immortals present did not notice at all that their leader had been replaced without their knowledge. This method of possession was precisely the means Li Fan used to create completely independent clones. It was just that now, the independent clone was replicating Xing Fu, not himself. After a moment, Li Fan adapted to this new body. He searched through Xing Fu’s memories for matters related to the invitation to the Realm of Birth and Death. “So it wasn’t just the Five Lords of the Same Tribulation alone issuing the invitation, but a large-scale, indiscriminate invitation targeting the remnant descendants of the Primordial Era.” “And the one writing the invitation…” Li Fan’s heart skipped a beat: “The Immortal Dao Master of the Primordial Era?” After the destruction of the Primordial Era, some surviving True Immortals lingered in the lower realms, while those with capabilities left the Primordial Era and went to other possibilities, with even some transcendent beings among them. One could say that the remnant descendants of the Primordial Era were everywhere. However, after all, Grandmaster Immortal Dao wrote the “Supreme Dao Scripture,” and more than half of the True Immortals of the Primordial Era had benefited from him. When they sensed the aura of the Immortal Dao Master left on the invitation letter, those willing to attend would definitely be numerous. Xing Fu, the Guangwu Immortal, was one of them. In fact, Xing Fu also had a glorious past. The reason he chose the path of “Xing Fu” was because he was a descendant of an Immortal Emperor! His ancestor was the [Wuji Immortal Emperor] who had a lifespan of ninety-nine million nine hundred and ninety-nine thousand years. After the fall of the Wuji Immortal Emperor, no new ruling Immortal Emperor appeared in the family. Thus, Xing Fu had aspired to revive his ancestor’s great undertaking since childhood. Xing Fu possessed extraordinary talent, and after a thousand years of arduous cultivation, he reached the Nameless realm. With the legacy of his ancestor, if he had accumulated a few tens of thousands more years, he might have truly become the second ruling Immortal Emperor of the family. It was just unfortunate that Dao Annihilation descended, and the Immortal Realm no longer existed. His dream of revival was shattered. At the moment of the apocalypse, Xing Fu fled in disarray. Relying on his Nameless cultivation, he barely survived and came to the lower star sea. However, he did not abandon his cultivation path. He rallied other surviving True Immortals here, forming the Guangwu faction. By using the method of fishing for Dao Annihilation, they collected several Immortal Treasures in hopes of leaving this land of destruction and finding another homeland to rebuild their immortal careers. Until the Immortal Dao Master’s letter arrived, which completely disrupted his plan. His prestige as Xing Fu was naturally incomparable to the Immortal Dao Master. In the Immortal Dao Master’s words, the Realm of Birth and Death was vividly described as a paradise, no less than the Immortal Realm of the past, and it could absolutely serve as a second homeland! The homeless Guangwu Immortals were naturally attracted. Even Xing Fu himself was moved! However, out of instinctual caution, Xing Fu had always harbored doubts about the authenticity of the beautiful world described by the Immortal Dao Master. But all these worries instantly vanished after he personally visited the Realm of Birth and Death! Li Fan carefully examined Xing Fu’s memories of the Realm of Birth and Death. “It is called the Realm of Birth and Death because this realm is the fusion of countless possibilities that have already been destroyed in Dao Annihilation!” A sharp glint flashed in Li Fan’s eyes: “It is not like True Reversion, which creates something from nothing and regenerates from void. Instead, it reconstructs the past memories into reality…” What Xing Fu saw was the Immortal Realm he was familiar with! “Perhaps this is why the Immortal Dao Master chose to remain in the Realm of Birth and Death all along. The Primordial Era was destroyed, and there was no home. Recreating one’s remembered homeland in the Realm of Birth and Death is naturally a good choice.” The scene Xing Fu saw was almost indistinguishable from the true Primordial Immortal Realm. Even Li Fan, observing as an outsider, could not find any flaws. “According to the Immortal Dao Master’s letter, the more past memories are gathered, the more real and stable the imagined possibility will be. If all surviving True Immortals of the Primordial Era can be gathered… perhaps a truly identical possibility can be reproduced! Not just a world, but even the living beings within it!” “This is also the fundamental reason why the Immortal Dao Master sent invitations to the Guangwu Immortals,” Li Fan exclaimed in surprise. This technique of Imaginary Reconstruction naturally could not compare to True Reversion. If a comparison had to be made, it could be considered the Mountain and Sea version of the Immortal Vanquishing Realm! However, the Xuanhuang Realm was merely a small world, small in size. With one person’s strength, perhaps memories could be reproduced. But a single possibility encompassed the vast star seas below and the boundless immortal realm built upon the Mountains and Seas. Even transcendent experts could not see and know everything. Let alone imaginary reconstruction. Perhaps Saints could do this, but it was clear that the Saints of the Mountains and Seas, who adhered to the belief of “irrelevant to the final outcome,” would not waste their energy on such trivial matters. Therefore, people in the Realm of Birth and Death needed to work together, pooling their strengths. It was not just the Primordial Era; every possibility Xing Fu saw in the Realm of Birth and Death represented countless surviving True Immortals of that possibility! “I must say, this is truly an extraordinary and vast power. And it is completely unknown to the public.” “But??” Li Fan snorted coldly: “Even with such a formidable force, after I lured disaster to the other shore and attracted the attention of the Saints of the Shore, they had no power to resist and were instantly annihilated into dust. Only the blank possibility itself remained.” Recalling the Realm of Birth and Death he had seen wiped out before, Li Fan couldn’t help but sigh: “This is the saying, ‘All beings below Saints are like ants’.” “Only by finding a method to counter Saints can one truly stand tall in the Mountains and Seas. Therefore, the Saint Creation Plan must succeed. If Bai Shuyue fails, find someone else! There are countless talented individuals in the Mountains and Seas, and there will always be someone who meets my needs.” Li Fan, having glimpsed the might of Saints again through fragmented clues, secretly made up his mind. After wandering in spirit for a long time, Li Fan’s thoughts returned to the Realm of Birth and Death. “The core of the Immortal Vanquishing Realm is the Supreme Dao Scripture, left behind by the Immortal Dao Master. Perhaps the construction of the Realm of Birth and Death is also related to the Immortal Dao Master.” “The invitation he sent to the Guangwu Immortals was also a means of reception, not directly indicating the specific location of the Realm of Birth and Death in the Mountains and Seas, but directly transporting them there.” “But it only handled the reception, not helping to resist the Dao Annihilation encountered during the passage. This is why the Guangwu Immortals, even after possessing nearly transcendent abilities, only then remembered the Realm of Birth and Death.” “As for the Shuoxing Sea, they also received an invitation from the Immortal Dao Master. The initial discovery of the Shuoxing Sea’s existence by the Guangwu Immortals was precisely due to the Immortal Dao Master’s guidance.” “However, no True Immortal in the Shuoxing Sea knew about this message…” Li Fan pondered, guessing that Cheng Dao must have intercepted the invitation letter and concealed it. Cheng Dao’s master, Old Man Shou Qiu, was one of the Saints of the Shore. He naturally disdained flocking to the Five Lords of the Same Tribulation, nor would he allow his subordinates in the Dao Net to engage in such degenerate acts. “The Realm of Birth and Death, although insignificant in the eyes of Saints, is still worth experiencing for me.” “This method of Imaginary Reconstruction…” “Perhaps it will be of great help to my comprehension of True-False Transformation.” Li Fan pondered, a vague premonition arising in his heart. Although he had already mastered the application of True-False Transformation, Li Fan still needed to rely on the moment when all things transformed from reality to void and then back from void to reality when True Reversion was activated each time to comprehend True-False Transformation. No other treasures in the Mountains and Seas could help him comprehend True-False Transformation. This was something that had always troubled Li Fan. But now, he vaguely glimpsed a turning point. How could he not go and investigate! “Anyway, with this new body, even if I am discovered, my life will not be in danger.” “No, it’s not a new body. I, am Xing Fu!” Within the body, the connection with Li Fan gradually faded completely. It was as if Xing Fu himself was directing the Guangwu Immortals to prepare for their journey to the Realm of Birth and Death. Whether it was his words, actions, or way of thinking, everything was the same as the Xing Fu of the past. Guangwu Immortals noticed no abnormality, and with everything ready, the Immortals united their strength and crushed the invitation letter left by the Immortal Dao Master. Although called an invitation letter, it had no physical form but existed as a line of text in Xing Fu’s memory. Moreover, the Immortal Dao Master’s methods came with concealment abilities. If an outsider looked at it with common soul-searching or memory-sensing techniques, they could not see the characters left by the Immortal Dao Master. Only Xing Fu, “himself,” could clearly remember and recall them. Thus, Li Fan had scoured the Guangwu Star Sea several times without discovering the existence of this invitation. This time, Li Fan used his True Reversion clone to possess Xing Fu, thus becoming Xing Fu himself. He was able to learn about the connection between the Guangwu Immortals and the Realm of Birth and Death by chance. As the line of characters in Xing Fu’s memory turned from void to reality, appearing in the real world. It was as if an unfathomable mystical power descended. It transformed into a thin line visible only to Xing Fu, pointing directly into the depths of the Mountains and Seas! “This direction is indeed the location of the Realm of Birth and Death!”

Chapter 1659: Imaginary Renewal of the Immortal Realm

Like a fisherman casting his line, he suddenly reeled it in.

From the other end of the thin line, immense power surged forth.

"Everyone, stand firm!"

With Xing Fu's low cry, the entire Guangwu Star Sea was pulled by this force, forcibly detached from its original possibility.

And shot towards the direction indicated by the thin line!

Upon entering the Mountains and Seas, the all-pervading Dao Annihilation instantly arrived.

Compared to the situation under the protection of possibility, this was truly a tumultuous tide!

In an instant, the peripheral areas of the Guangwu Star Sea were completely engulfed.

The immortals, however, had anticipated this and paid no attention.

Gathered within the Immortal Embankment, they stared with tense expressions at the numerous Heavenly Pillars within the embankment.

Turbulent waves ceaselessly struck the Immortal Embankment.

Hundreds of Heavenly Pillars trembled, affecting the hearts of all the immortals.

Fortunately, with the blessings of numerous immortal treasures, the stability of the Immortal Embankment was unprecedented. It ultimately withstood the external pressure of Dao Annihilation, allowing the Immortal Embankment to remain unmighty despite the surrounding Dao Annihilation erosion.

The Guangwu immortals, seeing this, finally breathed a sigh of relief and erupted in cheers.

"Do not be careless; there is still a long time before we reach our destination." Xing Fu, as the leader of the immortals, reminded them sternly at this moment.

He then arranged for the immortals to take turns monitoring the condition of the Immortal Embankment.

The rest of the group, however, jointly observed the Mountains and Seas and exchanged insights!

This journey to the Realm of Birth and Death, although initiated by an invitation, the Guangwu immortals knew that the treatment they would receive in the future would be directly proportional to their own strength.

And traversing in the Mountains and Seas was generally a realm accessible only to transcendent experts.

This was truly an opportunity not to be missed!

Thus, all the immortals were fully devoted to cultivation and comprehension.

Moreover, they offered mutual assistance, sharing their insights without reservation.

In hopes of progressing together.

Time flows like water in the Mountains and Seas.

With the guidance of Ascended Dao Immortal, the Guangwu Star Sea traversed at a considerable speed.

After adding three more True Immortals at the Nameless realm, they finally reached their destination.

The pulling force of the thin line, at the last moment, seemed to reach its peak.

As if being pulled out of its original possibility, it was now roughly stuffed into this new, unknown land.

After a flash of distorted and colorful light.

Outside the Immortal Embankment, the aura of Dao Annihilation had vanished.

In its place was a vast vitality that the immortals had not felt for a long time!

If the vitality of Shuoxing and Guangwu Seas were scattered candle flames, then the vitality contained in their surroundings was like the bright moon in the sky.

Completely incomparable!

Having stayed in the barren land of Primal for so long, arriving here suddenly, the Guangwu immortals were all stunned.

Some found it hard to believe.

In their brief daze, a True Immortal, unable to contain himself, shed tears on the spot.

"Wait! This aura..."

"Why is it so familiar?"

"Are we dreaming?"

A while later, a True Immortal finally reacted and exclaimed.

One stone stirred a thousand waves.

"Did my eyes deceive me? Isn't this the Celestial Realm's Cangtian Star Domain?"

"This is where I made my fortune! I have looked back at it countless nights in my memories. How could I possibly mistake it!"

"Could it be that we have returned to the time before the Primal Era was destroyed?"

The immortals discussed amongst themselves, full of doubt, looking at Xing Fu for an answer.

Although they had all seen the invitation letter from Ascended Dao Immortal, only Xing Fu had seen the Realm of Birth and Death beforehand and knew its specifics.

Xing Fu looked at the immortals' expressions of mixed joy and surprise, smiled faintly, and began to explain.

"Elders, you are not mistaken! The second home that Ascended Dao Immortal spoke of, which is perfectly suited for us, is indeed the Immortal Realm we were once so familiar with!"

Xing Fu slowly recounted the story of the Realm of Birth and Death being conceptually reconstructed from memory.

The immortals were even more astonished.

"Creating something from nothing, what kind of divine ability is this?"

"Now that you mention it, I do have some perception. The general scenery is consistent with the Cangtian Star Domain, but the overall number and quality of life forms are still lacking. Most notably, there are no ruling Immortals of the Star Domain, nor the majestic aura of their True Immortals."

"It is indeed somewhat imperfect. But isn't this exactly what we need? With our participation, perhaps we can truly recreate the Immortal Realm!"

The immortals discussed enthusiastically. They had never been so excited since the destruction of the Immortal Realm.

Xing Fu, however, did not participate in the discussion but continuously scanned his surroundings.

Trying to find the trace of Ascended Dao Immortal.

Logically, since Ascended Dao Immortal had guided them here, he should have appeared by now.

But he was nowhere to be seen.

Being new arrivals, Xing Fu did not dare to wander around recklessly.

He could only restrain the immortals and wait patiently in place.

Time passed. Three years later, in the Cangtian Star Domain.

Someone finally arrived late.

"Jiu Xuan?"

Someone recognized the newcomer and exclaimed in surprise.

"Weren't you killed by Dao Annihilation back then! How are you resurrected?"

As if he had expected the immortals' reaction, Jiu Xuan smiled faintly: "The me of the past did indeed perish in Dao Annihilation. But the me of today was conceptually created from your memories by your venerables, and I have no memories of dying back then."

Jiu Xuan's words undoubtedly confirmed Xing Fu's account of the Realm of Birth and Death, causing an uproar.

"All who come to the Realm of Birth and Death are settled according to their original place of origin."

"This place is our former homeland."

"Like a stream, while the Realm of Birth and Death contains countless such conceptual reconstructions, like myriad rivers converging, there are countless of them!" Jiu Xuan said proudly.

"However, for some reason, it is inconvenient to take you on a tour. Of course, if your strength reaches transcendence, or if you make outstanding contributions to conceptual reconstruction, you might be received by the venerables and get a glimpse of the true face of the Realm of Birth and Death."

The experience after arriving in the Realm of Birth and Death was somewhat different from what the Guangwu immortals had imagined.

There was no exclusion, nor was there a warm welcome.

They were simply settled in their former homeland, left to fend for themselves to some extent.

Especially after saying a few simple words, Jiu Xuan seemed to have urgent matters to attend to and left in a hurry.

Seeing the immortals' disappointment, Xing Fu had to speak up to encourage them.

"Elders, don't be discouraged! Haven't we achieved our goal now?"

"We have escaped the troubles of Dao Annihilation and have a new homeland where we can settle safely."

"Everything will proceed step by step! As fellow Daoist Jiu Xuan said, it's not mandatory to contribute to conceptual reconstruction; you can just go with the flow. If anyone has the ability and is willing to contribute, that would be even better."

The immortals felt somewhat relieved.

"It's just that we didn't even get to meet Ascended Dao Immortal, which is still a bit disappointing," the immortals said regretfully.

After all, they had come here because of Ascended Dao Immortal's invitation letter, and now Ascended Dao Immortal had never shown himself, naturally leading to a sense of unmet expectations.

Some who were unwilling immediately began to study the method of [conceptual reconstruction] that Jiu Xuan had mentioned before he left.

Conceptual reconstruction required a yellow crystal as a medium, which reflected the entire world.

The power of the yellow crystal radiated to all conceptualized possibilities, present everywhere.

However, it was imperceptible to outsiders; only through special techniques could it be sensed.

The method was simple enough, and the immortals spontaneously activated it, raising their heads.

Indeed, they saw the yellow crystal in the sky, like a great sun.

It emitted a warm and hazy light, illuminating countless beings within the possibilities.

"Everything we see is born from this? Truly incredible."

"Pouring one's mind into it, recalling past memories..."

Following Jiu Xuan's instructions, the immortals began to attempt reconstruction.

Xing Fu, however, was extremely cautious and chose to observe for the time being.

There were no imagined conspiracies. After completing a round of conceptual recall, the immortals only felt mentally fatigued, with no other abnormal conditions.

After resting for a while, they quickly recovered.

As if addicted, they immediately plunged into another round of conceptual construction.

"I understand now. Conceptual reconstruction is like 'Myriad Immortals Painting'! After all, everyone's memories are different, so the scenery of the Immortal Realm from memory will naturally have some discrepancies."

"And this yellow crystal can record and compare all our conceptual memories. The parts that are completely identical can be used as the foundation for conceptual reconstruction!"

Among the immortals of the Guangwu Star Sea who had survived the great calamity of the Immortal Realm's destruction, none were foolish. They quickly grasped the basic principles of [conceptual reconstruction].

Thus, they became even more inspired.

After all, being able to personally paint the finishing strokes for the reconstruction of their homeland was truly an honor.

Everyone followed suit, and Xing Fu naturally couldn't just watch.

He poured his spiritual consciousness into the yellow crystal in the sky, recalling the details of the Immortal Realm from the past.

There was no need to consider how to conceptually construct it; the warm light of the yellow crystal guided everything.

As if it were a natural process, a past scene appeared vividly.

Xing Fu stared at his own creation. After a moment, above and below the painting, countless overlaps appeared.

All these paintings depicted the same scene.

But they all had subtle differences.

With flashes of light, these paintings began to be compressed and merged together.

All the redundant lines in the painting were preserved.

And their "differences" were erased.

Ultimately, Xing Fu's magnificent masterpiece was reduced to a few strokes, becoming an inconspicuous speck of light, which then flew into the yellow crystal above.

As that wisp of light was absorbed, Xing Fu felt as if a trace of power had been drawn from his body.

Carefully savoring the disappeared part, Xing Fu discovered that it was not immortal energy, physical strength, nor soul power.

Instead, it was a source of power that was inexplicable and only related to [conceptualization].

"It seems the Realm of Birth and Death truly has no malice."

"It is truly working to reconstruct the lost possibilities of the past."

"Of course, this is only a preliminary conclusion."

Within the Realm of Birth and Death, there was no quantifiable measure of contribution.

Even with repeated conceptual reconstructions, there were no additional rewards.

It was driven solely by one's own passion.

The vast majority of True Immortals lost their motivation after trying a few times and became disheartened.

They settled in the reconstructed Immortal Realm star domain, finding a place to live and cultivating on their own.

Only a very small number, without reservation, continued to contribute their conceptual power every so often.

Not for anything else.

Only to do their part in reconstructing their homeland.

Xing Fu was among them.

Days turned into weeks, weeks into months.

Since their arrival, Jiu Xuan and the other inhabitants of the Realm of Birth and Death had not reappeared.

Gradually, most of them almost forgot about them and subconsciously accepted this place as their former homeland in the Immortal Realm.

Only the True Immortals who occasionally performed conceptual reconstruction remembered the true situation here.

The yellow crystal in the sky seemed unchanging, as if for ten thousand years.

The persistent conceptual reconstructions of the Guangwu immortals had no effect on it.

After more than six hundred conceptual reconstructions, Xing Fu stared at the countless paintings presented before him, a strange feeling suddenly arising in his heart.

The "common" paintings created by the united efforts of the immortals of the Realm of Birth and Death served as the blueprint for the reconstruction of this place.

Although the Immortal Realm created based on this blueprint was extremely similar to the homeland in their memories,

Xing Fu always felt that there was some fundamental difference between the two.

This sense of disharmony had lingered in Xing Fu's heart since his arrival in the Realm of Birth and Death.

As time passed, instead of fading,

It grew stronger.

"Where exactly is the problem?"

Xing Fu frowned, ignoring his mental fatigue, and performed another conceptual reconstruction.

The result was still the same.

The process of conceptual reconstruction went smoothly, but as countless paintings were superimposed and compressed into points of light that flew into the yellow crystal.

That discordant feeling surged in Xing Fu's heart again.

"Again!"

Xing Fu, somewhat unwilling, continued to perform conceptual reconstruction again and again.

With each repeated conceptual reconstruction, Xing Fu's vitality seemed to be drained.

His True Immortal body, however, grew increasingly gaunt.

But Xing Fu's eyes grew brighter and brighter.

There was no sign of fatigue.

It was as if he had glimpsed some profound secret, and he couldn't stop the excitement.

"So that's how it is. Our Immortal Realm in memory differs subtly from the Immortal Realm that truly existed in the Mountains and Seas!"

"How did the Immortal Realm perish? It was due to the erosion of the Dao Annihilation tribulation!"

"The Dao Annihilation devoured everything, and the Immortal Realm ceased to exist. Perhaps it even took away our ability to remember forever..."

Xing Fu performed another conceptual reconstruction.

Recalling everything in detail, guided by the yellow crystal, he formed a magnificent picture of the Immortal Realm.

But...

This painting itself was incomplete.

It was as if an invisible hand had smudged certain parts of the painting, erasing some details.

"These missing parts are..."

"The traces left by Dao Annihilation."

Li Fan reached out and slowly caressed the abnormal parts of the painting he sensed.

It was as if he was personally touching Dao Annihilation.

At this very moment...

The yellow crystal in the sky suddenly erupted with an incredibly brilliant radiance, its brightness even surpassing all other scenes within this possibility.

But apart from Xing Fu, all other beings were blind to it.

Endless light descended, enveloping Xing Fu.

Under the warm embrace, it seemed to be taking him to another place.

A vague premonition arose in his heart. Xing Fu did not resist.

The yellow radiance engulfed him.

When he opened his eyes again...

Eight figures sat around him.

"Five Concurrent Calamity Saints, Ascended Dao Immortal!"

Xing Fu's heart recognized the identities of two of the figures, respectively.

Chapter 1660: The Primordial Birth of Mountains and Seas

"I didn't expect that the one awakened this time wouldn't even be at the Transcendent realm..."

"Truly, heaven favors our Realm of Birth and Death!"

The speaker was not one of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables or Dao Scribe Immortal, but one of the remaining two figures. He had white hair and a white beard but appeared youthful.

He looked at Xing Fu, surrounded by everyone, with a hint of excitement.

"Seniors, what exactly..."

Xing Fu first bowed towards Dao Scribe Immortal, then paid his respects to the others in turn. At the same time, he asked with confusion, "Could it be that what I experienced before was not real, but an illusion?"

"A test for us?"

This time, the answer came from one of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables. His form flickered, like rolling crimson clouds stretching for countless miles, ablaze with fiery destruction.

Observing his form, one could understand his path, and so Xing Fu knew his identity: [Jin Xiao].

As Jin Xiao's words fell upon Xing Fu's ears, his body felt a slight scorching sensation, as if he were truly being roasted by flames.

"Of course, it wasn't an illusion. The immortal realm you were in before was indeed a construct of imagination, a real existence. Of course, you can return at any time."

As Jin Xiao spoke, below everyone, a flowing river-like projection quietly appeared. It displayed the Primordial Immortal Realm, including the Cangtian Star Domain. Xing Fu could even vaguely see the Immortals of the Guangwu group within it.

"It's just that the divine ability of conceptual construction is not perfected. The possibility that was reproduced still has fatal flaws. It appears as solid as rock, no different from a true possibility. In reality... "

Another flowing river projection appeared side by side.

It was as real as the Primordial Immortal Realm.

But after a moment...

The veil of "reality" covering it suddenly peeled away. Like a painting doused in water, the paint faded, and the artwork vanished. Within the flowing river projection, a terrifying tribulation descended.

It was an apocalypse that could nearly rival the Tribulation of Dao Annihilation,

Even the speed at which this tribulation destroyed possibilities was faster than Dao Annihilation's engulfment.

Dao Annihilation required gradual erosion, but here, the foundation of the flowing river projection disappeared, and it disintegrated in an instant.

That possibility, along with the countless beings within it, was buried in the blink of an eye.

Witnessing the tragic scene, it seemed to stir Xing Fu's memories of the destruction of the Primordial Immortal Realm, and his expression became somewhat stiff.

"This apocalyptic scene was not fabricated. It was a real event that happened not long ago in the Realm of Birth and Death."

The words of another of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables made Xing Fu's heart tremble.

As he heard the words, Xing Fu seemed to hear the clashing of countless weapons, followed by the sound of them all breaking.

Thus, Xing Fu also learned of this Venerable's identity: [Feng Cang].

"Since you have awakened, you must also know why the flaw in the method of conceptual construction has arisen."

Xing Fu nodded in response: "It's because of the characteristics of Dao Annihilation."

Feng Cang continued: "Possibilities are born within the Mountains and Seas, like pictures drawn on a sandy beach by the sea.

"The waves of Dao Annihilation wash them away. Among them, those with residual traces are the anchors of our memories. As for those places that are completely blank..."

"They are the foundation stones of our conceptual constructs that we can no longer recall and have been truly erased from the Mountains and Seas."

"Possibilities are born from the great power of the Mountains and Seas. Their fundamental essence is not something that we can yet comprehend. We can only imitate, and it must be flawless."

"If a few strokes are missing, it's like a tiger painted without dog-like attributes. It's worlds apart from a true possibility and can crumble at any moment."

Feng Cang waved his hand, and several flowing river projections appeared. They were almost identical to true possibilities, but after existing for different durations, they all eventually failed to hold on and returned to nothingness.

Xing Fu became somewhat anxious upon hearing this: "Then aren't the Guangwu Immortals who came with me in danger?"

This time, it was another of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables who smiled.

He spoke to comfort Xing Fu: "You don't need to worry about that. Although the collapse of conceptual constructs might seem instantaneous to you, the Realm of Birth and Death is entirely within our perception. Before the tribulation occurs, we will sense it and rescue them in advance."

Xing Fu breathed a sigh of relief upon hearing this.

However, the pressure in his heart never dissipated. It wasn't from the truth of the Realm of Birth and Death, but from the words of the Venerable himself.

As the words still echoed in his ears, Xing Fu seemed to face an abyss.

The abyss was unfathomable, formless, and shapeless.

And anyone who witnessed it would uncontrollably fall into it.

"Yuan Zang." Thus, Xing Fu learned of this Venerable's identity.

Fortunately, Yuan Zang did not make things difficult for Xing Fu and retracted his pervasive power.

The invisible pressure in Xing Fu's heart slowly dissipated.

"Venerables, since the method of conceptual construction has such flaws, is there a solution?"

He did not question why the Immortals were placed in conceptual possibilities, performing useless tasks. Instead, he directly inquired about the solution.

The white-haired young man burst into laughter upon hearing this: "As expected of someone who awakened before Transcending, his thoughts and aspirations are beyond reach of ordinary people. Maintaining conceptual constructs consumes immense resources. If we didn't see a solution, why would we be so persistent?"

"Those like you, who can pass the test, are the solution!" the white-haired young man said solemnly.

"Me?" Xing Fu recalled the various sensations he had experienced in the Primordial conceptual realm and faintly understood something.

"Dao Annihilation erases cleanly and thoroughly. We cannot track Dao Annihilation, but we can sense the difference between a conceptual construct and a true possibility. That subtle feeling of disharmony!"

"Through continuous construction and repeated fine-tuning, until..."

Xing Fu suddenly understood and blurted out: "The feeling of disharmony disappears. This means that the possibility constructed conceptually is exactly the same as the possibility that truly existed back then."

"Although we cannot see the white, we can infer it from the identifiable parts. I see now!"

The white-haired young man smiled and did not continue.

It was clear that Xing Fu's guess was very close to the truth.

"Your personal premonition is still lacking. We need to jointly deliberate and anchor it." Dao Scribe Immortal finally spoke at this moment.

Xing Fu was very respectful of this senior with a illustrious reputation. He tidied his expression and listened to the teachings.

"In the past, even holding the Supreme Dao Scripture, I could not fully comprehend the principles of the Immortal Realm. Everyone's cognition has its limitations. Therefore, more diverse perspectives are needed." Dao Scribe Immortal spoke sparingly, offering only these two sentences before falling silent.

"Conceptual construction doesn't necessarily need to be exactly identical to what existed in memory. What can be confirmed now is that the closer it is, the higher the reliability of the conceptual construct. And the lower the probability of instant collapse." Yuan Zang continued to supplement.

"By filling in these 'gaps' erased by Dao Annihilation, we can perfectly restore the foundation stones of the possibilities of the Mountains and Seas. This is the source of the Mountains and Seas' fundamental power, and also the focus of Dao Annihilation's plundering after the fusion of the Mountains and Seas."

"Conceptually reconstructing past possibilities is acting in accordance with the current situation. Through this, we can glimpse the mysteries of Dao Annihilation, or more accurately, the mysteries of [God], which is what we truly seek." Yuan Zang's words were astonishing.

"God?" Xing Fu was startled and then somewhat confused.

"May I ask, Venerables, what is this so-called [God]?" he asked cautiously.

The Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death seemed to regard Xing Fu with great importance, answering all his questions.

Dao Scribe Immortal wrote a few scenes with a few strokes.

"Someone once walked to the end of the Mountains and Seas and witnessed the scene of the Mountains and Seas' birth. Its form was unfathomable, its scene indescribable, its momentum imperceptible, and its appearance undefinable."

"It cannot be described in words or recorded in text or images."

"That person could not convey what exactly happened in the Mountains and Seas, but they made one point clear. Mountains and Seas both originated from [God]."

"That person then walked to the end of the Mountains and Seas and saw the future where the Mountains and Seas perished and returned to [Stars]."

"The boundless and infinite characteristic of Mountains and Seas was stolen from [God]. Although it has operated for countless years, it is ultimately not the power of the Mountains and Seas themselves. Born from God, it will eventually return to God. This is the destined outcome for the Mountains and Seas."

The beginning of the Mountains and Seas, the end of the Mountains and Seas.

Two scenes floated before Xing Fu.

The amount of information was too overwhelming, and Xing Fu was momentarily stunned, seeming unable to accept it.

"God, Stars. The beginning of creation, the end of the Mountains and Seas."

He muttered, suddenly seeming to understand something, and his face turned pale: "If this is the case for the Mountains and Seas, then we beings born within the Mountains and Seas, wouldn't we too..."

"This is the essence of 'irrelevant to the final outcome.' All our attempts to save ourselves are like jokes in the face of God's unfathomable power. Ultimately, it will be in vain."

"Is that so?" The white-haired youth suddenly counter-questioned.

"Hmm?" Xing Fu was immediately at a loss for words.

"Of course not," he then said without thinking, as if struck by inspiration.

Upon hearing this, the white-haired youth burst into hearty laughter.

The other Venerables present also smiled.

Dao Scribe Immortal even nodded slightly and said, "Good."

Xing Fu was somewhat confused by the reactions of the Venerables.

The white-haired youth then continued, "The outcome of the Mountains and Seas seems predetermined. However, Stars are ultimately not God. The Mountains and Seas will flow for an eternity and will not simply sit and wait for death."

"Everything is still undecided. In the end, whether it is the Mountains and Seas, the Stars, or even..."

"Us beings from the Mountains and Seas who emerge victorious. These are all unknowns!" the white-haired youth said with absolute certainty.

"We beings, though born in the Mountains and Seas, also possess the ability to comprehend the Dao. The more power we acquire from the Mountains and Seas, the weaker the Mountains and Seas and the Stars will become. The Saints on the Shore are attempting to connect the broken Mountains and Seas with a spark of life, their figures covering the beginning and end of the Mountains and Seas. While saving the Mountains and Seas, they also aim to achieve parity with the Mountains and Seas."

"Emperor Taiwei, with his own great power, reflects infinite possibilities, like a parasitic seed eroding the Mountains and Seas. Even if he cannot ultimately contend with the Mountains and Seas, perhaps he can forcibly detach himself from the Mountains and Seas and establish his own domain."

...

The Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death detailed the paths of the two major forces within the Mountains and Seas for Xing Fu.

Xing Fu had not even reached Transcending yet, and to suddenly hear so many secrets, he felt dizzy and dazzled.

"The power of Saints is truly unimaginable, and their plans are not something we can shake. But the weak also have their ways of survival. Conceptual construction, to glimpse the secrets of Dao Annihilation, is our confidence in overcoming the strong!"

Of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, [Sheng Shi], who had remained silent until now, slowly spoke.

As Sheng Shi opened his mouth, Xing Fu felt as if his life force was being drained, and his body began to turn cold. He couldn't help but shiver.

He exhaled, and frost formed, appearing in the air.

However, Sheng Shi was clearly restraining his power and did not pose a real threat to Xing Fu.

"Those 'blanks' erased by Dao Annihilation, the foundation stones of the Mountains and Seas, are, in our view, the main point of contention between the Mountains and Seas and the Stars."

"Deifying the Mountains and Seas, turning the Mountains and Seas into Stars, some things are easy, some are constant."

"In the flow of the Mountains and Seas, what remains immutable is true great power!"

"If one can glimpse it..."

"Even an ant can transform one day and achieve parity with the Mountains and Seas!"

"Parity with the Mountains and Seas." Xing Fu's lips moved, repeating these four words.

Before Xing Fu could ponder further, he heard Dao Scribe Immortal ask, "Do you know of Duke Shou Qiu?"

Xing Fu naturally nodded: "The virtuous reputation of Duke Shou Qiu is known throughout the Immortal Realm, to everyone."

"Then do you know that Duke Shou Qiu is one of the Saints on the Shore?"

"Is that so?" This time, Xing Fu was so shocked he couldn't speak.

"When Duke Shou Qiu was guarding the Immortal Realm back then, I also saw him. Observing his destiny and fortune. Nameless was his limit. Yet after many years, he surprisingly has the potential for Transcending and Sainthood. Do you know why?" Dao Scribe Immortal asked calmly.

"..."

Xing Fu naturally did not know Duke Shou Qiu's background.

But recalling what the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death had said earlier, inspiration struck him, and he couldn't help but boldly guess: "Could it be that Duke Shou Qiu found that immutable great power of the Mountains and Seas?"

Dao Scribe Immortal nodded.

"He upholds the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas, which is [Eternal Life]!"

"[Eternal Life]."

These two words seemed to possess infinite magic. Xing Fu repeatedly murmured them.

"I wonder, how does this Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas differ from the ordinary Dao paths we wield?"

Dao Scribe Immortal waved his hand, and a long scroll suddenly unfurled before Xing Fu.

Originally, it should have contained countless characters, but now, all those characters seemed to have vanished, leaving only a blank scroll.

"Ordinary Great Daos are born in the Mountains and Seas, merely an evolution of the Mountains and Seas themselves."

"But the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas..."

"Like Eternal Life of Duke Shou Qiu, perhaps it was inherited from [God]. But the part that was not fully absorbed and transformed."

"All Dao paths in the Mountains and Seas can almost be seen as an extension of [God]'s power. However, what we can access is only the part that has been assimilated by the Mountains and Seas."

"Only a select few retain the nature of [God]."

Dao Scribe Immortal attempted to write something on the blank scroll.

However, he lifted his brush several times, only to stop midway.

In the end, he couldn't write a single word. He sighed and rolled up the blank scroll.

"The method of conceptual construction, to glimpse the secrets of the Mountains and Seas."

"These secrets refer to the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas!"

"Those mysterious powers that have undergone the trials of the Mountains and Seas and will eventually return to [God]!"

Chapter 1661: Wonderful Method of the End of Time

"Merely by imagining, one can glimpse the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas."

The scene depicted by Ming Dao Immortal deeply shook Xing Fu.

But he immediately felt dejected: "Even transcendence is difficult for me to achieve. How can I hope to glimpse this Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas? Perhaps esteemed seniors can do it, but I..."

At this moment, the last of the Concurrent Calamity Venerables reprimanded him, interrupting, "When Duke Shou Qiu obtained the Great Dao of Eternal Life, his strength was not even as great as yours! Who says you cannot?"

"Whether one can attain the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas depends entirely on personal fortune and opportunity, with little correlation to individual strength. Perhaps even a mortal can control the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas! Why can we not?"

As the words fell, Xing Fu felt the surroundings grow dim.

As if falling into Dao Oblivion, isolated from the vitality and light of the Mountains and Seas.

Xing Fu thus learned his honorific title: Guang Mo.

Not daring to retort, he could only force a smile and say, "Seniors' teachings are correct."

The Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death calamities all knew that Xing Fu was still not speaking his true mind and merely laughed.

However, they could understand; this concept was completely contrary to the fundamental cultivation systems within the Mountains and Seas.

Ming Dao Immortal spoke again: "This matter is not our blind optimism. First, as Guang Mo said, there are precedents in the Mountains and Seas. Second..."

"There have indeed been signs of other unknown Grand Daos of Mountains and Seas appearing in our probability. However, we were unable to capture them. They vanished without a trace thereafter, and we have heard no news."

"And the location where that Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas appeared was not in the Immortal Realm, but in the star sea of the lower realm."

This was the first time Xing Fu had heard such a secret. He was both surprised and confused.

"Before reaching the Nameless realm, in the face of the Mountains and Seas, we are all ants that can be ignored. What is the difference between transcendence and mortals? It's all a matter of personal fortune and opportunity," Ming Dao Immortal chuckled.

After this explanation, Xing Fu finally managed to accept it, albeit reluctantly.

However, new questions welled up in his heart: "Duke Shou Qiu came from our homeland. Besides him, there's news of another Grand Dao of Eternal Life appearing? Could it be that the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas is not actually rare? Otherwise, why would they all appear in the same probability?"

"Perhaps it is merely a coincidence. Or perhaps..." Ming Dao Immortal exchanged glances with the other Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death calamities and slowly said, "It is precisely because Duke Shou Qiu obtained the Great Dao of Eternal Life that it attracted the appearance of another Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas."

"Hmm?" This was something Xing Fu had never considered, and he was instantly stunned.

"Do birds of a feather flock together?"

"Yes, that can be understood this way. In fact, there are very few remaining Grand Daos of Mountains and Seas. Moreover, if one is adorned with the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, it is extremely easy to hide oneself. Others can hardly detect it. Unless one actively reveals it like Duke Shou Qiu, even Saints cannot track them down."

"So it was truly fortunate that two Grand Daos of Mountains and Seas appeared in our homeland back then," Ming Dao Immortal sighed slightly.

"It's a pity it was all for naught. The Immortal Realm was ultimately destroyed," Xing Fu also sighed.

"Destroyed... not necessarily," Ming Dao Immortal's tone shifted.

Xing Fu blinked, about to ask further, but Ming Dao Immortal bypassed the topic.

"Compared to the Shore and the Saintly Dynasty, the Realm of Birth and Death is indeed somewhat weaker. But unlike their philosophy of [Irrelevant to the Final Outcome], we still have feelings for our former homeland."

"The method of ideation can save a destroyed homeland. At the same time, it can be used to search for traces of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas. It is a plan with multiple benefits. Therefore, compared to other forces in the Mountains and Seas, we also have our unique advantages."

"However, the Dao of Mountains and Seas is of great importance, and only awakened individuals like you are qualified to know. Others, whether they live peacefully or assist in conceptual construction, are up to them. We will not force them," Guang Mo spoke articulately.

Xing Fu lowered his head and said, "Your Venerable Mercies!"

"May I dare to ask, esteemed seniors, how many 'awakened ones' like myself are there in the Realm of Birth and Death?"

"There are not many to speak of, nor few. Including you, excluding us, there are twenty-three. You will meet them later," Guang Mo replied.

Upon hearing this, Xing Fu was secretly startled.

From the Venerables' previous words, it seemed that the previous awakened ones were all at the transcendent realm.

Including the Venerables, the strength of the Realm of Birth and Death was indeed not to be underestimated.

"Do you have any other questions? You may ask them all at once. After all, we will not always have time to see you in the future."

After a moment of thought, Xing Fu shook his head.

"Very well. Next, we will bestow upon you the true divine ability of conceptual construction. This is the key to touching and sketching the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas; you must comprehend it carefully!" Ming Dao Immortal said in a deep voice.

With that, the figures of the eight Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death calamities vanished from Xing Fu's sight.

In their place, a radiant yellow crystal appeared.

It was very similar to what Xing Fu had seen in the Primal Immortal Realm of ideation.

But it was even more complex.

On every facet of the crystal, countless lights and shadows seemed to flicker.

And upon closer inspection, each facet seemed to be infinitely divisible, endless.

Xing Fu's spirit was captivated, and the voices of the Venerables also echoed in his ears simultaneously.

"The method of ideational reconstruction originates from that Walker of Mountains and Seas."

"He himself was not the original creator of this divine ability. The true origin comes from the last prodigy among our cultivators in the final epoch of the Mountains and Seas."

"At that time, only one possibility remained stubbornly supporting itself in the Mountains and Seas, which was the hope of all surviving beings in the Mountains and Seas."

"All the Saints perished in the years of battling Dao Oblivion."

"Even in such desperate circumstances, we cultivators did not give up. Astonishing figures still emerged, truly the last dirge of our beings."

"And the creator of the method of ideational construction was the most dazzling star among them. Her talent was so high that she even surpassed that Walker of Mountains and Seas. And it was precisely with his help that the Walker of Mountains and Seas was able to go from the end of the Mountains and Seas to the beginning, and safely traverse the Eternal Void."

After explaining the origin of the divine ability and the method, Xing Fu seemed to see the flickering images of the end of the Mountains and Seas within this infinitely faceted yellow crystal.

Each facet reflected the traces left by possibilities that had once existed in the Mountains and Seas.

An infinite number of possibilities converged at the end of time.

At the moment of the Mountains and Seas' annihilation, they transformed into a radiant yellow gem.

By observing its traces, one could recall one's own memories.

By touching the scene and evoking emotions, comparing the two.

Reappearing from emptiness, reconstructing from ideation.

"Immensely profound!"

Xing Fu exclaimed loudly, unable to contain his excitement.

The yellow crystal suddenly erupted with countless beams of light, filling his entire vision and perception, and then disappeared into Xing Fu's sea of consciousness.

When Xing Fu could see again, the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death calamities had vanished.

Below him, thousands of river phantoms stood side by side, roaring and surging.

More than a dozen figures hovered above them, seemingly observing something.

Xing Fu could sense the aura of ideational construction occasionally flashing from them.

As for the Venerables...

They did not seem to be in this space.

Although Xing Fu had become an awakened one, the Realm of Birth and Death calamities did not have mandatory missions.

Everything was carried out according to one's own will.

Of course, if one could contribute to the search for the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, the Venerables would not be stingy with rewards.

Whether it was discussing cultivation with the Venerables themselves, or the Venerables personally helping to stabilize the homeland of ideation, as long as the demands were not excessive, the Venerables would satisfy them.

Xing Fu had indeed wondered, if he were to truly sketch the appearance of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, who would ultimately possess this path to the heavens?

Would the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death calamities turn on each other and fight for it?
