However, without the Venerables' explanation, Xing Fu soon understood on his own.

The Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas could not be snatched or seized.

It all depended on one's own fortune and opportunity.

In the Realm of Birth and Death, who ultimately controlled the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas was not the key. The key was that the cultivators of the Realm of Birth and Death controlled the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

"In other words, everyone has the chance to achieve transcendence like Duke Shou Qiu." As this thought arose, Xing Fu's fighting spirit surged.

Without resting, he activated the method of ideation and began to sketch and compare.

Ideational construction, repeated comparison, to explore the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

This action was like sketching one painting after another.

In the beginning, one might still feel novelty.

But gradually, one would begin to feel bored.

Because one would discover that as one slowly approached the truth, no matter how many paintings were replicated, all these paintings would be identical.

There would be no difference.

How could what was erased by Dao Oblivion be so easily deciphered and reproduced?

It could only be achieved through accidental flashes of inspiration in repeated attempts.

"No wonder there are twenty-three awakened ones, but only sixteen here," Xing Fu vaguely understood.

Those people had seen no hope and chosen to give up.

The choices of others did not affect Xing Fu.

As if tireless, he continued to perform ideational construction repeatedly. Relying on his keen intuition and memories of the past, he conscientiously compared them.

Although each repetition yielded no results and was extremely tedious,

He found joy in it.

Immersed in it, he lost track of time.

New awakened ones arrived, and those in despair gave up.

Xing Fu always stood above the surging river phantoms, creating painting after painting.

But...

Heaven's Dao does not always reward diligence, and effort does not always yield results.

Even with Xing Fu's tireless attempts, he made no progress.

The Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas was like an invisible ghost.

No matter what method was used, it was impossible to capture it.

Even with Xing Fu's resolute will, he could not help but feel a bit dejected after a while.

In a trance, he suddenly remembered the matter of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas appearing simultaneously in the Primal Immortal Realm.

"Birds of a feather flock together; people of the same kind group together."

"This kind of aimless ideation is too inefficient. Even if I continue until the end of the Mountains and Seas, I might not even glimpse half its shadow."

"If only I could wield the Great Dao of Eternal Life like Duke Shou Qiu. With the Great Dao of Eternal Life as a guide, perhaps I could lure out this hidden ghost."

Thinking of this, Xing Fu's eyes suddenly narrowed.

As if touching something crucial, the depths of his eyes shifted several times.

It was as if he had completely changed into someone else in an instant, or perhaps it was just an illusion.

This epiphany seemed to have not happened, as Xing Fu continued his repetitive labor.

Until one day, the peace of the Realm of Birth and Death was broken.

It was unclear how much time had passed since Xing Fu arrived in the Realm of Birth and Death.

When a rift was suddenly torn open above the ten thousand river phantoms, revealing the scenery of the outside Mountains and Seas, Xing Fu finally realized.

The Mountains and Seas seemed to have undergone a drastic change during this period.

Having repeatedly copied possibility diagrams countless times, Xing Fu's perception of the Mountains and Seas and Dao Oblivion had become thousands of times sharper than before.

At this moment, he could clearly feel the surging of Dao Oblivion outside.

Just like when he had sensed the True Meaning of the Solitary Sail Transcendence in the Guangwu Star Sea, Dao Oblivion had become extremely active, its aggressiveness tens of times greater than usual.

And this hostility of Dao Oblivion was not limited to a single area.

Instead, it seemed to be...

Everywhere!

"What exactly happened?"

Xing Fu felt confused.

Before he could delve deeper, the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death calamities, including Ming Dao Immortal, all appeared, blocking the rift that had been torn open.

The pressure from the Mountains and Seas' Dao Oblivion was only then slightly weakened.

Thus, the myriad ideational flows were able to be maintained.

"I didn't expect this to be an unexpected gain."

A cold voice came from above.

A figure in purple robes, with a red mole between his brows like a third eye, scanned everyone below coldly.

Behind the purple-robed figure stood three other figures.

The aura emanating from each of them was no weaker than that of the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death.

"We have always minded our own business. Why are you pressuring us today?" Guang Mo, one of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, asked, suppressing his anger.

The purple-robed figure said coldly, "On the orders of the Saints, we are searching the Mountains and Seas! Do not bring about your own doom!"

"Saints... How arrogant. Why don't you go search the Tai Wei Saint Dynasty?" the white-haired young man said sarcastically.

"Do you think they haven't searched the Saint Dynasty?" the purple-robed figure sneered.

Upon hearing this, everyone from the Realm of Birth and Death calamities turned pale.

Something that could make the Saints of the Shore and Emperor Tai Wei so concerned...

The Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas?

Countless thoughts flashed through the Venerables' minds. The purple-robed figure, impatient, said, "I repeat, do not bring about your own doom!"

A purple lightning bolt suddenly flared.

With a deafening roar, it almost shattered the Realm of Birth and Death.

"There is nothing you are looking for here," Ming Dao Immortal said.

The purple-robed figure narrowed his eyes and smiled. "Just because you say there isn't, doesn't mean there isn't?"

"Ridiculous!"

The purple figure instantly expanded billions of times.

It was even larger than all the surging river phantoms below combined, intending to uncover all the secrets of this realm.

This act also enraged everyone from the Realm of Birth and Death calamities.

Ming Dao Immortal threw out a long scroll. Although it was blank, it seemed to be filled with dense, myriad characters.

Among them, one seemed to correspond to the purple-robed figure's Dao.

On the blank scroll, this character materialized from虚 into 实.

And the purple figure's expanding form seemed to be pulled by some force, gradually shrinking back to its original shape.

"Since that is the case... then do not blame me for being ruthless."

"After we have scoured this place upside down, we will naturally know what you are hiding."

Rumbling thunder came from outside the Realm of Birth and Death calamities.

Although the purple figure's celestial form was shattered, a pair of even larger hands stretched out from beyond the rift.

"We can't hide it anymore. Let's make a move,"

Seeing this, Ming Dao Immortal sighed.

Chapter 1662: The Great Way of Mountains and Seas Appears

The light suddenly vanished, and boundless darkness enveloped the Realm of Birth and Death.

From the bizarre abyss, countless sludge-like tentacles seemed to extend, tightly entangling the giant hands of the purple-robed figure.

The sea of fiery clouds, stretching for millions of miles, was like a sharp sword, slashing towards the abyss. The purple-robed figure's startled roar flashed and was then drowned out by an endless series of violent explosions.

…

While the same-tribulation Five Venerables made their move, intercepting the purple-robed figure from the other shore, the entire Realm of Birth and Death also underwent inexplicable changes.

Thousands of long rivers flowed concurrently, as if drawn by something, they curled back, connecting head to tail, transforming into circles of closed rings.

In an instant, they wove into a gem radiating pure yellow light!

Under the cover of a mystical rhythm, the sounds of clashing weapons from the outside world gradually weakened. Eight figures shielded the central yellow gem. Although they appeared motionless,

with the flickering of light and shadow, they had already traversed countless mountains and seas!

“We’ve temporarily shaken off their pursuit. However, even if we can transfer again, it ultimately won’t be a long-term solution,” Ming Dao Immortal said with a heavy tone.

“I never expected another Great Dao to appear in the Mountains and Seas. It was truly unforeseen. Did it cause us to be exposed prematurely??”

“The comparison of paintings is almost complete. We absolutely cannot stop halfway. If it becomes truly critical, I will actively manifest the Realm of Birth and Death through imagination and lure the enemy, buying you time,” the white-haired youth said with a solemn expression.

The others did not object: “Rest assured, we will not forget your contribution.”

The white-haired youth smiled and shook his head: “I am already a dead person. Reborn from imagination and gaining another experience, I am already content. If it can help everyone achieve their Great Dao, it will not have been in vain.”

After a period of silence, the eight figures’ gazes once again focused on the yellow gem in the center.

Reaching a safe place, the lines that formed the gem unfurled once more, transforming back into thousands of flowing lights and shadows.

And within the flowing lights and shadows, the beings in the imagined possibility seemed to be frozen, their concept of time’s passage lost.

They were unaware of the various changes happening outside.

After receiving the safety notification from the Venerables, they soon returned to their former way of life.

Xing Fu was among them.

However, he would occasionally look towards the outside of the Realm of Birth and Death, his expression subtle.

“I cannot see the scenery of the outside Mountains and Seas. The Venerables must have used their power to seal it.”

“I just don’t know how long it can hold.”

Far from fearing that his identity might be exposed at any moment, Xing Fu felt a hint of anticipation.

“The Great Tribulation of Dao Annihilation is likely far simpler than what the Venerables described. Otherwise, even with the purple-robed figure arriving, they wouldn’t have been able to flee so quickly after a thorough search. There must be something the Saints of the Shore are concerned about within??”

The answer was obvious.

The Great Dao of Mountains and Seas!

“The method they passed down for comparing paintings and replicating the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas should also be real. However, they concealed some information about the progress!”

Xing Fu looked up at the formless yellow gem hovering above the thousands of flowing river shadows.

“Regardless of whether it was intentional or unintentional, proactive or passive, within the Realm of Birth and Death, including myself, the so-called awakened ones, every time we perform a replication, we are likely being recorded. It counts towards the overall comparison progress.”

“But the Venerables did not lie. Once the progress is complete and the Great Dao of Longevity appears, whoever becomes its master within the Realm of Birth and Death will depend entirely on personal destiny and opportunity.”

“Fighting or seizing is useless.”

“The reason for not making this information public…”

“Knowing too much would only lead to unease and difficulty in imaginative replication.”

Xing Fu took a long time to suppress the surging thoughts.

This discovery, in reality, did not bring any change to Xing Fu’s life.

Even if the progress was 99.99%, it was no different from zero until it was truly complete.

He didn’t know when he would truly glimpse the appearance of the unknown Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, but the pursuit from the other shore was real and might descend again.

Xing Fu keenly sensed that the overall atmosphere within the Realm of Birth and Death had subtly changed compared to before.

Especially among those awakened ones.

No longer were they as focused as before, and the efficiency of their imaginative constructions was also affected.

“They are already distracted. Their ability to withstand pressure is indeed too poor.”

Noticing this, Xing Fu felt strange.

Logically, these awakened ones all possessed Transcendent strength.

Their resolve should not be so weak.

“Unless??”

“Forced growth is not true self-growth into transcendence.”

Xing Fu’s attention, firstly, was on his colleagues.

“Those whose states of mind were not significantly affected did not notice any anomalies.”

“As for those whose minds were disturbed…”

“It’s like imaginative construction – although extremely real, it is ultimately not true!”

After years of accumulation, Xing Fu had developed his own unique understanding of imaginative construction.

Upon careful observation this time, he finally discovered the hidden mechanism.

“Furthermore, this sense of incongruity and illusion??”

Xing Fu frowned and recalled, and with a sense of familiar similarity, he suddenly remembered the white-haired Venerable he had met earlier.

“He is also a creation of imaginative construction?”

“The art of imaginative construction in the Great Tribulation of Dao Annihilation has reached such a level of realism?”

Xing Fu’s suspicion was immediately aroused.

Just as the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas attracted each other, painters would also develop a sense of mutual appreciation.

Xing Fu’s imaginative construction had now gotten started.

But he did not feel that the cultivation attainments of the Venerables of the same tribulation in this path would surpass his own by much.

Although there was no substantial evidence, only an inexplicable guess in his heart.

But Xing Fu was almost certain that it was highly probable.

Xing Fu himself did not know where his confidence came from.

“Perhaps it is my talent shown in the divine ability of imaginative construction?”

“Although the white-haired youth is a creation of imagination, the Five Venerables of the same tribulation and Ming Dao Immortal treat him as an equal??”

“If I were in their shoes, would I treat my own creations of imagination as equals? Certainly not!”

Xing Fu’s eyes flickered with a trace of light, and he already had an answer in his heart.

“It was created by someone else, and left behind as an aid.”

“As for who…”

“The answer is obvious. It must be that Walker of Mountains and Seas who taught the Five Venerables of the same tribulation!”

With a rapid flow of thoughts, Xing Fu had already deduced part of the truth.

“Imagination can transform from void to reality, it must be generated from one’s own familiar memories. If the white-haired youth was imaginatively constructed by the Walker of Mountains and Seas, then his original identity…”

“Comes from the end of the Mountains and Seas?”

Xing Fu could not help but think of the words of the Five Venerables of the same tribulation.

“He himself is not the original creator of this divine ability. The true origin comes from the last prodigy among our cultivators in the final epoch of the Mountains and Seas.”

“…Whose talent was so high that she even surpassed that Walker of Mountains and Seas.”

Xing Fu nodded inwardly: “Perhaps it is precisely because of her extraordinary original identity that the Venerables treat this imagined creation with such respect.”

He desperately wanted to know the specific situation of the end of the Mountains and Seas from the white-haired youth’s memories.

But since the purple-robed figure from the other shore attacked, the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death had rarely appeared in front of everyone.

It seemed they were all busy with something collectively.

Xing Fu could only think about it.

Even though he had uncovered part of the secrets of the Realm of Birth and Death, Xing Fu buried it deep in his heart without revealing a single bit to others.

For the remainder of his time, he continued to diligently perform imaginative constructions, adding a bit of progress towards the final depiction of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas.

After an unknown period, even longer than before.

On this day, just as Xing Fu finished a replication, his heart was suddenly filled with an inexplicable tremor.

Then, tears unexpectedly flowed down.

Xing Fu wiped them away, shocked. At the same time, doubts arose in his heart: “What’s going on? My mind instinctively feels grief, and I can’t help but cry.”

“This must be a phenomenon that occurs after close relatives perish, but all my family members have already perished in the calamity of the Immortal Realm’s destruction years ago. What exactly??”

Xing Fu pondered endlessly.

He wanted to investigate further but had no means.

Ultimately, he could only bury this question in the deepest part of his heart.

After that, countless years passed.

Regarding the final completion of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas replication, it seemed only a sliver was missing.

But this sliver was like a chasm, a world apart.

No matter how diligently the beings within the Realm of Birth and Death persisted, they always failed to fill it.

However, as the “progress bar” was filled closer and closer to completion, corresponding changes also occurred within the Realm of Birth and Death.

The most noticeable was the thousands of flowing river shadows.

They were originally just imagined creations. Xing Fu could see their reality and illusion at a glance.

But now, they were almost indistinguishable from reality!

With Xing Fu’s attainments in the way of imagination, he had to carefully distinguish to discern the subtle differences between them and the true possibilities in the Mountains and Seas.

For those who were not masters of this path, it would be impossible to detect their “imagined characteristics.”

“No longer facing the immediate danger of destruction, the people of the Guangwu Star Sea are living more and more freely and leisurely. They have almost completely forgotten about me.” Xing Fu’s expression flickered with a trace of trance.

Besides these imagined possibilities, the yellow gem suspended above the flowing river shadows had also changed greatly.

It was still not in a state of extreme reality-imagination.

But it existed in a state between reality and illusion.

When not observed, it was merely composed of myriad illusory projections.

But if one observed closely, every facet of the yellow gem was incredibly lifelike.

It was indistinguishable from reality when it manifested.

This superposition of real and illusory states made Xing Fu even more captivated.

He would often look up and observe, and suddenly, he felt a sense.

The day of its true transformation was not far off.

Xing Fu’s premonition was always accurate.

Three thousand five hundred and sixty-nine years passed.

On this day, Xing Fu’s replication was inexplicably interrupted.

For Xing Fu, who had already reached the pinnacle of the divine ability of imagination, this was almost an impossible event.

But it truly happened.

Because…

Instantly realizing something, Xing Fu’s body trembled violently with extreme excitement.

“Exclude all lines that feel discordant.”

“The Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, hidden in the blankness, has finally been depicted and outlined by us.”

Like the countless beings in the flowing river shadows, Xing Fu looked up at the supremely radiant yellow gem above his head.

Figures, one after another, floated around the gem.

They were the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death, who had not appeared for a long time.

However, there were not eight, but only five of the same-tribulation Venerables.

The other Venerables, including Ming Dao Immortal, had vanished.

Under the gaze of everyone, this yellow gem, formed by the painstaking efforts of countless painters in the Realm of Birth and Death over countless years, began to gradually disintegrate.

As if endless lines surged forth.

Becoming denser and denser, like countless paintbrushes, outlining a Great Dao that should not exist in the Mountains and Seas.

With the emergence of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, the Realm of Birth and Death, which had been hidden for many years, could no longer remain concealed.

The isolation of the breath was severed, and a rift was suddenly torn open.

Xing Fu could clearly see a sacred circular ring standing majestically not far away.

The white ring seemed to stand amidst the Mountains and Seas. Although it appeared extremely distant, it was also extremely close.

In an instant, it sealed and suppressed the Realm of Birth and Death.

But at this moment, the Five Venerables of the same tribulation, and even the beings within the Realm of Birth and Death, were no longer important.

All attention was focused on the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas that was about to be born.

Within the white ring, light and shadow flickered.

The Saints of the Shore revealed solemn expressions.

And at the same time, a figure wearing black dragon robes and a crown quietly descended.

Sitting alone on the imperial throne, though alone,

The oppressive aura he brought was no weaker than that of the Saintly projections.

The might of the Saints was like a storm.

Although they had tried their best to restrain themselves, and even with mutual checks and balances, their power was somewhat diminished.

However, for the beings here, it was still unbearable.

The vast majority fainted the moment the Saints descended.

As for the few who could maintain consciousness, they dared not look at the Saints’ figures.

They could only try their best to focus their attention on the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, which was on the verge of disappearing.

Rather than disappearing, it was more like being replicated from nothingness and then hidden within the Mountains and Seas.

Xing Fu vaguely felt a premonition. Whether the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas could be controlled by the people present at this moment depended on its descent.

“If it deliberately hides…”

“Even Saints might not be able to find it.”

Everyone held their breath, waiting for that moment.

When the lines of the yellow gem completely vanished, fully merging with the Mountains and Seas.

Tai Wei Saint Emperor suddenly let out a cold snort and vanished while manipulating his imperial throne.

This action even surprised the Saints of the Shore.

“Still so arrogant,”

Vaguely, the Saints’ evaluations could be heard from within the white ring.

The departure of Tai Wei Saint Emperor did not affect the birth of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas.

Soon after, everyone present sensed an ancient, vast, yet recently born, contradictory aura.

It flashed and disappeared.

“Dao Annihilation plunders the fundamental essence of the Mountains and Seas, the key to the decline of the Mountains and Seas.”

“The root of heaven and earth, giving birth to all things.”

“This is the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin]!”

A rumbling voice echoed from the white ring on the other shore.

The speaker was Duke Shou Qiu, who wielded the Great Dao of [Eternal Life]!

Within the light and shadow, as the Saints were about to make a move.

The entire Mountains and Seas seemed to suddenly freeze.

Endless white mist emerged from the void.

Enveloping the Mountains and Seas.

“True Reversion!”

All beings could only faintly hear a voice emanating from the white mist.

Chapter 1663: The First True Mysterious Womb

Like a fish about to take the bait, startled by a stone suddenly thrown into the water.

Or like a colossal shadow emerging from the depths of the water, quietly approaching, and forcefully swallowing the fish that should have taken the bait.

The moment the white mist appeared, the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao, which the Saints of the Shore and Emperor Tai Wei had been waiting for, vanished like ice melting in water.

But at this moment, the Saints of the Shore were no longer focused on the fleeing Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

In the vast white mist, all living beings who could still move had their attention focused on the phrase [True Return].

"After searching the Mountains and Seas, it has finally appeared. It hid so deeply!"

"This power..."

The Saints' illusions around the white circle of the Shore jointly unleashed a brilliant halo, attempting to resist the erosion of the white mist.

Deep within the white mist, there was constant vibration. Vaguely, a figure could be seen struggling forward. It was Emperor Tai Wei, who had already left, returning.

The Mountains and Seas were frozen, and only the Saints could be spared.

But the vast white mist was even more powerful than Dao Oblivion. Even the combined efforts of the Saints were ultimately futile.

Numerous figures were submerged in the white mist.

Motionless and unseen.

And besides the Saints, Xing Fu, who witnessed the entire scene, could still maintain normal thought processes within the white mist at this moment!

"[True Return]..."

"So that's how it is."

Xing Fu was speechless in astonishment.

Then, he silently chanted in his heart: "[True Return]!"

The rolling white mist surged, swallowing the Mountains and Seas.

After an unknown period, or perhaps an instant.

The white mist receded, and the Mountains and Seas reappeared as before!

However, the Saints of the Mountains and Seas, who had been eagerly searching for [True Return], were suddenly somewhat bewildered.

After a moment of recovery, they were all utterly astonished: "Where is the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao? Why has it disappeared without a trace?"

Only Xing Fu, a strange expression flickered in his eyes.

He frowned, repeatedly pondering in his mind: "[True Return]... "

"What is [True Return]?"

...

Anchored for 1 year!

Xuanhuang Realm!

Li Fan's eyes suddenly snapped open.

The [True Return] panel suddenly appeared before him.

Compared to before, a line of dazzling, seven-colored, dreamlike characters had been added.

Dao Integration: First Xuan Pin.

The moment Li Fan's will touched this line of text, the seven-colored characters instantly disintegrated, turning into a wisp of profound and mystical imagery.

"Vague and existent, the root of heaven and earth."

"Deep and mysterious, immeasurable."

"In stillness quiescent, in movement nascent, all things emerge."

...

Even though Li Fan knew nothing about the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] before this,

Now, with the seven-colored characters entering his view, countless insights into the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] spontaneously surged into his mind.

Even though this Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas should have been incredibly difficult and obscure, even for Nameless True Immortals, they might not comprehend it in their entire lifetimes.

But in Li Fan's eyes, it was like a transparent book.

There was no difficulty at all.

This was certainly not because Li Fan had suddenly gained enlightenment and his talent had become heaven-defying.

All the changes originated from [True Return]!

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan mentally suppressed the insights into the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] for the time being.

Li Fan stared intently at the four words [Dao Integration] on the [True Return] panel.

"[Dao Integration], [Dao Integration]..."

"And the emergent [First Xuan Pin]."

"Has [True Return] captured this Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas?"

Li Fan's heart was like a surging tide, filled with horror.

This was completely beyond his expectations.

In fact, he had no idea how [True Return] had achieved this.

Li Fan recalled his experiences from his previous life.

After sending his clone, Xing Fu, into the Realm of Birth and Death, he had anticipated that the Saints of the Shore would search the Mountains and Seas for traces of [True Return]. Thus, he had quietly hidden himself in advance.

Relying on his past experiences of traveling throughout the Mountains and Seas, he had hidden himself well.

Even when the transcendent beings of the Shore joined forces with the Tai Wei Saint Dynasty and almost turned the Mountains and Seas upside down,

He had not been exposed.

Just as the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables had said, if the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas intentionally hid itself, it would be extremely difficult for others to detect its location.

However, later, as the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] manifested, the Saints of the Shore and Emperor Tai Wei all appeared. The commotion grew larger and larger, and Li Fan was also secretly alarmed. Seeing that things were about to get out of hand, Li Fan resolutely decided to activate [True Return].

Even though the true form of the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] had not yet manifested at that time.

Adhering to the principle of safety first, Li Fan decisively chose to activate [True Return].

But what Li Fan did not expect happened.

[True Return] once again did not respond.

And unlike the past when it lost control, this time there was no external force, such as the Saints obstructing it.

Nor was it that [True Return] was severely injured from the tribulation of the Three Dao Merging.

The reason it failed was entirely because...

[True Return] seemed to have detached itself from Li Fan's body.

Even recalling it now, Li Fan could still personally feel the fear he had at that time.

Unlike when [True Return] fell into a slumber in the past.

At that time, although [True Return] could not be used, Li Fan always had a subtle thought in his heart that it would awaken one day. As long as he persisted, he could wait for that day to arrive.

But after [True Return] truly left Li Fan's body...

Only in loss can one appreciate the preciousness of possession.

That short yet infinitely long period was perhaps the most painful experience for Li Fan since his reincarnation.

Li Fan did not want to dwell on it.

Even though [True Return] later returned and responded to his summons, and even activated again.

Li Fan still harbored resentment towards [True Return]'s brief departure without notice.

It was not until the arrival of a new life and he saw the new line on the [True Return] panel that all his doubts and worries vanished.

All turned into pleasant surprise.

Li Fan also understood the reason for [True Return]'s inexplicable departure.

It had released a vast white mist, feigning its appearance, to attract the attention of the Saints of the Mountains and Seas.

In reality, it had secretly descended and successfully captured the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao that was about to manifest!

"[Dao Integration]."

"[Returning to Truth]."

"What a wonderful description!"

Li Fan was overjoyed.

Every time he thought he had seen the limit of [True Return], but each time.

[True Return] would give him new surprises.

Li Fan never expected that [True Return] could actually capture the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

"How exactly was it done?"

"[True Return] should be on par with the Mountains and Seas. The [Xuan Pin] is also one of the Grand Daos of Mountains and Seas, yet it seemed to have no room for resistance and was easily captured by [True Return]."

Recalling the severe damage [True Return] sustained during the Three Dao Merging,

And feeling the well-restrained [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao within [True Return], Li Fan was baffled.

However, as always.

Even though it had performed such a world-shattering feat, [True Return] still refused to offer any explanation.

No matter how Li Fan inquired, it remained silent.

This made Li Fan almost gnash his teeth in frustration.

"However, it is ultimately a great blessing."

Li Fan was helpless and stopped dwelling on it.

Happily, he began to comprehend the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao after its integration into [True Return].

At the same time, he did not forget to check Bai Shuyue's memories from her previous life.

"Hiss..."

The moment he chose to accept Bai Shuyue's memories, Li Fan's sea of consciousness felt as if it were pierced by a needle, causing a faint stinging pain.

The memory capacity after transcendence was far beyond what it was before.

If Li Fan were not also a strong being of the same caliber, and had not undergone the trials of reincarnation through [True Return], he might have had his mind shattered the moment he inherited Bai Shuyue's memories.

After a long while, Li Fan slowly recovered and began to digest his aunt's memories.

"The time it took Aunt to reach the Shore was shorter than I imagined."

"Perhaps it was truly due to her heaven-defying talent. It was as if something was guiding her, and without anyone leading the way, she found the Shore with almost no detours," Li Fan exclaimed in admiration.

"Then, as I predicted. In front of the Saints of the Shore, Aunt's secret of continuous reincarnation was directly exposed."

"However, Aunt had never done anything heinous. And after the Saints conducted a thorough investigation and ultimately determined that the reincarnation was not Aunt's own doing but due to someone acting behind the scenes, they finally imprisoned Aunt in the Eternal Heavenly Steps of the Shore and did not trouble her further."

"At the same time, they ordered people to search for my whereabouts..."

Li Fan chuckled softly.

"In the Eternal Heavenly Steps, one could not even die if they wished. Aunt could only honestly toil day and night, diligently crafting bluestones for transcendent beings to traverse the river of time."

"Until she was released, Aunt decisively chose to end her own life and start a new life. Hmm?"

Seeing this, Li Fan's eyes narrowed.

He vaguely sensed that something was wrong.

The Saints of the Shore had not yet found any trace of the person behind the scenes, so why would they suddenly release Aunt?

Li Fan re-read Aunt's memories over and over again.

He confirmed that there were no omissions in the records.

And the Saints of the Shore had never revealed the reason for the matter to Aunt from beginning to end.

The person behind him had also not been exposed.

But Li Fan still felt a vague sense of unease.

Choosing to trust his intuition, Li Fan did not rashly decide to have Bai Shuyue inherit the memories of her previous life.

"Better to work harder and start a new Saint Creation plan than to make a misstep due to momentary carelessness."

"However, the Saint Creation plan is indeed time-consuming. If only Aunt could inherit the memories from the life before the previous one, skipping the previous life's experiences."

As if sensing Li Fan's request,

The [True Return] panel suddenly moved.

From the seven-colored characters of the First True [Xuan Pin], a wisp of light detached.

It transformed into a mystical brush, using it to write and modify the selection text on [True Return].

As Li Fan wished, the moment the thought arose, the text changed.

"[True Return] can reflect my thoughts and perfectly restore the memories of inheriting only the life before the previous one?"

This unexpected development left Li Fan dumbfounded.

"It seems I have far from comprehended the profound wonders of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas."

After a long while, Li Fan sighed deeply.

Since [True Return] had provided a solution, Li Fan was no longer in a hurry.

He carefully pondered his current situation.

"The initial reason I wanted to activate the [Saint Creation Plan] was precisely because in the simulation activated by [True Return], I encountered a situation where I, unprepared, broke into the Shore and was subsequently discovered by the Saints."

"Therefore, I wanted to find a way to deal with the Saints. And since I couldn't meet the Saints myself, I had to find a substitute. [True Return] gave me a hint at that time."

"Aunt, being the person I am most familiar with, naturally became my chosen target."

"Aunt's reincarnation and transformation allowed her talent and spiritual aptitude to continuously stack."

"And I also gained greatly from these reincarnations. This [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao is the most important among them."

"[True Return] requires the energy of the Mountains and Seas to activate the simulation. The previous simulation exhausted all the power of Eternal Life I gained from Duke Shou Qiu."

"But my Eternal Life was not a complete Great Dao of Eternal Life, but only a small part shared by Duke Shou Qiu. Now, I have a complete Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas..."

"Does this mean I can activate the simulation now?"

Li Fan's heart stirred.

This time, [True Return] did not remain silent.

Instead, it provided an answer.

"Indeed, it is feasible!"

"Using the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] as energy, it is possible to activate a simulation. It can cover the simulation of the current segment of the Mountains and Seas!"

"However??" Receiving the faint information from [True Return], Li Fan frowned and pondered.

"Involving the Saints, this single simulation will consume a massive amount of energy. Although it will not exhaust the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] in one go, it will have a significant impact on it."

"After extracting it once, it will require a considerable period to recover slowly. If one were to disregard its damage and perform simulations continuously..."

"At most, it can only last for three times?"

Li Fan's heart trembled.

The consumption of activating [True Return]'s simulation was far greater than he had imagined.

"I cannot act rashly."

At the same time, Li Fan also sensed [True Return]'s attitude towards the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] from its answers.

"It seems... it doesn't particularly care?"

Li Fan was astonished.

This seemed contradictory to [True Return] leaving his body entirely to capture it.

After careful consideration, Li Fan slowly came to his senses.

"The reason should be the same as with the Heavenly Curiosities of the past and the Eternal Remnants."

"From nothingness to the first possession. The first instance is the most important."

"Once [True Return] has occupied it, whether it still exists or not is irrelevant."

Li Fan looked again at the four words [Dao Integration] on the [True Return] panel.

"If my guess is correct, [True Return] already possesses the complete nature of the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao?"

With a slight shift of his thoughts, the four words [First Xuan Pin] erupted with seven-colored light.

Brilliant and colorful, it filled Li Fan's mind.

Just like in the past, when Li Fan simulated and disguised the True Meaning of the Solitary Sail using the transformation of True and False,

Now, bathed in the seven-colored light, his body manifested an ancient, vast, and profound aura of [Xuan Pin], on par with the Mountains and Seas.

"But unlike pure simulation."

"It is more like, because the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] has returned to its true form, [True Return] can now wield the power of its rhythm."

[True Return] could fully manifest [Xuan Pin].

But Li Fan could not grasp its essence completely.

Therefore, even under the enhancement of the seven-colored light, Li Fan could not reconstruct [Xuan Pin] to the level of a Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

"It's as if I've fallen into a strange loop."

This sense of déjà vu caused Li Fan to mutter inwardly.

"However, after [Xuan Pin] returned to its true form, I can now glimpse its secrets at any time. It is only a matter of time and effort to perfectly imitate the [Xuan Pin] Saint."

The Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas was extraordinary and profound.

Especially now, exposed to Li Fan without any defenses, letting him probe.

Every time Li Fan cast his gaze, his mind felt as if it were about to sink.

Fortunately, Li Fan could always regain his senses in time.

"My foundation is ultimately [True Return], the transformation of True and False."

"If I truly become immersed in comprehending the Dao, wouldn't it be like discarding the core and keeping the extraneous, making a fool of myself?"

Chapter 1664: The Heavenly Net Once Captured the Dao

The Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas was indeed mesmerizing.

If not for Li Fan's experience of a hundred reincarnations and his cultivation at the same level of Dao paths,

He might have been unable to extricate himself and become lost in it.

But now, he could purely appreciate and examine the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas captured by [True Return] from a spectator's perspective.

In his previous life, after Li Fan sent his clone, Xing Fu, into the Realm of Birth and Death, although he had completely severed contact with his main body to avoid exposure and become an independent entity, Li Fan could not know what he had experienced.

However, after activating [True Return], Xing Fu's memories returned as usual.

"According to the account of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, and my own insights from years of ideational replication, I can broadly confirm. The Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] originally belonged to the power of the [Gods]. It was first absorbed by the Mountains and Seas, then invaded by Dao Oblivion, and then stripped from the Mountains and Seas."

"Or rather, everything in the Mountains and Seas originally came from the [Gods]. Although it transformed into Mountains and Seas, with the fragmentation of the Mountains and Seas under the erosion of Dao Oblivion..."

"Many Grand Daos of Mountains and Seas will reappear in the world!"

Li Fan's eyes flickered: "According to the prophecy left by that Walker of Mountains and Seas, the ultimate destination of the Grand Daos of Mountains and Seas was to return to the [Stars]. That is, from whence it came, to where it returns."

"The annihilation of the Mountains and Seas, the solitary Star hanging high, the birth of a new God. This is the fate and ending of these Mountains and Seas."

"But..."

"The Mountains and Seas did not manage to completely absorb the power of the [Gods]. For example, Shou Qiu possessed [Eternal Life]."

"And with the invasion of Dao Oblivion and the arrival of the end times, the Grand Daos originally absorbed by the Mountains and Seas are more likely to be stripped away. For example, this time, [Xuan Pin]."

"In other words, the more the Mountains and Seas collapse, the more likely it is for [Saints] to be born."

"Currently, the flow of all power in the world is from Gods to Mountains and Seas, then to Stars. But because of the birth of Saints, a part of the Grand Dao that should have returned to the Stars is occupied by the Saints."

"Therefore, the Stars are destined to be inferior to the [Gods]. And the more Saints there are, the weaker the Stars become."

"Currently, it is known that the Stars are the source driving the descent of Dao Oblivion. Therefore..."

Li Fan understood in his heart: "Preventing the annihilation of the world by Dao Oblivion is not a fantasy."

"In fact, there is hope. With each Sage born in the Mountains and Seas, the power disparity between them and the Stars is lessened. As fire follows fire, saving the Mountains and Seas."

"And besides the conflict between the Mountains and Seas, Saints, and Stars??"

"There is also [True Return]."

Li Fan still cannot understand what the essence of [True Return] is.

He originally thought it was just a wondrous treasure that materialized the transformation of True and False.

But after [True Return] unlocked the ability of [Dao Integration], everything became even more mysterious.

Li Fan deeply understood the terrifying nature of this ability to claim the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas as one's own.

"From initially being a mortal to capturing [Xuan Pin]. I have only reincarnated a little less than two hundred times, not counting the first hundred lifetimes for foundation building."

"With infinite spiritual essence as a fallback, it is almost imaginable that with each reset, I might truly be able to take possession of the portions belonging to the Mountains and Seas, Saints, and [Stars] with [True Return]..."

"What will happen in the end?"

Almost instantly, the answer arose in Li Fan's heart.

Making his mind tremble.

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, [True Return] transmitted an inexplicable fluctuation.

Li Fan wanted to probe further, but the fluctuation vanished in an instant.

Leaving him bewildered for a time.

"The most important thing is, after [Dao Integration], does this current segment of the Mountains and Seas still contain the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin]?"

"Theoretically speaking, since the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin] has returned to [True Return], even if [True Return] resets the Mountains and Seas, it will not appear out of thin air. But??"

Li Fan vaguely felt something was wrong.

To verify his guess, Li Fan needed to go to the Realm of Birth and Death again to repeat the story.

With the experience from his previous life, he would be even more cautious about putting himself in danger.

He still chose to find Xing Fu as a substitute.

His main body disguised his identity and went to impart the method of [Ideational Form Dao Construction]. He also casually resolved the crisis of fishing for Dao Oblivion.

After usurping Xing Fu's body, his main body drifted away, hiding in the Mountains and Seas.

And his clone, Xing Fu, after sufficient preparations, once again led the Guangwu immortals to accept the invitation and head to the Realm of Birth and Death.

The subsequent experiences in the Realm of Birth and Death were no different from his previous life.

It was just that without Bai Shuyue going to the Shore and alarming the Saints' illusions.

The ideational construction plan of the Realm of Birth and Death was never exposed.

It allowed them to make more thorough preparations without interruption.

Quietly performing ideational replication for a million years, greatly advancing the progress of completing the painting. Xing Fu had gained the absolute trust of the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death.

On this day, they summoned Xing Fu.

"May I ask what is the reason for the Venerables' summons?" Xing Fu asked very respectfully.

The one who replied was the white-haired youth, whose origin was from the end of the Mountains and Seas and who was reproduced through ideation.

"Among all the awakened ones, your mastery of ideational construction is the deepest. You have even faintly surpassed us. Therefore, there are things you should know."

Xing Fu's expression remained unchanged: "The Venerables flatter me. My talent should be mediocre. The reason I perform better than others is likely due to my unwavering focus over the years."

The white-haired youth smiled and did not refute.

He then asked: "How long do you think it will take for the painting to be completely completed?"

Sensing the eyes of all the Venerables focused on him, Xing Fu did not answer lightly. After a long period of contemplation, he finally said solemnly and in a low voice, "If we proceed at the current pace, at most within a hundred years, the mysterious Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas will surely reveal its form!"

Upon hearing this, the white-haired youth burst into laughter: "You are indeed more optimistic than the rest of us!"

"Regardless, once the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas manifests, it will surely cause a tremendous stir. The Saints of the Shore and Emperor Tai Wei will sense it and come."

Xing Fu's expression turned solemn.

"To be honest, although we are called Venerables, our strength is far inferior to theirs," Ming Dao Immortal said at this moment.

"But it does not mean we have no ability to stall for time. The Venerables are in the open, and we are in the dark. As long as we can delay until the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas fully descends, and if someone can control it before the Saints perceive it."

"And even if we fail..."

The white-haired youth smiled. "The Saints will naturally pursue the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas. They will likely not pay much attention to us."

Xing Fu cupped his hands, a look of doubt on his face: "Venerables, didn't you say before that whoever attains the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas depends entirely on their own fortune and opportunity? Such an ethereal and uncontrollable matter?..."

Yuan Zang, one of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, interrupted Xing Fu's words with a cold snort, "Secrets should not be spoken lightly. However, it was merely a pretext to appease you when you first arrived."

"If it were truly completely uncontrollable, why would we have poured so much effort into this plan over the years?"

Upon hearing this, Xing Fu's expression showed surprise.

Ming Dao Immortal explained with a smile: "Do you still remember I mentioned that event where a Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas appeared in our destroyed homeland, in the lower star sea?"

Xing Fu nodded: "Seniors once said that birds of a feather flock together. This Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas in the lower star sea was perhaps attracted by Duke Shou Qiu's attainment of [Eternal Life]."

"In fact, this Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas did not disappear. It was truly found by someone."

Ming Dao Immortal spoke slowly, and Xing Fu's heart trembled violently.

"What?"

"In fact, since ancient times, there has been a prophecy circulating in the Immortal Realm about a savior descending from heaven. Therefore, when facing the increasingly rampant Dao Oblivion and the powerlessness of all immortals, the Immortal Emperors began to search for that legendary savior."

"According to various calculations, the conclusion was that it would appear in the lower star sea. Thus, they secretly built an experimental dojo in the lower star sea, wove a trap, and waited for the miraculous object to descend."

"Did they eventually find it?" Xing Fu listened intently and could not help but ask.

"Naturally, they captured it. It was precisely that Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas that was attracted!" Ming Dao Immortal sighed.

"It was also because of obtaining this fortune that Emperor Tian Luo had that extreme and insane idea."

Xing Fu finally reacted and exclaimed in disbelief: "No wonder Emperor Tian Luo declared with certainty back then that he had found the ultimate method to counter Dao Oblivion. Many believed him, while countless others cursed him. It turns out!"

"If one possessed the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, one would indeed have the confidence to resist Dao Oblivion."

Xing Fu was lost in thought, and after a long while, he finally reacted and quickly asked again, "Then, did Emperor Tian Luo ultimately succeed or fail?"

As if recalling Ming Dao Immortal's hesitant words from years ago, Xing Fu suddenly realized: "Seniors once said not necessarily failed, does that mean he truly...?"

Ming Dao Immortal shook his head: "Not necessarily failed, nor necessarily succeeded. The moment the Immortal Realm was destroyed, Emperor Tian Luo led his followers and disappeared into the Mountains and Seas. No matter what method was used, contact could no longer be established."

"But after that, many inexplicable changes did occur. The most significant was that the potential of the surviving remnants of the Immortal Realm greatly increased. Numerous beings could certify Nameless, which was unheard of during the time the Immortal Realm still existed."

Xing Fu murmured: "Thus, it is indeed strange. The saying goes that a nation is destroyed and its family is ruined, yet we True Immortals, instead of perishing with the destruction of the Immortal Realm, have seen our cultivation advance repeatedly amidst the difficult end times..."

"Thus, I always felt that practicing cultivation in the lower star seas was easier than in the Immortal Realm. I thought it was because I had undergone various tribulations and my state of mind and talent had been transformed. I never thought I was benefiting from Emperor Tian Luo!"

Xing Fu was completely stunned.

Ming Dao Immortal sighed: "This is also the reason I sent you an invitation."

"On one hand, having obtained good fortune, your average talent is indeed slightly superior to other True Immortals in other possibilities. And on the other hand..."

"If we can truly recreate the Immortal Realm through ideation, allowing Emperor Tian Luo to be reborn."

At this point, Ming Dao Immortal paused. He glanced at the white-haired youth beside him before continuing, "Perhaps, by relying on the ideational Emperor Tian Luo, we can establish contact with his true form."

"But it seems that the destruction back then took away something vitally important. The difficulty of ideationally reconstructing our homeland is far greater than I imagined. We can only postpone it for now."

"So that's how it is. There's actually such an origin behind it," Xing Fu murmured.

"Before Emperor Tian Luo executed his plan, he invited me to assist him. However, I ultimately refused."

"Although he was somewhat disappointed, he still secretly passed on the experience of capturing the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas. This is our confidence." Ming Dao Immortal continued.

"If the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas manifests, we have a ninety percent chance of controlling and restraining it. Of course, who can ultimately control it will truly depend on individual fortune and opportunity."

"The Realm of Birth and Death is home to countless beings. As long as it benefits those who share the same aspirations, we can accept it," the white-haired youth said at this moment.

After finishing speaking, the eight Venerables jointly cast their spells, displaying the "trap" used to capture the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas to Xing Fu.

Relying on the Realm of Birth and Death itself, it was like a meticulously woven net.

And the myriad ideational flows flowing within the Realm of Birth and Death served as the threads forming the net.

"Of course, this net is only superficial. The core of the trap is the bait used to attract the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas."

The yellow crystal suspended above the myriad river phantoms within the Realm of Birth and Death had its infinite facets unfold, revealing its core.

In the boundless darkness, there were myriad starlight fragments, floating and rotating.

Among them, the few light shadows in the center were the most dazzling.

The brilliance of the light was comparable to the sum of all other starlight.

"This is??"

Xing Fu stared at the magnificent scene before him, and for some reason, he felt a sense of familiarity from this starlight.

Sheng Shi, one of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, spoke in a deep voice: "These are the foundational essences of the Dao that we stole from various probabilities in the Mountains and Seas. Initially, we intended to use them to construct a more solid Realm of Birth and Death. Originally, the starlight here was mostly of equal strength. But one day??"

"Some of them suddenly erupted with dazzling light, making it impossible to look directly."

Ming Dao Immortal continued: "These Dao paths were written by me personally, reflecting the foundational essences of the Immortal Realm's Dao. But now..."

"Even I can no longer see them clearly."

Xing Fu narrowed his eyes, trying to see the true inscriptions within the dazzling light.

But it was clearly futile.

Ming Dao Immortal did not mind Xing Fu's actions and continued: "Although they have not yet reached the level of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, they are already incomparable to ordinary possibility Dao paths."

"They are sufficient to form a certain attraction to the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, and can be used as bait."

Chapter 1665: Li Fan Pretends to Be a Saint

The True Immortal inscriptions that had undergone metamorphosis radiated an aura that was extraordinary. When merely exposed for a short while, waves of disturbance, like surging tides, emanated from outside the Realm of Birth and Death.

It was as if something unknown within Dao Oblivion had been attracted.

Only when the Venerables cast spells to conceal it again did the heart-pounding feeling of being targeted subside.

Ming Dao Immortal and the others were already accustomed to it, their faces unchanged as they said, "As one of the most outstanding awakened ones, you might have a chance to capture that Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas. Therefore, we are warning you in advance."

"Furthermore, this plan to deceive the heavens and cross the sea also requires your cooperation."

Xing Fu naturally nodded in agreement.

"None of us have truly seen the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas manifest, so all preparations can only be based on estimations. However, unexpected events can always happen, so..."

Ming Dao Immortal paused, looking at Xing Fu, and said, "We must be prepared for the worst-case scenario."

Unfolding a blank scroll out of thin air, Jin Xiao, Feng Cang, Yuan Zang, Sheng Shi, and Guang Mo, the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, all lightly exclaimed in unison.

They projected their figures onto the scroll.

As if five characters had been added to the scroll, or perhaps five lifelike miniature figures leaping onto the paper, Ming Dao Immortal's scroll instantly became extraordinary.

Then came the remaining two.

The white-haired youth from the end of the Mountains and Seas, a product of ideational construction.

And the taciturn middle-aged man.

The white-haired youth was fine; Xing Fu had already received guidance from him when they first met.

But the middle-aged man had an extremely low presence.

In the many years Xing Fu had been in the Realm of Birth and Death, he had never heard him speak a single word.

The two of them also followed suit, leaving their imprints on Ming Dao Immortal's scroll.

What the white-haired youth left was an eye.

Its gaze was cold and piercing, devoid of any emotion, as if it had witnessed all the sorrows of the world and experienced countless destructions.

When Xing Fu met the gaze from within the painting, he inexplicably felt as if he were in the end of the Mountains and Seas, surrounded by Dao Oblivion.

And the imprint left by the middle-aged man was even more peculiar.

It was a complete replica of himself!

As if his entire being had been sliced into two pieces, one remaining in reality, the other leaping into the painting!

With the imprints of seven more Venerables, the scroll seemed to weigh ten thousand times more.

Ming Dao Immortal's action of closing and tucking it away was clearly more strenuous.

"Condense!"

With a soft chant, the scroll was slowly put away.

Transforming into a thin sheet of white paper.

Then, Ming Dao Immortal blew a light breath, and the white paper instantly disintegrated into countless fragments, like a snow-white dragon, leaping into the myriad river phantoms below.

Xing Fu, who had gazed countless times at the ideational probabilities of the Realm of Birth and Death, keenly sensed that with the infusion of the Venerables' scroll,

The entire Realm of Birth and Death had subtly changed.

"If any accidents occur, the Realm of Birth and Death will automatically withdraw.

"With this backup, even if we unfortunately perish, we can be reborn from ideation in the future."

"Your mission is to become the new [Venerable] of the Realm of Birth and Death and await our return," Ming Dao Immortal said sternly.

"???" Burdened with such a heavy responsibility, Xing Fu seemed somewhat at a loss for a moment.

But he still nodded heavily in response: "Xing Fu will certainly not fail the intentions of all seniors."

Next, Ming Dao Immortal taught Xing Fu the method to control the myriad ideational river phantoms of the Realm of Birth and Death.

And reiterated his instructions: "If the situation gets out of control, just escape. Don't worry about us. With you all here, we would only be a burden."

"I understand," Xing Fu replied very seriously.

With everything prepared, the next step was to wait for the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas to descend.

As for how to attract the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas with bait and block its descent aura, Ming Dao Immortal did not mention it to Xing Fu.

Clearly, it was not something his current strength could participate in.

A hundred years passed in a flash.

It was a bit longer than Xing Fu had estimated.

On this day, the ideational replication was finally complete.

Stimulated by its aura, the countless lines of the yellow gem suspended above the heads of all beings in the Realm of Birth and Death began to writhe wildly, like a swarm of snakes.

A net of heaven and earth was quietly laid.

As for the metamorphosed True Immortal inscriptions used as bait, they were nowhere to be seen. Or perhaps, they had merged into the entire net.

Even Xing Fu, who was observing, could tell that this creation woven from countless lines was extraordinary.

Although dim, it still shone brightly in the darkness!

The eight Venerables stood in a circle.

Suspended within the net.

Ming Dao Immortal, with a long laugh, transformed into a boundless white scroll.

The remaining Venerables, like the backup plan from before, were not their own imprints but their true bodies personally entering the Ming Dao scroll.

The previously blank scroll instantly became a riot of colors.

The scroll instantly expanded countless times.

Rustling, it covered the net of heaven and earth.

Using the countless lines emerging from the yellow gem as its bones, the Ming Dao scroll transformed into a giant pocket.

Encompassing the entire Realm of Birth and Death within it!

Inside the pocket, it seemed as if it were isolated from the Mountains and Seas.

The turbulent waves caused by the impending descent of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas instantly vanished.

Xing Fu was even more shocked to discover that when he was within this pocket, his cultivation was uncontrollably decreasing.

"Is this because I have truly left the Mountains and Seas?" Xing Fu suddenly understood.

Xing Fu's entire cultivation and life force originated from the Mountains and Seas.

And when he was confined by the pocket, in a sense, his foundation of existence began to recede.

"It's like being in the Eternal Void!"

"Simulating the creation of the void without being a Saint. The Venerables' strength is truly extraordinary!" Xing Fu could not help but marvel.

Of course, what the pocket divine ability did was only a partial simulation.

The speed at which Xing Fu's foundation of existence disappeared was definitely incomparable to being in the Eternal Void.

Therefore, he was not worried about his own safety at all and stared intently at the changes in the field.

With the pocket formed, the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas had not noticed that it was a trap.

It was only attracted by the aura of its "kin" that descended as planned.

As if a strong wind, blowing from the void.

The pocket instantly expanded thousands of times.

It expanded beyond Xing Fu's range of perception in an instant.

And it seemed to continue to fill indefinitely.

"Dao Oblivion plunders the fundamental essence of the Mountains and Seas, the key to the decline of the Mountains and Seas."

"The root of heaven and earth, giving birth to all things."

"This is the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin]!"

At this moment, Ming Dao Immortal's voice, tinged with excitement, could be faintly heard.

"Everyone, since the Grand Dao has entered the net, let us rely on our own abilities."

"The Myriad Heaven Bag can only last for a limited time. Whether we can subdue it before it shatters depends on our fortune!"

Waves of fluctuations came from various parts of the Myriad Heaven Bag.

As if responding to the Venerables.

However, the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, which had been captured, paid no attention to the exchanges between the Venerables.

Like a hurricane, it continuously dashed and probed within the bag.

Attempting to find its "kin."

Within the Myriad Heaven Bag, countless lights and shadows seemed to surge in secret.

It was the Venerables trying to sense and capture the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

But the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas was formless and intangible.

Even knowing that it was within at this moment, it was still as difficult as reaching the heavens to truly touch it.

An unknown amount of time passed, and still no change occurred.

Although the Myriad Heaven Bag was a divine ability cast by the combined efforts of the eight Venerables, it had not yet reached the Saint level.

While it could contain the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas for a time, it could not restrain it for eternity.

The [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao, having searched fruitlessly for a long time, seemed to be losing patience.

It abandoned the futile chase and search, and turned to leave.

At this very moment, the Myriad Heaven Bag was stretched to its limit.

The yellow gem lines, serving as its bones, were twisted to the extreme. Ming Dao's scroll could no longer support it.

The entire Myriad Heaven Bag was about to turn into dust under the impact of the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao.

Just then, all the pressure inexplicably dissipated.

Without external forces driving it, the Myriad Heaven Bag, which had expanded to its limit, immediately contracted in reverse. In a breath, it returned to its normal size.

The eight Venerables, somewhat disheveled, emerged from the Ming Dao scroll.

They all looked around in bewilderment.

"What... what is happening?"

"Where is the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao?"

The eight looked at each other, confirming that none of them had captured it.

Then, they instinctively scanned their surroundings.

And then, a figure caught their attention.

Initially, in their eyes, this figure was merely a mortal ant.

But with each passing second it remained in their sight, it grew tens of thousands of times larger. Just like the Myriad Heaven Bag before it.

In a short time, it had grown to fill the heavens and earth, resembling the Mountains and Seas.

Exceeding their range of "sight"!

"Ah!"

Their eyes were pierced by light, and amidst cries of pain, Ming Dao Immortal and the others were forced to look away.

At the same time, they were filled with unimaginable horror.

"This is... becoming a Saint?"

They naturally recognized the figure.

It was Xing Fu, who had defected and was willing to sit in seclusion for countless years for the great cause of ideation.

However, even though they had known beforehand that the attainment of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas depended on personal fortune and opportunity, and not on battle. At this moment, witnessing the long-sought Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas being seized by a junior.

For a moment, their hearts felt a sense of imbalance.

And, naturally, the thought of plundering it arose.

It was not their original intention, but the natural reaction of cultivators upon witnessing the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas changing hands.

Soon, the eight Venerables recovered from their momentary daze.

"Hehehe, I truly never expected that he would be the one to seize it."

"It is fate, destiny, and fortune, not a fault of battle," said the silent middle-aged figure, one of the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables. He let out a long sigh and shook his head helplessly.

"However, has he truly become a Saint? Why do I feel..." Sheng Shi stared intently at Xing Fu, his brow furrowed.

Ming Dao Immortal shook his head: "Becoming a Saint is not so easy. Although he now possesses the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin], completely controlling it is likely not a simple matter."

"And the reason we mistakenly thought he had become a Saint just now was because of the sudden sight. It was not him, but the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin]. Compared to the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, his own cultivation is almost negligible. Thus, we made a misjudgment."

"Indeed, looking again now, that oppressive feeling has slowly disappeared," Jin Xiao agreed.

The white-haired youth chuckled: "In any case, it is a good thing that the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas has been retained. This person was invited by Ming Dao and has been in the Realm of Birth and Death for so many years, so we know him thoroughly."

"Wielding the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, with one foot already stepping into the path of Sainthood. If we can get the help of a Saint, our plan..."

As the eight Venerables whispered amongst themselves, Xing Fu finally opened his eyes.

His strength and aura were completely contained, appearing no different from a mortal at first glance.

"Congratulations, fellow Daoist!" the Venerables said in various tones.

"I still have to thank all of you for your assistance!" Xing Fu, or rather, Li Fan, responded with a smile.

The Venerables felt a sour taste in their mouths upon hearing Li Fan's words.

The scene became awkward for a moment.

Fortunately, Li Fan quickly extended his hand, presenting an invisible and profound aura to everyone.

"Esteemed seniors, please observe."

Without Li Fan needing to speak, his action immediately drew the attention of Ming Dao Immortal and the others.

"This is the [Xuan Pin] Grand Dao?"

"It seems to be no different from the Dao of the Mountains and Seas?"

Everyone looked at Ming Dao Immortal with doubt.

With [Ming Dao] as his Dao, when it came to comprehending the Dao, Ming Dao was surely far superior to everyone else.

Ming Dao Immortal observed for a long time before finally speaking: "The true Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas is not something we can see. This... perhaps it can be called the [Xuan Pin] Dao that fellow Daoist Xing Fu has comprehended."

"It is only a minuscule part of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas."

Upon hearing this, everyone suddenly understood.

Li Fan smiled and nodded: "Ming Dao speaks rightly! Obtaining the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas is like entering a treasure mountain. However, one's arm strength is limited; only a small portion can be carried out."

"The boundless treasures I have seen, with my strength, I do not know how many years it would take to excavate them all."

"However, to possess treasure without sin invites disaster. I am worried that if outsiders discover this, it might bring about calamity. Therefore, I earnestly ask all fellow Daoists to look after me until I achieve enlightenment and become a Saint!" With that, Li Fan bowed sincerely to everyone.

Seeing this, the Venerables felt a little better.

They worried about outsiders coveting the treasure, yet sincerely requested everyone to protect him.

Clearly, they considered them "their own people."

Ming Dao Immortal was the first to respond: "Naturally. The path to sainthood is not achieved overnight. Duke Shou Qiu also spent over a hundred epochs to attain Eternal Life before becoming a Saint."

"Before you achieve success, you can meditate and cultivate here. With us here, no outsider will dare to disturb you."

The remaining Venerables also voiced their agreement.

"In that case, I thank you all first." Li Fan looked grateful.

"What are your plans next?" Li Fan suddenly asked, changing the subject.

Even though he had obtained the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas and was on the verge of becoming a Saint.

He still cared about the future of the Realm of Birth and Death.

Ming Dao Immortal and the others exchanged glances, all feeling that "Xing Fu" was reliable.

"In fact, ideationally manifesting the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas and obtaining the power of a Saint is only one part of our plan."

"Our true goal is to gain enough self-preservation ability to maintain the circulation of the Realm of Birth and Death, until..."

"The end of the Mountains and Seas!"

The white-haired youth spoke.

Upon mentioning the end of the Mountains and Seas, his eyes flickered slightly, as if recalling something.

Chapter 1666: The End of Mountains and Seas is Received Once and For All

"The end of the Mountains and Seas?"

"If one were to go against the flow, towards the beginning of the Mountains and Seas, returning to the time when everything began. I could understand that. But the end of time, when the Mountains and Seas are about to be devoured, when all will return to nothingness. To stubbornly persist until then??"

"Why is that?" Li Fan's face showed a look of confusion.

The one who answered Li Fan was still the white-haired youth.

"To know the answer to this question, one must understand what the true end of the Mountains and Seas is like."

A dim light erupted in the youth's eyes.

His snow-white hair and beard seemed to ignite, turning into billions of ash-like fragments.

Like a vast snowstorm, it suddenly blew.

In a trance, Li Fan saw a great conflagration sweeping across the Mountains and Seas.

Countless possibilities were incinerated.

Myriad lights were plunged into darkness, Dao Annihilation surged, the Mountains and Seas decayed, ushering in an unstoppable doomsday.

The safe possibilities left to shelter in became fewer and fewer, until finally, only a solitary boat remained.

Outside, there was endless oblivion!

Li Fan had once come into close contact with the Eternal Silence Void. Even before truly entering, at a considerable distance from it, the very foundation of his existence began to show signs of disintegration.

Like countless ink threads dispersing in water, irretrievably fading.

Li Fan looked at the scene before him, the last surviving possibility of the Mountains and Seas, and had a premonition.

To be amidst it was truly like purgatory.

Even if it wasn't as powerful as the pressure he had felt from the Void Realm, it wouldn't be much weaker.

"Living there would absolutely be a form of torture."

"But due to the instinct to survive, one is forced to struggle and cling to life..."

"However, thinking in reverse, for one to live freely under such circumstances."

"Although not a Saint, one would already possess the ability to survive in the Eternal Silence Void.

Thinking of this, Li Fan couldn't help but look at the white-haired youth.

"This manifestation constructed from imagination is definitely not ordinary."

The white-haired youth's voice came from the scene of the end of the Mountains and Seas: "Did you feel anything?"

"The pervasive aura of the Void Realm, making one tremble and feel uncomfortable," Li Fan replied truthfully.

"Anything else?"

"Anything else?" Li Fan was slightly stunned.

After carefully observing again and remaining silent for a long time, he shook his head in response.

The white-haired youth was momentarily speechless.

"As expected, the attribution of the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas seems to have little to do with strength or talent."

"Esteemed Venerables of the same tribulation, and Ming Dao, all saw the uniqueness of the end of the Mountains and Seas at a glance. Yet you, favored by the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin..." The white-haired youth felt a pang of bitterness, shaking his head repeatedly.

Li Fan's expression remained normal, he could only smile.

He couldn't possibly tell him that the reason he attracted the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin was entirely due to the four words [True Return], having nothing to do with him personally!

To be honest, the changes in the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin after True Return were truly beyond Li Fan's expectations.

The moment he saw the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin descend, Li Fan thought it would, like everything else in the Mountains and Seas, be reset when True Return was activated.

But soon, Li Fan sensed that something was wrong.

As the four words “Dao Integration: First Xuan Pin” on the True Return panel emitted a dreamlike seven-colored flowing light.

That Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, which had seemed insurmountable in Li Fan's eyes, instantly became familiar.

It was both the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas newly replicated and emerging in this era, and the First Xuan Pin subdued and returned by True Return!

Thus, what happened next was without suspense.

Almost as if an extension of his own arm, Li Fan, with his transcendent cultivation, effortlessly attracted the allegiance of the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin.

Li Fan was unsure whether the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin was altered before its descent, or if it was influenced by True Return after appearing in the Mountains and Seas, thus being labeled with [True Return].

In reality, the difference between these two would have no impact on the outcome.

Li Fan only cared whether the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas captured in this new era could be used as energy for True Return's simulation and deduction.

Unfortunately, the answer was no.

"With the activation of True Return and the reset of the Mountains and Seas, a new Grand Dao of Xuan Pin has indeed appeared. Because I do not feel a decrease in the power of the First Xuan Pin within [Dao Integration]."

"But precisely because Xuan Pin has returned to True Return, whether it is the past, future, present, or any point in time, all [Xuan Pin] belong to True Return."

"To True Return, it is like having eaten something before; there is no new appetite. A Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas that has truly returned will naturally not produce new simulation energy."

"Even so, this ability of [Absolute Collection] is truly too overbearing."

If viewed from the perspective of the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin in this era, the terrifying nature of True Return could be highlighted.

It was like you had been living a good life all along, with a happy life and no worries about family.

Then suddenly, someone jumped out and claimed to be your master.

You must obey their commands unconditionally.

And you can only accept this sudden fate without resistance.

"Forever and ever, there is no hope of turning the tables. Tsk tsk tsk..."

"However, I like it."

"It's just that I don't know what exactly is needed for True Return's simulation. I previously thought that because it involved Saints, it required a Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas of the same caliber as energy. But now it seems to be related to True Return's own consumption?"

Numerous thoughts flashed through Li Fan's mind.

And the white-haired youth before him, after sighing repeatedly, no longer played coy.

He explained the reason for their plan to go directly to the end of the Mountains and Seas, telling him everything.

"We all originated from the Mountains and Seas. As the saying goes, if the skin is gone, the hair cannot attach to it, so if the Mountains and Seas are devoured by Dao Annihilation, we too will return to nothingness."

"Even now, with the Mountains and Seas still existing, if we were to leave the Mountains and Seas, the very foundation of our existence would dissipate."

Li Fan nodded slightly: "Indeed, that is the principle."

"Only Saints, who are comparable to the Mountains and Seas, can exist without relying on the power of the Mountains and Seas. But when the river of time reaches the end of the Mountains and Seas, this situation will change."

The white-haired youth's eyes flashed with a bright light: "At that time, the Mountains and Seas will be weakened to their limit. The constraints they place on the beings within them will also reach the weakest moment since the birth of the Mountains and Seas."

"Especially in the instant before the Mountains and Seas perish."

Li Fan's heart stirred, recalling the countless rivers of possibilities in the Realm of Birth and Death, and he vaguely began to understand.

"So, our plan is..."

"That's right!" Ming Dao Immortal said with assurance. "In the instant the Mountains and Seas perish due to Dao Annihilation, we will use these countless imagined possibilities to leap out of the Mountains and Seas and stand on our own."

"The Mountains and Seas will have no time to take care of themselves, and we will not encounter too much resistance."

"The only threat we need to face is the Eternal Silence Void."

"However, being in the Mountains and Seas, and outside the Mountains and Seas, the pressure faced before Dao Annihilation is entirely different," the white-haired youth added slowly.

Chapter 1667: Time Terminator
