As if having experienced it personally, the white-haired youth fell into recollection and said wistfully, "If we can successfully detach ourselves from the identity of these [Mountains and Seas], even if we haven't reached the Saint realm, we can still survive in the Eternal Silence Void!"

"Compared to still being within the Mountains and Seas, the destructive power of Dao Annihilation is more than a little weaker. This gives us a sliver of hope for self-preservation."

Li Fan narrowed his eyes, observing the white-haired youth.

The other Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death seemed to place immense trust in the white-haired youth. Everyone believed his conclusions without question.

However, Li Fan's internal doubts could not be so easily dispelled.

"What happens after breaking free from the Mountains and Seas?"

"Even if, as you say, we can survive in the Eternal Silence Void. But how long can we last?"

Facing Li Fan's questioning, the white-haired youth said faintly, "Once the Mountains and Seas are destroyed, the Stars will naturally reappear. In a sense, we will enter the next cycle of reincarnation. Perhaps one day, new Mountains and Seas will emerge and devour the Stars. But we will have secured a place in this new era."

"Moreover, perhaps the Stars will even show leniency towards us, who have pledged allegiance from the Mountains and Seas."

"This is purely speculation, isn't it?" After hearing the white-haired youth's grand plan, Li Fan's expression became somewhat nuanced.

"Yes and no."

The white-haired youth did not elaborate further, merely saying this brief sentence before falling silent.

Seeing that the situation seemed to have reached an impasse, Dao Scribe Immortal stepped forward to mediate: "One must understand that for cultivators like us who have not reached the Saint realm, this is the last method of survival that we can deduce. Among all the plans, this one has the highest probability of survival."

"In other words, even if we fail to become independent at the moment the Mountains and Seas return to the Stars, we have, after all, lived until the end of the Mountains and Seas, have we not?"

"Of course..."

Dao Scribe Immortal changed the subject, looking at Li Fan: "Fellow Daoist, you are naturally different from us. You now wield the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin], and if there are no unforeseen circumstances, your future attainment of Sainthood is almost a certainty. If you do not wish to participate in our actions, we will understand."

"Whether you choose to join the Shore or the Saint Dynasty, you are free to do as you please! We will never obstruct you."

"We only hope that out of consideration for our many years of companionship, you will not leak the secrets of the Realm of Birth and Death," Dao Scribe Immortal said earnestly.

Li Fan sighed, pondering in silence.

"Let me think about it, and then I will give you my answer."

Li Fan's reaction was within the expectations of all the Venerables.

After all, he was already a "quasi-Saint."

If he had readily agreed to join the Realm of Birth and Death's plan without hesitation, the Dao Scribe Immortals and the others would have found it strange.

Li Fan pondered for a full three years before replying to the Venerables.

"Compared to the nameless Saints on the Shore, I still trust you all more."

Upon hearing this, even with the composure of Dao Scribe Immortal and the others, they could not help but be overjoyed.

"After all, my attainment of the Grand Dao of Xuan Pin is also thanks to all of you. How could I betray you in a matter of life and death?"

"Once I diligently cultivate and achieve Sainthood soon, our plan will have a greater chance of success in the future," Li Fan said righteously.

The Venerables all repeatedly praised his words.

After this incident, Li Fan finally gained the complete trust of Dao Scribe Immortal and the others, truly integrating into the ranks of the Realm of Birth and Death Venerables.

In the subsequent exchanges, Li Fan gradually learned more of their secrets.

The white-haired youth was indeed a reproduction generated out of thin air through ideational methods by that Walker of Mountains and Seas.

A long time ago, the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables encountered the Walker of Mountains and Seas.

The Walker of Mountains and Seas told the Five Venerables about the ideational method and the state of the end of the Mountains and Seas.

At first, the Five Venerables did not believe it.

Thus, the Walker of Mountains and Seas personally demonstrated the great divine ability of ideational construction in front of the Five Venerables.

Amidst surging, blurry light and shadow, the white-haired youth slowly emerged.

Arriving in an unfamiliar territory, the white-haired youth was initially bewildered. However, upon sensing the situation of the Mountains and Seas he was in, and seeing the Walker of Mountains and Seas, who was greatly weakened by the ideational construction, he sighed sadly, "It seems I have ultimately failed."

The Walker of Mountains and Seas smiled and said, "But there is still a chance to salvage everything."

"Let's hope so. You go do your thing. If I fail again..."

"I will return," the Walker of Mountains and Seas stated confidently.

And then, he vanished from the sight of the Five Venerables.

The white-haired youth was named Qiu Xinhui. He was originally the most astonishing genius cultivator among the last remaining possibilities at the end of time.

A peerless genius who could still prove the Saintly position in the era of Dharma destruction, when all Saints had perished and the Great Dao was nearly extinguished!

However, Qiu Xinhui was born in the wrong era.

The Saints of the End of Time were not as powerful as those of the present era.

After Qiu Xinhui's calculations, even if he could traverse the Eternal Silence Void and successfully reach the previous epoch of the Mountains and Seas, he would be severely injured and degenerate into a mere transcendent cultivator.

Without the status of a Saint, what was the point of traveling to other timelines?

Thus, Qiu Xinhui abandoned the plan of personally traversing.

Instead, he created a [Walker of Mountains and Seas] to travel against the current, conveying the message to the Saints of past epochs.

To warn them not to give up, to unite, and to save the Mountains and Seas.

After nearly exhausting the power of the Saints, he finally succeeded in creating the Walker of Mountains and Seas.

Qiu Xinhui then began to execute his second plan.

This was a desperate gamble: at the final moment of the Mountains and Seas' return to the Stars, to go all out for self-preservation.

"So, that Walker of Mountains and Seas traveled against the current, from the end of the Mountains and Seas to the beginning. After completing his mission, he returned to the end of the Mountains and Seas. Seeing your original body's failed outcome, in order to salvage your fate, he then imparted the ideational method to the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables and reproduced you?" After hearing Qiu Xinhui's account, Li Fan vaguely understood.

The white-haired youth nodded.

"I have a few questions. Your original body could not freely travel the Mountains and Seas without being threatened by the Eternal Silence Void, so how did that Walker of Mountains and Seas manage it?" Li Fan frowned and asked.

"It's not that I cannot traverse and travel," Qiu Xinhui corrected Li Fan's mistake.

"It's just that after traversing, I would be severely weakened and lose my Saintly cultivation."

"Falling from Sainthood, and then attempting to recover through cultivation again is exceedingly difficult. Even I do not have absolute confidence."

"But that Walker of Mountains and Seas..."

"Has a special physique and possesses the ability to overcome countless setbacks."

"Even if he falls into the dust, as long as he is given enough resources and time, he can definitely recover to his former peak cultivation. He is the most suitable person to act as this Walker of Mountains and Seas, and I personally raised him, so he can be absolutely trusted," Qiu Xinhui explained.

This explanation somewhat made sense.

However, Li Fan still felt that Qiu Xinhui had not revealed everything.

Chapter 1668: The Two Approaches to Saving the World

“Second question. Being in the Realm of Birth and Death, how can we survive and persist until the end of the Mountains and Seas?”

“Separating the Mountains and Seas from the Eternal Silence Void, although it cannot compare to the great terror when the Mountains and Seas truly perish. However, it is not something ordinary people can withstand. Even if I become a Saint, I can only protect myself. I cannot ensure your safety,” Li Fan asked with a frown.

Qiu Xinhui exchanged glances with the other Venerables and smiled: “There is no need to trouble you, fellow Daoist. Traveling against the current, we are indeed powerless. But if we go with the flow, persisting towards the end of the Mountains and Seas…”

“With our accumulation over the years, it should still be barely possible.”

Qiu Xinhui then explained the specific method to Li Fan in detail.

“The [End of Mountains and Seas Saint] Qiu Xinhui, although ultimately perishing along with the destruction of the Mountains and Seas. However, in the Mountains and Seas before the end, he still existed.”

“I don’t know if you can understand what I’m saying,”

Li Fan nodded naturally: “This is like how the entire span of the Mountains and Seas is destined to head towards destruction, but we are currently in the prosperous Mountains and Seas, which is the same principle.”

Qiu Xinhui continued, “The existence of the [End of Mountains and Seas Saint] is like a lighthouse standing in the darkness. It dimly illuminates the direction of travel in the Eternal Silence Void. And by virtue of the connection I had with him before, if we use secret arts, we can instantly traverse thousands of mountains and rivers, even crossing several blocked sections of the Mountains and Seas to return.”

“Once this return process begins, it cannot be stopped. We cannot stop in any passing Mountains and Seas along the way. But originally, there was a fifty percent chance of successfully reaching the end of the Mountains and Seas. If we have your support again??”

“The possibility of success is more than seventy percent!”

“Relying on the mysterious power released at the moment of a clone returning to its main body?” Li Fan was an expert in the art of cloning himself. The power erupted at the moment a clone returned to its main body could indeed be exploited. But merely this, and expecting to fly across the Eternal Silence Void, was likely far from enough!

But Qiu Xinhui seemed to be speaking the truth.

Li Fan pondered for a moment, and a thought flickered in his heart: “I suppose this return process also involved significant effort from that Walker of Mountains and Seas.”

The white-haired youth nodded slightly: “Precisely. Without his footprints from walking and traversing, no matter how close the connection with the main body, it would be extremely dangerous to traverse smoothly, with a zero percent chance of survival.”

Li Fan, his guess confirmed, sighed with emotion: “This Walker of Mountains and Seas, although not a Saint, his actions and deeds are no less than those of a Saint!”

Li Fan had once thought that Sun Piaomiao was the Walker of Mountains and Seas.

However, from the appearance Qiu Xinhui had described, it did not match the image of Sun Piaomiao that Li Fan had glimpsed before.

“Perhaps Sun Piaomiao, like the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, also received a gift from the Walker of Mountains and Seas.”

“After all, according to Qiu Xinhui, every time the Walker of Mountains and Seas successfully traverses, he needs to rest for a long time to slowly recover his cultivation. During this time, his footprints would be spread throughout the Mountains and Seas, which is logical.”

While Li Fan was pondering, Qiu Xinhui continued to explain their plan.

“Once we successfully reach the end of the Mountains and Seas, I will return to my main body. Gaining the memories of these years out of thin air, and the support of an entire Realm of Birth and Death, might play a crucial role in reversing the final fate.”

Li Fan slowly reacted at this moment.

With an expression of astonishment, “If that’s the case, then throughout the entire span of the Mountains and Seas, from the beginning to the end, there are likely not just one such conceptual construct like yours.”

Qiu Xinhui, as if he had already accepted his destiny, smiled with ease.

“There are two saviors of the Mountains and Seas. One is countless Saints, who, in different time periods of the Mountains and Seas, like sparks, move towards the beginning of the Mountains and Seas, working together to resist the end times.”

“The second is that the Walker of Mountains and Seas, while traveling against the current, scattered my spiritual light everywhere. I, from every past segment of the Mountains and Seas, carried support power and returned one after another, also uniting the strength of the Mountains and Seas to find a way to break the predicament!”

Qiu Xinhui’s eyes shone brightly: “I am not the true body of that End of Mountains and Seas Saint, but a creation summoned from imagination. The memories I inherited are not complete, and I am even but one of countless conceptual constructs, not special. My ultimate fate has long been determined.”

“But my pursuit, the pursuit of all Qiu Xinhuis, has never changed.”

Qiu Xinhui looked at Li Fan and frankly stated: “That is, to truly lead the masses and walk out of the apocalypse of the Mountains and Seas!”

“Two attempts, one entrusted to the world, one from oneself. Perhaps by working together, complementing each other, there is truly a chance to reverse the situation.”

Li Fan seemed moved, and also shocked.

He remained silent for a long time.

“Truly a great talent, the [End of Mountains and Seas Saint]. Far from being comparable to me, a lucky one!”

“No wonder the Dao Scribe Immortals and all the others place such trust in you.”

Li Fan sighed in admiration, then said with surging emotions: “If that’s the case, then why not accompany a gentleman to the death?”

“Even if we cannot truly save the Mountains and Seas, to be able to meet the [End of Mountains and Seas Saint], would be a life without regret!”

Li Fan’s words also resonated with the other Venerables.

After a period of emotion, they discussed the specific details of that instant when the Mountains and Seas returned to the Stars.

“Through our deductions, the myriad possibilities flowing within the Realm of Birth and Death will truly be reborn at that moment, and will also be a great driving force for us to break free from the Mountains and Seas.”

“One must know that the number of imagined possibilities currently existing in the Realm of Birth and Death is only tens of thousands, but it can be barely considered a miniature reflection of our Mountains and Seas. If the plan proceeds smoothly, and fellow Daoists from other time-space segments also return…”

“Then the imagined constructs we gather will be like a miniaturized version of the entire span of the Mountains and Seas.”

“The Mountains and Seas will be completely destroyed, and the Stars will be born anew. An imagined world of Mountains and Seas will suddenly appear, perhaps with the might to overturn the heavens!”

…

Li Fan, with his quasi-Saint body, gained the absolute trust of all the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death.

Therefore, he learned of their plan to save the world.

Although the truthfulness of their depicted grand ambition could not be confirmed until the final moment, it must be said that Qiu Xinhui’s two attempts were indeed inspiring.

If Li Fan did not rely on [True Return], he might have truly tried it.

It was a pity…

With [True Return] by his side, Li Fan, who could always start over, would not be like Ming Dao Immortal and the others, who would fight until the end when the Mountains and Seas returned to the Stars.

“Of course, if it’s just to broaden one’s horizons, there’s no harm in trying.”

“The end of the Mountains and Seas, traversing the Eternal Silence Void…”

“In the simulation, I exposed the existence of [True Return] in front of the Saints of the Shore, which was because my own cultivation was too far behind the Saints.”

“But now, I possess the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin]. With the control [True Return] has over it, before I meet that End of Mountains and Seas Saint, achieving [Saint] status should not be difficult.”

“With Saint against Saint, even if I am slightly weaker than the opponent, I should not be completely seen through, right?”

Li Fan pondered in his heart, and at the same time, because it involved Saints, and furthermore, one standing at the end of the Mountains and Seas, being one of the most powerful in the entire span of the Mountains and Seas.

He was also very cautious and asked [True Return] for its opinion.

[True Return] remained silent and did not object.

Li Fan's own spiritual sense also did not issue a warning.

Thus, the plan was finalized.

The goal of the beings in the Realm of Birth and Death was the end of the Mountains and Seas.

Therefore, they paid almost no attention to the various aspects of the current time-space span of the Mountains and Seas.

They only secretly gathered talents for conceptual construction and accumulated strength.

While Li Fan comprehended the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin], he also did not forget to care about the matters of conceptual construction.

Despite the path to Sainthood being right before him, he could still resist the temptation and step aside to care about the cause of saving the world. Li Fan's actions were deeply admired by all the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death.

Only Li Fan himself knew that compared to the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, the conceptual method actually benefited him more.

“Qiu Xinhui is indeed worthy of being the [End of Mountains and Seas Saint]. This conceptual method has almost touched the threshold of the transformation between True and False.”

“However, the conceptual method still requires the foundation of memories of past real existences, while the transformation of True and False…”

Thinking of this, Li Fan was slightly stunned.

For a moment, he could not distinguish the specific differences between the conceptual method and the transformation of True and False.

He could not help but marvel even more at Qiu Xinhui’s talent.

“Although it is not any Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, it vaguely surpasses it by a margin.”

“If one must say, the conceptual method will eventually be exhausted by mental fatigue. While the transformation of True and False relies entirely on one’s own thoughts.”

“It surpasses by far!”

Li Fan inwardly chuckled with satisfaction.

As if sensing Li Fan's thoughts, [True Return] emitted some indecipherable fluctuations for some reason.

It vanished in an instant.

Li Fan could not delve deeper.

Years passed without notice in the Mountains and Seas.

After an unknown period, when the accumulation of the Realm of Birth and Death was finally sufficient.

Li Fan was also only one step away from achieving the [Xuan Pin] Great Saint.

“Achieving Sainthood in the Mountains and Seas is far more difficult than I imagined.”

Standing in the void, Li Fan let out a long sigh filled with worldly weariness.

The time required for this enlightenment was hundreds of times longer than the sum of his past reincarnations.

Fortunately, it was purely dry enlightenment, without too many worldly distractions interfering.

Furthermore, with the [True Return] panel occasionally flashing before his eyes, constantly reminding Li Fan of the past.

Li Fan ultimately did not forget his true identity.

“Achieving Sainthood is today.”

He solemnly chanted softly.

And around him, all the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death were silently watching over him, protecting him.

“The commotion generated by the path to becoming a Saint is too great; it’s impossible to conceal.”

“Therefore, the moment of becoming a Saint is the moment we travel and return.”

Li Fan instructed, then took a step forward.

“Great Dao returns to Truth.”

As he silently chanted in his heart, on the [True Return] panel, the dreamy, colorful light of the four words [First Xuan Pin] erupted with unprecedented brilliance.

Its radiance was so dazzling that it almost overshadowed all other characters on the panel.

Li Fan, as if he had truly transformed into the master of [Xuan Pin], wielding this Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

Just like when a mortal ascended to immortality in the past, Li Fan’s vision saw the appearance of the Mountains and Seas gradually change.

Although the Mountains and Seas remained boundless,

Mountains could be climbed, and seas could be crossed.

Floating on the sea, standing on the mountaintop.

Li Fan’s state of mind and perspective were naturally different.

The black Dao annihilation that permeated the Mountains and Seas in his sight also gradually changed.

“Still as terrifying as dark snakes, instilling fear. But if one fights desperately…”

“There might not be no chance of survival.”

Li Fan understood in his heart.

The path to becoming a Saint had just begun.

Body and Mountains and Seas as one, Li Fan seemed to be bathed in a peculiar aura.

Vague and unclear images flashed before his eyes.

They seemed to originate from the most ancient memories of the Mountains and Seas, even older than the Mountains and Seas themselves.

The images were indistinct, but Li Fan could clearly feel the awe and greed of the Mountains and Seas.

“ [God] . ”

“The source of all power in the Mountains and Seas,” Li Fan suddenly realized.

The moment this consciousness arose in his mind, the blurry images before him began to leap frantically.

Like primitive beasts, they violently collided within his vision.

Countless lines twisted, and something seemed about to leap out of sight, suddenly falling into reality!

At the same time, Li Fan's originally perfectly calm heart began to beat in sync uncontrollably.

Not from fear.

But from instinctive excitement, trembling.

“Xuan Pin returns!”

As inspiration struck, Li Fan suddenly chanted inwardly.

*Creak, creak, creak…*

The countless interwoven lines in his vision suddenly shattered.

Instantly fading into darkness.

Only one shadow became clearer and clearer.

Leaping out from a void perspective, descending into the Mountains and Seas.

*Whoosh!*

The Mountains and Seas instantly boiled!

Like a gust of strong wind, waves of terrifying magnitude surged from the sea, and giant trees on the mountains toppled.

In an instant, several gazes were cast from various parts of the Mountains and Seas.

And the Mountains and Seas themselves, after a brief period of calm, reacted even more violently.

Boiling and seething!

“Go!”

Li Fan slowly absorbed the shadow in his vision, speaking with extreme calmness.

At the same time, he exhaled a turbid breath, blocking all the wind and waves from the Mountains and Seas.

With the turbid breath expelled, heaven and earth were born, and all things evolved.

Amidst a resplendent brilliance, countless beings were born.

The cries of new life resounded, weaving into a grand symphony.

Drifting within the Mountains and Seas, it was lively for a time.

It even briefly suppressed the wind and thunder of the Mountains and Seas.

At the same time, it also concealed the sight of the Saints to a certain extent.

Although after a moment, this vibrant life turned into utter silence, like a collapsing mansion.

But in that instant.

Li Fan, along with the beings from the Realm of Birth and Death, vanished under the illumination of an orange-yellow radiance.

Heading towards the end of the Mountains and Seas.

They came and went as quickly as they arrived.

In the blink of an eye, the Mountains and Seas reappeared as they were.

However, due to the departure of the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin], the current Mountains and Seas now seemed to show signs of aging.

In a short period, thousands of possibilities collapsed violently, falling into the Dao annihilation.

Within the white circle of the Shore, the illusory figures of the Saints stood in succession.

“Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin]…”

“Strange.”

Within the white circle, the light and shadow flickered rapidly.

Deducing and calculating something.

Under normal circumstances, everything in this span of the Mountains and Seas should be under their control.

Regardless of what variable appeared, it was like water in a pool.

Even if ripples appeared, they could ultimately not create waves beyond a predetermined height.

But now…

The calm pool under the Saints’ eyes had somehow generated a waterspout, which was truly terrifying.

The light and shadow within the white circle shattered violently, and the Saints closed their illusory eyes, then simultaneously opened them.

In an instant, it was as if countless thoughts had been communicated.

But after a moment, they closed them again.

“No need to pursue.”

“Going to the end of the Mountains and Seas might be a turning point after all.”

“Let us focus on watching this span of the Mountains and Seas.”

“Regardless of the beginning or the end, regardless of unity or separation, exhausting all efforts, we cannot find a way to salvation. Now that a variable has appeared??”

“Perhaps it is a good thing.”

Chapter 1669: Infusing Infinity Spirit

Golden light wove a path forward.

Specks of footprints drifted from the void, serving both to point the way for everyone and to act as stepping stones as they traversed the Eternal Silence Void.

Perception of the outside world was distorted.

It felt as though the crossing took but an instant, yet also consumed millions of years of time.

Beyond the golden light lay boundless ink-black darkness.

Though shielded by the golden light, each passage through the blackness was but a fleeting touch.

Still, the Eternal Silence Void imparted a terrifying, chilling pressure upon them all.

Except for Li Fan, the very foundation of existence for everyone else, including all the Venerables, began to slowly crumble. The most direct manifestation was the reduction of their cultivation to varying degrees.

Even their very spirits were subtly affected.

A fall in cultivation realm could perhaps be slowly recovered through diligent practice, but a deficit in spirit…

Prodigies would perish, and the once-celebrated would become ordinary.

Under normal circumstances, the consequences were irreversible.

However…

Just as everyone was steadying their minds and seeking self-preservation,

Li Fan’s gaze was sharp, fixed intently on the Eternal Silence Void outside.

He vaguely sensed that within that boundless darkness, beyond the cold desolation, there was something else lurking.

“What is this…?”

“An aura of coalescing spirits?”

“How can the Eternal Silence Void, which should be completely empty, possess such a rich presence of true spirits?”

Initially, Li Fan was perplexed.

But after observing for a while, he quickly understood.

“The spiritual essence residue produced after the Mountains and Seas were devoured by Dao Annihilation. It’s akin to the ashes left after a mountain is incinerated by fire, or the fine sand and pebbles brought forth by the surging waves of the sea.”

Li Fan, blessed with infinite spiritual essence himself, naturally felt no inclination towards this spiritual residue within the Eternal Silence Void.

However, sensing the desperate struggle of the beings from the Realm of Birth and Death, he had a sudden thought.

“Though I possess infinite spiritual essence, I can only use it myself. If I wish to bestow it upon others, I can only achieve it indirectly through the 'Inheritance of True Return' option.”

“But what about these masterless things before me?”

“I have now attained the Saint realm, but my strength seems to have a significant gap compared to the 'Saints' I imagined. Only by successfully traversing the Eternal Silence Void can I truly be worthy of the name 'Saint.' Navigating this void will inevitably lead to contact with this spiritual residue. Could it be that the Holy Ones of the Shore's immense power is related to acquiring more spiritual essence?”

A myriad of thoughts flashed through his mind. Li Fan reached out his hand towards the boundless darkness above him.

It was as if an invisible vortex suddenly formed out of nowhere.

An unimaginable accumulation of sludge was stirred by Li Fan’s gentle wave of his hand.

Like a spring erupting violently, it was drawn from the Eternal Silence Void and descended.

The golden light protecting everyone suddenly distorted, as if it might shatter at any moment.

But this gust of wind came and went swiftly.

As Li Fan retracted his hand, the spiritual residue in the Eternal Silence Void ceased its surge.

And in Li Fan’s hand…

A mass of true spirit convergence, almost imperceptible by any means, yet Li Fan could sense its existence, swirling and refusing to dissipate.

“Summoned at will, dispersed at will.”

“Is it truly this easy to manipulate the accumulated spiritual essence?”

Li Fan mused, perplexed.

His intuition told him that the reality was likely not so straightforward.

Looking at the people from the Realm of Birth and Death who were jointly traversing the void, they seemed entirely unaware of the boundless spiritual residue accumulating outside, as if they had discovered nothing.

They could only steadfastly endure on their own.

Unable to even perceive it, let alone absorb and utilize it.

Li Fan felt a subtle realization.

The reason he could so effortlessly extract it was perhaps related to his own infinite spiritual essence.

Although the spiritual residue extracted from the Eternal Silence Void did not belong to him, he could still manipulate it with perfect control, as if commanding troops.

First, Li Fan attempted to absorb this spiritual essence himself.

Like a stone sinking into the sea, the extracted spiritual essence was instantly swallowed by more than half, yet it had no effect whatsoever.

This result was within Li Fan’s expectations.

After all, his own spiritual essence was already “infinite,” so absorbing more from the outside world could hardly bring about any change.

Li Fan shook his head inwardly, ceasing such meaningless actions.

Next, looking at the slowly dissipating beings of the Realm of Birth and Death, Li Fan slowly began to attempt to refine and distribute the remaining accumulated spiritual essence to everyone.

It was much more strenuous than Li Fan had imagined.

Though the formless accumulated spiritual essence was indeed under Li Fan’s control to a certain extent, it quickly divided into seven portions, gathering above the heads of the Venerables, excluding Qiu Xinhui.

But they only got close.

They did not truly integrate into them.

It seemed as if a layer of invisible barrier existed between their bodies and the accumulated spiritual essence, creating a separation.

Li Fan applied slight pressure, but this barrier remained unyielding.

“It seems I was being too presumptuous. If increasing spiritual essence were truly this easy, this world would likely be teeming with Saints.”

However, Li Fan did not give up so easily.

Before reaching the end of the Mountains and Seas, seizing this rare opportunity for traversal, he continued to research the accumulated spiritual essence.

The path of traversal seemed endless.

The golden light that protected them weaved and drifted, and the traces left by the Walker of Mountains and Seas flashed continuously.

Li Fan could keenly sense that the passing mountain and sea sceneries ahead, flashing by, were becoming increasingly dim.

And the pressure emanating from the Eternal Silence Void outside grew ever more immense.

The golden light that protected them was forced to shrink.

The trend of collapse for the beings of the Realm of Birth and Death also gradually increased.

“If things continue like this, even if they succeed in reaching the end of the Mountains and Seas, they will all become cripples.”

“Only the imagined torrents they brought along will have some use.”

Though he possessed a boundless treasure trove, he could not share even a sliver with others.

“It seems it is up to your own fortune.”

However, perhaps due to the blessing of infinite spiritual essence, Li Fan’s research proceeded with unexpected smoothness.

As the path of traversal along the current was nearing its end, he actually found a method to forcefully infuse true spirits into others!

He didn’t directly act on the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death. Instead, he began an experiment on one of the former inhabitants of Guangwu Star Sea who was on the verge of dissipating.

“The reason I can absorb without hindrance is because I have infinite spiritual essence within me. The return of true spirits is like a hundred rivers flowing into the sea, a natural and effortless process.”

“But for others, the true spirits they possess are even less than the stronger spiritual essence about to be infused. Towards this intruder that surpasses their own, they naturally raise a high wall…”

“If that’s the case, then let’s unleash a boundless flood that will drown this wall!”

With this thought, Li Fan reached out violently towards the Eternal Silence Void.

With a fierce grasp, he drew out an unimaginable amount of concentrated spiritual residue.

Manipulating it, he shaped it into what resembled a waterfall descending from the heavens, and forcefully poured it onto the experiment subject’s head.

The true spirit did not enter the body, but instead continued to accumulate above the head.

Though undergoing the experiment, the subject was completely unaware of its own predicament and felt a subtle unease.

With extreme alertness, it looked around.

However, it could not find the source of its fear.

The true spirit continued to accumulate, forming a dark cloud hundreds of feet thick.

But the barrier within the subject’s body was incredibly resilient. Even with a hundredfold pressure of external true spirits, it did not collapse.

Li Fan had to increase the intensity again.

After all, he was only drawing from the accumulated spiritual residue in the Eternal Silence Void, so it was not a waste.

Finally, when the spiritual level used for the impact was thousands of times greater than that of the experiment subject,

The invisible barrier shattered with a resounding crack.

In an instant, as if receiving a divine epiphany, the subject’s eyes widened, and their being was fundamentally transformed.

Almost at a speed visible to the naked eye, their spiritual essence became incredibly potent.

They could even faintly sense their own attributes and looked sharply in Li Fan’s direction.

However, it was precisely this glance that brought about their demise.

Li Fan frowned slightly, stopping the infusion.

He remotely grasped the experiment subject with his hand and examined it closely.

After a thousandfold consumption of corrosive force, less than one-thousandth of the successfully infused true spirit actually entered the subject’s body.

Even so, for the experiment subject, it was a transformative change.

“Compared to the method of increasing spiritual essence through inheritance, my infusion method is simple and crude. But the price is??”

Though their spiritual essence had multiplied, they also suddenly glimpsed many things beyond their cognition within a short period.

Fear, terror, unease, the unknown – such emotions began to surround the experiment subject’s heart.

Their originally clear and intelligent gaze gradually took on a hint of madness.

More importantly, as Li Fan had forcefully broken through the invisible barrier within their body earlier.

This experiment subject now had no resistance to the external accumulated spiritual essence.

The torrent of accumulated spirit that had not been absorbed by him returned again.

The experiment subject could still absorb a portion.

However, the speed of its progress and transformation was ultimately limited.

It was far from keeping pace with the surging mud.

With repeated scouring, something that made Li Fan quite horrified occurred.

The experiment subject’s soul, body, and consciousness, finally under the impact of accumulated true spirit, completely dissolved and disintegrated.

In that instant, it vanished without a sound.

Becoming another part of the abundant true spirit accumulating beside Li Fan’s hand.

This process of demise was too rapid.

Li Fan had initially anticipated the extent of the experiment subject’s transformation. But after a moment, the other party had already merged into the surge of true spirit.

The infusion experiment was both successful and a failure.

“In theory, one only needs to control the intensity of the infusion to avoid such a fatal outcome.”

“However…”

Li Fan looked at the swirling mass of accumulated spiritual essence beside him, as if seeing the origin of their coming.

Countless ancient beings who once existed in the Mountains and Seas.

Like numerous ghosts, standing solemnly and solemnly, staring fixedly at Li Fan with eerie smiles.

A sense of discomfort inexplicably arose in Li Fan’s heart. He flicked his hand, and threw these accumulated spiritual essences back into the Eternal Silence Void.

“The Mountains and Seas perished, yet spiritual essence accumulated.”

“When the Mountains and Seas are fully restored, the Stars will be born from the Eternal Silence Void. In that case, wouldn’t this endless accumulated spiritual essence be the incubator for the birth of the [Stars]?”

Instinctively, Li Fan felt a sense of extreme caution towards this spiritual essence that he could manipulate at will.

He temporarily put aside the idea of further experimentation.

“From the discovery on that experiment subject, the invisible barrier within my body is the fundamental reason why I, despite having infinite spiritual essence, cannot freely utilize it. If this barrier were to be removed…”

The moment this thought arose, the 'True Return', which usually remained silent, immediately emitted a trembling warning!

Li Fan had never experienced 'True Return' reacting so strongly.

It was as if if he were to truly break the barrier within his body, a catastrophe that even 'True Return' could not reverse would descend.

Such a reaction frightened Li Fan, and he immediately abandoned his speculative thoughts.

As if still not feeling at ease, the warning from True Return echoed, its residual waves lingering in Li Fan’s heart for a long time.

It wasn't until this journey of traversing along the current finally concluded, and they leaped out of the Eternal Silence Void to the end of the Mountains and Seas, that Li Fan finally understood the reason for True Return’s solemn warning.

“For ordinary people in the Mountains and Seas, if the barrier were removed, at most their own spiritual essence would disappear, or external spiritual essence would be infused. Whether they achieve Sainthood or perish, it would hardly affect the overall situation of the Mountains and Seas.”

“But within me, there is infinite spiritual essence.”

“Perhaps, compared to the entirety of the accumulated spiritual essence in the Eternal Silence Void after the complete annihilation of the Mountains and Seas, it is not even comparable.”

“If the barrier within me were to be broken…”

Li Fan suddenly shivered.

“Not only myself would be in peril.”

“Perhaps the remaining Mountains and Seas would also be…”

Li Fan’s vision seemed to show endless true spirits, pouring out from his body due to the collapse of the barrier.

Like a raging flood after a broken dam, rolling forth.

Intending to instantly overturn the Mountains and Seas.

“Already barely surviving under Dao Annihilation, if such a disaster were to occur again.”

“The Mountains and Seas would perish in an instant.”

Realizing this, Li Fan understood True Return’s reaction.

At the same time, a greater doubt arose in the depths of his heart.

“Where did the infinite spiritual essence within me come from?”

“If…?”

“After I truly die, what will happen to these unfettered true spirits?”

“Did True Return find me because of my infinite spiritual essence, or did it impose itself upon me out of fear that my unbound infinite true spirits would destroy the Mountains and Seas?”

Heavy doubts assailed him,

Causing Li Fan, who had now reached the Saint realm, to momentarily lose his composure.

Fortunately, the intense changes in the outside world quickly forced him to shift his attention.

A ray of light above, barely holding back the darkness. Although they had left the Eternal Silence Void, they had not truly escaped.

It was as if they could be pulled back into that boundless, cold darkness at any moment.

“Hold your breath and steady your will.”

The one speaking was Qiu Xinhui, who had become extremely weak during the traversal, almost annihilating himself directly.

But now, he was like a changed person.

A charismatic aura that inspired people and commanded instinctive admiration surged from him.

Li Fan immediately understood.

The person before him was not the imagined creation Qiu Xinhui, but the true body of Qiu Xinhui – the End of Mountains and Seas Saint!

Li Fan’s gaze met Qiu Xinhui’s eyes, as if he were facing the Holy Ones of the Shore once again.

The outer layer, serving as a disguise, was about to be peeled away, revealing the core within.

But unlike in the past.

The Mystic Orb Great Dao, like clothing, lightly veiled the secrets about to be revealed.

Chapter 1670: All Saints Display Their Divine Powers

The Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, by its very nature, possessed its own rhythm. Its profundity and myriad transformations were such that even Saints found it difficult to fully comprehend at a single glance.

Adorned with the guise of the Mysterious Conception, Li Fan had successfully managed to shield himself from the scrutiny of the End of Mountains and Seas Saint.

However, Li Fan harbored a nagging intuition that this "garment" used for concealment would not remain effective indefinitely.

"If he were to continue observing, it is likely that the existence of [True Return] would be exposed before long."

Fortunately, Qiu Xinhui did not press his inquiry further.

The sensation of being scrutinized gradually faded. Qiu Xinhui's voice, filled with emotion, resonated, "To traverse the Mountains and Seas, enduring hardship to arrive here…?"

"You have labored, fellow Daoist."

"The End of Mountains and Seas is a peculiar state. Perhaps it differs from the timing of the Mountains and Seas you are familiar with. For now, please observe."

"I shall first attend to their needs."

With these words, countless yellow gemstones erupted from Qiu Xinhui's hand, scattering like stars into the Realm of Birth and Death.

Their radiant brilliance illuminated all beings.

Upon the forehead of each living creature, an imprint of a yellow crystalline gem was etched. Nourished by their luminescence, those whose existential foundations had slowly begun to crumble due to the traversal, felt as if they were being replenished. Not only was their perilous situation alleviated, but many were even restored to their former state on the spot.

It was not merely the living beings.

The myriad streams of ideation within the Realm of Birth and Death, which had been on the verge of collapse, instantly solidified with this assistance.

They were now indistinguishable from true possibilities within the Mountains and Seas.

Even with Li Fan's current accomplishments, he found it difficult to discern their true nature for a time.

The End of Mountains and Seas Saint, with a single move, had displayed unfathomable, extraordinary power.

Li Fan looked at the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death, who, under his healing, had become vigorous once more in the blink of an eye.

"It is not that their lost true spirits in the Eternal Silence Void have been replenished. Rather, Qiu Xinhui, using the ultimate art of ideation, has filled the gaps that were diminished."

"Although their cultivation talent is surely not as great as before, at least their lives have been preserved, and their strength can still be utilized about seventy to eighty percent."

"This End of Mountains and Seas Saint is truly formidable!"

Li Fan inwardly marveled.

Having previously delved deeply into the Dao of Ideation, Li Fan naturally knew how incredible it was to effortlessly fill the deficiencies of others. It implied that Qiu Xinhui's understanding of each person's respective Dao path was so profound that he could manipulate it with ease, making the imitation indistinguishable from the original.

And the fact that the replenished and stabilized myriad possibilities also indicated that Qiu Xinhui's comprehension of the Mountains and Seas had reached an unimaginable height.

However, what puzzled Li Fan was that Qiu Xinhui resided at the End of Mountains and Seas. Even with his monstrous talent, capable of easily comprehending all the Daos in existence, how could he possess knowledge of the past glories of the Mountains and Seas?

As if sensing Li Fan's internal query, the End of Mountains and Seas Saint calmly repeated, "Fellow Daoist, please observe the Mountains and Seas."

"All your doubts will be dispelled."

Li Fan then shifted his focus from Qiu Xinhui to the so-called End of Mountains and Seas.

The place where they were gathered was enveloped by a thick, earthy yellow light. Therefore, Li Fan did not feel the pressure of the Eternal Silence Void outside.

Everything seemed outwardly normal.

But when Li Fan's gaze attempted to pierce through this protective layer and look beyond the Mountains and Seas,

An boundless, icy sense of solitude assailed him from all directions.

This was vastly different from his experience during the traversal of the Eternal Silence Void.

During the traversal, it was merely pure oppressive pressure.

But at the End of Mountains and Seas, this pervasive darkness was filled with intense aggression.

Sensing Li Fan's gaze, it surged violently as if a stormy sea crashing against the shore, impacting them fiercely.

Li Fan distinctly felt that the entire enveloped Mountains and Seas, within the yellow light, was violently shaking.

And once the attack commenced, it did not cease easily.

The impacts from the Eternal Silence Void came wave after wave.

Like a tiny boat in a torrential storm, it seemed liable to be engulfed by the behemoth waves at any moment.

Li Fan's expression turned grim, and he subconsciously withdrew his gaze from the outside world.

The End of Mountains and Seas Saint, however, seemed accustomed to all this.

Without a word, he merely stimulated the ideational yellow light to stabilize the situation.

Like an experienced captain calmly guiding his crew through a sudden storm.

However, this storm was incredibly protracted and showed no signs of weakening.

"Is the Eternal Silence Void truly this tempestuous?" Li Fan inquired, astonished.

"If we consider the long war between the Mountains and Seas and Dao Annihilation, then at this moment, this war is finally nearing its end. The soldiers' killing intent is at its fiercest, seeking a conclusive victory to utterly annihilate the Mountains and Seas."

"What you perceive as the Eternal Silence Void may simply be the nascent stage of the war, its aggression not yet fully manifest." The darkness's encroachment from the outside was commonplace for Qiu Xinhui.

While simultaneously aiding the newly arrived, and fending off the intrusion of the Eternal Silence Void, he still had the capacity to explain the specific circumstances of the End of Mountains and Seas to Li Fan.

"However, what I wished to invite fellow Daoist to observe is not the void itself, but these…?"

Following Qiu Xinhui's guidance, Li Fan discovered that amidst the surging tide outside, there were occasional flashes of extremely faint points of light.

Dimmer than fireflies, they hid in the darkness, almost impossible to discern.

If one wasn't careful, they would be overlooked.

Li Fan vaguely sensed images of the past Mountains and Seas within these light points.

"Are these… fragments of the Mountains and Seas?"

Qiu Xinhui nodded: "Precisely, the remnants of the Mountains and Seas, shattered by Dao Annihilation."

"They are the last proof of the Mountains and Seas' past existence."

"Like gravel and debris, scattered in the darkness. Perhaps the Eternal Silence Void intentionally placed them, as a testament to its achievements. Or perhaps…"

"A form of intimidation towards us, the last resisters."

Qiu Xinhui smiled.

"Like dead coral on the seabed, constantly battered ashore by the rolling waves."

"Within these intermittently surfacing fragments, though I reside at the End of Mountains and Seas, I am able to witness the glorious scenes of the past Mountains and Seas."

"Coupled with…"

"The memories of all of you travelling from the past to arrive here from time to time."

Li Fan gradually began to understand.

This End of Mountains and Seas Saint had managed to weave his understanding of the Mountains and Seas solely from the scattered fragments of the past.

It was truly unimaginable; if he had lived in a normal temporal existence within the Mountains and Seas, what heights would he have reached?

"However, fellow Daoist, you do not seem to have achieved Sainthood through the Dao of Ideation?"

During their previous exchange, it wasn't just Li Fan who had been scrutinized.

Li Fan had also perceived some mysteries from Qiu Xinhui.

Although the Dao of Ideation was pervasive at the End of Mountains and Seas, it was not Qiu Xinhui's foundational cultivation.

Qiu Xinhui did not deny it: "Although the method of ideation is exceptionally profound, in this waning era of the Mountains and Seas, it is incapable of supporting the last bastion of purity."

"If I were to achieve Sainthood through this path, my own existence might be preserved, but this place would surely have long since vanished into Dao Annihilation."

Qiu Xinhui did not explicitly state his own Dao path.

But Li Fan vaguely felt that this End of Mountains and Seas Saint was different from Saints who achieved their status through the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas.

"The fate of the Mountains and Seas all rests upon me."

"Contemplating ancient remnants, comprehending divine abilities for salvation in despair."

"If not for this person urging the Walker of Mountains and Seas to journey upstream, traversing all of history. The powerful beings of all epochs of the Mountains and Seas might still be fighting individually."

Li Fan remained silent, gazing at the so-called End of Mountains and Seas shrouded in darkness.

Unlike the Mountains and Seas where Li Fan was from, time no longer existed here.

Only the "present moment" remained.

Without past or future, all events occurred simultaneously within this single point.

As Li Fan gradually adapted, various scenes naturally emerged before his eyes.

These were the people from various past segments of the Mountains and Seas, who, like himself, had come to offer support.

Compared to Li Fan, their predicament was even more tragic.

The vast majority had become individuals without cultivation talent upon their arrival.

Although Qiu Xinhui had helped them with the Dao of Ideation, their state was thereafter fixed at the moment of their arrival.

The number of Saints who had successfully reached the End of Mountains and Seas was pitifully small.

Including Li Fan, there were only five.

Together, they guarded the last hope of all beings.

Before Li Fan floated a vision of the Mountains and Seas, a starry expanse glittering in the void.

This was precisely the collective ideation gathered from the past Mountains and Seas.

"What is the success rate now?"

One figure pointed towards the illusory Mountains and Seas ahead.

Instantly, the darkness outside seemed to surge. The vision of the Mountains and Seas flickered for a moment, then dimmed.

This process was repeated countless times in an instant.

However, not once was the light of the Mountains and Seas rekindled.

"Still falling short," that figure sighed.

"Everyone, do not be disheartened. The end of the Mountains and Seas was already set. For us to defy fate and alter it is naturally not an easy task. I have intercepted the river of time, fixing it at the moment before destruction. As long as my power does not dissipate, there will be ample time to accumulate more strength."

The speaker was a white-haired scholar.

It was he who had created the current state of the End of Mountains and Seas, where time was suspended.

"The materials for ideation are practically sufficient. However, at the moment the Mountains and Seas are fully restored, the swallowing force unleashed by the Eternal Silence Void, even if we combine our strengths, we can barely escape it," the figure who was deducing the illusory Mountains and Seas spoke again.

This Saint's form was indistinct, as if in constant flux, lacking a fixed shape.

"If only we had more helpers."

Silence filled the air.

Qiu Xinhui appeased them: "Having the assistance of all of you is already a great fortune. This plan for the End of Mountains and Seas, after all, is less stable than heading towards the beginning of the Mountains and Seas. After all, for the vast majority of people, the future is unknown. But what has already happened is fixed and unchangeable."

The white-haired scholar stroked his beard and sighed: "This is only natural human sentiment, and cannot be forced. Even if the plan succeeds, the ultimate destination remains uncertain. Unlike that other plan, which even holds the hope of stealing the power of the Mountains and Seas to achieve something greater."

At this remark, all the Saints in the hall let out cold snorts.

Li Fan naturally understood what the white-haired scholar was referring to.

If, at the beginning of time, they had successfully prevented the Mountains and Seas from being devoured by the Gods.

Then, it would indeed have been possible to claim the power of the [Gods] for themselves.

Much like what the Mountains and Seas had done in the past.

For the Saints within the Mountains and Seas, the temptation was indeed immense.

"It's just a pity that, observing the river of time flowing and transforming, there seems to be no sign of this plan succeeding."

The white-haired scholar's gaze seemed to pierce through the obstructions of the Eternal Silence Void, looking towards the ancient Mountains and Seas.

He spoke with a sneer.

"Fellow Daoist, what are your thoughts?"

After the Saints had expressed their opinions, Qiu Xinhui turned to the ever-silent Li Fan.

The shroud of the Mysterious Conception Dao weaved around him, desperately attempting to block the gazes of the Saints.

Li Fan pondered for a moment before speaking: "I cultivate the Dao of [Mysterious Conception]."

"By infusing ideation into the Mountains and Seas, I can induce spontaneous life force."

Saying this, Li Fan's hand moved like a brush, painting wisps of life force into the illusory Mountains and Seas before him.

As the vision of the Mountains and Seas received the infusion of life force, various changes began to occur.

If previously it was merely an impressionistic landscape painting, it was now transforming into something akin to a realistic oil painting.

"However, this can only assist the ideational Mountains and Seas and sustain them for a while longer. The key to the plan still lies with all of you," Li Fan said apologetically.

"With your assistance, our chances of success increase by a few points," the ever-changing Saint spoke again after further deduction.

Although the starry light of the Mountains and Seas had not been reignited, he still spoke thus.

"However, I have an idea. I wonder if it is feasible."

After another long period of silence, Li Fan suddenly spoke.

"Fellow Daoist, please speak freely." Qiu Xinhui nodded.

"Those dormant true spirits within the Eternal Silence Void, could they be utilized as assistance?"

"Since the assistance from the past is insufficient, then we shall create our own."

"During the traversal of the void, I discovered the accumulation of true spirits within it, more than enough to elevate someone to Sainthood…"

The Saints listened to Li Fan's words, their eyes showing surprise.

"Creating Saints?"

They did not directly reject Li Fan's plan, but instead inquired cautiously: "Although we can absorb a minuscule portion of the accumulated true spirits and utilize them for ourselves, firstly, these true spirits originate from the void and will impact our minds. More importantly, mobilizing even a fraction of true spirit requires intense effort, making it unsustainable. Does fellow Daoist possess some unique method?"

Li Fan did not deny it, nodding proudly.

"Everyone, please observe!"

Saying this, Li Fan beckoned towards the dark void at the End of Mountains and Seas.

What happened was far more significant than during the traversal.

The End of Mountains and Seas, as if situated at the bottom of an endless abyss. All the accumulated true spirits, transformed from the devoured Mountains and Seas, were piled here.

When Li Fan stirred them slightly, it was as if the sky was collapsing.

The impact of the storm, which was already fierce, was now compounded by the violent collision of an unknown ferocious beast.

The combined efforts of the Saints stabilized the situation.

When the wind and rain eventually subsided, they all looked at Li Fan's hand with expressions of utter horror.

There, although no entity could be seen,

They could sense the aura of accumulated true spirits.

"How can this be?!"

The white-haired scholar's beard and hair bristled, looking at Li Fan in disbelief.

His ancient eyes seemed to rewind the river of time, attempting to trace Li Fan's origins.

He felt they had just been talking about the people of the Realm of Birth and Death, but it was only a guess.

Chapter 1671: Treasures in the Eyes of the Saints

The long river churned, its currents of time flowing backward, witnessing countless years.

Yet, it ultimately failed to reflect the figure of Li Fan.

As if he had leaped beyond the Three Realms and was no longer bound by the Five Elements.

The white-haired scholar's expression grew increasingly solemn.

The other venerable Saints, witnessing this utterly unbelievable event, all turned their gaze towards Li Fan.

They had all arrived from different timelines, having traversed the desolate void. Therefore, they understood how immensely difficult it was to summon the accumulated true spirits from that realm.

Yet, the person before them, with a mere wave of his hand, had summoned countless true spirits, causing them to surge forth.

Could it be that this individual represented the will of the desolate void itself?

At this thought, all the Saints became wary.

Facing the Saints' imposing pressure, Li Fan remained unperturbed.

Empowered by the Profound Embryo Great Dao, he stood on equal footing with these Saints. Whatever might happen, he would have the capacity to calmly return to truth.

Amidst the tense atmosphere, it was Qiu Xin Hui, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, who stepped forward to mediate.

"The currents of the Mountains and Seas are vast, and the Saints are all unique. In the past, the Mountains and Seas were filled with countless capable individuals, so the emergence of any extraordinary divine ability is not surprising."

"Although the accumulated true spirits of the desolate void have been drawn here, I have not sensed any fluctuations from the darkness. I believe this is a unique capability of our Daoist friend."

Although the other Saints harbored doubts about Li Fan, they placed their unwavering trust in Qiu Xin Hui.

Upon hearing this, their expressions softened slightly.

Li Fan did not seek to prove himself but smiled and said, "In truth, I too only discovered this special ability while traversing the void. I am also curious about its origin. However, at this moment, none of that is important."

"The crucial point is whether these endless accumulated true spirits within the void can be utilized by us."

Sensing the magnitude of the true spirits piled in Li Fan's palm, the Saints fell silent.

"Daoist friend speaks the truth. If we can truly seize their fortune, even in this era where the Great Dao is in decline and the Mountains and Seas are at their end, and where Saints do not emerge, it would be sufficient for us to create helpers capable of turning the tide."

"Even if they are not Saints, as long as their numbers are sufficient..." the white-haired scholar agreed with a nod.

"Furthermore, we ourselves could absorb the accumulated true spirits to replenish our own essence." the shifting figure said, its form becoming even more indistinct, as if contemplating its future after merging with a large quantity of accumulated true spirits.

"If that is the case, allow me to experiment first." A golden figure, shrouded in the ethereal glow of imagination, emerged from Qiu Xin Hui's body. It seemed to be a clone born from Qiu Xin Hui's thoughts, yet it represented Qiu Xin Hui's own will.

The imaginary clone drifted slowly towards the accumulated true spirits, as if drawn by some force.

Its speed increased, instantly transforming into a thin line that rapidly traversed the marsh of accumulated spirits.

It circled back to Qiu Xin Hui's location.

As everyone watched, the imaginary form indeed carried a faint shadow after passing through the accumulated true spirits.

"The effect is indeed akin to traversing the desolate void, though the efficiency of attaching true spirits has been significantly reduced."

After a long pause, Qiu Xin Hui slowly spoke.

The Saints' expressions became even more astonished.

"However, it is far less dangerous than in the desolate void, and there is no risk of mental peril. Does this not imply..." Before the shifting figure could finish speaking, it surged into the cluster of accumulated true spirits.

In an instant, it felt as though it had traversed dozens of times, causing ripples and disturbances.

It stopped, still full of lingering excitement, when it could no longer absorb any more true spirits in a short period.

As if having had a full meal, the shifting figure became noticeably clearer.

Simultaneously, its speed of transformation also improved.

"Incredible." a voice of astonishment echoed from beyond this figure.

The shifting figure, which had ventured into the accumulated true spirits and gained significant rewards through its risky endeavor, shattered the moment this voice sounded.

It transformed into a streak of light and returned to its source.

Li Fan observed clearly.

The final Saint of the Mountains and Seas and the shifting figure had, within moments, used their clones to test the dangers and intricacies of the accumulated true spirits.

Qiu Xin Hui had used an imaginary clone, while the shifting figure...

"It appeared as if he acted personally, yet he was in a state of being simultaneously fixed and unfixed, with countless future possibilities intertwined. At any moment, he could have rendered the outcome as merely a fictional state within his deductions. Conversely, he could also have declared this trial result as absolute truth."

As if confirming Li Fan's judgment, the true shifting figure, after the stream of light merged, revealed results similar to its trial clone: it had benefited greatly from absorbing a certain amount of accumulated true spirits.

With these two paving the way, the remaining Saints cast aside their lingering concerns.

Each displayed their divine abilities and absorbed the accumulated true spirits brought forth by Li Fan.

The auras of the Saints fluctuated, indicating clear progress.

"Could it be that, aside from myself, the other Saints find it this easy to absorb the accumulated true spirits?"

Witnessing this scene, Li Fan mused inwardly.

However, after the Saints finished absorbing the true spirits, their complexions and expressions all seemed to improve. Li Fan then understood.

The Concurrent Calamity Venerables had likely sustained varying degrees of damage during their confrontation with the desolate void.

Their very spirits had gradually depleted.

Without repairing it through ordinary means, the accumulated damage had worsened over time.

Even for a Saintly body, it had become a hidden danger.

Indeed, there were accumulated true spirits within the desolate void that could be utilized. However, venturing deep into the void, one risked annihilation at the slightest misstep. To gain one portion of true spirit required ten portions of depletion – a truly unfavorable trade.

Therefore, the idea of healing and enhancing true spirits by entering the void was baseless.

But now…

It turned out that Saints could transport the accumulated true spirits from the desolate void to the present Mountains and Seas out of thin air.

Furthermore, these true spirits were proven to be uncontaminated by the void and could be absorbed by everyone without worry.

After a round of healing, the Saints looked at Li Fan with newfound respect.

Though Li Fan had remained unfazed when pressured by the Saints, being gazed upon as if he were a treasure made him inwardly uneasy.

"Our chances of victory were still lacking."

"But now, with the help of Daoist friend, victory is within reach!" the shifting figure exclaimed with joy.

Only now did Li Fan understand that their so-called "lacking chances" referred to having no probability of success at all.

"It is truly our fortune that Daoist friend has come," Qiu Xin Hui lamented.

His eyes flickered with an inexplicable emotion as he gazed towards the past of the Mountains and Seas.

"Truly, by some unseen destiny, there are predetermined arrangements." Recalling something, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas became momentarily lost in thought, murmuring to himself.

"May I ask, esteemed elders, how feasible do you consider my Saint Creation plan?" Li Fan asked the Saints, his voice resonating.

"Dare I ask, Daoist friend, what is the cost of summoning the accumulated true spirits?" the white-haired scholar asked with utmost solemnity.

"Effortless," Li Fan replied proudly.

The Saints' expressions shifted further.

From the shifting figure, a beam of light erupted.

It seemed to contain billions of light and shadows, simultaneously projecting different future possibilities.

In the blink of an eye, the beam, initially bright, began to fade and wither.

Yet, it did not entirely descend into darkness; a sliver of light ultimately remained.

Returning to the shifting figure, the beam seemed to have merged with it.

"If what you say is true, that you can summon the accumulated true spirits freely and without harm,"

"The success rate of our plan has already surpassed one-tenth!"

Upon hearing this, the expressions of all the Saints and Li Fan drastically changed.

"So high!"

"So low?"

A gasp of surprise was followed by Li Fan and the Saints exchanging bewildered glances.

"However, a one-tenth chance of success is hardly considered high," Li Fan frowned.

Qiu Xin Hui smiled and shook his head. "We are already seeking a sliver of hope from the impossible. A one-tenth chance is already a wonderful outlook we never dared to imagine before. In my previous deductions, even a one-percent chance of success would have been worth fighting for with all our might!"

The other Saints agreed, only Li Fan remained somewhat perplexed.

However, he did not argue further.

Once the shifting figure's deduction was revealed, Li Fan keenly sensed that the oppressive atmosphere that had pervaded the end of the Mountains and Seas had subtly dissipated.

As the Saints conversed, their demeanor became noticeably more relaxed.

"Using the accumulated true spirits to nurture the imagined Mountains and Seas."

"When the aid within the Mountains and Seas becomes abundant and reaches a certain scale, that will be the time our plan is put into motion."

The white-haired scholar stroked his beard and said: "At that time, I should still have some time left before my lifespan is exhausted. Perhaps I will have the chance to witness the true face of the [Stars]. What fortune indeed!"

As the Saints conversed, Li Fan also gained a deeper understanding of how others utilized [True Spirits].

For the vast majority of beings in the Mountains and Seas, true spirits were the embodiment of their spiritual essence and cultivation aptitude. The Saints speculated that true spirits originated from the [Gods] who created the Mountains and Seas.

Below the Saintly level, true spirits were predetermined by destiny.

One could only slightly increase them by absorbing other versions of oneself from different possibilities.

However, the extent of growth was limited.

Once one ascended to the Saintly realm, replenishment could be obtained from the outside world by traversing the desolate void.

Yet, the same problem persisted: traversing the void was exceedingly perilous.

Survival itself was difficult, let alone enhancing one's spiritual essence.

Only among the most powerful Saints, whose strength allowed them to replenish more than they depleted during each traversal, did they possess the qualification to continuously travel against the current, reaching the earliest moments of the Mountains and Seas.

The Saints dwelling at the end of the Mountains and Seas had not yet reached this level.

"All those possessing such power would choose to journey to the beginning of the Mountains and Seas, vying for the power of the [Gods] to further advance themselves."

"And the invisible barrier I sensed, which limits the connection between my own true spirits and the outside world, does indeed exist."

"Only by achieving Sainthood, with a power equivalent to that of the Mountains and Seas, can it be shaken."

"If a massive amount of accumulated true spirits were forcefully injected to impact it..."

Li Fan's mind flashed with the image of an experimental subject submerged by accumulated true spirits and vanishing into nothingness.

However, for the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas, this was not an insurmountable problem.

Their research fervor surpassed even Li Fan's.

They even began conducting experiments on themselves.

Qiu Xin Hui and the shifting figure's methods were beyond description.

As for the others, the white-haired scholar's eyes surged with the river of time.

It flowed forth, appearing almost tangible, roaring mightily.

Then, fleeting images of the scholar in his youth, adulthood, and middle age leaped out from the river of time.

Whether the experiments conducted on them would affect the white-haired scholar downstream in the river of time was entirely within his control.

Another Saint held a scale.

Towards the direction of the accumulated true spirits, he reached out and grabbed.

It was as if he had pulled them into the scale.

And on the other side, numerous light and shadow figures soon appeared.

The scale swayed continuously, indicating different experimental outcomes.

...

The Saint Li Fan found most astonishing was the outwardly most leisurely one.

A nonchalant middle-aged man with a large belly, his expression carefree.

However, whenever the experimental results of other Saints proved beneficial,

this stout man's face would light up with joy, and he would repeatedly flick his fingers.

Orbs of light were drawn into his palm.

These orbs collided and merged, gradually becoming one.

The final orb, it seemed, contained the optimal solution that all the Saints sought to verify.

The Saints displayed their unique abilities and arts, filling Li Fan with awe.

However, for some inexplicable reason, Li Fan gradually felt a strange sense of familiarity welling up within him.

"The method of imagination, the art of deducing indeterminate futures, reversing the river of time, inheriting through celestial selection..."

Observing the Saints' methods, Li Fan increasingly felt a sense of uncanny familiarity.

Without needing to dwell on it, Li Fan quickly identified the source of this familiarity.

"The transformation of True and False."

"Every Saintly divine ability seemed to be related to the transformation of True and False, existing in a state of being almost, yet not quite."

"Exactly..."

Li Fan's astonishment grew.

"Could it be that the transformation of True and False is too profound, encompassing all aspects of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas? Thus, when I truly began to interact with the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas wielded by the Saints, I perceived it as if glimpsing the transformation of True and False from a specific angle?"

"Then truly..."

Li Fan's thoughts raced. He felt a sudden impulse to inquire of 'True Return' once more.

However, since arriving at the end of the Mountains and Seas, 'True Return' had fallen into a deep slumber, more profound than ever before. It seemed as if there was something in the external environment that it wished to avoid.

The only thing that brought Li Fan peace was that he could still summon the 'True Return' panel.

With a single thought, he could activate it, reversing everything and returning to a safe anchor point.

"Let's wait a while longer and listen to the Saints' research findings."

At the end of the Mountains and Seas, the white-haired scholar had temporarily halted the river of time. Time seemed to have lost all meaning. After an unknown duration, and after countless joint experiments by the Saints, they finally reached a conclusion.

A look of long-unseen excitement appeared on Qiu Xin Hui's face.

"The barrier of true spirits, though naturally formed, is not irreversible."

"Through our combined efforts, we have finally discovered its flaw. While injecting a massive amount of true spirits can be destructive like a torrent, it also brings about annihilation. Thus, it is not a viable approach."

"However, if we were to create hundreds and thousands of ourselves, all receiving the injection of true spirits simultaneously..."

As Qiu Xin Hui spoke, he pointed forward at an experimental subject.

A dreamlike golden light enveloped the seated, closed-eyed experimental subject.

Instantly, hundreds and thousands of his imaginary forms appeared, as if replicated.

"The method of transcending to become a Saint is the unification of all fragmented selves. Yet, this method of true spirit injection, conversely, makes 'infinite selves,' born from one!"

Chapter 1672: Desire to Leave But Body Remains

"Infinite selves!"

The experimental subject, using the method of imagination, replicated countless versions of himself.

Facing the cascading torrent of accumulated spiritual essence, which threatened destruction, he became a dam, momentarily withstanding its impact!

"I perceive true spirits!"

At this instant, all the experimental subjects opened their eyes.

Through the immense pressure they felt, they seemed to have truly "seen" the formless, intangible multitude of true spirits!

Though there were numerous experimental subjects present, they all originated from the same source. More importantly, they were all countless clones created by one specific entity through imagination.

Thus, they seemed to share the same barrier of true spirits.

At Qiu Xin Hui's signal, Li Fan increased the intensity of the accumulated true spirit impact.

The dam formed by thousands of experimental subjects, though strong, eventually began to falter. Under the immense pressure, a crack appeared.

The accumulated true spirits seized this opportunity, silently invading with their destructive power, like wind and thunder.

If only one experimental subject had borne this ordeal, his fate would have been to be engulfed and dissipate within the accumulated true spirits.

But at this moment…

Facing this terrifying calamity, the myriad experimental subjects remained undaunted.

With the main body as the core of defense, they collectively distributed the immense pressure from the accumulated true spirits evenly.

One person facing it would be like an ant trying to shake Mount Tai, annihilation would be instantaneous.

But what about thousands, or billions?

Moreover, from the main experimental subject, waves of golden light continuously flickered and pulsed. With the constant influx of new imaginary forces, although the accumulated true spirits surged ferociously, they could not shake the dam of the multitude for a time.

What was once a surging dragon had now transformed into countless converging streams.

The individual streams of accumulated true spirits, after the initial impact, were naturally beyond the capacity of one experimental subject to absorb. But for a fraction of a stream, absorbing it was no longer so difficult.

Although the absorption and utilization rate of the accumulated true spirits summoned by Li Fan further decreased,

The initial objective had been achieved!

The true spirits were nourished, and the previously hazy eyes of the experimental subject gradually sharpened and became intelligent.

He looked around, seemingly understanding his situation.

He did not blame the surrounding Saints who were observing him.

Seeing the countless other versions of himself beside him, he intuitively calmed his mind.

He began to recall the imaginary clones that were used to share the pressure of the accumulated true spirits.

This experimental subject had not previously studied the Dao of Imagination; these imaginary clones were all generated by Qiu Xin Hui's intervention.

Therefore, the speed of recall was not ideal at first.

The vast majority of the imaginary clones dissipated without a trace after fulfilling their purpose.

And the true spirits they carried, having lost their vessels, flowed away silently like water.

However, those chosen as experimental subjects were all extraordinary by nature.

Now, having been infused with true spirits, their spiritual essence was superior to before.

He learned quickly.

And he remained unshaken despite the constant and rapid dissipation of his surrounding imaginary clones.

He simply adapted, doing his best.

Initially, only one or two figures were drawn to return.

Later, as the experimental subject's speed of recalling imaginary clones accelerated,

Like countless stars returning to a single entity.

Brilliant light converged upon the experimental subject.

...

The white-haired scholar stroked his beard and praised: "Although the imaginary clones carrying true spirits cannot be fully absorbed instantly, they are ultimately stored within the body, becoming a source of future growth. It is akin to possessing an inexhaustible treasure mountain within, from which one can continuously mine and enhance one's potential as strength increases."

"One can benefit from this until the moment of achieving Sainthood."

The shifting figure's visions flickered, seemingly deducing the possibilities of the Mountains and Seas where the 'Infinite Selves' method of the Great Dao flourished.

The Saints' gazes once again converged on Li Fan.

"It is regrettable that while the method of imagination can be learned by anyone, the ability to summon and manipulate the accumulated true spirits from the void is unique to our Mountains and Seas."

"Since we are already at the end of the Mountains and Seas, we cannot go back."

The Saints sighed inwardly.
