"The past is past, and those who lived it will bear its consequences. We must now focus on our future," Qiu Xin Hui said with a smile, drawing the Saints' attention away from Li Fan.

"With Daoist friend Fan's assistance, all our deficiencies can be rectified. Furthermore, we can create far more helpers than anticipated??"

The shifting figure spoke at this moment: "Our chances of success have now surpassed fifty percent!"

"Fifty percent and beyond – further increases in probability are insignificant. Esteemed elders, let us each unleash our divine abilities and impart the 'Infinite Selves' method. We need not rely on Saints' help; merely a thousand or so half-Saints..."

"It is time for Scholar to break the seal of the river of time and face the end of the Mountains and Seas directly," Qiu Xin Hui said, cupping his hands towards the white-haired scholar.

The white-haired scholar nodded proudly, appearing somewhat impatient.

Among the Saints present, only Li Fan hesitated.

"Is this not perhaps... a bit too hasty?"

"Since we have a method to continuously strengthen ourselves, why not accumulate more power?" Li Fan questioned, confused.

Qiu Xin Hui merely smiled and offered no reply.

"Only through battle can victory be achieved."

"Countless strategies and meticulous calculations are ultimately no match for a direct confrontation."

Qiu Xin Hui was undoubtedly the core among the Saints. Since his mind was made up, Li Fan had no reason to object further.

Li Fan now had two choices:

Whether to immediately activate "True Return" or to wait.

To observe the outcome of the final battle between the Mountains and Seas and the desolate void, and the desperate gambit of the Saints, before departing.

Although the final decisive battle at the end of the Mountains and Seas was indeed captivating, Li Fan had not lost his reason.

At the moment of the end of the Mountains and Seas and the arrival of the final battle, the danger would be immense.

Even Saints could perish in an instant.

And Li Fan, unlike the other Saints, had not made sufficient preparations.

"Using the power of the First Profound Embryo, I successfully traversed the desolate void. I obtained the method to control the accumulated true spirits, and with the Saints' power, I deduced the method of 'Infinite Selves' for true spirit infusion."

"The gains in this life have far exceeded my expectations. It is time to return."

After all, Li Fan was not a true Saint, but merely a transcendent cultivator clad in the semblance of the Profound Embryo Great Dao.

Although the Saints' attention had been focused on the true spirit infusion technique during their long seclusion,

They had rarely turned their gaze towards Li Fan.

But now that the method was deduced, the probability of the Saints' attention falling upon Li Fan was increasing.

The longer he stayed, the greater the risk of his secrets, and the secrets of 'True Return,' being exposed.

"This place is not suitable for lingering."

Finding an opportune moment when the Saints were distracted, Li Fan silently summoned 'True Return' in his heart.

The mysterious power of "True and False Transformation" began to surge once more, intending to reverse everything as before.

But suddenly, Li Fan sensed something was amiss.

As if sensing his impending departure, currents of power inexplicably emerged from the surrounding Mountains and Seas. Like tendrils, they coiled around Li Fan's body.

Preventing his 'True Return' from leaving!

Li Fan's expression shifted slightly. He scanned his surroundings, searching for the source of this power.

However, the Saints seemed oblivious to the changes in their midst, their expressions unchanged.

It was only then that Li Fan realized that it was not external forces preventing his departure.

What bound him were the very foundations of his Sainthood – the Profound Embryo Great Dao!

"This..."

Being restrained by his own power was truly ironic.

Li Fan felt a mixture of shock and anger. He tried to break free from his shackles with all his might.

It was indeed effective.

As a Saint of the Profound Embryo, his control over the Profound Embryo Great Dao still existed.

But...

To achieve full effect required some time.

Li Fan forced himself to calm down and carefully pondered, finally understanding what had happened.

In this life, using the First Profound Embryo Great Dao, he had achieved the status of a Saint of the Mountains and Seas.

Having attained Sainthood, he had gradually become the embodiment of the Profound Embryo itself within the Mountains and Seas.

As previously stated, Li Fan's core was ultimately the "True and False Transformation," with the Profound Embryo being merely an outer garment he wore, which could be shed at any time.

But now, this thick garment had been worn for too long.

It had become somewhat adhered to his person, making it difficult to remove in a short period.

The Profound Embryo Great Dao and the current Mountains and Seas were inextricably linked.

When Li Fan wished to activate 'True Return,' these connections became obstacles.

"To actuate 'True Return,' I must first shed the outer garment of the Profound Embryo."

"This is not something that can be achieved in a day or two."

"Given the time I have existed as a Saint, how long will it take to completely detach myself? Perhaps one-tenth of that time?"

In reality, it was already quite efficient, but to Li Fan, it was unacceptable.

He truly never expected that pretending to be a Saint would have such consequences!

He had already spent a considerable amount of time at the end of the Mountains and Seas in this life, and now, the final decisive battle at the end of the Mountains and Seas was imminent.

Yet, at this critical juncture, he was unable to activate 'True Return.'

"This..."

"'True Return! True Return!'" Li Fan repeated inwardly, not to activate it, but to awaken the slumbering 'True Return.'

But in this current situation, it was precisely as he had experienced in his simulations. 'True Return' remained silent.

"Without the severe injuries from the Three Dao Mergers, it's simply feigning ignorance."

Having understood this, Li Fan's shock and anger quickly subsided.

"If there were true danger, 'True Return' would not remain so indifferent."

"Furthermore, my spiritual intuition has not issued any warnings."

"What exactly..."

Li Fan's unease eventually caught the attention of the Saints.

"Daoist friend, do not worry. Simply proceed with your tasks,"

To divert the Saints' attention from himself, Li Fan could only nod silently.

Compared to the long years of research preceding this, the preparations for the final decisive battle appeared remarkably hasty.

The method of true spirit infusion had produced over a thousand cultivators on the verge of Sainthood.

The shifting figure performed some calculations and nodded his head.

The white-haired scholar then pointed a finger, severing the frozen river of time.

As if ice shattering, the stagnant currents roared like thunder.

Li Fan felt a momentary dizziness.

As the river of time resumed its flow, the years he had experienced in isolation suddenly erupted.

Countless scenes flashed before his eyes, and millennia passed in an instant.

Without any time for preparation, the end of the Mountains and Seas had arrived!

The last rays of the sun were about to dip below the horizon.

The final fragment of the iceberg was about to be swallowed by the ocean's surface.

The final possibility where they could take refuge was about to sink into endless Dao Annihilation.

As if to celebrate the ultimate victory of this prolonged battle, strange, echoing fluctuations emanated from the cold, silent desolate void.

Li Fan could clearly feel something lurking beneath the accumulated true spirits, moving slowly at times, and rapidly at others.

It watched like a predator, fixed on the perishing Mountains and Seas.

Darkness pressed in, drawing ever closer.

And the doomed Mountains and Seas uttered their final lament!

Li Fan had heard the voice of the Mountains and Seas before.

But never had he felt such profound sorrow and unwillingness as he did now!

Images of the Mountains and Seas in their nascent glory flashed before Li Fan's eyes.

The Mountains and Seas resonated in unison, celebrating their theft from the Gods, their rebirth.

But their rise was as swift as their fall.

The Mountains and Seas, having endured countless ages, seemed but a fleeting moment in Li Fan's eyes.

Images flickered by at an indiscernible speed.

By the time Li Fan regained his senses, they had already merged with the current reality of the Mountains and Seas' demise.

In their twilight years, their destruction was inevitable.

The great lament was the last sound the Mountains and Seas could emit.

And it did not last long.

As darkness completely engulfed them, the echoes of the Mountains and Seas also vanished.

The Mountains and Seas perished at this moment!

Their bodies, after all, originated from the Mountains and Seas.

Now that the Mountains and Seas were destroyed, Li Fan's emotions were affected, and his own existence began to dissipate as well.

As if empowered by the final victory, the corrosive force of the desolate void intensified a hundredfold compared to his previous traversal.

From all perceivable dimensions, it surged inward.

Li Fan's disintegration progressed at an unimaginable speed.

"Why haven't they acted yet?"

Li Fan tried to locate Qiu Xin Hui and the others within the darkness.

But they seemed to have been affected by the demise of the Mountains and Seas, showing no signs of activity.

"Has their struggle failed?"

Just as this thought crossed Li Fan's mind.

A beam of light illuminated the desolate void once more.

The Mountains and Seas, which had been completely swallowed, inexplicably returned, reappearing in the desolate void!

However, this brief resurgence lasted only for a fleeting moment.

The landscape of the Mountains and Seas had already become distorted.

Soon, it was compressed by the desolate void into two white dots.

Yet, the tenacity of these two white dots seemed to surpass that of the entire Mountains and Seas.

Despite the surging black tides, their faint light could not be entirely extinguished for a time.

As they remained in a stalemate, another anomaly occurred.

Two thin lines emerged from the white dots of the Mountains and Seas.

They delved into the void.

Instantly, the darkness churned.

The pressure exerted upon the white dots lessened slightly.

The white dots shone brightly, seemingly regenerating the phenomena of the Mountains and Seas.

"This is..."

Li Fan, struggling to maintain his existence, felt a familiar aura from one of the white lines.

It was the terrifying aura he had sensed upon first entering the Infinite Sea.

At this moment, even though 'True Return' was by his side, it was too occupied to intervene.

It was engaged in a life-or-death struggle with the desolate void.

Waves of intense fluctuations swept over him, further disintegrating Li Fan's existential foundation.

"True Return!" Li Fan called out again, unable to protect himself.

But the result was the same.

Just as the Mountains and Seas and the desolate void were locked in their most critical struggle, and Li Fan was reduced to mere remnants of his being.

The final Saints of the Mountains and Seas, who had been waiting for this moment, finally acted.

They had not been consumed by the desolate void.

In fact, as if they had known what would transpire at the end of the Mountains and Seas, they had been awaiting this opportune moment.

Chapter 1673: The True Form Finally Appears

Myriad imaginary currents surged forth like a cascade of stars, illuminating the cold, dark desolate void.

Like threads, they instantly wove a phantom image of the Mountains and Seas.

However, this scene did not last long.

The true Mountains and Seas had already been annihilated within the desolate void; how much less could this imaginary Mountains and Seas endure?

The surrounding darkness seemed to press down heavily, suppressing the light emitted by the phantom image.

Turbulent waves surged, attempting to drag it into eternal darkness.

"All Saints are present!"

The voice of Qiu Xin Hui, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, suddenly echoed through the void.

He repelled a wave of energy.

The phantom image of the Mountains and Seas momentarily beamed with light, and simultaneously, from the myriad flowing rivers within the Mountains and Seas, a single thread of possibility emerged, and several figures flew out, standing proudly.

These were the transcendent cultivators born from the "Infinite Selves" true spirit infusion plan.

"Infinite Selves" had created over a thousand half-Saints.

And ordinary transcendents were countless.

All transcendents could traverse the Dao Annihilation.

They possessed a certain degree of resistance against the encroachment of Dao Annihilation.

At this moment, countless transcendents joined forces, each contributing their meager strength, collectively supporting the imaginary Mountains and Seas on the verge of sinking into the desolate void.

In every passing moment, numerous lights representing cultivators dissipated.

Though it was destined to be unable to alter the ultimate fate of the imaginary Mountains and Seas, it bought invaluable time for the subsequent actions of the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas!

A phantom long river suddenly drifted out, spanning the imaginary Mountains and Seas.

Within the Mountains and Seas, time began to flow.

"Old man, farewell!"

The shifting figure's voice echoed, and within the imaginary Mountains and Seas, ripples seemed to spread with the sound.

Li Fan observed clearly that countless possibilities within the imaginary Mountains and Seas began to manifest.

If the initial imaginary Mountains and Seas were merely a blank canvas drawn from collective memory,

Then, with the addition of the power of the river of time and the ability to infinitely deduce possibilities, the imaginary Mountains and Seas began to grow on two different dimensions. Taking on characteristics of what once was a real Mountains and Seas.

The aura of "imagination" slowly faded.

It began to resemble the Mountains and Seas that had truly existed in reality.

The newly born Mountains and Seas, though weak, pulsed with vitality.

The sacrifice of the two Saints was like a wildfire, igniting an unstoppable blaze.

Increasingly, endless possibilities began to grow wildly.

The river of time, from ancient to present, extended infinitely.

The aura of the newborn Mountains and Seas expanded exponentially with each passing moment, growing millions of times faster than before, in the darkness.

Though still minuscule compared to the desolate void,

It was sufficient to capture its attention.

Even a small portion of the desolate void's power, diverted from surrounding the residual Mountains and Seas, was still too much for the newborn Mountains and Seas to bear.

In an instant, it fell into a precarious state, its light dimming. It seemed on the verge of complete submersion into darkness.

At this critical juncture, over a thousand half-Saints appeared within the Mountains and Seas.

Their expressions were fearless, unwavering.

Their bodies dissolved as if consumed by fire, streams of light, carrying the true spirits they had absorbed, pouring into the newborn Mountains and Seas.

Like a powerful stimulant, the precarious Mountains and Seas temporarily withstood the tide of darkness.

Though the newborn Mountains and Seas had grown manifold,

It was still incomparable to the desolate void.

Once the desolate void finished dealing with the two residual light dots in the darkness, the newborn Mountains and Seas would ultimately face annihilation.

"I have seen fragments of the Mountains and Seas' flowing years, and I know what the Mountains and Seas once looked like."

The voice of Qiu Xin Hui, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, resonated.

With a gentle wave of his sleeve, he scattered countless light orbs.

As if guided by an unseen hand, these fragments were placed in their rightful positions.

As if awakening ancient memories and obtaining the main framework, the newborn Mountains and Seas began to grow in a structured manner.

They could now occasionally suppress the encroaching waves from the void.

This action seemed to have thoroughly angered the surrounding darkness.

Determined to give the newborn Mountains and Seas no chance to grow, the desolate void's corrosive pressure suddenly increased a thousandfold!

Almost instantly, the brilliance of the newborn Mountains and Seas became almost imperceptible.

It faced the same fate as the residual Mountains and Seas.

Though several streams of light circulated, protecting it,

Under the pressure of the desolate void, they gradually faded into nothingness.

"Facing the desolate void in its full power, even Saints can only endure for such a short time!" Li Fan saw the figures of the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas within the dissipating streams of light. His condition worsened, and he couldn't help but feel a hint of fear.

Fortunately, with the presence of the new and old Mountains and Seas attracting the enemy's attention, the pressure on Li Fan was slightly reduced compared to when he first fell into the void.

Therefore, he could still hold on.

"Haven't I watched enough of this show? Why can't I still activate 'True Return'!" Li Fan felt extremely exasperated.

He could sense that while the desolate void was destroying the foundation of his existence, it was also dissolving the Profound Embryo Great Dao itself.

Therefore, the force binding him was gradually weakening.

Theoretically, he should now be able to activate 'True Return.'

But for some reason, 'True Return' remained stubbornly inactive.

Li Fan was powerless and could only do his best to maintain his existence, quietly observing the unfolding events.

Even after the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas perished, Qiu Xin Hui had not given up.

"All Saints are present!"

Endless golden light erupted from the newborn Mountains and Seas.

As guardians, they reduced the desolate void's corrosive force.

Simultaneously, Saintly figures emerged one after another from the void.

These were precisely the Saints who had perished earlier!

However, they were not their true forms, but imaginary bodies.

But their existence was distinctly different from ordinary imaginary bodies; they surprisingly possessed the ability to manipulate their respective Mountains and Seas Great Daos!

The river of time reappeared, with countless shifting figures.

The newborn Mountains and Seas received another wave of nourishment and expansion!

"How is this possible?"

Li Fan was utterly shocked by this scene.

These imaginary Saints were clearly Qiu Xin Hui's creation.

Although they were not true bodies, merely imaginary forms, they could still wield Saintly authority.

This indicated…

"Qiu Xin Hui, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, is intimately familiar with the Great Daos of other Saints!"

"Just as I know of the Profound Embryo, although I am not a Profound Embryo Saint, I can wear its guise and wield its authority as a Saint."

"He possesses the art of 'Imaginary Reconstruction of Saints,' capable of acting as a Saint!"

Li Fan's mind trembled as he watched Qiu Xin Hui single-handedly turn the tide.

Each time the protective streams of light from the imaginary Saints were erased by the desolate void,

With Qiu Xin Hui's declaration of "All Saints are present," new imaginary Saints would appear out of thin air,

Nourishing the Mountains and Seas anew.

In this manner, cyclically repeating,

The power of this final Saint of the Mountains and Seas seemed inexhaustible,

As if there was no limit to his strength!

"This..." Li Fan was awestruck into speechlessness.

During the end of time, they had coexisted for a long period, yet he had never realized that this person's strength was so terrifying and unfathomable!

"Furthermore, I recall that the Dao of Imagination is not his own path."

"What is his path to Sainthood?"

Li Fan silently watched as the newborn Mountains and Seas, nurtured by the Saints, flourished within the desolate void, his mind filled with even greater questions.

"I truly underestimated this final Saint of the Mountains and Seas."

"With the strength he has displayed... could the newborn Mountains and Seas actually have a chance?"

The desolate void churned with waves.

Although every instant of impact could destroy the newborn Mountains and Seas to the point of annihilation,

As long as even a sliver of light remained, Qiu Xin Hui could restore it.

Thus, under the continuous erosion of the desolate void, the newborn Mountains and Seas managed to grow amidst constant destruction!

If this were to continue indefinitely, it seemed even the desolate void would be powerless against it!

As if sensing this, the cold darkness fell into a moment of silence.

Then...

The boundless void was torn asunder.

As if a solitary star hung high, or a divine eye opened.

An unknown entity within the desolate void descended.

The newborn Mountains and Seas froze.

Then shattered layer by layer.

Even with countless imaginary Saints appearing repeatedly, desperately trying to intervene,

Its destructive speed was too great.

No matter how they repaired it, it was all in vain.

"Finally, the face of the [Star]..."

"Heh heh. Daoist Fan, why have you not acted yet?"

Qiu Xin Hui's voice suddenly echoed.

Li Fan, still in shock at the emergence of the [Star], was startled by Qiu Xin Hui's words.

"Act?"

"Me?"

The mere Profound Embryo Great Dao could barely withstand the dark tides stirred by the desolate void. How could it possibly contend with the [Star]?

Li Fan found the situation absurd.

At the same time, a sense of panic arose within him.

Given Qiu Xin Hui's displayed strength, he would not utter such baseless words.

"Unless..."

Realizing this, Li Fan's body moved involuntarily.

Not by his own will, but out of necessity.

Emerging from the darkness, he floated out.

Towards the invisible rift torn in the desolate void, he gently pointed at the [Star] that appeared within.

"When true becomes false..."

"False also becomes true."

A Cànyu sound, both ancient yet youthful, echoed.

The solitary star seemed to vanish.

And the imaginary Mountains and Seas, in an instant, spawned infinite phantoms. Moments later, these phantoms solidified from illusion to reality, boundless and filling the field of vision.

As if the Mountains and Seas were reborn!

"True becomes false" naturally referred to the obscured Star.

And "false becomes true" referred to the newborn imaginary Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan, with his own power, had completely reversed the situation.

Or rather, it was not Li Fan.

It was 'True Return'!

"When true becomes false, false also becomes true. What a brilliant description!"

Qiu Xin Hui, appearing amidst the resurrected infinite Mountains and Seas, approached Li Fan.

"The transformation of True and False is indeed infinitely profound."

However, Li Fan smiled wryly and remarked: "True cannot become true, and false cannot become false."

He pointed in the direction where the Star had disappeared, his expression unreadable. "One can block the Star for a moment, but not for a lifetime."

This answer was beyond Qiu Xin Hui's expectations.

He looked at the boundless, seemingly resurrected Mountains and Seas and asked: "How long can this last?"

"Unknown," Li Fan replied with only four words.

Qiu Xin Hui finally fell into complete silence.

He sincerely asked: "Daoist Friend Fan, what do you think of our plan?"

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then slowly evaluated: "If the Star were not the Star, the plan could succeed. Unfortunately..."

Upon hearing this, Qiu Xin Hui's expression grew solemn, and he cupped his hands in salutation, seeking guidance: "Dare I ask Daoist Friend, what is the Star?"

"I am also in pursuit of that answer,"

Li Fan's response left Qiu Xin Hui speechless.

The two stood within the desolate void, quietly observing the momentarily resurrected Mountains and Seas.

With the newborn Mountains and Seas as their foundation, the surging dark tides of the desolate void seemed unable to harm them.

After an unknown period, the Mountains and Seas seemed to have returned to their former peak state.

The destruction of the Mountains and Seas appeared to have been a mere illusion.

Qiu Xin Hui finally spoke again: "Daoist Friend Fan, regarding our previous...

"Have we met before?"

Li Fan finally managed a smile.

"If we had never met, where would my 'True Return' have come from?"

Qiu Xin Hui looked puzzled.

Li Fan smiled again, offering no further explanation.

Instead, he said: "Let us return. There is no point in lingering here any longer."

Qiu Xin Hui sighed, but ultimately did not refuse.

*Thump thump thump...*

The clear sound of a heartbeat inexplicably arose.

It grew heavier, resounding throughout the area.

Outside the desolate void, the Star seemed to be reappearing.

But a mysterious and powerful force was slowly permeating,

Reversing everything.

The heartbeat grew faster and faster.

As if a rewind button had been pressed, the scenes that had transpired here replayed themselves,

But in reverse.

The flow of light and shadow accelerated, while the heartbeat grew fainter and fainter.

When the sound completely faded...

At the end of the Mountains and Seas.

Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes, scanning his surroundings.

"What is this?"

He looked at Qiu Xin Hui, who was smiling and observing him, as if he had just arrived at the end of the Mountains and Seas after traversing it, just like before.

"I succeeded in activating 'True Return'?"

"No. This is??"

Faint images flickered in his mind. Just as Li Fan was about to investigate further, an intense pain struck him,

Rendering him unable to concentrate and think.

His entire body ached as if after a great battle, utterly exhausted.

"What exactly happened? I remember it was supposed to be the final battle between the Mountains and Seas and the desolate void."

Li Fan pressed his temples, trying to clear his muddled mind.

"'True Return', right, 'True Return'!"

Li Fan seemed to recall something, realizing with a jolt that 'True Return' might have been exposed and looked up sharply at Qiu Xin Hui.

However, Qiu Xin Hui was still attending to the people of the Realm of Birth and Death, stabilizing their injuries, just as he had in his memory.

"I know Daoist Friend Fan may have many questions."

"Please be patient for a moment longer, and I will provide a full explanation."

Following his inner call, Li Fan's 'True Return' panel reappeared before his eyes.

And at this point in time, shortly after he had donned the guise of the Profound Embryo, the binding force had not yet solidified.

He could activate 'True Return' at any time.

With newfound confidence, Li Fan nodded silently, waiting patiently for Qiu Xin Hui to finish resolving matters.

During this period, Li Fan finally saw the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas again.

However, apart from Qiu Xin Hui, they seemed completely unaware of what had transpired.

"This scene... could it be?"

Recalling the similarities he had sensed between the Saints and 'True Return,'

Li Fan began to form a conjecture about Qiu Xin Hui's true Dao.

Chapter 1674: Lone Star Suddenly Hangs High

"The annihilation of the Mountains and Seas, the descent of the Star. What I witnessed just now was not a mere illusion, but a true event."

The solitary star hung high, tearing through the desolate void like a divine gaze.

Whenever Li Fan recalled this scene, a chill ran down his spine, as if an unknown entity within the desolate void was staring at him.

But now, the Star was nowhere to be seen, and the Mountains and Seas had returned to their final, dilapidated state.

"The river of time exists only in reliance on the Mountains and Seas. After the destruction of the Mountains and Seas, it can return to its origin. This is not simply a matter of time reversal."

"It is the reversal of everything that has already occurred."

"The transformation of True and False?"

Though filled with disbelief, everything Li Fan had experienced at the end of the Mountains and Seas seemed to unequivocally point to this conclusion.

A fire seemed to burn in Li Fan's throat.

If Qiu Xin Hui's path to Sainthood was the transformation of True and False,

Then what exactly was 'True Return'?

Li Fan stared intently at the phrase "True becomes false, false also becomes true" on the 'True Return' panel, countless questions swirling in his mind.

Until Qiu Xin Hui, who had just healed the people of the Realm of Birth and Death, stood before him once more.

Since the existence of 'True Return' had already been exposed, Li Fan had nothing left to hide. He directly voiced his doubts.

"The Great Dao of True and False..."

The white-haired Qiu Xin Hui's eyes shimmered with longing, momentarily lost in thought.

Then, with a sigh, he shook his head. "Only possesses [False becomes True], but not [True becomes False]."

This answer was both unexpected and reasonable.

"False becomes True" was a further manifestation of the imaginary Dao.

Recalling carefully, after the annihilation of the Mountains and Seas and the demise of the Saints, Qiu Xin Hui had single-handedly reversed the tide by continuously summoning Saints from nothingness to uphold the imaginary Mountains and Seas against the desolate void. This did indeed exhibit the essence of "[False becomes True]."

Li Fan let out a long sigh of relief.

At the same time, his doubts only grew.

He had not expected that the "True and False Transformation" of 'True Return' would have a counterpart in this world.

"A long time ago, before I achieved Sainthood, I witnessed the scene of the Mountains and Seas' annihilation."

"All the past events were vivid in my mind. Despair and regret filled my chest."

"As my own existence was about to vanish, guided by an unseen force, I comprehended the Dao of [False becomes True] amidst the final light of the Mountains and Seas."

"In the midst of annihilation and nothingness, I recreated the [End of the Mountains and Seas]..."

Qiu Xin Hui spoke slowly, filled with emotion.

As if sensing Li Fan's doubts, he continued without waiting for a question: "I was born at the end of the Mountains and Seas, and I grew up at the end of the Mountains and Seas."

"Furthermore, I achieved my Dao at the end of the Mountains and Seas. My entire life has been confined to this place. Although I can glimpse the past of the Mountains and Seas through mere fragments of light and shadow, it is only a limited perspective. To recreate the imaginary Mountains and Seas, I still have enough power."

"To truly recreate the full glory of the Mountains and Seas..."

Qiu Xin Hui sighed, "My strength is insufficient."

"If you were to traverse {backwards in time} to the more ancient Mountains and Seas, to witness their complete form, would you not be able to achieve it?" Li Fan asked thoughtfully.

"With your strength, surely you could do it?"

Li Fan was naturally referring to Qiu Xin Hui's ability to continuously summon Saints to resist the desolate void's encroachment.

To his surprise, Qiu Xin Hui gently shook his head, negating it.

"Traversing downstream is already arduous."

"To travel upstream is even more difficult. Daoist Friend Fan, you underestimate the dangers involved."

"Furthermore, if the Saints are still present, how can I recreate them?" Qiu Xin Hui pointed out the most critical factor.

Li Fan suddenly understood.

The Qiu Xin Hui he witnessed previously displaying his divine abilities was after the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas had sacrificed themselves. The Great Daos wielded by the Saints were now vacant, left unclaimed.

Therefore, Qiu Xin Hui could summon phantom bodies and re-appropriate the Great Daos, wielding Saintly power.

But in the current timeline, with the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas still alive…

Imagination could only conjure the form, but not the power.

Though the reasoning was sound, Li Fan felt a sense of skepticism.

"How does it matter? Telling the Saints the specific situation and reasons, I believe they would be willing to sacrifice themselves for the salvation of the Mountains and Seas. If that doesn't work, then find an opportunity..." Li Fan narrowed his eyes,

His gaze carrying a hidden glint of ruthlessness.

Qiu Xin Hui immediately saw through Li Fan's thoughts and could only offer a wry smile.

"All the Saints came here at my summons, so how could I betray their trust?"

"We are united in our efforts to save the world. Their sacrifice represents one matter."

"Harm them while they are alive, even plotting against them, is another matter entirely."

"I will not do that," the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, Qiu Xin Hui, stated with utmost seriousness.

"Pedantic," Li Fan muttered inwardly, shaking his head.

However, he did not argue with Qiu Xin Hui.

Instead, he suddenly recalled something else.

If, according to this final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, the Great Daos wielded by the Saints were inaccessible to others while they were alive,

Then...

"What is the relationship between 'True Return's' transformation of True and False and Qiu Xin Hui's control?"

Qiu Xin Hui continued, "In the beginning of the Mountains and Seas, other Saints went there. My plan is indeed as I stated earlier: to use the imaginary Mountains and Seas, at the juncture of old and new, to seek a sliver of hope for survival."

"Through our repeated attempts, we seem to have finally glimpsed a glimmer of hope."

"Until... today, when we finally witnessed the face of the [Star]."

The terrifying image of the solitary Star hanging high flashed before Li Fan's eyes.

Faint, forgotten memories resurfaced.

"After you called me to act... what exactly happened?" Li Fan's heart skipped a beat, and he hastily asked.

Qiu Xin Hui looked at him carefully and shook his head slightly. "Daoist Friend Fan has his own destiny. If I were to easily reveal it, it would be detrimental to you."

"What happened is ultimately irrelevant. You only need to know that our struggle was futile the moment the [Star] appeared."

"Fortunately, there was still a turning point..." Qiu Xin Hui looked directly at Li Fan.

Even though the enigmatic Qiu Xin Hui spoke ambiguously, Li Fan could broadly guess what had happened to him.

It was also what he had always feared.

'True Return' had lost control and acted on its own, seemingly possessing his body.

A shadow flickered in his eyes, and Li Fan felt a fire ignite within him.

Though extremely angry, Li Fan pondered and realized he had no effective countermeasures.

After all, he couldn't truly break his own barrier of true spirits and bring about mutual destruction.

The situation had not yet reached that point.

Without Qiu Xin Hui needing to persuade him, Li Fan quickly convinced himself, forcibly suppressing the anger in his eyes.

Witnessing the change in Li Fan's expression, Qiu Xin Hui nodded inwardly.

"For this operation, Daoist friend need not act. Simply observe silently."

"When everything settles down, you can then..."

"'Return to True.'"

When Qiu Xin Hui uttered the words "[True Return]," Li Fan's heart couldn't help but skip a beat.

This was the first time since his reincarnation that Li Fan had heard his 'True Return' mentioned by another person.

Even though he had anticipated the exposure of 'True Return's' existence,

The confirmation of his suspicions filled him with extreme unease.

"What about the true spirit infusion?" He chose to change the subject.

"It was merely futile; Daoist Friend Fan need not trouble himself," Qiu Xin Hui said with a smile, cupping his hands and departing.

Thus, in this cycle of reincarnation at the end of the Mountains and Seas, Li Fan was like an invisible bystander.

Although the other Saints knew of his existence, they only recognized him by his [Profound Embryo] identity.

He did not participate in the Saints' plan to save the world.

In the frozen end of the Mountains and Seas, time held no true significance.

After an unknown period, not by the white-haired scholar's own will, but due to his exhaustion and demise.

The river of time surged forth, carrying everyone towards their final destination.

Without Li Fan's true spirit infusion, the imaginary Mountains and Seas performed even worse.

They could barely withstand the full power of the desolate void's encroachment,

Let alone face the solitary Star.

Before even glimpsing the Star's face, the imaginary Mountains and Seas, along with the Saints, perished.

"All Saints are present!"

Qiu Xin Hui's solemn declaration echoed alone in the darkness.

Even though he knew his fate and the predetermined end, he did not abandon his struggle.

Until, the desolate void's surging tides attacked, completely engulfing the imaginary light.

"Daoist Friend Fan..."

"It is time."

"This time, the experience may be different from before."

Qiu Xin Hui's final words drifted through the air.

And within the dark tide, Li Fan, having finally broken free from the confines of the Profound Embryo Great Dao, softly called out to 'True Return' once more.

His heart leaped, his expression tense.

Fortunately, there were no surprises.

That familiar sensation finally returned.

And as Qiu Xin Hui had said, this time the experience was indeed different.

The characteristic billowing white mist of 'True Return' did not appear.

Instead, Li Fan felt a peculiar and immense power isolating him from the surrounding desolate void, protecting his safety.

It was as if he had returned to the womb; all restlessness and anxiety vanished, replaced by complete tranquility.

Even though 'True Return' had not yet activated, seemingly waiting for some change to occur,

Li Fan felt no tension whatsoever.

He waited quietly alongside it.

When the last spark of light from the imaginary Mountains and Seas was swallowed by darkness.

When the two residual light dots of the original Mountains and Seas finally vanished.

The turbulent desolate void fell into a brief silence.

Then, the void unleashed unprecedented, rampaging waves, as if celebrating in wild revelry, heralding the arrival of an Emperor.

Though unable to perceive these turbulent waves, Li Fan could sense their presence through the increasingly vibrating tremors within himself.

Their power was several times greater than when they had engulfed the Mountains and Seas, and even 'True Return's' protection was severely impacted.

"This is the true full power of the desolate void."

At the same time, Li Fan understood what 'True Return' had been waiting for.

It was waiting for the descent of the [Star].

Compared to before, when it directly tore through the desolate void and appeared in view.

This time, the [Star] rose like the morning sun above the horizon.

Initially, the Star's radiance was not very dazzling.

But with each passing moment of its existence, the pressure it exerted on the outside world increased exponentially.

'True Return's' protection, like being caught in a hurricane, creaked and groaned.

The desolate void also churned as if boiling.

Bathed in the Star's unique radiance, the darkness evaporated completely.

Where darkness had been, there was now only the peculiar brilliance of the Star.

The Star's power was simply too overbearing.

Except for itself, it tolerated no other existence.

Not even the desolate void.

Under the Star's illumination, the darkness evaporated.

All that could be seen was the solitary Star, beginning to expand endlessly.

Before the Star.

Li Fan, protected by the power of 'True Return,' felt an uncontrollable urge to flee.

At the same time, he understood the futility of Qiu Xin Hui's plan.

Schemes of leaping out, of merging with the [Star].

All were pure nonsense.

After the Star's descent, all would cease to exist.

Except for the Star itself.

What a terrifying power!

Li Fan trembled uncontrollably.

Even though he closed his eyes and severed his spiritual senses,

Coupled with 'True Return's' protection.

He could not stop the Star from slowly ascending within his mind.

Its image grew larger and larger, as if poised to consume him entirely.

The Star's divine pressure, the unfathomable disparity in strength, left Li Fan's mind blank. He could not even muster the thought of escape.

His mind went blank, and he could only face his impending doom, silently awaiting death.

Just then.

A stream of seven-colored light drifted from nowhere.

It was the familiar phrase Li Fan knew so well: "When true becomes false, false also becomes true!"

The stream of light seemed to be cleaved in two, scattering with a resounding boom.

The portion "When true becomes false" transformed into a sky full of light and shadows, confronting the solitary Star.

The Star's endless expansion abruptly halted.

As if a hand emerged from beneath the horizon,

Forcibly dragging back the [Star] that had already leaped above the sea!

This power was slow but firm.

Irresistible and immutable, even for the Star!

The solitary star trembled, filled with extreme rage.

The Star's radiance seemed to erupt, blindingly intense a thousandfold.

Judging from its previous display, perhaps the entire desolate void would have evaporated under this sudden burst of starlight.

But at this moment, all that radiance was blocked by the four words of brilliance, "When true becomes false."

The Star's fury, compared to before, seemed to have no effect.

The two lights competed fiercely.

Li Fan, who had witnessed the entire scene, was utterly stunned.

Even though he was like an ant compared to the Star and 'True Return,'

He was not completely incapable of understanding.

His reincarnations through countless lifetimes, and his comprehension of the "True and False Transformation," were not in vain!

At this moment, Li Fan's fear of the Star had completely vanished, replaced by an overwhelming excitement. He muttered to himself,

"When true becomes false, when true becomes false..."

"So that's how it is."

"It's actually like this!"

Li Fan had always believed that "true becomes false" referred to all Great Dao entities within the Mountains and Seas.

Only now, after personally witnessing the brilliance of 'True Return' contending with the Star, did Li Fan finally comprehend.

"[True becomes False] does not refer to the myriad things within the Mountains and Seas."

"Or rather, it's not just the Mountains and Seas."

"Most importantly..."

"To erase the light of the Star's descent!"

"To eliminate the Star's influence!"

Li Fan's mind roared.

"Only possesses [False becomes True], but not [True becomes False]," Qiu Xin Hui's complex expression recurred.

Only now did Li Fan understand the meaning of those words.

"Could the power of 'True Return' be limited to this?" Li Fan exclaimed in disbelief.

Li Fan's internal emotions did not affect the external world in the slightest.

In the direct confrontation, 'True Return' ultimately prevailed.

The Star's radiance slowly dissipated.

The darkness of the desolate void reappeared.

When all returned to calm, the remaining three characters of "False becomes True" from the seven-colored stream of light...

Exploded silently.

Transforming into boundless Mountains and Seas, pushing back the desolate void.

Li Fan, without time to fully process his emotions, was enveloped and drawn into it.

Chapter 1675: Starlight Lingering Fragment

Although it felt like an instant.

This time, the process of 'True Return' seemed less prolonged.

When Li Fan's consciousness reawakened, the first thing that surfaced in his mind was this peculiar and contradictory sensation.

He stared blankly at the characters that appeared before him.

【Simulation Complete】

【You may choose one of the following options to retain:

1. One item held by yourself during this simulation.

2. Your cultivation realm during this simulation.

3. The simulated memories of a close associate during this simulation. These memories can be passed on to that individual.

4. Forgo the above choices and accelerate the recharge progress.】

...

Compared to the stable state of the text previously, the few lines of characters now before him flickered with a strange black-red glow.

This ominous luminescence reminded Li Fan of the scene at the very end of his previous life, where 'True Return' and the Star confronted each other.

Furthermore, these instructional texts appeared as if they could collapse at any moment.

It was not Li Fan's illusion.

As Li Fan focused his intent further upon them.

The inheritance instructions disintegrated like crumbling ashes, collapsing in an instant.

However, Li Fan felt no sense of panic.

He had already understood that the changes in 'True Return' this time were a good thing.

After the text shattered, Li Fan's vision plunged into brief darkness.

But soon, new flashes of light were born in the darkness.

New lines of text began to reassemble, leaping into Li Fan's view.

【Simulation Complete】

【You may choose one of the following options to retain:

1. Your cultivation realm, possessions, or the Dao you wield during this simulation.

2. The simulated outcome of any close companion during this simulation. This outcome can overwrite the current Mountains and Seas.

3. The outline of the changes in the Mountains and Seas during this simulation.

4. The Star's radiant movement principles during this simulation.

5. Forgo the above choices and accelerate the recharge progress.】

...

The four options had become five,

And the specific content of the options had undergone a radical transformation compared to before. With each line he read, it felt as if an invisible hand was fiercely gripping Li Fan's heart.

"This is the consequence of finally achieving Sainthood, witnessing the end of the Mountains and Seas, and the appearance of the solitary Star."

"Or perhaps, I have finally witnessed the true power of 'True Return,' and the truth behind each activation of 'True Return.' Thus, it has become more open to me?"

Li Fan was unsure of the exact reason, or perhaps it was a combination of both.

But in any case, the change in 'True Return's' inheritance content this time was likely extraordinary.

Taking a deep breath, Li Fan closed his eyes, ignoring the content of the inheritance options.

Only after completely calming himself did he re-examine them carefully.

The original first and second inheritance options had now been merged into one. Moreover, this new option encompassed even more.

It was not limited to his own cultivation, but also included his possessions and the Dao he wielded.

He could understand retaining his own cultivation and possessions.

But what did "the Dao he wielded" refer to?

"Ordinary Daos are no longer noteworthy to me. This Dao must refer to the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas. However, 'True Return' possesses the divine ability of [Great Dao Returns to Truth], so once captured, it is forever captured. For example, even if I don't choose to inherit the Dao option now, [The First Profound Embryo] is still under 'True Return's' control. What significance would inheriting it again have?"

Li Fan frowned, contemplating.

He did not believe 'True Return' would offer pointless options.

Especially after truly witnessing 'True Return's' divine might,

He deeply understood how laughable his previous speculations about 'True Return' had been. Li Fan needed to approach 'True Return' with a new perspective.

"Inheriting existing assets... there seems to be a precedent."

After a long time, Li Fan's eyes flickered, recalling his experience of inheriting the Worldly Curiosities of the Xuanhuang Realm.

"The Worldly Curiosities of Xuanhuang should have been unique in the world. But after 'True Return' used its power to create a new one, two instances existed concurrently."

"However... the unique nature was not altered. Therefore..."

Li Fan's heart skipped a beat as he reached a conclusion.

"The fusion of the two, leading to further advancement!"

If it were merely a matter of a realm's curiosity, it would be insignificant.

But now, the object to be enhanced was a Great Dao equivalent to the Mountains and Seas, capable of achieving Sainthood!

What would be its manifestation after being further enhanced by 'True Return'?

Recalling his past life, where he wielded and cultivated the Profound Embryo Great Dao, and looking at the shimmering characters "[The First Profound Embryo]" on the 'True Return' panel, Li Fan felt an impulse surge within him. He was about to choose this option immediately to observe the specific changes.

"If it is as I imagine, then it will be of great significance, directly paving a path for me."

"As long as I continue to strengthen it, even if I only wear its guise, perhaps I could rival the Saints of the Shore."

Having almost made up his mind.

But Li Fan suppressed his impulse and did not immediately choose to inherit.

Instead, he carefully read through the remaining options.

If the first inheritance option was for his own benefit, then the second option was for dealing with others.

Compared to before, the effect was transformative.

Previously, he could only inherit memories along with his own spiritual essence.

Like Bai Shuyue, even if she cultivated diligently to the Transcendent realm in her past life, she would have to start anew from the mortal realm in her next life.

But now…

"Directly inherit the simulation outcome, and overwrite the current Mountains and Seas."

The seven characters "overwrite the current Mountains and Seas" appeared in Li Fan's mind. He had seen these words in 'True Return's' 'simulation' and deduction of the entire Mountains and Seas.

There was nothing difficult to understand.

It was akin to Li Fan, inheriting the entirety of his past life's simulated gains!

As the greatest beneficiary of this inheritance feature of 'True Return,' Li Fan naturally knew its terrifying power.

It could even be used to guide others to Sainthood.

"However, there are also drawbacks."

"The simulation outcome naturally includes complete memories of the past life. The power of a Saint is comparable to my own. If I were to truly guide someone to Sainthood, even if I concealed myself perfectly, it would be difficult to avoid revealing flaws."

"This is a great weapon, and a double-edged sword, not to be used lightly. Even for my aunt, this applies."

Given Li Fan's temperament, there was no one in the entire Mountains and Seas who could make him use this second inheritance option without reservations.

"Perhaps in the future, when I am once again in dire straits, I will utilize it," Li Fan thought to himself.

Li Fan harbored many concerns.

Fortunately, a faint fluctuation transmitted, and 'True Return' promptly provided a prompt: the option to simply inherit memories, as in the past, was still available.

However, it was a significant waste and not highly recommended.

But ultimately, the decision rested with Li Fan.

"Wasting it?"

Li Fan gave a soft snort and skipped it, looking towards the third and fourth inheritance options.

These were possibilities that arose after experiencing the cataclysm of his previous life.

And...

Judging by the wording, they were extraordinary.

Li Fan's expression grew solemn as he slowly read.

"Outline of the Mountains and Seas' changes, Star's radiant movement principles."

One pertained to the Mountains and Seas, the other to the solitary Star.

There was no doubt that with 'True Return's' ability, it should be able to observe and record the changes in the Mountains and Seas and the Star.

But the key question was...

What exactly were these two items?

And what benefits would they bring to Li Fan if he inherited them?

"Too profound."

"I have not even reached the Saintly realm. If I were to rashly inherit them, it might be more harmful than beneficial."

Staring at these two lines for a long time, Li Fan sighed wistfully.

"The fact that they now appear on the 'True Return' panel simply indicates that I finally possess the qualification to examine the [Mountains and Seas Outline] and [Star Principles]. However, whether the outcome after examining them will be good or bad is uncertain."

"As for before..."

"I likely didn't even have the right to glance at them."

The terrifying scene of the Mountains and Seas collapsing and the Star's radiance engulfing everything resurfaced in his mind.

He had no doubt that if his mortal self had encountered

Such a scene, he would have directly succumbed, driven to madness.

"Only by truly achieving Sainthood myself, not by borrowing the guise of the Mountains and Seas Great Dao, can I harmlessly accept both." Li Fan vaguely understood.

"Of course, since 'True Return' has listed them, it means that with my current strength, even if I forcibly read them, I will not suffer fatal damage."

"I can indeed examine the mysteries of both. However..."

"The other options bring benefit, while these two options are harmful."

Li Fan shook his head slightly and, after prolonged hesitation, ultimately chose neither.

"To play it safe is always the right choice."

"It is, after all, just one simulation cycle."

After calming his thoughts, Li Fan's gaze finally settled on the last option.

"Accelerate recharge progress..."

His thoughts momentarily stalled.

'True Return' required recharging; this had been a constant rule since the very beginning.

Even though the recharge time had been progressively decreasing with Li Fan's increasing strength and various fortuitous encounters,

It still required time to recharge.

In the past, Li Fan would have instinctively skipped this option, deeming it insignificant.

But now, after 'True Return's' inheritance options had undergone a change, and his own options for inheriting cultivation and possessions had been merged into one.

This option to accelerate recharging still existed.

Even occupying a line by itself.

"Could there be some hidden meaning?"

Judging by 'True Return's' current behavior, the answer was almost obvious.

But the benefits of choosing this option were too low. After a moment of contemplation, Li Fan ultimately skipped it.

"I choose to inherit the Dao I wielded in my previous life."

Li Fan's expression was solemn, his decision made.

From the depths of his heart, indistinct fluctuations from 'True Return' transmitted.

Fleeting and ephemeral.

Just as 'True Return' had conveyed before, everything was subject to Li Fan's final decision.

Moments later, a mystical and familiar rhythm descended.

"The Profound Embryo Great Dao..."

At the end of the Mountains and Seas, having spent countless years with it, Li Fan immediately recognized the aura of the Profound Embryo.

Due to 'True Return's' concealment, the descent of this Great Dao did not emanate beyond the Xuanhuang Realm.

It was confined to within three feet of Li Fan.

As the Great Dao embraced him, it felt like donning a well-worn garment, familiar and comfortable. Li Fan put it on with ease.

It was like the Emperor's new clothes, donned yet not worn.

It existed on Li Fan for only a moment before vanishing like a fleeting dream.

But this change was well within Li Fan's expectations.

He gazed into the distance, beyond the Primal Origin.

Towards the original location of the Profound Embryo Great Dao in the Mountains and Seas.

Carefully sensing it.

"Indeed, the Profound Embryo has been strengthened."

"Although not as exaggerated as doubling, it is already astonishing."

"And..."

A complex expression flashed across Li Fan's face.

"Having inherited the sliver of the Profound Embryo Great Dao that I wielded for so many years, the Profound Embryo of the current Mountains and Seas has been marked with my aura?"

At the same time, Li Fan noticed the characters "[The First Profound Embryo]" on the 'True Return' panel, after [Great Dao Returns to Truth].

The moment he chose to inherit, they changed from seven-colored to transparent.

"'True Return' still maintains control over the Profound Embryo."

"However, today's Profound Embryo is not the same as yesterday's."

"It requires re-acquisition to stabilize."

As a former Saint of the Profound Embryo, Li Fan could naturally discern the reason for this change.

"After my inheritance today, the Profound Embryo in the Mountains and Seas has undergone a permanent transformation."

"Even if I were to reincarnate again, and 'True Return' were to reshape the Mountains and Seas at the end of time, the Profound Embryo in the new reincarnation would still be the Profound Embryo I have already altered."

A sense of clarity washed over Li Fan.

At the same time, a sense of unease surfaced inexplicably.

The source of his unease was not a looming crisis.

But rather, "The 'undo' button no longer exists."

In the past, regardless of the choices he made, he could always use 'True Return' to return to the initial anchor point, nullifying all consequences.

But now, as his strength gradually increased and he glimpsed the true face of 'True Return,'

This "privilege" of not having to bear any consequences had vanished.

"It seems that any modification involving the Great Dao of the Mountains and Seas requires utmost caution."

In reality, Li Fan still suspected that 'True Return' had the ability to reset the Mountains and Seas to their "pure" state from when he first arrived.

However, 'True Return' had now deliberately informed him and made this change.

Even if Li Fan insisted on opposing it, it would be futile.

He could only accept it silently.

"Overall, the changes to the Profound Embryo Great Dao itself are beneficial to me."

Firstly, it would be easier for Li Fan to once again don the guise of the Profound Embryo.

Secondly...

Li Fan had a feeling.

If he were to mark all the Great Daos of the Mountains and Seas using this inheritance method,

Then, even without achieving Sainthood, his true strength would not be inferior to that of the Saints of the Shore.

"For now, the priority is to enhance my own strength."

"As for the conflicts between the Mountains and Seas, 'True Return,' and the Star..."

"Perhaps in the future, I will have the opportunity to participate."

In this difficult situation, Li Fan had his own way of survival.

To lie low when weak.

To seize every opportunity to grow stronger.

Until the situation completely reversed, and it was time for retribution!

Li Fan did not feel unable to accept the fact that 'True Return' had taken control of his body.

He did not descend into despair.

He had already realized that with 'True Return's' power, it could have completely taken over his body and will at any time.

But it had not done so.

There must be a purpose.

Whether it was the uniqueness of his infinite spiritual essence, or his identity as a "transmigrator."

In any case, 'True Return's' special treatment was the capital he could use to continue the game.

"Let's just wait and see."

"There is still a long way to go."

"Hmph."

Without any fear of 'True Return' potentially perceiving his thoughts, Li Fan thought to himself.

Chapter 1676: The True Spirit Entices and Becomes a Sage

In the previous life, Li Fan donned the guise of the Mysterious Conception, proceeding directly to the end of the Mountains and Seas. He lived through countless years.

Having already gained a profound understanding of the Mysterious Conception Great Dao.

This life, through the "True Return" inheritance option, the Mysterious Conception Great Dao now bore a unique mark of his own.

"No longer needing the imagined depictions of beings in the Realm of Birth and Death. I can achieve the same by myself."

"However, the descent of the Mountains and Seas Great Dao will surely alert the Saints on the Shore. Unless True Return helps me conceal it a little..."

Unfortunately, after completing its inheritance mission, True Return seemed to have fallen into slumber again. There was no response to Li Fan's request.

"It seems I have to find a way myself."

In his previous life, besides witnessing the true power of True Return, Li Fan's greatest gain was the method of "Infinite Selves" deduced by the combined efforts of the Saints at the end of the Mountains and Seas to nourish true spirits.

Even Saints as powerful as Qiu Xinhui could benefit from nourishing true spirits. The profundity of this method was evident.

"I can summon and manipulate the accumulated true spirits in the void at will. It has little to do with the Mysterious Conception outer garment. Even with my current transcendent strength, I can summon them at will!"

Li Fan's eyes flickered, and he leaped out of the Primal Origin possibility, rushing towards the earliest moments of this segment of the Mountains and Seas. Only when the Void Realm, exuding a terrifying aura, was within sight did he slowly reduce his speed.

"Before the Eternal Silence Void, the principle of 'having experienced the immense, the mundane becomes insignificant' no longer applies."

Even though he had seen the full power of the Void Realm that completely devoured the Mountains and Seas in his previous life, Li Fan still felt instinctive fear when facing the darkness before him.

It was as if there was no difference between the two.

The foundation of his own existence was continuously disintegrating as he approached.

"It seems that merely witnessing it offers no help in resisting the Void Realm. One must at least possess Saintly strength to survive briefly in the Void Realm."

Li Fan tried to approach slowly, but the limit of his advance distance was the same as before, when he and the Moral True Immortal had attempted it together.

There was no progress.

"It seems this is indeed the limit that the transcendent realm can reach."

Suppressing the unease in his heart, Li Fan no longer forced himself.

"Fortunately, it is already enough for me to sense the magnificent true spirits accumulated in the Void Realm."

Li Fan looked into the distance. In the absolute stillness of the darkness, he seemed to see countless soldiers of true spirits, lined up neatly, awaiting his command.

"The reason why accumulated true spirits can be easily manipulated by me should stem from my infinite spiritual essence."

Li Fan waved his hand gently. Just as he had performed at the end of the Mountains and Seas in his previous life, a mass of formless, accumulated true spirits was summoned.

"Mm... this segment of the Mountains and Seas is still relatively intact. Unlike the Void Realm and the end of the Mountains and Seas. With the same force, the scale of true spirits that can be summoned seems to be only half."

"But it doesn't matter, I just need to wave my hand a few more times." Li Fan

Estimated, and nodded in his heart.

"With the materials in hand, the next step is to select suitable candidates."

To conceal the commotion of the Mysterious Conception Great Dao's descent, with Li Fan's current strength, the best method was to create a disturbance of comparable magnitude.

First, draw the attention of all the Saints.

"The birth of a new Saint is enough to attract attention. Incidentally, I can also test my plan to crown Saints."

"As for a suitable candidate..."

The face of the Moral True Immortal immediately appeared in Li Fan's mind.

"I once said that if there was an opportunity, I would help you all become Saints. Now is the time to fulfill my promise." Li Fan said with a sinister low laugh.

"The Moral True Immortal is already only one step away from the Saint realm. He can even break free from the nature of the Great Dao through the method of moral division and achieve an alternative form of Sainthood. If he can receive the help of this mass of accumulated true spirits..."

"Uh, I'm afraid it's not enough."

In his previous life, Li Fan had personally witnessed Qiu Xinhui and the others' plan to create Saints, and he knew how astonishing the amount of true spirits required to create a Saint was. So he pondered for a moment, and with some effort, captured more accumulated true spirits from the Void Realm.

He opened his mouth slightly and swallowed them. Then, he leisurely departed.

In the eternally unchanging realm of eternal silence, as if due to the disappearance of this mass of accumulated true spirits, a brief surge of undercurrents occurred.

It was as if a consciousness quickly swept through.

But Li Fan had already withdrawn. This surging undercurrent naturally went unnoticed.

So it quickly subsided.

Li Fan was unaware of the anomalies in the Void Realm.

After all, whether it was during his traversal or at the end of the Mountains and Seas in his previous life.

He had arbitrarily extracted accumulated true spirits countless times without any abnormality.

The resulting fixed mindset led him to naturally let down his guard.

However, he forgot that during his traversal, he was quickly passing through different time periods of the Mountains and Seas, and the end of the Mountains and Seas was also the end of time. Besides the Saints, no one else would visit.

But in the current period...

There were the Nine Saints of the Shore, including the Guardian Qiu Gong, who entered and exited the Void Realm from time to time.

An unintended loophole left behind, but let's not mention it for now.

Let's talk about Li Fan quickly finding He Ganxian.

He Ganxian was naturally on guard against Li Fan, this uninvited guest who appeared inexplicably.

"Fellow Daoist, do you wish to become a Saint?" Li Fan asked directly, getting straight to the point.

"Ha?" Hearing Li Fan's inexplicably strange words, He Ganxian narrowed his eyes, his expression hostile.

"Could it be that you fellow Daoists are bored with your cultivation and have come to amuse yourselves with me?"

He Ganxian cautiously scanned his surroundings, as if looking for potential ambushes.

Li Fan chuckled: "Fellow Daoist worries too much. There's no complex meaning, just a simple question."

"Fellow Daoist, do you want to prove your Dao and become a Saint of the Mountains and Seas?"

He Ganxian stared at Li Fan for a long time, then sneered: "What you say, could it be that among the transcendent beings in the Mountains and Seas, there are those who do not wish to take this step?"

"This strange question, what is its profound meaning? Can you help me?"

"Yes! If you have my help, becoming a Saint will be as easy as flipping your palm!" Li Fan immediately interjected, speaking with righteous confidence.

"Heh heh..."

If the person saying this were a Saint of the Mountains and Seas, He Ganxian might have believed him.

But Li Fan's outward appearance was also only at the transcendent realm.

He Ganxian naturally dismissed Li Fan's words as a joke.

He did not choose to respond.

"Why am I stumbling upon this kind of person..."

"Could it be that another version of me is plotting in secret?"

Thinking this, He Ganxian was about to cloak himself and leave.

However, he suddenly glimpsed the scene ahead, and his figure froze in astonishment.

Within the hazy yellow light, two energies, one black and one white, revolved around each other.

Finally, when the black and white energies dispersed, two figures were born out of thin air.

They floated before He Ganxian, smiling and bowing.

"Greetings, fellow Daoist!"

He Ganxian recognized the appearances of these two from himself!

Or rather, the figures that appeared out of thin air were He Ganxian and the Faceless Immortal!

Not only their external appearances, but also the Dao energy flowing from them, undoubtedly belonged to the "Moral" path.

He Ganxian was extremely shocked, as if he had seen a ghost, and immediately retreated.

"Who exactly are you!" he asked Li Fan sternly.

"Just an old acquaintance." Li Fan smiled and remained silent.

"There's no need to be wary, no need to worry. Before, you did not believe my words that I could help you become a Saint..."

"Please observe first, and then make your judgment."

Li Fan revealed a mysterious smile, then whispered softly: "My existence is limitless."

Black and white energies were generated again.

Spinning rapidly, resembling a Tai Chi diagram.

Countless imaginary figures of He Ganxian and the Faceless Immortal continuously floated out from this Tai Chi diagram. Like countless ghostly soldiers in formation.

Although they were merely phantom projections, like ghosts, and not the actual transcendent powerhouses themselves.

This extremely bizarre scene still made He Ganxian's scalp tingle and his mind bewildered.

He looked at the countless figures of himself before him, superimposed upon each other. Recalling Li Fan's earlier words "just an old acquaintance."

His thoughts became chaotic, leading to wild speculation.

"Although I don't know the method by which the other party created my phantom images, to possess such knowledge and attain such skill in the Great Dao of Morality..."

"Could it be that he is truly someone I knew in the past?"

"But who could it be?"

Faces constantly flashed through He Ganxian's mind, but no matter how hard he racked his brain, he could not deduce Li Fan's true identity.

Meanwhile, in the center of the arena, when the number of imaginary phantom figures was sufficient, Li Fan let out another low shout: "All Saints are present!"

With a gentle flick of his finger, a large amount of accumulated true spirits poured down like a torrential waterfall from the sky.

Received by the countless phantom figures of the Moral True Immortal.

Although He Ganxian could not see the majestic pouring down of accumulated true spirits, he could keenly sense the miraculous changes occurring on the countless phantom figures of himself.

If before, they were merely soulless imitation paintings.

Then, now, these phantom figures had all slowly come alive for some unknown reason.

He Ganxian became even more terrified, but his feet were rooted to the spot, not moving an inch.

Because he had a vague premonition that the metamorphosis of these phantom figures about to occur would be a great fortune for him!

"Could it be that what this person just said..."

As the thought arose, it spread like wildfire, becoming impossible to suppress.

Countless He Ganxians came alive, each with a different expression.

But with another gentle gesture from Li Fan, they were all drawn back into the constantly rotating black and white Tai Chi diagram.

When the Tai Chi diagram finally stopped spinning, only one solid figure remained, sitting cross-legged.

The solid figure suddenly opened its eyes.

Meeting He Ganxian's gaze.

He Ganxian momentarily had the illusion that "he" was looking at himself!

"The opportunity to become a Saint lies ahead. Why are you still hesitating, fellow Daoist?" Li Fan's voice drifted over.

He Ganxian was so shocked by Li Fan's unfathomable methods that he remained silent for the time being, his body trembling slightly as he desperately suppressed his inner desires.

He Ganxian did not know how long it had been since he had last experienced such an intense craving of "want."

The figure of himself ahead seemed to possess infinite magical power and temptation.

The steadfastness accumulated over countless years of cultivation was easily broken.

Even when he first comprehended and captured the Great Dao of Morality, he had not lost his composure like this.

"What exactly..."

He Ganxian wanted to close his eyes and stop observing the figure before him.

And he wanted to escape this trap immediately.

But the phantom figure seemed to sense his thoughts and drifted towards him.

"It seems you still misunderstand me deeply."

"These phantom figures, condensed with accumulated true spirits, cannot remain in the Mountains and Seas for too long. If you hesitate further, all your efforts will be wasted. Allow me to lend you a hand." Li Fan's faint sigh drifted over.

To He Ganxian's ears, it was like thunder. Especially the words "accumulated true spirits," which instantly made him understand the fatal temptation he was sensing!

He knew himself best.

If it were an ordinary transcendent powerhouse, perhaps their desire for these true spirit figures would be less.

But he had experienced the division of morality, and his own true spirit had been split in two.

It was as if he was born incomplete.

The current nourishment of true spirits made it even more tempting.

Facing the phantom figure slowly approaching, even though a trace of caution arose in He Ganxian's mind, it was quickly suppressed by instinct.

Ultimately, he stood there motionless, accepting it entirely.

In an instant, it was as if he saw countless different possible versions of himself.

Their life experiences were blank slates.

But they seemed to exist as if they were real.

What's more, they had comprehended the Great Dao of Morality that he presided over. Although weaker than him, they still played a role in facilitating integration.

Almost without any obstacles, He Ganxian completely devoured these phantom figures that existed solely for his consumption.

The damage caused by the division of morality seemed to be replenished at this moment.

Like a feast after extreme hunger, He Ganxian felt an indescribable sense of satisfaction.

Most importantly, he could feel that his own aptitude and abilities had clearly improved compared to before.

"True spirits??"

"What this person said is not false!"

A storm surged in He Ganxian's mind. He could not afford to digest the lingering true spirits from the phantom figures.

He quickly bowed to Li Fan, showing utmost gratitude: "Fellow Daoist's kindness is like a rebirth. I am overwhelmed with gratitude and do not know how I can repay you!"

At the same time, he showed guilt on his face: "I actually misinterpreted Fellow Daoist's good intentions..."

Li Fan chuckled: "Astonishing words are naturally disbelieved at first. However, facts speak louder than words. After receiving the true spirits, you will naturally know the truth of my words. So I was too lazy to say more."

"How do you feel?"

He Ganxian closed his eyes to sense, and after a long time, let out a long sigh, replying: "Like a newborn. The Saint realm is indeed within reach!"

Saying this, He Ganxian bowed again to Li Fan with immense gratitude.

Although he did not know the other party's identity or purpose, the benefits he received were real. He Ganxian's gratitude was sincere.

"My assistance today is not without conditions. Fellow Daoist, when you prove your Dao in the future, I have one request."

When Li Fan said this, He Ganxian felt a sense of relief.

He feared most that Li Fan would disappear without a word after saying this.

If that were the case, even if he eventually proved his Dao as a Saint, he would still feel remorse about this matter.

Now that Li Fan had a request, he could use this to repay the karmic debt.

"Fellow Daoist, please speak. I will surely not fail your trust." He Ganxian said very solemnly.

Chapter 1677: Whereabouts of King Xuantian

Suddenly, the light vanished, and endless darkness enveloped the Realm of Birth and Death. From the bizarre abyss, it seemed as if countless mud-like tentacles emerged, tightly entwining the purple figure's giant hands. The sea of fiery clouds, stretching for millions of miles, acted like a sharp sword, slashing towards the abyss. The purple figure's surprised roar flashed and then was drowned out by endless, violent explosions.

...

While the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables acted to hold back the purple figure from the Shore, mysterious changes were occurring throughout the Realm of Birth and Death. Thousands of rivers flowed side by side, as if attracted by something, coiling backward and connecting end to end, forming circles. In an instant, they wove into a gem radiating pure yellow light! Under the cover of a mystical rhythm, the sounds of clashing weapons from the outside world gradually weakened. The eight figures were surrounding the central yellow gem, appearing majestic and unmoving. But in reality, between flashes of light and shadow, they had already crossed thousands of mountains and seas!

"We've temporarily shaken off their pursuit. However, even if we can transfer again, it's ultimately not a long-term solution," Ming Dao Immortal's tone was heavy.

"I didn't expect another Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas to appear in the Mountains and Seas. This was truly unexpected. Has it exposed us prematurely??"

"The comparison of paintings is almost complete. We absolutely cannot abandon it halfway. If it becomes critical, I will ideationally construct the Realm of Birth and Death and actively lure the enemy, buying you time," the white-haired youth said with a solemn expression.

The others did not object: "Don't worry, we will not forget your contribution."

The white-haired youth smiled and shook his head: "I am already a dead person. Being reborn from ideation and having experienced another lifetime, I am content. If I can help you all achieve your Grand Dao, then my life will not have been in vain."

After a period of silence, the eight figures refocused their gazms on the yellow gem in the center. Having reached a safe haven, the lines forming the gem slowly unraveled, transforming back into thousands of flowing lights and shadows. And within the lights and shadows, the beings within the ideational probabilities seemed frozen in time, having lost the concept of the passage of time. They were unaware of the outside events.

After receiving the safety notification from the Venerables, they soon returned to their former lives. Xing Fu was among them. However, he occasionally looked towards the outside of the Realm of Birth and Death, his expression subtle.

"I cannot see the scenery of the outside Mountains and Seas. It must be the Venerables using their power to blockade it."

"I just don't know how long it will last."

Xing Fu felt no fear of being exposed at any moment; instead, he carried a hint of anticipation.

"The calamities of the Realm of Birth and Death should not be as simple as the Venerables described. Otherwise, even with the purple-robed figure's arrival, they would not have been able to escape so quickly during a thorough search. It must be that there is something the Saints of the Shore care about..."

The answer was obvious. The Great Dao of Mountains and Seas!

"The method of ideation comparison and replication to sketch the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas that they passed down should also be true. However, they have concealed the progress!"

Xing Fu looked up at the yellow gem suspended above the myriad river phantoms, formless and intangible.

"Regardless of whether it's intentional or unintentional, active or passive, the awakened ones within the Realm of Birth and Death, including myself, are likely being recorded with each replication, counting towards the overall comparison progress."

"But the Venerables did not lie. Once the progress is complete and the Great Dao of Eternal Life appears, whoever becomes its master within the Realm of Birth and Death will depend entirely on personal fortune and creation."

"To snatch or seize is useless."

"The reason for not making this information public..."

"Knowing too much would only lead to unease and hinder ideational replication."

Xing Fu took a long time to suppress his turbulent thoughts. This discovery did not actually change Xing Fu's life in any way. Even though the progress was 99.99%, it was still equivalent to zero before true completion.
