Unsure when he would truly glimpse the appearance of the unknown Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas, the pursuit from the Shore, however, was real and likely to descend again.

Xing Fu keenly sensed that the overall atmosphere within the Realm of Birth and Death had slowly changed compared to before. Especially those awakened ones. Their previous unwavering focus was gone, and the efficiency of ideational construction was consequently affected.

"They are already getting distracted. Their ability to withstand pressure is too poor."

Noticing this, Xing Fu felt strange. Logically speaking, these awakened ones all possessed transcendent strength. Their state of mind should not be so unstable.

"Unless..."

"Forced growth is not true self-growth. Transcendence achieved through forceful means."

Xing Fu's attention first fell on his companions.

"Those who were not significantly affected and whose state of mind remained stable did not notice any anomalies."

"And those whose minds were in turmoil..."

"As if ideational construction, though extremely real, is ultimately not true!"

After accumulating for an unknown number of years, Xing Fu had developed his own unique understanding of ideational construction. Upon careful observation this time, he finally discovered the secret.

"Furthermore, this sense of disharmony and unreality..."

Xing Fu frowned and recalled, based on a sense of familiar similarity from the depths of his heart, he suddenly thought of the white-haired young Venerable he had met before.

"Is he also a creation of ideation?"

"Has the ideational technique of the Realm of Birth and Death reached such a point that it is almost indistinguishable from reality?"

Xing Fu immediately harbored suspicion. Just as the Grand Dao of Mountains and Seas attracted each other, painters would also develop a sense of mutual appreciation. Although Xing Fu had now gained an入门(beginner's) level in ideational construction, He did not feel that the Venerables of the Five Concurrent Calamity were significantly superior to him in this art. Although there was no concrete evidence, only a vague guess in his heart, Xing Fu was almost certain. Xing Fu himself did not know where his confidence came from.

"Perhaps it is my talent shown in ideational construction?"

"The white-haired youth, although a creation of ideation, is treated as an equal by the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables and Ming Dao Immortal??"

"If I were in their position, would I treat my own ideational creations with equality? It's impossible!"

Xing Fu's eyes flashed with light, and he already had an answer in his heart.

"It was created by others through ideation and left behind as assistance."

"As for who..."

"The answer is obvious. It should be that Walker of Mountains and Seas who taught the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables!"

As his thoughts turned rapidly, Xing Fu had already deduced part of the truth.

"Since ideation can transform from emptiness to reality, it must be generated from one's own familiar memories. If the white-haired youth was ideationally constructed by the Walker of Mountains and Seas, then his original identity..."

"From the end of the Mountains and Seas?"

Xing Fu could not help but think of what the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables had said earlier.

"He himself was not the original creator of this divine ability. The true origin comes from the last prodigy among our cultivators in the final epoch of the Mountains and Seas."

"...His talent was so high that she even surpassed that Walker of Mountains and Seas."

Xing Fu nodded inwardly: "Perhaps precisely because of his extraordinary original identity, the Venerables hold such respect for this created being."

He desperately wanted to know the specific situation of the end of the Mountains and Seas from the white-haired youth's memories. However, ever since the purple-robed figure from the Shore attacked, the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death had rarely appeared in front of everyone. They seemed to be working together on something. Xing Fu could only sigh and forgo his desire.

Even though he had uncovered some secrets of the Realm of Birth and Death, Xing Fu kept them buried in his heart without revealing them to anyone. In the remaining time, he continued to perform ideational construction silently, adding a bit to the progress of finally sketching the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas.

Approximately another period, even longer than before, of time passed. On this day, after completing a replication, Xing Fu suddenly felt a strange tremor in his heart. Then, tears inexplicably streamed down his face. Xing Fu wiped them away, utterly shocked. At the same time, doubt arose in his heart: "What is happening? My mind instinctively feels sorrow, and I cannot help but shed tears."

"This should be a phenomenon that occurs after the death of a close relative by blood. But all my relatives perished in the destruction of the Immortal Realm back then. What exactly...?"

Xing Fu pondered endlessly, unable to find an answer. He wanted to investigate further but had no method. Ultimately, he could only bury this question deep in his heart.

After this, untold years passed. Regarding the ultimate completion of sketching the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, it seemed that only a sliver was missing. But this sliver was like the difference between heaven and earth. No matter how diligently the beings within the Realm of Birth and Death tried, they could never fill it. However, as the "progress bar" was increasingly filled towards completion, corresponding changes also occurred within the Realm of Birth and Death. The most noticeable was the ten thousand river phantoms. They were originally mere ideational creations. Xing Fu could discern their reality from illusion at a glance.

But now, they had become almost indistinguishable from reality! With Xing Fu's mastery of the Dao of Ideation, it would take careful examination to distinguish the subtle differences between them and the true probabilities in the Mountains and Seas. For those not skilled in this Dao, it would be difficult to detect their "ideational characteristics."

"There is no immediate danger of destruction. Those people from the Guangwu Star Sea, who lived so leisurely and freely, have almost forgotten about me," Xing Fu's expression became momentarily dazed. Aside from these ideational probabilities, the yellow gem suspended above the myriad river phantoms had also changed dramatically. It was still not in a state of ultimate ideational reality. It existed between reality and illusion. When not observed, it was merely composed of myriad dao phantoms.

But if observed carefully, every facet of the yellow gem was so lifelike. It was indistinguishable from a real arrival. This superposition of dual states, true and false, further captivated Xing Fu. He looked up and observed from time to time, and suddenly a feeling arose in his heart. The day of its true transformation was not far off. Xing Fu's premonition was always accurate.

Three thousand five hundred and sixty-nine years later. On this day, Xing Fu's replication was inexplicably interrupted. For Xing Fu, whose mastery of ideational construction had reached consummation, this was an almost impossible event. But it truly happened. Because...

Instantly realizing something, Xing Fu's body trembled uncontrollably with extreme excitement.

"Exclude all lines that feel discordant."

"The Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, hidden in the void, has finally been sketched and outlined by us."

Like the beings within the ten thousand river phantoms, Xing Fu looked up at the radiant yellow gem above his head. Figures appeared one after another, surrounding the gem. They were the Venerables of the Realm of Birth and Death calamities, who had not appeared for a long time. However, there were only five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, not eight. Ming Dao Immortal and the other Venerables were nowhere to be seen.

Under the gaze of all, the yellow gem, which had been painstakingly recreated by the countless painters of the Realm of Birth and Death over countless years, actually began to disintegrate. As if infinite lines surged from it. Becoming denser and denser, like countless paintbrushes, sketching a Grand Dao that should not exist in the Mountains and Seas.

The Great Dao of Mountains and Seas manifested, and the Realm of Birth and Death, which had been hidden for many years, could no longer remain concealed. The isolation of their aura was broken, and a rift was suddenly torn open. Xing Fu could clearly see a majestic sacred circle standing not far away. The white circle seemed to stand amidst the Mountains and Seas. Although it appeared extremely distant, it was also extremely close. In an instant, it arrived, sealing and suppressing the Realm of Birth and Death.

But at this moment, the Five Concurrent Calamity Venerables, and even the beings within the Realm of Birth and Death, were no longer important. All eyes were focused on the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas that was about to be born. Within the white circle, light and shadow fluctuated. The Saints of the Shore revealed solemn expressions. And at the same time, a figure dressed in a black dragon robe, wearing a crown, quietly descended into this space. Sitting alone on the imperial throne, although he was alone. The palpable pressure he brought was no less than that of the Saints' illusions. The might of the Saints was like a tempest. Although they had restrained themselves as much as possible and were mutually checking, their power was still diminished. But for the beings in this realm, it was still unbearable. The vast majority fainted the moment the Saints appeared. And among the few who could maintain clarity, they dared not look at the figures of the Saints. They merely forced their attention onto the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas, which was on the verge of disappearing. Rather than disappearing, it was being replicated from nothingness and then hidden within the Mountains and Seas.

Xing Fu felt a faint premonition. Whether the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas could be controlled by those present at this moment depended on its descent.

"If it intends to hide..."

"Perhaps even Saints would not be able to find it."

All breathing stopped, and they all waited for that moment. When the lines of the yellow gem completely vanished, completely merging with the Mountains and Seas. Suddenly, Emperor Tai Wei snorted coldly and disappeared, driving his imperial seat. This action surprised even the Saints of the Shore.

"Still so arrogant."

Faintly, the evaluations of the Saints could be heard from within the white circle. Emperor Tai Wei's departure did not affect the descent of the Great Dao of Mountains and Seas. Shortly after, everyone present sensed an ancient, vast, yet newly born aura. It flashed and disappeared.

"Dao Oblivion plunders the fundamental essence of the Mountains and Seas, the key to the decline of the Mountains and Seas."

"The root of heaven and earth, giving birth to all things."

"This is the Grand Dao of [Xuan Pin]!"

The voice boomed from the white circle of the Shore. The speaker was Duke Shou Qiu, who presided over [Eternal Life]! In the midst of the light, the Saints were about to make a move. The entire Mountains and Seas seemed to suddenly freeze. Endless white mist emerged from the void. Enveloping the Mountains and Seas.

"True Return!"

Only a faint voice could be heard from the white mist.

Chapter 1678: The Mountains and Seas Hold Strange Fortunes

"Infinite selves!" The experimental subject, using the method of imagination, replicated countless versions of himself. Facing the cascading torrent of accumulated spiritual essence, which threatened destruction, he became a dam, momentarily withstanding its impact!

"I perceive true spirits!" At this instant, all the experimental subjects opened their eyes. Through the immense pressure they felt, they seemed to have truly "seen" the formless, intangible multitude of true spirits! Though there were numerous experimental subjects present, they all originated from the same source. More importantly, they were all countless clones created by one specific entity through imagination. Thus, they seemed to share the same barrier of true spirits.

At Qiu Xin Hui's signal, Li Fan increased the intensity of the accumulated true spirit impact. The dam formed by thousands of experimental subjects, though strong, eventually began to falter. Under the immense pressure, a crack appeared. The accumulated true spirits seized this opportunity, silently invading with their destructive power, like wind and thunder. If only one experimental subject had borne this ordeal, his fate would have been to be engulfed and dissipate within the accumulated true spirits. But at this moment… Facing this terrifying calamity, the myriad experimental subjects remained undaunted. With the main body as the core of defense, they collectively distributed the immense pressure from the accumulated true spirits evenly. One person facing it would be like an ant trying to shake Mount Tai, annihilation would be instantaneous. But what about thousands, or billions? Moreover, from the main experimental subject, waves of golden light continuously flickered and pulsed. With the constant influx of new imaginary forces, although the accumulated true spirits surged ferociously, they could not shake the dam of the multitude for a time. What was once a surging dragon had now transformed into countless converging streams. The individual streams of accumulated true spirits, after the initial impact, were naturally beyond the capacity of one experimental subject to absorb. But for a fraction of a stream, absorbing it was no longer so difficult. Although the absorption and utilization rate of the accumulated true spirits summoned by Li Fan further decreased, The initial objective had been achieved! The true spirits were nourished, and the previously hazy eyes of the experimental subject gradually sharpened and became intelligent. He looked around, seemingly understanding his situation. He did not blame the surrounding Saints who were observing him. Seeing the countless other versions of himself beside him, he intuitively calmed his mind. He began to recall the imaginary clones that were used to share the pressure of the accumulated true spirits. This experimental subject had not previously studied the Dao of Imagination; these imaginary clones were all generated by Qiu Xin Hui's intervention. Therefore, the speed of recall was not ideal at first. The vast majority of the imaginary clones dissipated without a trace after fulfilling their purpose. And the true spirits they carried, having lost their vessels, flowed away silently like water. However, those chosen as experimental subjects were all extraordinary by nature. Now, having been infused with true spirits, their spiritual essence was superior to before. He learned quickly. And he remained unshaken despite the constant and rapid dissipation of his surrounding imaginary clones. He simply adapted, doing his best. Initially, only one or two figures were drawn to return. Later, as the experimental subject's speed of recalling imaginary clones accelerated, Like countless stars returning to a single entity. Brilliant light converged upon the experimental subject.

...

The white-haired scholar stroked his beard and praised: "Although the imaginary clones carrying true spirits cannot be fully absorbed instantly, they are ultimately stored within the body, becoming a source of future growth. It is akin to possessing an inexhaustible treasure mountain within, from which one can continuously mine and enhance one's potential as strength increases."

"One can benefit from this until the moment of achieving Sainthood."

The shifting figure's visions flickered, seemingly deducing the possibilities of the Mountains and Seas where the 'Infinite Selves' method of the Great Dao flourished.

The Saints' gazes once again converged on Li Fan.

"It is regrettable that while the method of imagination can be learned by anyone, the ability to summon and manipulate the accumulated true spirits from the void is unique to our Mountains and Seas."

"Since we are already at the end of the Mountains and Seas, we cannot go back."

The Saints sighed inwardly.

"The past is past, and those who lived it will bear its consequences. We must now focus on our future," Qiu Xin Hui said with a smile, drawing the Saints' attention away from Li Fan.

"With Daoist friend Fan's assistance, all our deficiencies can be rectified. Furthermore, we can create far more helpers than anticipated??"

The shifting figure spoke at this moment: "Our chances of success have now surpassed fifty percent!"

"Fifty percent and beyond – further increases in probability are insignificant. Esteemed elders, let us each unleash our divine abilities and impart the 'Infinite Selves' method. We need not rely on Saints' help; merely a thousand or so half-Saints..."

"It is time for Scholar to break the seal of the river of time and face the end of the Mountains and Seas directly," Qiu Xin Hui said, cupping his hands towards the white-haired scholar.

The white-haired scholar nodded proudly, appearing somewhat impatient.

Among the Saints present, only Li Fan hesitated.

"Is this not perhaps... a bit too hasty?"

"Since we have a method to continuously strengthen ourselves, why not accumulate more power?" Li Fan questioned, confused.

Qiu Xin Hui merely smiled and offered no reply.

"Only through battle can victory be achieved."

"Countless strategies and meticulous calculations are ultimately no match for a direct confrontation."

Qiu Xin Hui was undoubtedly the core among the Saints. Since his mind was made up, Li Fan had no reason to object further. Li Fan now had two choices: Whether to immediately activate "True Return" or to wait. To observe the outcome of the final battle between the Mountains and Seas and the desolate void, and the desperate gambit of the Saints, before departing. Although the final decisive battle at the end of the Mountains and Seas was indeed captivating, Li Fan had not lost his reason. At the moment of the end of the Mountains and Seas and the arrival of the final battle, the danger would be immense. Even Saints could perish in an instant. And Li Fan, unlike the other Saints, had not made sufficient preparations.

"Using the power of the First Profound Embryo, I successfully traversed the desolate void. I obtained the method to control the accumulated true spirits, and with the Saints' power, I deduced the method of 'Infinite Selves' for true spirit infusion."

"The gains in this life have far exceeded my expectations. It is time to return."

After all, Li Fan was not a true Saint, but merely a transcendent cultivator clad in the semblance of the Profound Embryo Great Dao. Although the Saints' attention had been focused on the true spirit infusion technique during their long seclusion, They had rarely turned their gaze towards Li Fan. But now that the method was deduced, the probability of the Saints' attention falling upon Li Fan was increasing. The longer he stayed, the greater the risk of his secrets, and the secrets of 'True Return,' being exposed.

"This place is not suitable for lingering."

Finding an opportune moment when the Saints were distracted, Li Fan silently summoned 'True Return' in his heart. The mysterious power of "True and False Transformation" began to surge once more, intending to reverse everything as before. But suddenly, Li Fan sensed something was amiss. As if sensing his impending departure, currents of power inexplicably emerged from the surrounding Mountains and Seas. Like tendrils, they coiled around Li Fan's body. Preventing his 'True Return' from leaving!

Li Fan's expression shifted slightly. He scanned his surroundings, searching for the source of this power. However, the Saints seemed oblivious to the changes in their midst, their expressions unchanged. It was only then that Li Fan realized that it was not external forces preventing his departure. What bound him were the very foundations of his Sainthood – the Profound Embryo Great Dao!

"This..." Being restrained by his own power was truly ironic. Li Fan felt a mixture of shock and anger. He tried to break free from his shackles with all his might. It was indeed effective. As a Saint of the Profound Embryo, his control over the Profound Embryo Great Dao still existed. But... To achieve full effect required some time. Li Fan forced himself to calm down and carefully pondered, finally understanding what had happened. In this life, using the First Profound Embryo Great Dao, he had achieved the status of a Saint of the Mountains and Seas. Having attained Sainthood, he had gradually become the embodiment of the Profound Embryo itself within the Mountains and Seas. As previously stated, Li Fan's core was ultimately the "True and False Transformation," with the Profound Embryo being merely an outer garment he wore, which could be shed at any time. But now, this thick garment had been worn for too long. It had become somewhat adhered to his person, making it difficult to remove in a short period. The Profound Embryo Great Dao and the current Mountains and Seas were inextricably linked. When Li Fan wished to activate 'True Return,' these connections became obstacles.

"To actuate 'True Return,' I must first shed the outer garment of the Profound Embryo."

"This is not something that can be achieved in a day or two."

"Given the time I have existed as a Saint, how long will it take to completely detach myself? Perhaps one-tenth of that time?" In reality, it was already quite efficient, but to Li Fan, it was unacceptable. He truly never expected that pretending to be a Saint would have such consequences! He had already spent a considerable amount of time at the end of the Mountains and Seas in this life, and now, the final decisive battle at the end of the Mountains and Seas was imminent. Yet, at this critical juncture, he was unable to activate 'True Return.'

"This..."

"'True Return! True Return!'" Li Fan repeated inwardly, not to activate it, but to awaken the slumbering 'True Return.' But in this current situation, it was precisely as he had experienced in his simulations. 'True Return' remained silent.

"Without the severe injuries from the Three Dao Mergers, it's simply feigning ignorance."

Having understood this, Li Fan's shock and anger quickly subsided.

"If there were true danger, 'True Return' would not remain so indifferent."

"Furthermore, my spiritual intuition has not issued any warnings."

"What exactly..." Li Fan's unease eventually caught the attention of the Saints.

"Daoist friend, do not worry. Simply proceed with your tasks," To divert the Saints' attention from himself, Li Fan could only nod silently. Compared to the long years of research preceding this, the preparations for the final decisive battle appeared remarkably hasty. The method of true spirit infusion had produced over a thousand cultivators on the verge of Sainthood. The shifting figure performed some calculations and nodded his head. The white-haired scholar then pointed a finger, severing the frozen river of time. As if ice shattering, the stagnant currents roared like thunder. Li Fan felt a momentary dizziness. As the river of time resumed its flow, the years he had experienced in isolation suddenly erupted. Countless scenes flashed before his eyes, and millennia passed in an instant. Without any time for preparation, the end of the Mountains and Seas had arrived! The last rays of the sun were about to dip below the horizon. The final fragment of the iceberg was about to be swallowed by the ocean's surface. The final possibility where they could take refuge was about to sink into endless Dao Annihilation. As if to celebrate the ultimate victory of this prolonged battle, strange, echoing fluctuations emanated from the cold, silent desolate void. Li Fan could clearly feel something lurking beneath the accumulated true spirits, moving slowly at times, and rapidly at others. It watched like a predator, fixed on the perishing Mountains and Seas. Darkness pressed in, drawing ever closer. And the doomed Mountains and Seas uttered their final lament! Li Fan had heard the voice of the Mountains and Seas before. But never had he felt such profound sorrow and unwillingness as he did now! Images of the Mountains and Seas in their nascent glory flashed before Li Fan's eyes. The Mountains and Seas resonated in unison, celebrating their theft from the Gods, their rebirth. But their rise was as swift as their fall. The Mountains and Seas, having endured countless ages, seemed but a fleeting moment in Li Fan's eyes. Images flickered by at an indiscernible speed. By the time Li Fan regained his senses, they had already merged with the current reality of the Mountains and Seas' demise. In their twilight years, their destruction was inevitable. The great lament was the last sound the Mountains and Seas could emit. And it did not last long. As darkness completely engulfed them, the echoes of the Mountains and Seas also vanished. The Mountains and Seas perished at this moment! Their bodies, after all, originated from the Mountains and Seas. Now that the Mountains and Seas were destroyed, Li Fan's emotions were affected, and his own existence began to dissipate as well. As if empowered by the final victory, the corrosive force of the desolate void intensified a hundredfold compared to his previous traversal. From all perceivable dimensions, it surged inward. Li Fan's disintegration progressed at an unimaginable speed.

"Why haven't they acted yet?" Li Fan tried to locate Qiu Xin Hui and the others within the darkness. But they seemed to have been affected by the demise of the Mountains and Seas, showing no signs of activity.

"Has their struggle failed?"

Just as this thought crossed Li Fan's mind. A beam of light illuminated the desolate void once more. The Mountains and Seas, which had been completely swallowed, inexplicably returned, reappearing in the desolate void! However, this brief resurgence lasted only for a fleeting moment. The landscape of the Mountains and Seas had already become distorted. Soon, it was compressed by the desolate void into two white dots. Yet, the tenacity of these two white dots seemed to surpass that of the entire Mountains and Seas. Despite the surging black tides, their faint light could not be entirely extinguished for a time. As they remained in a stalemate, another anomaly occurred. Two thin lines emerged from the white dots of the Mountains and Seas. They delved into the void. Instantly, the darkness churned. The pressure exerted upon the white dots lessened slightly. The white dots shone brightly, seemingly regenerating the phenomena of the Mountains and Seas.

"This is..." Li Fan, struggling to maintain his existence, felt a familiar aura from one of the white lines. It was the terrifying aura he had sensed upon first entering the Infinite Sea. At this moment, even though 'True Return' was by his side, it was too occupied to intervene. It was engaged in a life-or-death struggle with the desolate void. Waves of intense fluctuations swept over him, further disintegrating Li Fan's existential foundation.

"True Return!" Li Fan called out again, unable to protect himself. But the result was the same. Just as the Mountains and Seas and the desolate void were locked in their most critical struggle, and Li Fan was reduced to mere remnants of his being. The final Saints of the Mountains and Seas, who had been waiting for this moment, finally acted. They had not been consumed by the desolate void. In fact, as if they had known what would transpire at the end of the Mountains and Seas, they had been awaiting this opportune moment.

Chapter 1679: Three Saints Established on the Same Day

Myriad imaginary currents surged forth like a cascade of stars, illuminating the cold, dark desolate void. Like threads, they instantly wove a phantom image of the Mountains and Seas. However, this scene did not last long. The true Mountains and Seas had already been annihilated within the desolate void; how much less could this imaginary Mountains and Seas endure? The surrounding darkness seemed to press down heavily, suppressing the light emitted by the phantom image. Turbulent waves surged, attempting to drag it into eternal darkness.

"All Saints are present!" The voice of Qiu Xin Hui, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, suddenly echoed through the void. He repelled a wave of energy. The phantom image of the Mountains and Seas momentarily beamed with light, and simultaneously, from the myriad flowing rivers within the Mountains and Seas, a single thread of possibility emerged, and several figures flew out, standing proudly. These were the transcendent cultivators born from the "Infinite Selves" true spirit infusion plan. "Infinite Selves" had created over a thousand half-Saints. And ordinary transcendents were countless. All transcendents could traverse the Dao Annihilation. They possessed a certain degree of resistance against the encroachment of Dao Annihilation. At this moment, countless transcendents joined forces, each contributing their meager strength, collectively supporting the imaginary Mountains and Seas on the verge of sinking into the desolate void. In every passing moment, numerous lights representing cultivators dissipated. Though it was destined to be unable to alter the ultimate fate of the imaginary Mountains and Seas, it bought invaluable time for the subsequent actions of the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas!

A phantom long river suddenly drifted out, spanning the imaginary Mountains and Seas. Within the Mountains and Seas, time began to flow. "Old man, farewell!" The shifting figure's voice echoed, and within the imaginary Mountains and Seas, ripples seemed to spread with the sound. Li Fan observed clearly that countless possibilities within the imaginary Mountains and Seas began to manifest. If the initial imaginary Mountains and Seas were merely a blank canvas drawn from collective memory, Then, with the addition of the power of the river of time and the ability to infinitely deduce possibilities, the imaginary Mountains and Seas began to grow on two different dimensions. Taking on characteristics of what once was a real Mountains and Seas. The aura of "imagination" slowly faded. It began to resemble the Mountains and Seas that had truly existed in reality. The newly born Mountains and Seas, though weak, pulsed with vitality. The sacrifice of the two Saints was like a wildfire, igniting an unstoppable blaze. Increasing, endless possibilities began to grow wildly. The river of time, from ancient to present, extended infinitely. The aura of the newborn Mountains and Seas expanded exponentially with each passing moment, growing millions of times faster than before, in the darkness. Though still minuscule compared to the desolate void, It was sufficient to capture its attention. Even a small portion of the desolate void's power, diverted from surrounding the residual Mountains and Seas, was still too much for the newborn Mountains and Seas to bear. In an instant, it fell into a precarious state, its light dimming. It seemed on the verge of complete submersion into darkness. At this critical juncture, over a thousand half-Saints appeared within the Mountains and Seas. Their expressions were fearless, unwavering. Their bodies dissolved as if consumed by fire, streams of light, carrying the true spirits they had absorbed, pouring into the newborn Mountains and Seas. Like a powerful stimulant, the precarious Mountains and Seas temporarily withstood the tide of darkness. Though the newborn Mountains and Seas had grown manifold, It was still incomparable to the desolate void. Once the desolate void finished dealing with the two residual light dots in the darkness, the newborn Mountains and Seas would ultimately face annihilation.

"I have seen fragments of the Mountains and Seas' flowing years, and I know what the Mountains and Seas once looked like." The voice of Qiu Xin Hui, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, resonated. With a gentle wave of his sleeve, he scattered countless light orbs. As if guided by an unseen hand, these fragments were placed in their rightful positions. As if awakening ancient memories and obtaining the main framework, the newborn Mountains and Seas began to grow in a structured manner. They could now occasionally suppress the encroaching waves from the void. This action seemed to have thoroughly angered the surrounding darkness. Determined to give the newborn Mountains and Seas no chance to grow, the desolate void's corrosive pressure suddenly increased a thousandfold! Almost instantly, the brilliance of the newborn Mountains and Seas became almost imperceptible. It faced the same fate as the residual Mountains and Seas. Though several streams of light circulated, protecting it, Under the pressure of the desolate void, they gradually faded into nothingness.

"Facing the desolate void in its full power, even Saints can only endure for such a short time!" Li Fan saw the figures of the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas within the dissipating streams of light. His condition worsened, and he couldn't help but feel a hint of fear. Fortunately, with the presence of the new and old Mountains and Seas attracting the enemy's attention, the pressure on Li Fan was slightly reduced compared to when he first fell into the void. Therefore, he could still hold on. "Haven't I watched enough of this show? Why can't I still activate 'True Return'!" Li Fan felt extremely exasperated. He could sense that while the desolate void was destroying the foundation of his existence, it was also dissolving the Profound Embryo Great Dao itself. Therefore, the force binding him was gradually weakening. Theoretically, he should now be able to activate 'True Return.' But for some reason, 'True Return' remained stubbornly inactive. Li Fan was powerless and could only do his best to maintain his existence, quietly observing the unfolding events. Even after the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas perished, Qiu Xin Hui had not given up.

"All Saints are present!" Endless golden light erupted from the newborn Mountains and Seas. As guardians, they reduced the desolate void's corrosive force. Simultaneously, Saintly figures emerged one after another from the void. These were precisely the Saints who had perished earlier! However, they were not their true forms, but imaginary bodies. But their existence was distinctly different from ordinary imaginary bodies; they surprisingly possessed the ability to manipulate their respective Mountains and Seas Great Daos! The river of time reappeared, with countless shifting figures. The newborn Mountains and Seas received another wave of nourishment and expansion!

"How is this possible?" Li Fan was utterly shocked by this scene. These imaginary Saints were clearly Qiu Xin Hui's creation. Although they were not true bodies, merely imaginary forms, they could still wield Saintly authority. This indicated…

"Qiu Xin Hui, the final Saint of the Mountains and Seas, is intimately familiar with the Great Daos of other Saints!"

"Just as I know of the Profound Embryo, although I am not a Profound Embryo Saint, I can wear its guise and wield its authority as a Saint."

"He possesses the art of 'Imaginary Reconstruction of Saints,' capable of acting as a Saint!"

Li Fan's mind trembled as he watched Qiu Xin Hui single-handedly turn the tide. Each time the protective streams of light from the imaginary Saints were erased by the desolate void, With Qiu Xin Hui's declaration of "All Saints are present," new imaginary Saints would appear out of thin air, Nourishing the Mountains and Seas anew. In this manner, cyclically repeating, The power of this final Saint of the Mountains and Seas seemed inexhaustible, As if there was no limit to his strength!

"This..." Li Fan was awestruck into speechlessness. During the end of time, they had coexisted for a long period, yet he had never realized that this person's strength was so terrifying and unfathomable!

"Furthermore, I recall that the Dao of Imagination is not his own path."

"What is his path to Sainthood?"

Li Fan silently watched as the newborn Mountains and Seas, nurtured by the Saints, flourished within the desolate void, his mind filled with even greater questions.

"I truly underestimated this final Saint of the Mountains and Seas."

"With the strength he has displayed... could the newborn Mountains and Seas actually have a chance?"

The desolate void churned with waves. Although every instant of impact could destroy the newborn Mountains and Seas to the point of annihilation, As long as even a sliver of light remained, Qiu Xin Hui could restore it. Thus, under the continuous erosion of the desolate void, the newborn Mountains and Seas managed to grow amidst constant destruction! If this were to continue indefinitely, it seemed even the desolate void would be powerless against it! As if sensing this, the cold darkness fell into a moment of silence. Then... The boundless void was torn asunder. As if a solitary star hung high, or a divine eye opened. An unknown entity within the desolate void descended. The newborn Mountains and Seas froze. Then shattered layer by layer. Even with countless imaginary Saints appearing repeatedly, desperately trying to intervene, Its destructive speed was too great. No matter how they repaired it, it was all in vain.

"Finally, the face of the [Star]..."

"Heh heh. Daoist Fan, why have you not acted yet?" Qiu Xin Hui's voice suddenly echoed. Li Fan, still in shock at the emergence of the [Star], was startled by Qiu Xin Hui's words.

"Act?"

"Me?" The mere Profound Embryo Great Dao could barely withstand the dark tides stirred by the desolate void. How could it possibly contend with the [Star]? Li Fan found the situation absurd. At the same time, a sense of panic arose within him. Given Qiu Xin Hui's displayed strength, he would not utter such baseless words.

"Unless..." Realizing this, Li Fan's body moved involuntarily. Not by his own will, but out of necessity. Emerging from the darkness, he floated out. Towards the invisible rift torn in the desolate void, he gently pointed at the [Star] that appeared within.

"When true becomes false..."

"False also becomes true."

A Cànyu sound, both ancient yet youthful, echoed. The solitary star seemed to vanish. And the imaginary Mountains and Seas, in an instant, spawned infinite phantoms. Moments later, these phantoms solidified from illusion to reality, boundless and filling the field of vision. As if the Mountains and Seas were reborn!

"True becomes false" naturally referred to the obscured Star. And "false becomes true" referred to the newborn imaginary Mountains and Seas. Li Fan, with his own power, had completely reversed the situation. Or rather, it was not Li Fan. It was 'True Return'!

"When true becomes false, false also becomes true. What a brilliant description!" Qiu Xin Hui, appearing amidst the resurrected infinite Mountains and Seas, approached Li Fan.

"The transformation of True and False is indeed infinitely profound."

However, Li Fan smiled wryly and remarked: "True cannot become true, and false cannot become false." He pointed in the direction where the Star had disappeared, his expression unreadable. "One can block the Star for a moment, but not for a lifetime."

This answer was beyond Qiu Xin Hui's expectations. He looked at the boundless, seemingly resurrected Mountains and Seas and asked: "How long can this last?"

"Unknown," Li Fan replied with only four words.

Qiu Xin Hui finally fell into complete silence. He sincerely asked: "Daoist Friend Fan, what do you think of our plan?"

Li Fan pondered for a moment, then slowly evaluated: "If the Star were not the Star, the plan could succeed. Unfortunately..."

Upon hearing this, Qiu Xin Hui's expression grew solemn, and he cupped his hands in salutation, seeking guidance: "Dare I ask Daoist Friend, what is the Star?"

"I am also in pursuit of that answer," Li Fan's response left Qiu Xin Hui speechless. The two stood within the desolate void, quietly observing the momentarily resurrected Mountains and Seas. With the newborn Mountains and Seas as their foundation, the surging dark tides of the desolate void seemed unable to harm them. After an unknown period, the Mountains and Seas seemed to have returned to their former peak state. The destruction of the Mountains and Seas appeared to have been a mere illusion.

Qiu Xin Hui finally spoke again: "Daoist Friend Fan, regarding our previous... 'Have we met before?'"

Li Fan finally managed a smile. "If we had never met, where would my 'True Return' have come from?"

Qiu Xin Hui looked puzzled. Li Fan smiled again, offering no further explanation. Instead, he said: "Let us return. There is no point in lingering here any longer."

Qiu Xin Hui sighed, but ultimately did not refuse.

*Thump thump thump...*

The clear sound of a heartbeat inexplicably arose. It grew heavier, resounding throughout the area. Outside the desolate void, the Star seemed to be reappearing. But a mysterious and powerful force was slowly permeating, Reversing everything. The heartbeat grew faster and faster. As if a rewind button had been pressed, the scenes that had transpired here replayed themselves, But in reverse. The flow of light and shadow accelerated, while the heartbeat grew fainter and fainter. When the sound completely faded...

At the end of the Mountains and Seas. Li Fan suddenly opened his eyes, scanning his surroundings. "What is this?" He looked at Qiu Xin Hui, who was smiling and observing him, as if he had just arrived at the end of the Mountains and Seas after traversing it, just like before. "I succeeded in activating 'True Return'?" "No. This is??" Faint images flickered in his mind. Just as Li Fan was about to investigate further, an intense pain struck him, Rendering him unable to concentrate and think. His entire body ached as if after a great battle, utterly exhausted. "What exactly happened? I remember it was supposed to be the final battle between the Mountains and Seas and the desolate void." Li Fan pressed his temples, trying to clear his muddled mind. "'True Return', right, 'True Return'!" Li Fan seemed to recall something, realizing with a jolt that 'True Return' might have been exposed and looked up sharply at Qiu Xin Hui. However, Qiu Xin Hui was still attending to the people of the Realm of Birth and Death, stabilizing their injuries, just as he had in his memory.

"I know Daoist Friend Fan may have many questions."

"Please be patient for a moment longer, and I will provide a full explanation."

Following his inner call, Li Fan's 'True Return' panel reappeared before his eyes. And at this point in time, shortly after he had donned the guise of the Profound Embryo, the binding force had not yet solidified. He could activate 'True Return' at any time. With newfound confidence, Li Fan nodded silently, waiting patiently for Qiu Xin Hui to finish resolving matters. During this period, Li Fan finally saw the final Saints of the Mountains and Seas again. However, apart from Qiu Xin Hui, they seemed completely unaware of what had transpired.

"This scene... could it be?" Recalling the similarities he had sensed between the Saints and 'True Return,' Li Fan began to form a conjecture about Qiu Xin Hui's true Dao.
